yuṣmad asmat gocarayoḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ tamaḥ viruddha svabhāvayoḥ aupapattau siddhāyām dharmāṇām sutarām aupapattiḥ asmad gocare viṣayiṇi cit ātmake yuṣmad gocarasya viṣayasya dharmāṇām adhyāsaḥ viṣayiṇaḥ dharmāṇām viṣaye adhyāsaḥ mithyā bhavitum yuktam ayoyasmi ayoya tām ayoya dharmān adhyasya aviveke atyata viviktayoḥ dharmiṇoḥ mithyājñā aimittaḥ aṛte mithuīkṛtya aham idam mama idam aisārgikaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ āhakaḥ ayam adhyāsaḥ ucyate rūpaḥ paratra avabhāsaḥ tam kecid yad adhyāsaḥ bhrama aye yad adhyāsaḥ viparīta kalpa ām vyabhicarati aubhavaḥ śuktikā rajata avabhāsate ekaḥ cadraḥ dvitīya katham puas pratyagātmay viṣaye adhyāsaḥ viṣaya dharmāṇām sarvaḥ puras avasthite viṣaye viṣayātaram adhyasyati yuṣmad apetasya aviṣaya bravīṣi ucyate tāvat ayam asmad viṣaya aparokṣa pratyagātma ayam viṣaye viṣayātaram adhyasitavyam apratyakṣe bālāḥ tala mali atā adhyasyati aviruddhaḥ pratyagātmay adhyāsaḥ tam etam evaṃlakṣaṇam adhyāsam paṇḍitāḥ avidyā mayate vastu avadhāraṇam vidyām āhuḥ yad adhyāsaḥ doṣeṇa aṇu mātreṇa sambadhyate tam etam avidyā ākhyam adhyasam puraskṛtya pramāṇa prameya vyavahārāḥ laukikāḥ vaidikāḥ pravṛttāḥ śāstrāṇi parāṇi katham avidyāvat viṣayāṇi pramāṇāi śāstrāṇi ucyate idriya pramātṛ aupapattau pramāṇa pravṛtti aupapatteḥ idriyāṇi vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati adhiṣṭhāam vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati adhyasta dehe kaścid vyāpriyate etasmin sarvasmin asaṅgasya pramātṛ pramātṛ atareṇa pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ tasmāt avidyāvat viṣayāṇi ādīni śāstrāṇi paśu ādibhiḥ paśu ādibhiḥ śrotra ādīnām vijñāe pratikūle jāte aukūle pravartate daṇḍa udyata karam abhimukham upalabhya gām hatum ayam icchati palāyitum ārabhate harita pūrṇa pāṇim upalabhya tam abhimukhībhavati puruṣāḥ krūra dṛṣṭī ākrośataḥ khaḍga udyata karāḥ balavataḥ upalabhya viparītā pravartate paśu ādibhiḥ puruṣāṇām pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ paśu ādīām prasiddhaḥ aviveka puraḥasaraḥ vyavahāraḥ vyutpattimatām puruṣāṇām vyavahāraḥ kālaḥ śāstrīye vyavahāre yadi kārī adhikriyate adhikāre apekṣyate aupayogāt tathābhūta vijñāāt pravartamāam śāstram avidyāvat viṣaya ātivartate brāhmaṇaḥ yajeta ityādī śāstrāṇi varṇa āśrama vayaḥ adhyāsam āśritya pravartate adhyāsaḥ buddhiḥ avocāma bhāryā vikaleṣu sakaleṣu aham vikalaḥ sakalaḥ bāhya dharmāḥ adhyasyati dharmāḥ sthūlaḥ aham kṛśaḥ aham gauḥ aham tiṣṭhāmi gacchāmi laṅghayāmi idriya dharmā mūkaḥ kāṇaḥ klībaḥ badhiraḥ adhas aham ataḥkaraṇa dharmā saṃkalpa vicikitsā adhyavasāya ādī aham aśeṣa isva pracāra sākṣiṇi pratyagātmay adhyasya tam sākṣiṇam ataḥkaraṇa adhyasyati ayam aisargikaḥ adhyāsaḥ mithyā rūpaḥ pravartakaḥ pratyakṣaḥ hetoḥ prahāṇāya pratipattaye ārabhyate ayam vayam asyām śārīraka mīmāṃsāyām pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ vedāta mīmāṃsā śāstrasya vyācikhyāsitasya idam ādimam sūtram prathama udhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ adhikaraṇam atra parigṛhyate ādhikāra jijñāsāyāḥ adhikārya maṅgalasya arthe samavayā atara prayuktaḥ athaśabdaḥ śrutyāḥ maṅgala prayojaḥ bhavati apekṣāyāḥ phalataḥ āataryā vyatirekāt āataryā tve vṛttam veda adhyayam vṛttam vaktavyam svādhyāya adhyaya āataryam avabodha āataryam viśeṣaḥ jijñāsāyāḥ kramasya kramaḥ vivakṣitaḥ śeṣi tve adhikṛta adhikāre pramāṇa jijñāsayoḥ jijñāsya abhyudaya jñāam iḥśreyasa jñāam bhavyaḥ dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ jñā kāle jijñāsyam tatram coda pravṛtti yā codaā dharmasya lakṣaṇam viṣaye iyuñjāā avabodhayati brahmacodaā avabodhayati kevalam avabodhasya akṣa saṃikarṣeṇa avabodhe tasmāt kim vaktavyam upadiśyate ucyate amutra virāgaḥ sādha saṃpad mumukṣu teṣu satsu jijñāsāyāḥ ūrdhvam śakyate jijñāsitum jñātum viparyaye tasmāt athaśabde upadiśyate hetvarthaḥ yasmāt vedaḥ agihotra ādīām śreyaḥ sādhaāām aitya phalatām citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate amutra puṇya citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate jñāāt ityādiḥ tasmāt kartavyā brahmaṇaḥ vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇam jāti ataram āśaṅkitavyam brahmaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭhī śeṣe jijñāsya jijñāsāyāḥ ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe brahmaṇaḥ as virudhyate eṣṭha pratyakṣam brahmaṇaḥ utsṛjya sāmāya dvāreṇa parokṣam kalpayataḥ vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ vyarthaḥ aśeṣa vicāra ārtha pradhā parigrahe apekṣitāām ākṣipta tasmi pradhāe parigṛhīte yaiḥ jijñāsitaiḥ jijñāsitam bhavati ākṣiptāy sūtrayitavyāi rājā asau gacchati ukte parivārasya rājñaḥ bhavati augamāt vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ vijijñāsasva pratyakṣam brahmaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe bhavati tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭhī jñātum icchā avagati paryatam vācyāyāḥ icchāyāḥ viṣaya icchāyāḥ pramāṇeā avagatum iṣṭam avagatiḥ tasmāt jijñāsitavyam puar prasiddham aprasiddham yadi prasiddham jijñāsitavyam aprasiddham śakyam jijñāsitum ucyate tāvat aśuddha buddha svabhāvam sarvajñam samavitam pratīyate bṛṃhateḥ dhātoḥ augamāt sarvasya astitva prasiddhiḥ sarvaḥ astitvam pratyeti aham asmi yadi astitva prasiddhiḥ sarvaḥ lokaḥ aham asmi pratīyāt yadi tarhi prasiddham jñātam ajijñāsya vipratipatteḥ caitaya viśiṣṭam prākṛtāḥ laukāyatikāḥ idriyāṇi apare vijñāa kṣaṇikam apare vyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī bhoktā apare bhoktā kevalam vyatiriktaḥ īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ śaktiḥ kecid bhoktuḥ apare bahavaḥ vipratipaāḥ yukti ābhāsa samāśrayāḥ vicārya kiṃcid iḥśreyasāt iyāt tasmāt avirodhi upakaraṇā prastūyate jijñāsitavyam kiṃlakṣaṇam bhagavān sūtrakāraḥ jama adhikaraṇam jamaḥ utpattiḥ saṃvijñāḥ bahuvrīhiḥ jama bhaṅgam samāsa śrutiirdeśa vastu vṛtta śrutiirdeśaḥ tāvat imā idam anyā any bhūtāi jāyate asmi vākye krama darśaāt vastu vṛttam labdha sattākasya dharmiṇaḥ pralaya saṃidhāpitasya dharmiṇaḥ idam irdeśaḥ ṣaṣṭhī kāraṇaiḥ deśaḥ jagataḥ āma rūpābhyām vyākṛtasya saṃyuktasya pratiiyata deśa kā laimitta āśrayasya citya raca rūpasya sarvajñāt śakteḥ kāraṇāt bhavati śeṣaḥ vikārāṇām triṣu grahaṇam yāska paripaṭhitāām jāyate ityādīām grahaṇe jagataḥ kāle mūlakāraṇāt sthitiāḥ jagataḥ gṛhītāḥ syuḥ āśaṅkyeta yā utpattiḥ brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇāt sthitiḥ pralayaḥ gṛhyate ukta viśeṣaṇasya jagataḥ ukta viśeṣaṇam īśvaram muktvā ayataḥ aṇubhyaḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyam svabhāvataḥ deśa kāla aimittāām upādāāt etat saṃsāri vyatirikta īśvara astitva sādhaam sūtrāṇām sūtraiḥ udāhṛtya vicāryate vicāraṇa adhyavasāaiḥ vṛttā avagatiḥ āumā pramāṇa ataraiḥ vṛttā satsu vedāta vākyeṣu jagataḥ vādiṣu ārḍhyāya vedāta avirodhi pramāṇam śrutyā tarkasya abhyupeta śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ śrutiḥ paṇḍitaḥ medhāvī upasaṃpadyeta ācārya puruṣaḥ veda sāhāyyam jijñasāyām iva pramāṇam jijñāsāyām kiṃtu ubhava yathāsaṃbhavam pramāṇam vastu viṣaya jñāasya kartavye viṣaye āubhava ādīām prāmāṇyam adhī lābha kartavyasya kartum kartum ayathā kartum śakyam laukikam vaidikam gacchati padbhyām ayathā gacchati atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti udite juhoti audite juhoti pratiṣedhāḥ atra arthavataḥ syuḥ utsarga apavādāḥ vastu aivam āsti vikalpyate vikalpaāḥ apekṣāḥ kim tarhi vastutatram sthāṇau sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ tattva jñāam bhavati puruṣaḥ yaḥ mithyā jñāam sthāṇuḥ tattva jñāam vastu vastu viṣayāṇām prāmāṇyam vastu tatram vastu viṣaya vastu viṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇa atara viṣaya arthikā prāptā svabhāvataḥ viṣaya viṣayāṇi idriyāṇi viṣayāṇi idriya viṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ idam brahmaṇā saṃbaddham gṛhyeta gṛhyamāṇam kim brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kim keacid saṃbaddham śakyam tasmāt jama sūtram kim tarhi vedāta pradarśa kim puas vedāta vākyam sūtreṇa bhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ varuṇam pitaram upasasāra adhīhi bhagavaḥ upakramya vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate jīvati prayati abhisaṃviśati vijijñāsasva irṇaya vākyam āadāt khalu imāi bhūtāi jāyate jīvati prayati abhisaṃviśati evaṃjātīyakāi vākyāi aśuddha buddham ukta svabhāva sarvajña viṣayāṇi udāhartavyāi sarvajñam upakṣiptam śāstrayoitvāt sarvajñam upakṣiptam mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya avadyotiḥ sarvajña kalpasya kāraṇam īdṛśasya śāstrasya ṛgveda lakṣaṇasya sarvajña āvitasya sarvajña ādayataḥ vistara śāstram yasmāt saṃbhavati vyākaraṇa deśa prasiddham kimu vaktavyam tiryak mauṣya varṇa āśrama pravibhāga hetoḥ ṛgveda ākhyasya sarvajña ākarasya yasmai mahataḥ bhūtāt saṃbhavaḥ mahataḥ etat ṛgvedaḥ ityādi mahataḥ sarvajña śaktimat athavā ṛgveda śāstram kāraṇam pramāṇam brahmaṇaḥ yathāvat śāstrāt pramāṇāt jagataḥ jama kāraṇam adhigamyate abhiprāyaḥ śāstram udāhṛtam sūtre imāi bhūtāi jāyate ityādi kimartham tarhi idam sūtram yāvatā sūtreṇa evaṃjātīyakam śāstram udāharatā brahmaṇaḥ darśitam ucyate sūtra akṣareṇa spaṣṭam jama sūtreṇa kevalam upayastam āśaṅkyeta tām āśaṅkām ivartayitum idam sūtram pravavṛte katham brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇaka ucyate yāvatā āmāyasya āarthakyam śāstrasya pradarśitam saṃbhavati viṣaya upādeya rahite arodīt evamādīām āarthakyam mā bhūt ekavākya arthe syuḥ stāvaka tve ārthavat matrāṇām iṣe tvā ityādīām samavāyi kvacid veda vākyāām saṃsparśam dṛṣṭā pariiṣṭhite vastu svarūpe saṃbhavati viṣaya tasmāt apekṣita brahmaṇaḥ prāpte ucyate samavayāt samavayā adhikaraṇam tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣa vyāvṛtti sarvajñam laya kāraṇam vedāta śāstrāt avagamyate katham samavayāt sarveṣu tātparyeṇa etasya arthasya samaugatāi sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam vai idam ekaḥ agre āsīt etat aparam ataram bāhyam ayam idam amṛtam purastāt gatāām padāām viṣaye samavaye yuktā yuktā pratipāda apara avasīyate kam paśyet ityādi kāraka phalaiḥ ākaraṇa pariiṣṭhita vastu tve viṣaya brahmaṇaḥ asi bhāvasya śāstram upādeya rahita āarthakyam eṣa upādeya śūya ātmatā avagamāt kleśa prahāṇāt pratipāda gata upāsa tve kaścid brahmaṇaḥ upāsaā saṃbhavati ekatve upādeya śūya kāraka dvaita vijñā upamarda dvaita vijñāasya brahmaṇaḥ pratipādyeta yadi veda vākyāām saṃsparśam vijñāasya paryata tvā viṣayasya śāstrasya prāmāṇyam śakyam pratyākhyātum prāmāṇyam prāmāṇyam apekṣyeta tasmāt siddham brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇaka atra apare pratyavatiṣṭhate yadi pramāṇakam pratipatti viṣaya śāstreṇa samarpyate alaukikāy śāstreṇa samarpyate kutas etat pravṛtti ivṛtti prayoja aparatvāt śāstrasya tātparya vidām avabodha kriyāyāḥ pravartakam bhūtāām samāmāyaḥ āmāyasya āarthakyam kvacid viṣaya viśeṣe pravartayat kutaścid viṣaya viśeṣāḥ śāstram upayuktam paratve vidhīyate kāmasya jñāam vidhīyate yuktam jijñāsya vailakṣaṇyam karmakāṇḍe bhavya dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ ityaiḥ vṛttam jijñāsyam jñā phalāt vilakṣaṇam jñā bhavitum arhati ārhati bhavitum prayuktasya brahmaṇaḥ vai are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ apahata pāpmā veṣṭavyaḥ vijijñāsitavyaḥ upāsīta ātmāam lokam upāsīta veda brahmā bhavati ityādiṣu satsu satsu aḥ kim ākāṅkṣāyām upayuktāḥ ityaḥ sarvajñaḥ gataḥ aśuddha buddha svabhāvaḥ evamādayaḥ upāsaāt mokṣaḥ bhaviṣyati saptadvīpā vasumatī rājā asau gacchati ityādi āarthakyam rajjuḥ iyam sarpaḥ ityādau etat yadi rajju mātreṇa iva sarpa bhrātiḥ saṃsāri bhrātiḥ mātreṇa iva ṛtate brahmaṇaḥ yathāpūrvam duḥkha saṃsāri darśaāt śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ kālayoḥ darśaāt tasmāt pratipatti viṣaya pramāṇakam abhyupagatavyam atra abhidhīyate phalayoḥ śārīram vācikam māasam siddham ākhyam yad viṣayā sūtritā adharmaḥ hiṃsā coda ālakṣaṇa jijñāsyaḥ parihārāya tayoḥ coda ālakṣaṇayoḥ aarthayoḥ adharmayoḥ phale pratyakṣe duḥkhe viṣaya idriya saṃyoga jaye sthāvarāteṣu prasiddhe mauṣya ārabhya brahmāteṣu dehavatsu tāratamyam hetoḥ dharmasya tāratamyam gamyate tāratamyāt adhikāri tāratamyam prasiddham arthi sāmarthya vidvas kṛtam adhikāri tāratamyam uttareṇa pathā gamaam kevalaiḥ dhūma pathā gamaam tāratamyam sādhaa tāramyam śāstrāt yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā asmāt gamyate mauṣī lavaḥ gamyate tāratamye ūrdhva gateṣu adhas gateṣu dehavatsu duḥkha tāratamya darśaāt hetoḥ adharmasya tāratamyam gamyate avidyā doṣavatām adharma tāratamya aimittam upādāa pūrvakam duḥkha tāratamyam aityam rūpam yāya prasiddham śrutiḥ ha vai śarīrasya apriyayoḥ apahatiḥ varṇitam rūpam auvadati aśarīram vāva satam apriye spṛśataḥ apriya sparśa ākhyasya aśarīra tvasya pratiṣidhyate gamyate tve apriya sparśa pratiṣedhaḥ opapadyeta aśarīra svābhāvika aśarīram śarīreṣu avastheṣu avasthitam vibhum matvā dhīraḥ śocati aprāṇaḥ śubhraḥ saṅgaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ākhyam aśarīra ityam siddham kiṃcid pariṇāmi ityam vikriyamāṇe idam buddhiḥ sāṃkhyāām guṇāḥ idam pāramārthikam kūṭasthaityam vyāpi vikriyā rahitam atṛptam svayam svabhāvam adharmau kāryeṇa kāla trayam opāvartete etat aśarīra ākhyam ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt bhavyāt ityādi śrutibhyaḥ yasya iyam prastutā yadi kartavya tve upadiśyeta kartavyea sādhyaḥ mokṣaḥ abhyupagamyeta aityaḥ ukta phaleṣu tāratamya avasthiteṣu aityeṣu kaścid atiśayaḥ mokṣaḥ prasajyeta ityaḥ mokṣaḥ sarvaiḥ vādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate yuktaḥ veda bhavati kṣīyate karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare brahmaṇaḥ vidvā bibheti kutas caa abhayam vai si am avet aham asmi tasmāt sarvam abhavat kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ mokṣam darśayatyaḥ madhye kāryātaram vārayati ha etat paśya ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham mauḥ abhavam sūryaḥ darśa bhāvayoḥ madhye kartavya ātara vāraṇāya udāhāryam tiṣṭha gāyati tiṣṭhati gāyatyoḥ madhye kartṛkam ātaram āsti gamyate pitā smākam avidyāyāḥ pāram tārayasi me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram bhagavā evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ ācārya praṇītam yāya upabṛṃhitam sūtram apāye apavargaḥ mithyājñā apāyaḥ vijñāāt bhavati idam vijñāam saṃpad rūpam vai viśvedevāḥ tea lokam jayati adhyāsa rūpam mao upāsīta ādityaḥ ādeśaḥ maaāditya adhyāsaḥ yaḥ gaimittam vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ itivat āpi ājya avekṣaṇa rūpam saṃpad rūpe vijñāe bhyupagamyamāe asi aham asmi ayam evamādīām vākyāām vastu pratipāda pīḍyeta bhidyate hṛdayagrathiḥ chidyate saṃśayāḥ evamādīn avidyā vṛtti śravaṇāy uparudhyera veda brahmā bhavati saṃpad tve saṃpad tve saṃpad rūpam vijñāam kim tarhi vastu evaṃbhūtasya brahmaṇas kayācid yuktyā śakyaḥ āupraveśaḥ kalpayitum brahmaṇaḥ viditāt viditāt adhi vidi tam ke vijāīyāt upāsti pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati vācā abhyuditam abhyudyate aviṣaya brahmaṇaḥ viddhi idam idam upāsate aviṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ avidyā kalpita evṛtti paratvāt śāstrasya śāstram idaṃtayā viṣaya pratipipādayiṣati kim tarhi pratyagātma tve aviṣaya pratipādayat avidyā kalpitam vedya veditṛ veda bhedam apaayati śāstram yasya amatam matam matam yasya veda avijñātam vijāatām vijñātam avijāatām draṣṭāram paśyeḥ śrotāram śrṛṇuyāḥ mateḥ matāram mavīthāḥ vijñāteḥ vijñātāram evamādi samarpaṇā mokṣasya aitya yasya utpādyaḥ mokṣaḥ māasam vācikam kāyikam apekṣate yuktam vikārya tve tayoḥ pakṣayoḥ mokṣasya dhruvam aitya dadhi vikāryam utpādyam ghaṭa svātma tve satī āpya vyatirikta tve brahmaṇaḥ āpya tve āpta sarveṇa brahmaṇaḥ ākāśasya iva saṃskāryaḥ mokṣaḥ vyāpāram apekṣeta saṃskāraḥ saṃskāryasya tāvat saṃbhavati mokṣasya āpi aśuddha tvā mokṣasya dharmaḥ tirobhūtaḥ mokṣaḥ kriyayā ātmai saṃskriyamāṇe bhivyajyate ādarśe saṃskriyamāṇe bhāsvara dharmaḥ aupapatteḥ yad āśrayā tam vikurvatī labhate yadi kriyayā vikriyeta aitya prasajyeta avikāryaḥ yam ucyate bādhyera aiṣṭam āśrayā ātman saṃbhavati kriyāyāḥ aviṣaya tvā saṃskriyate āśrayayā kriyayā dehī saṃskriyamāṇaḥ saṃhatasya avidyā gṛhītasya ātmaaḥ saṃskriyamāṇa pratyakṣam sāācama ādeḥ samavāyi āśrayayā saṃhataḥ kaścid avidyayā tve parigṛhītaḥ saṃskriyate yuktam dhātu sāmyea saṃhatasya ārogya aham arogaḥ buddhiḥ utpadyate aham śuddhaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ buddhiḥ utpadyate saṃskriyate saṃhataḥ ahaṃkartrā ahaṃpratyaya viṣayeṇa sarvāḥ kriyāḥ āśāti tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti ayaḥ bhicākaśīti matra bhoktā āhuḥ maīṣiṇaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ gūḍhaḥ vyāpī atarātmā adhyakṣaḥ adhivāsaḥ sākṣī cetā kevalaḥ irguṇaḥ paryāgāt śukram akāyam avraṇam sāviram śuddham pāpa viddham etau matrau aśuddha tām brahmaṇaḥ mokṣaḥ saṃskāryaḥ mokṣaḥ mokṣam śakyam keacid darśayitum tasmāt ekam muktvā kriyāyāḥ opapadyate jñāam vastu svarūpaiḥ codyate yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam tām maasā dhyāyet vaṣaṭ kariṣye saṃdhyām maasā dhyāyet evamādiṣu citaam yadi māasam puruṣeṇa kartum kartum ayathā kartum śakyam pramāṇa jayam pramāṇam vastu viṣayam kartum kartum ayathā kartum śakyam kevalam vastutatram puruṣatatram tasmāt māasa tve vailakṣaṇyam puruṣaḥ vāva gautama āgiḥ yoṣā vāva gautama āgiḥ atra yoṣit puruṣayoḥ agi buddhiḥ māasī bhavati kevala coda ājaya tatrā yā prasiddhe gau gi buddhiḥ tatrā kim tarhi viṣaya vastu etat pramāṇa viṣaya vastuṣu veditavyam viṣayam viṣaye liṅ śrūyamāṇāḥ aiyojya viṣaya kuṇṭhībhavati upala prayukta kṣura taikṣṇya aheya aupādeya vastu viṣaya tarhi are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ ityādīi chāyāi svābhāvika pravṛtti viṣaya vimukhīkaraṇa arthāi brūmaḥ yaḥ bahirmukhaḥ pravartate puruṣaḥ iṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣ me bhūyāt aiṣṭam mā bhūt ātyatikam labhate tam ātyatika vāñchiam svābhāvikāt karaṇa saṃghāta pravṛtti gocarāt vimukhīkṛtya pratyagātma srotaḥ pravartayati are draṣṭavyaḥ ityādi āveṣaṇāya pravṛttasya aheyam aupādeyam tattvam upadiśyate idam sarvam ayam sarvam abhūt kam paśyet vijñātāram are vijñātāram are ayam ityādibhiḥ kartavya pradhāam jñāam bhavati abhyupagamyate alaṃkāraḥ ayam asmākam ātmau agatau satyām kartavya hāiḥ kṛtakṛtya śrutiḥ vijāīyāt ayam asmi pūruṣaḥ kim iccha kasya kāmāya etat buddhvā buddhim āsyāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ bhārataḥ smṛtiḥ pratipatti brahmaṇaḥ samarpaṇam kecid āhuḥ kevala vastu vādī veda bhāgaḥ āsti aupaiṣadasya puruṣasya yaśeṣa adhigataḥ saṃsārī rūpaḥ utpādi caturvidha dravya vilakṣaṇaḥ sthaḥ āsau āsti ādhigamyate śakyam vaditum eṣaḥ eti eti pratyākhyātum aśakya yaḥ irā ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya upaiṣatsu vijñāyate aupapaam pratyukta ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya vyatirekeṇa sākṣī sthaḥ samaḥ ekaḥ kūṭasthaityaḥ puruṣaḥ kāṇḍe samaye kaścid adhigataḥ sarvasya kaścid pratyākhyātum śakyaḥ etum heyaḥ āpī upādeyaḥ sarvam viaśyat jātam viaśyati puruṣaḥ vikriyā kūṭasthaityaḥ aśuddha buddha svabhāvaḥ tasmāt puruṣāḥ kiṃcid kāṣṭhā parā gatiḥ tam aupaiṣadam pṛcchāmi aupaiṣada viśeṣaṇam puruṣasya upaiṣatsu vastu veda bhāgaḥ sāhasa tātparya vidām evamādi viṣaya abhiprāyam draṣṭavyam āmāyasya āarthakyam arthāām etat upadeśāām āarthakya vastu upadiśati kūṭasthaityam upadiśati kaḥ hetuḥ bhavati akriyā tve sādhaa eṣa tve bhavati yadi kim tava ucyate aavagata vastu bhavitum arhati avagatyā mithyājñāasya hetoḥ kriyate aviśiṣṭam brāhmaṇaḥ hatavyaḥ evamādyā upadiśyate sādhaam akriyā arthāām arthakaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ hatavyaḥ ityādi ivṛtti upadeśāām āarthakyam prāptam aiṣṭam svabhāva prāpta hati au rāgeṇa añaḥ śakyam aprāpta kalpayitum vyatirekeṇa añaḥ eṣa svabhāvaḥ bodhayati buddhiḥ audāsīye kāraṇam svayam upaśāmyati tasmāt prasakta aivṛtti audāsīyam brāhmaṇaḥ hatavyaḥ ityādiṣu mayāmahe prajāpati vrata tasmāt draṣṭavyam vastu aarthakam saptadvīpā vasumatī ityādi parihṛtam rajjuḥ iyam sarpaḥ brahmaṇaḥ yathāpūrvam saṃsāri darśaāḥ rajju kathaa atra ucyate āvagata bhāvasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri śakyam darśayitum veda pramāṇa jaita abhimāiḥ duḥkha bhaya veda pramāṇa jaita avagame abhimāai vṛttau mithyājñā aimittam duḥkha bhaya bhavati śakyam kalpayitum gṛhasthasya dhaā abhimāiḥ dhaā apahāra aimittam duḥkham pravrajitasya dhaā abhimāa rahitasya dhaā apahāra aimittam duḥkham bhavati kuṇḍaliaḥ kuṇḍali abhimāaimittam sukham viyuktasya kuṇḍali abhimāa rahitasya kuṇḍali abhimāaimittam sukham bhavati śrutyā aśarīram vāva satam apriye spṛśataḥ patite jīvataḥ mithyājñā aimitta ātmaaḥ abhimā lakṣaṇam mithyājñāam muktvā ayataḥ śakyam kalpayitum aśarīra aimitta avocāma adharma aimittam aśarīra saṃbadhasya asiddha adharmayoḥ asiddheḥ saṃbadhasya adharmayoḥ tvasya aupapatteḥ rāja prabhṛtīām ādibhiḥ svāmi saṃbadha nimittam kiṃcid śakyam kalpayitum mithyā abhimāaḥ pratyakṣaḥ atra āhuḥ vyatiriktasya ātmīye ādau aham mithyā vastu bhedasya gauṇa yasya prasiddhaḥ vastu bhedaḥ kesara māā ākṛti viśeṣaḥ vaya vyatirekābhyām siṃha mukhyaḥ yaḥ siddhaḥ ayaḥ puruṣaḥ prāyikaiḥ kraurya śaurya ādibhiḥ siṃha guṇaiḥ siddhaḥ tasmin puruṣe siṃha pratyayau gauṇau bhavataḥ vastu bhedasya bhavataḥ gauṇau mada adhakāre sthāṇuḥ ayam gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣe pratyayau sthāṇu viṣayau śuktikāyām akasmāt rajatam idam pratyayau saṃghāte aham pratyayau avivekena utpadyamāau katham gauṇau śakyau vaditum paṇḍitāām aja avi pālāām iva viviktau pratyayau bhavataḥ tasmāt vyatirikta astitva vādiām dehāt āvaham pratyayaḥ mithyā tasmāt mithyāpratyaya tvasya siddham jīvataḥ viduṣaḥ vidviṣayā śrutiḥ valmīke mṛtā pratyastā śayīta idam śete ayam aśarīraḥ mṛtaḥ iva karṇaḥ karṇaḥ iva avāc iva maāḥ amaāḥ iva prāṇo iva smṛtiḥ sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā ityādyā sthita prajñasya lakṣaṇāya ācakṣāṇāḥ viduṣaḥ avagata bhāvasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri yasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri asau avagata aavadyam parācīayoḥ maa aididhyāsayoḥ paryavasāyi avagati tvā maa aididhyāsayoḥ yadi ārabhyamāṇam ārabhyeta pariśiṣṭa kratu arthayoḥ jijñāsāḥ aikya avagatiḥ apratijñātā yuktaḥ ārambhaḥ tasmāt aham asmi etat vidhayaḥ itarāṇi aheya aupādeya advaita avagatau satyām apramātṛkāṇi pramāṇāi bhavitum arhati āhuḥ gauṇa mithyā sattve bādhaāt sat aham bodhe katham bhavet pramātṛ aḥ aviṣṭaḥ pramātā pāpma varjitaḥ pratyayaḥ kalpitaḥ laukikam idam pramāṇam aiścayāt tāvat avagati prayojaāām ātmai tātparyeṇa atareṇa sarvajñam laya kāraṇam sāṃkhya pariiṣṭhitam vastu pramāṇa atara gamyam yojayati sarveṣu vedātavākyeṣu sṛṣṭi viṣayeṣu kāryeṇa kāraṇam pradhā apuruṣa saṃyogāḥ āumeyāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ pratipattayaḥ pūrvapakṣīkṛtya sāṃkhyāḥ pradhāam triguṇam acetaam svatatram kāraṇam āhuḥ sarvajñasya śakteḥ brahmaṇaḥ pradarśayati avocaḥ yojayitum śakyate tāvat viṣayam sarvajña katham sattva dharmaḥ sattvāt saṃjāyate sattva dharmeṇa karaṇavataḥ puruṣāḥ sarvajñāḥ yogiḥ prasiddhāḥ sattvasya sarvajña prasiddham kevalasya karaṇasya puruṣasya mātrasya sarvajña kiṃcijjñatvam kalpayitum śakyam triguṇa pradhā sarvajñā akāraṇa sattvam pradhā avasthāyām vidyate pradhā acetaasya sarvajña upacaryate vedāta vākyeṣu avaśyam tvayā sarvajñam abhyupagacchatā sarvajña aśaktimat sarvajña abhyupagatavyam sarvadā viṣayam jñāam kurvat vartate jñā itya tve jñā akriyām svātatryam brahmaṇaḥ hīyeta aityam jñā akriyāyāḥ uparame uparameta sarvajña aśaktimat tve sarvajña āpatati utpatteḥ iṣyate tvayā idriya ādīām jñā utpattiḥ kasyacid pradhāasya ātmakasya pariṇāma upapattiḥ mṛd āsaṃhatasya ātmakasya brahmaṇaḥ prāpte idam sūtram ārabhyate āśabdam adhikaraṇam sāṃkhya parikalpitam acetaam pradhāam jagataḥ kāraṇam śakyam āśrayitum aśabdam katham aśabda īkṣitṛ kāraṇasya katham śrūyate sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam upakramya aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya sṛjate idam vācyam āma vyākṛtam utpatteḥ sat avadhārya prakṛtasya sat vācyasya īkṣaṇa pūrvakam prabhṛteḥ sraṣṭṛ vai idam ekaḥ agre āsīt āyat kiṃcaa miṣat īkṣata lokāḥ sṛjai imān lokāḥ asṛjata īkṣā pūrvikām sṛṣṭim ācaṣṭe kvacid ṣoḍaśa kalam prastutya īkṣāṃcakre prāṇam asṛjata dhātvarthairdeśaḥ bhipretaḥ yajateḥ dhātuirdeśaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ yasya jñāa mayam tapaḥ tasmāt etat āma rūpam jāyate evamādīn sarvajña īśvara parāṇi vākyāi udāhartavyāi sattva dharmeṇa sarvajñam pradhāam bhaviṣyati pradhā avasthāyām sattva dharmaḥ saṃbhavati sarvajñam bhaviṣyati yadi sāmye sattva vyapāśrayām jñā aśaktim āśritya sarvajñam pradhā am ucyeta aimittam sarvajña upapam audāharaṇam puraḥ akṣi imittam īkṣitṛ pradhā kalpyeta ayaḥ piṇḍa ādeḥ dagdhṛ yaimittam īkṣitṛ pradhā sarvajñam mukhyam jagataḥ kāraṇam yuktam puar brahmaṇaḥ mukhyam sarvajña ajñā akriya tve jñā akriyām svātatrya atra ucyate idam tāvat praṣṭavyaḥ katham sarvajña hāiḥ yasya viṣaya avabhāsa akṣamam sarvajñaḥ vipratiṣiddham aitya tve jñāasya kadācid jñāaitya tve jñā aviṣayaḥ svātatrya opapadyate pratata auṣṇya prakāśe savitari dahati prakāśayati svātatrya darśaāt savituḥ dāhya prakāśya saṃyoge dahati prakāśayati brahmaṇaḥ utpatteḥ viṣamaḥ savitā prakāśate darśaāt jñā brahmaṇaḥ aikṣata vaiṣamyam apekṣāyām brahmaṇi īkṣitṛ śrutayaḥ sutarām kim puas utpatteḥ īśvara jñāasya viṣayaḥ bhavati tattva āyatvābhyām airvacaīye āma rūpe avyākṛte vyācikīrṣite brūmaḥ yad prasādāt yogiām atīta āāgata viṣayam pratyakṣam jñāam icchati yoga kim vaktavyam asiddhasya īśvarasya sṛṣṭi saṃhṛti viṣayam bhavati utpatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ codyam avatarati savitṛ brahmaṇaḥ avidyā ādimataḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ jñā utpattiḥ jñā pratibadha rahitasya īśvarasya matrau imau īśvarasya tām vidyate samaḥ abhyadhikaḥ parā śaktiḥ vividhā śrūyate svābhāvikī jñā abala pāṇi pādaḥ grahītā paśyati śrṛṇoti upādhi saṃbadhaḥ iṣyate ghaṭa karaka giri guhā upādhi saṃbadhaḥ iva vyomaḥ kṛtaḥ vyavahāraḥ lokasya ghaṭa chidram karaka chidram ityādiḥ vyatireke kṛtā ghaṭa mithyā buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā saṃghāta upādhi aupacārikam kalpyate aikṣata aikṣata cetaayoḥ ap tejasoḥ ceta upacāra darśaāt tasmāt sat kartṛkam īkṣaṇam aupacārikam gamyate upacāra prāye vacaāt prāpte idam sūtram ārabhyate pradhāam acetaam sat vācyam aupacārikam īkṣitṛ ap tejasoḥ iva kasmāt sat somya idam agre āsīt upakramya aikṣata asṛjata tejobaāām sṛṣṭim uktvā prakṛtam sat śabdea parāmṛśya iyam aikṣata hata aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ āma bhadraseaḥ apavargau kurvat upakaroti rājñaḥ iva bhṛtyaḥ saṃdhi vigraha athavā ekaḥ athavā ekaḥ bhaviṣyati bhūtātmā idriya prayoga darśaāt ekaḥ kutas etat gauṇa uttaram paṭhati taiṣṭhasya bhavitum arhati prakṛtam sat aṇimāam ādāya asi śvetaketo śvetaketoḥ mokṣayitavyasya taiṣṭhām upadiśya veda tāvat ciram saṃpatsye yadi acetaam pradhāam sat vācyam asi grāhayet mumukṣum viparīta vādi śāstram aartham ṛcchet tasmāt svarga arthi ogi hotra sādhaam yathābhūtam upadiśati mumukṣoḥ tattvam asi śvetaketo yathābhūtam ātmāam upadiśati yuktam abhisaṃdhasya ayathā amukhye sat tattva upadeśe aham puruṣasya prasiddham eha ucyate yaḥ prakṛtaḥ sat vācyaḥ tam apītaḥ bhavati apigataḥ bhavati pūrvasya eteḥ laya prasiddham prabhava apyayau pralayayoḥ prayoga darśaāt jīvaḥ jāgarti vāsaā viśiṣṭaḥ avasthāyām cetae apyayam cetaāām sat vācyam jagataḥ kāraṇam ācetaam pradhāam kutas pradhāam jagataḥ kāraṇam sāmāyāt yadi tārkika samaye iva bhiā avaga gatiḥ abhaviṣyat kvacid cetaam jagataḥ kāraṇam pārameśvaram rūpam upadiśyate bhavati śāstram aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam ityādi dharmaiḥ kaiścid viśiṣṭaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsya tve nirdiśyate karmā kāmaḥ gadhaḥ rasaḥ ityādi bhaviṣyati ādhāra jīvebhyaḥ yaḥ īśvara ūtaryāmī yaḥ āditye tiṣṭha ādityāt ataraḥ yam ādityaḥ ataraḥ ya veda yasya ādityaḥ yaḥ ādityam ataraḥ yamayati eṣa ataryāmī amṛtaḥ atare ādityāt ataraḥ yam ādityaḥ veda vedituḥ ādityāt vijñā oya utaryāmī spaṣṭam irdiśyate apyatara āditye puruṣaḥ bhavitum arhati sāmāyāt tasmāt parameśvaraḥ upadiśyate siddham adhikaraṇam idam āmaati lokasya kā gatiḥ ha uvāca ha vai imāi bhūtāy ākāśāt samutpadyate ākāśam astam yati ebhyaḥ jyāyāḥ parāyaṇam saṃśayaḥ kim śabdena abhidhīyate uta bhūtākāśam kutas saṃśayaḥ ubhayatra prayoga darśaāt viśeṣe tāvat su prasiddhaḥ vedayoḥ brahmaṇi kvacid vaśāt asādhāraṇa bhavati eṣaḥ ha vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ yad atarā evamādau saṃśayaḥ kim puar atra yuktam bhūtākāśam kutas prasiddhatareṇa prayogeṇa śīghram buddhim ārohati ayam sādhāraṇaḥ śakyaḥ vijñātum tasmāt brahmaṇi bhavitum arhati vibhu ādibhiḥ bahubhiḥ dharmaiḥ sadṛśam bhavati saṃbhave rthaḥ grahaṇam arhati saṃbhavati mukhyasya ākāśasya grahaṇam bhūtākāśa parigrahe śeṣaḥ o ha vai imāi bhūtāni ākāśāt samutpadyate ityādiḥ eṣa bhūtākāśasya vāyu vijñāyate tasmāt vai etasmāt saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ ityādi aparāyaṇa tve atara upapadyete bhūtākāśasya tasmāt bhūtākāśasya grahaṇam prāpte brūmaḥ śabdena brahmaṇaḥ grahaṇam yuktam kutas brahmaṇaḥ idam ha ākāśāt samutpadyate parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ bhūtāām utpattiḥ bhūtākāśasya vāyu darśitam satyam darśitam kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ parigrahāt ākāśāt avadhāraṇam viśeṣaṇam ākāśam astam yati ebhyaḥ jyāyāḥ parāyaṇam parāyaṇa tve āpekṣikam paramātman jyāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ jyāyāḥ atarikṣāt jyāyāḥ divaḥ jyāyāḥ ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ parāyaṇa parama upapaataram bhavati śrutiḥ rātiḥ dātuḥ parāyaṇam adoṣeṇa śālāvatyasya pakṣam kiṃcid kiṃcid parigṛhītaḥ tam ākāśam udgīthe saṃpādya upasaṃharati eṣa paras varīyāḥ udgīthaḥ eṣaḥ āatyam bhūtākāśam prasiddhi balea prathamataram pratīyate atra brūmaḥ prathamataram pratītam gatā guṇāḥ dṛṣṭvā darśitaḥ brahmaṇi ha vai āmaḥ ityādau paryāya vācī brahmaṇi prayogaḥ ṛcaḥ akṣare parame devāḥ adhi viśve adhikaraṇam udgīthe prastotar yā prastāvam avāyattā upakramya śrūyate katamā ha uvāca ha vai imāi bhūtāi prāṇam abhisaṃviśati prāṇam abhyujjihate eṣā prastāvam avāyattā saṃśayaiḥ ṇayau draṣṭavyau kim ādikam abhidhīyate kim atara viṣayasya viṣaya āsti vicāryate kim tāvat prāptam ādikam parigṛhyate kutas imau śabdau paraspara pratidva dvi viṣayau prasiddhau vṛtteḥ śārvara ādikam tamaḥ ucyate vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi atra ādibhiḥ karaṇaiḥ vyāpṛtasya karaṇa adhyakṣasya jīvasya vijñeya abhidhīyate khalu idam parigṛhya utthāpayati dhāraṇam prāṇasya dharmaḥ saṃvāde tau ariṣṭhaḥ uvāca mā moham āpat aham etat pañcadhā am pravibhajya etat bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi ye imam parigṛhya paṭhati imam jīvam idriya grāmam parigṛhya utthāpayati vyākhyeyam jīve tāvat ceta mukhye prāṇe parigrahe ātmaoḥ vṛtti abhedairdeśaḥ svarūpeṇa yaḥ vai yā vai etau vasataḥ utkrāmataḥ parigrahe kim kasmāt bhidyeta tasmāt prāṇayoḥ ubhau pratīyeyātām trividham upāsaam prasajyeta upāsaam upāsaam upāsaam yuktam upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām avagamyate mām vijāīhi upakramya asmi tam mām āyuḥ amṛtam upāssva uktvā ate eṣa rūpau upakrama upasaṃhārau dṛśyete yuktam āśrayitum pariṇetum śakyam bhūtamātrāṇām prajñāmātrāṇām brahmaṇaḥ arpaṇā vaśāt brahmaṇi hitatama upayāsa ayam gamyate darśitam idam parigṛhya utthāpayati vyāpārasya paramātma āyatta paramātmay upacaritum śakya martyaḥ jīvati kaḥ itareṇa jīvati yasmin etau upāśritau vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi darśitam pakṣam ivārayati brahmaṇaḥ tattvam asi aham asmi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ upādhi kṛtam āśritya jīvaḥ bhoktā ucyate upādhi parityāge svarūpam darśayitum vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādiā pratyagātma abhimukhīkaraṇa virudhyate vācā abhyuditam abhyudyate viddhi idam upāsate ityādi śrutyataram vacaḥ vyāpṛtasya brahmatvam puar etat etau vasataḥ utkrāmataḥ ātmaoḥ darśaam vādī opapadyate eṣa jñā akriyā dvaya āśrayayoḥ prāṇayoḥ pratyagātma upādhi bhūtayoḥ bhedaiḥ deśa upādhi dvaya upahitasya pratyagātmanaḥ svarūpeṇa abhedaḥ ekīkaraṇam aviruddham athavā opāsā ayam ayaḥ vākye virudhyate katham trividham brahmaṇaḥ upāsaam vivakṣitam dharmeṇa dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa āyuḥ amṛtam upāssva āyuḥ idam parigṛhya utthāpayati tasmāt etat uktham upāsīta dharmaḥ asyai prajñāyai bhūtāya ekībhavati vyākhyāsyāmaḥ upakramya asyāḥ ekam aṅgam adūduhat tasyai parastāt prativihitā bhūtamātrā prajñayā vācam samāruhya vācā āmāya apoti ityādiḥ dharmaḥ vai etāḥ daśa bhūtamātrāḥ adhiprajñam daśa prajñāmātrāḥ adhibhūtam yadi bhūtamātrāḥ syuḥ prajñāmātrāḥ syuḥ yadi prajñāmātrāḥ syuḥ bhūtamātrāḥ syuḥ rūpam sidhyet rathasya areṣu emiḥ arpitāḥ arpitāḥ etāḥ bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ īrpitāḥ eṣa ityādiḥ dharmaḥ tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ etat upādhi dvaya dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ekam upāsaam trividham vivakṣitam maomayaḥ śarīraḥ ityādau upādhi dharmeṇa brahmaṇaḥ upāsaam āśritam yujyate vākyasya upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām avagamāt avagamāt tasmāt vākyam etat siddham śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ murat prathamaḥ udhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ sarvatraprasiddhi adhikaraṇam idam āmāyate sarvam khalu idam jalāiti śātaḥ upāsīta khalu kratu puruṣaḥ asimat puruṣaḥ bhavati itas pretya bhavati kratum kurvīta maomayaḥ śarīraḥ ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim maomaya ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ upāsyatvena upadiśyate āhosvit kim tāvat prāptam kutas karaṇa adhipateḥ prasiddhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ āḥ śubhraḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ sarvam khalu idam upāttam katham śārīre upāsya tve āśaṅkyate eṣa vākyam upāsa kim tarhi yatkāraṇam sarvam khalu idam jalaiḥ śātaḥ upāsīta etat bhavati yasmāt sarvam idam jātam ja talla aa sarvasya tve rāga saṃbhavati tasmāt śātaḥ upāsīta tve vākye upāsaam śakyate kratum kurvīta vidhīyate saṃkalpaḥ śrūyate maomayaḥ śarīraḥ brūmaḥ viṣayam etat upāsaam karmā kāmaḥ ityādi śrūyamāṇam paryāyeṇa viṣayam eṣa me hṛdayeṇīyaḥ vrīheḥ yavāt hṛdaya āyata atvam aṇīyaḥ cāra agra mātrasya jīvasya avakalpate brahmaṇaḥ ityādi atra brūmaḥ tāvat aṇīyaḥ ubhayam samāśrayitum śakyam prathama aṇīyaḥ yuktam āśrayitum bhaviṣyati viṣaya tve etat parāmarśa ārtha viṣayam tasmāt aomaya ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ jīvaḥ upāsyaḥ prāpte brūmaḥ maomaya ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ upāsyam kutas sarveṣu prasiddham kāraṇam sarvam khalu idam upakrame maomaya dharmaiḥ viśiṣṭam upadiśyate yuktam hāā prakriye upakrame vivakṣayā vivakṣayā atra ucyate yadi vivakṣayā maomaya upadiśyamāeṣu saṃihitam bhavati jīvaḥ saṃihitaḥ śabdena upāttaḥ vaiṣamyam vaktum iṣṭāḥ vivakṣitāḥ yadi apauruṣeye vede ecchā saṃbhavati upādāea phaleā upacaryate yad abhihitam upādeyam bhavati vivakṣitam ucyate aupādeyam avivakṣitam vede upādeya tve abhihitam vivakṣitam bhavati avivakṣitam veda tātparyā tātparyābhyām avagamyete ye vivakṣitāḥ guṇāḥ upāsaāyām upādeya tve upadiṣṭāḥ saṃkalpa prabhṛtayaḥ parasmin brahmaṇi saṃkalpa as any sṛṣṭi saṃhāreṣu apratibaddha paramātmā avakalpate yaḥ apahata pāpmā atra kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ saṃbhavati sāmyam brahmaṇaḥ jyāyā pṛthivyāḥ ityādi etat vyākhyāyate saṃbhavati kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ karmā ityādi upāsya vivakṣitāḥ guṇāḥ brahmaṇi maomayaḥ śarīraḥ brahmaṇi brahmaṇi brūmaḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhavati viṣaye smṛtī bhavataḥ strī pumān asi kumāraḥ uta kumārī jīrṇaḥ vañcasi jātaḥ bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādam sarvatas akṣi mukham sarvatas śrutimat sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati aprāṇaḥ amaāḥ śubhraḥ śrutiḥ śuddha viṣayā iyam śrutiḥ maomayaḥ śarīraḥ saguṇa viṣayā viśeṣaḥ gamyate aupapatteḥ pūrveṇa sūtreṇa brahmaṇi vivakṣitāām guṇāām upapattiḥ uktā śārīre aupapattiḥ ucyate tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa uktea maomaya guṇam jīvaḥ maomaya guṇaḥ yatkāraṇam saṃkalpaḥ avākī aādaraḥ jyāyāpṛthivyāḥ evaṃjātīyakāḥ guṇāḥ śārīre śārīra bhavaḥ bhavati satyam bhavati bhavati jyāyā pṛthivyāḥ jyāyāḥ atarikṣāt gataḥ vyāpi jīvaḥ bhavati śarīrāt ayatra vṛtti itas yasmāt bhavati etam itas pretya abhisaṃbhavitāsmi etam prakṛtam maomaya guṇam upāsyam vyapadiśati abhisaṃbhavitāsmi śārīram upāsakam tvea prāpaka tvea abhisaṃbhavitāsmi prāptāsmi satyām gatau yuktaḥ upāsya upāsaka adhiṣṭhāaḥ tasmāt maomaya viśiṣṭaḥ itas ayaḥ maomaya guṇaḥ yasmāt viśeṣaḥ bhavati samāa prakaraṇe śrutyatare vrīhiḥ yavaḥ śyāmākaḥ śyāmāka taṇḍulaḥ ayam atarātma puruṣaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ śārīrasya yaḥ abhidhāyakaḥ saptamī atarātmā eti tasmāt viśiṣṭaḥ yaḥ prathamātaḥ tasmāt tayoḥ bhedaḥ adhigamyate smṛtiḥ śārīra paramātmaoḥ bhedam īśvaraḥ bhūtānām tiṣṭhati māyayā ityādyāḥ atra kaḥ yaḥ yaḥ pratiṣidhyate aupapatteḥ ityādiā śrutiḥ draṣṭā śrotā evaṃjātīyakā vārayati smṛtiḥ kṣetrajñam mām viddhi kṣetreṣu bhārataḥ evaṃjātīyakā parihartavyam atra ucyate tāvat paricchia deśasya katham sarvagatasya deśeṣu kayācid saṃbhavati samasta vasudhā ayodhyā kayā gataḥ aṇīyān icāyya brūmaḥ aṇīyaḥ gaṇa īśvaraḥ hṛdaya puṇḍarīke icāyyaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ upadiśyate sālagrāme hariḥ vijñāam grāhakam prasīdati etat draṣṭavyam gatam sat sūcī pāśa brahmā icāyya brahmaṇaḥ pāramārthikam āśaṅkyate hṛdaya āyata atvāt brahmaṇaḥ hṛdayāām pratiśarīram brahmaṇaḥ tāvat prāṇi hṛdaya saṃbadhāt cit śārīra brahmaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ bhavati śārīra parameśvarayoḥ ekaḥ bhoktā adharma sādhaḥ duḥkha ādimān ekaḥ viparītaḥ apahata pāpma guṇaḥ etasmāt ayoḥ bhogaḥ adhyavasitaḥ asi aham asmi āyaḥ vijñātā ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ yathāśāstram tarhi śāstrīyaḥ ūrthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ labhyam śāstram asi apahata pāpma viśeṣaṇam śārīrasya tve upadiśat śārīrasya tāvat samyagjñā adṛṣṭam vastu saṃspṛśyate śakyaḥ īśvarasya kalpayitum attṛ adhikaraṇam kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate yasya kṣatram ubhe bhavataḥ odaḥ mṛtyuḥ yasya upasecaam kaḥ itthā veda atra pratīyate kim darśaāt guhā praviṣṭa adhikaraṇam kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate ṛtam pibatau sukṛtasya parame ardhe chāyā ātapau āgayaḥ ye triṇāciketāḥ kaṭhaḥ saṃśayaḥ kim jīvau irdiṣṭau uta paramātmāām yadi jīvau karaṇa pratipāditaḥ bhavati pratipādayitavyam ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt bhavyāt paśyasi vada pṛṣṭa atra ākṣeptā ubhau etau pakṣau saṃbhavataḥ kasmāt ṛta pāam upabhogaḥ sukṛtasya cetaasya kṣetrajñasya saṃbhavati buddheḥ pibatau dvayoḥ śrutiḥ kṣetrajña pakṣaḥ tāvat saṃbhavati kṣetrajña paramātma pakṣaḥ saṃbhavati ayobhicākaśīti matra atra ucyate eṣa chatriṇaḥ gacchati āceta ayoḥ irdeśaḥ chāyā ātapa paraspara tasmāt kṣetrajñau ucyeyātām prāpte brūmaḥ vijñāātma paramātmāau ucyeyātām kasmāt ātmaau tau ubhau cetaau sama svabhāvau śravaṇe sama svabhāveṣu pratītiḥ goḥ dvitīyaḥ uveṣṭavyaḥ ukte gauḥ dvitīyaḥ uviṣyate āśvaḥ puruṣaḥ dvitīya āveṣaṇāyām cetaaḥ paramātmā pratīyate guhā hita darśaā paramātmā pratyetavyaḥ guhā hita darśaāt paramātmā pratyetavyaḥ vadāmaḥ guhā hita smṛtiṣu paramātma guhā hitam gahvareṣṭham purāṇam yaḥ veda ihitam guhāyām parame aviccha praviṣṭam ityādyāsu gatasya brahmaṇaḥ deśa virudhyata etat varti chatri aviruddham chāyā ātapau aviruddham chāyā ātapa paraspara saṃsāri asaṃsāri tvayoḥ avidyā saṃsāri tvasya pāramārthika asaṃsāri tvasya tasmāt vijñā paramātmau gṛhyete kutas vijñā paramātmau gṛhyete viśeṣaṇam vijñā paramātmaoḥ bhavati ātmāam rathiam viddhi ratham ityādiā rathi ratha kalpaayā vijñā ātmāam rathiam mokṣayoḥ kalpayati viṣṇoḥ paramam padam paramātmāam gatavyam kalpayati tam durdarśam gūḍham aupraviṣṭam guhā hitam gahvareṣṭham purāṇam devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti pūrvasmi grathe etau viśeṣitau prakaraṇam idam paramātmā kaṭhaḥ vaktṛ upādāam paramātma parigrahe ghaṭate tasmāt paramātma au ucyeyātām eṣaḥ yāyaḥ dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyau evamādiṣu adhikārāḥ prākṛtau suparṇau ucyete tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti ada vijñā bhavati aaśa aceta tvābhyām paramātmā tau draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya viśiaṣṭi vṛkṣe puruṣaḥ śocati juṣṭam yadā paśyati ayam īśam mahimā am vīta śokaḥ aparaḥ dvār suparṇāḥ siddhātam bhajate paiṅgi rahasyabrāhmaṇe ayathā vyākhyāta tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti sattvam aaśca ayaḥ abhicākaśīti aaśca ayaḥ abhipaśyati tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau sattva jīvaḥ kṣetrajña paramātmā ucyate taa sattva kṣetrajña śabdayoḥ ataḥkaraṇa śārīra vyākhyāta etat sattvam svapam paśyati yaḥ yam upadraṣṭā kṣetrajñaḥ tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau āpyasya adhikaraṇasya pūrvapakṣa bhajate atra kṣetrajñaḥ dharmeṇa vivakṣyate katham tarhi atītaḥ svabhāvaḥ caitaya vacaāt tattvam asi kṣetrajñam mām viddhi ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ tāvatā darśam avakalpate tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau ha evaṃvidi kiṃcaa rajaḥ ādhvaṃsate ityādi katham tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti sattvam acetae sattve ucyate śrutiḥ acetaasya sattve vacaam ucyate śrutiḥ acetaasya sattvasya vakṣyāmi pravṛttā kim tarhi cetaasya kṣetrajñasya abhoktṛ svabhāvatām vakṣyāmi duḥkha vikriyāvati sattve adhyāropayati idam sattva kṣetrajñayoḥ svabhāva aviveka kṛtam kalpyate paramārthataḥ āyatarasya saṃbhavati acetaa sattvasya avikriya kṣetrajñasya avidyā pratyupasthāpita svabhāva sattvasya sutarām saṃbhavati śrutiḥ vai ayat iva ayaḥ paśyet ityādiā avidyā viṣayaḥ vyavahāram sarvam abhūt kam paśyet ityādiā vivekiḥ vyavahāram iva ārayati ataraḥ atara adhikaraṇam yaḥ eṣa kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ eṣaḥ ha uvāca etat amṛtam abhayam etat yadi asmi sarpiḥ udakam siñcati gacchati ityādi śrūyate saṃśayaḥ kim ayam pratibimba akṣi adhikaraṇaḥ vijñā uta idriyasya adhiṣṭhātā athavā īśvara kim tāvat prāptam chāyā pratirūpaḥ kutas dṛśyamāa yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ vijñāātmao ayam iḥ deśaḥ yuktam cakṣuṣā rūpam paśyan cakṣuṣi saṃihitaḥ bhavati asmi pakṣe ukūlaḥ bhavati puruṣaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ grāhakaḥ pratīyate raśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ asmi pratiṣṭhitaḥ ādīām kathaṃcid eśvaraḥ prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ akṣiṇi abhyataraḥ puruṣaḥ upadiṣṭaḥ kasmāt parameśvare jātam ātmatvam tāva mukhyayā vṛttyā parameśvare asi abhaya tve śrūyete etat etat parameśvaraḥ doṣaiḥ aliptaḥ apahata pāpma akṣi sthāam lepa rahitam upadiṣṭam yadi asmi sarpiḥ udakam siñcati vartmaī gacchati saṃyat vāma avakalpate etam saṃyat vāma etam vāmāi abhisaṃyati eṣaḥ vāmaīḥ eṣa ayati eṣaḥ bhāmaīḥ eṣa sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti ataraḥ parameśvaraḥ sthā katham puar gatasya brahmaṇaḥ akṣi alpam atra ucyate bhavet eṣā avakḷptiḥ yadi etat ekam bhavet yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhe teṣu irdiṣṭam yaḥ cakṣuṣi tiṣṭhe sthā grahaṇe etat kevalam brahmaṇaḥ kim tarhi āma rūpam evaṃjātīyakam āma rūpasya uditi hiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi hirguṇam sat āma gataiḥ guṇaiḥ guṇam upāsa upadiśyate etat gatasya brahmaṇaḥ virudhyate sālagrāmaḥ iva viṣṇoḥ etat abhidhāāt vivaditavyam kim abhidhāāt siddham viśiṣṭam upakrame prakrātam kam kham abhihitam parigrahasya yāyya ācāryaḥ gatim vaktā abhidhāa pratijñāāt katham puar upakrame viśiṣṭam vijñāyate ucyate kam kham etat agīām vacaam śrutvā upakosalaḥ uvāca aham kam kham idam prativacaam vāva kam kham kham kam kham bhūtākāśe yadi kaṃ vācī opādīyeta kevale bhūtākāśe āma iva abhiprāyeṇa prayuktaḥ pratītiḥ kaṃ viṣaya idriya saṃparka ja sāmaye sukhe yadi khaṃśabdaḥ laukikam sukham pratītiḥ viśeṣitau kaṃ khaṃ śabdau ātmakam gamayataḥ dvitīye upādīyamāe kam kham ucyamāe kaṃ bhūt kaṃ khaṃ śabdayoḥ kam kham iṣṭam sukhasya guṇasya guṇi dhyeya upakrame viśiṣṭam upadiṣṭam gārhapatya yogayaḥ svam svam mahimā upadiśya eṣā somya upasaṃharataḥ pūrvatra jñāpayati ācāryaḥ gatim vaktā vārayati puṣkarapalāśe śliṣyate evaṃvidi pāpam śliṣyate akṣi sthāam vijāataḥ puruṣasya brahmatvam tasmāt prakṛtasya brahmaṇā ukṣi sthāatām saṃyat vāma guṇatām uktvā ādikām gatim vakṣyāmi upakramate yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ eṣaḥ ha uvāca itas akṣi sthāaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ yasmāt yā gatiḥ devayāā ākhyā prasiddhā śrutau uttareṇa tapasā brahmacaryeṇa śraddhayā ādityam abhijayate etat vai prāṇāām āyataam etat amṛtam abhayam etat parāyaṇam etasmāt puarāvartate smṛtau agiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam prayātā gacchati brahman akṣi śavyam kurvati yadi ārciṣam abhisaṃbhavati upakramya ādityāt cadramasam cadramasaḥ vidyutam puruṣaḥ umāavaḥ eābrahma gamayati eṣa pathaḥ pathaḥ pratipadyamāā imam āvartam āvartate viṣayayā prasiddhayā gatyā akṣi sthāasya brahmatvam etaraḥ puar chāyā vijñā akṣi sthāaḥ atra ucyate chāyā grahaṇam arhati kasmāt cakṣuṣi saṃbhavati yadā kaścid puruṣaḥ āsīdati cakṣuṣi chāyā apagate tasmin yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ śrutiḥ saṃidhāāt cakṣuṣi dṛśyamāam upāsya tve upadiśati upāsaā kāle chāyākaram kaṃcid samīpe saṃidhāpya upāste yuktam kalpayitum śarīrasya āśam aśyati śrutiḥ avasthita sādhāraṇe cakṣuṣi avasthita śakyam vaktum brahmaṇaḥ hṛdaya deśa ādīām guṇāām yadi vijñāātmā kām kṛtam martya adhyāropitam bhayam abhaya tve opapadyete saṃyat vāma etasmi aaiśvaryāt ātmaaḥ raśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ smi pratiṣṭhitaḥ yadi cakṣuṣi ātmatvam saṃbhavati parāk rūpatvāt saṃbhavati pralaya amara devāām cira kāla aiśvaryam parameśvara āyattam svābhāvikam bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣā udeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agiḥ idraḥ mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ matra tasmāt parameśvaraḥ ayam akṣi sthāaḥ pratyetavyaḥ pakṣe vidvat viṣayam praroca vyākhyeyam ataryāmi ataryāmi adhikaraṇam yaḥ imam lokam lokam bhūtāyataraḥ yamayati upakramya śrūyate yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭha pṛthivyāḥ ataraḥ yam veda yasya yaḥ pṛthivīm ataraḥ yamayati eṣa ataryāmī amṛtaḥ ityādi atra adhidaivatam adhilokam adhivedam adhiyajñam adhibhūtam adhyātmam kaścid avasthitaḥ yamayitā ataryāmī śrūyate kim abhimāī kaścid kim prāpta aṇima aiśvaryaḥ kaścid yogī kim paramātmā kim arthātaram kiṃcitaḥ darśaāt saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat pratibhāti saṃjñāyāḥ aprasiddha arthātareṇa kaścid bhavitavyam athavā āi rūpita rūpam arthātaram kiṃcid śakyam abhyupagatum ataryāmi tasmāt abhimāī kaścid śrūyate ityādi yuktam yamayitṛ kasyacid siddhasya yamayitṛ paramātmā pratīyate akārya karaṇa prāpte idam ucyate yotaryāmi śrūyate paramātmā āyaḥ kutas paramātmanaḥ dharmāḥ tāvat bhiam samastam jātam tiṣṭha yamayati paramātmanaḥ yamayitṛ dharmaḥ tve eṣa ataryāmī amṛtaḥ tve mukhye paramātma upapadyete yam veda devatāyāḥ avijñeyam ataryāmiṇam aham asmi ityādi ityādi karaṇasya yamayitṛ eṣa karaṇaiḥ ayaḥ iyatā saṃbhavati upapattiḥ tasmāt paramātmā ataryāmī ataddharma etat dharmāḥ sāṃkhya kalpitasya pradhā taiḥ apratarkyam avijñeyam prasuptam iva sarvatas smarati iyatṛ tasmāt pradhāam ataryāmi īkṣaterā atra irākṛtam sat uttaram ucyate pradhā mataryāmi bhavitum arhati kasmāt yadi pradhā saṃbhavati draṣṭṛ saṃbhavati taiḥ adṛṣṭaḥ draṣṭā aśrutaḥ śrotā amataḥ mata avijñātaḥ vijñātā vākyaśeṣaḥ bhavati ātmatvam pradhāasya yadi tarhi ataryāmī bhavatu ceta atvāt draṣṭā śrotā matā vijñātā bhavati pratyak amṛtaḥ adharma upabhoga dharmāḥ śārīre su prasiddhāḥ darśa kriyāyāḥ kartari pravṛtti draṣṭāram paśyeḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ karaṇa saṃghātam ataryamayitum śīlam tasmāt śārīra utaryāmī uttaram paṭhati ātaryāmī kasmāt yadi draṣṭṛ dharmāḥ saṃbhavati ghaṭa upādhi paricchia tvāa śakoti śākhiaḥ kāṇvāḥ mādhyaṃdiāḥ cātaryāmiṇaḥ śārīram śārīram ādhīyate yaḥ yaḥ tiṣṭhe kāṇvāḥ yaḥ ātmai tiṣṭhe mādhyaṃdiāḥ yaḥ ātmai tiṣṭhe tāvat pāṭhe bhavati śārīrasya vācakaḥ yaḥ vijñāe tiṣṭhe pāṭhe ucyate vijñā tasmāt śārīra īśvara utaryāmī siddham katham puar dehe dvau draṣṭārau upapadyete yaḥ ayam īśvara utaryāmī yaḥ ayam kā puariha upapattiḥ virudhyeta atra prakṛtāt ataryāmiṇaḥ yam draṣṭāram śrotāram matāram vijñātāram iyatratara etat vacam iyatratara aprasaṅgāt atra ucyate avidyā pratyupasthāpita karaṇa upādhi nimittaḥ yam śārīra ataryāmiṇoḥ pāramārthikaḥ ekaḥ pratyagātmā bhavati dvau pratyagātmāau saṃbhavataḥ vyavahāra upādhi kṛtaḥ ghaṭa mahā jñātṛ śrutayaḥ sarvam etat śrutiḥ dvaitam iva bhavati itaram paśyati avidyā viṣaye sarvam vyavahāram sarvam abhūt kea kam paśyet viṣaye sarvam vyavahāram vārayati adhikaraṇam parā yayā adhigamyate dreśyam grāhyam gotram varṇam śrotram apāṇi pādam vibhum gatam su avyayam bhūtayoim paripaśyati dhīrāḥ śrūyate saṃśayaḥ kim ayam uta āhosvit parameśvara pradhāam acetaam yuktam puruṣaḥ cetaau eti brūmaḥ kevalasya cetaasya keśa loma yoitvam dhiṣṭhitam acetaam ūrṇaābhi sūtrasya keśalomām prasiddham pūrvatra abhilāpa saṃbhave draṣṭṛ abhilāpa pradhāe abhyupagatam dharmāḥ pradhāe saṃbhavati atra dharmaḥ kaścid abhilapyate yaḥ sarvajñaḥ ayam katham yoiḥ pratijñāyate atra ucyate yayā adhigamyate adreśyam śabdena guṇakam śrāvayitvā śrāvayiṣyati akṣarāt paratas yaḥ parokṣarāt śrutaḥ sarvajñaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati yadā śabdaiḥ diṣṭam yadā imitta vācī adharmābhyām jātasya prāpte abhidhīyate yaḥ yam parameśvaraḥ āyaḥ katham etat avagamyate parameśvarasya dharmaḥ ucyamānaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvajña saṃbhavati avakṣara śabdaiḥ diṣṭāt bhūtayoḥ etat sarvajña atra ucyate saṃbhavati yatkāraṇam akṣarāt saṃbhavati viśvam prakṛtam saṃbhavati yatkāraṇam akṣarāt saṃbhavati viśvam prakṛtam sarvajñam irdiśya yaḥ sarvajñaḥ vidyasya jñāa mayam tapaḥ tasmāt etat āma rūpam aam jāyate sarvajña dharmaḥ ucyate gamyate akṣarāt paratas atra prakṛtāt kaścid abhidhīyate katham etat avagamyate provāca tām tvattaḥ bahma vidyām prakṛtasya akṣarasya pratijñāta katham tarhi akṣarāt paratas sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ atra dve vidye veditavye ukte parā aparā aparām ṛgveda lakṣaṇām vidyām uktvā parā yayā adhigamyate ityādi parasyāḥ vidyāyāḥ yadi parameśvarāt ayat guṇakam parikalpyeta parā apara ayam vidyayoḥ abhyudaya aiḥśreyasa parikalpyate iḥśreyasa phalā keacid abhyupagamyate tisraḥ vidyāḥ pratijñāyera paramātmanaḥ dve vidye veditavye kasmin bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati ātmake brahmaṇi ātmake brahmaṇi ātmake brahmaṇi pradhāe bhogya vyatirikte bhoktari vidyām pratiṣṭhām atharvāya jyeṣṭhaputrāya prāha vidyām prādhāye upakramya apara vibhāge parām vidyām adhigamaiḥ darśaya tasyāḥ samākhyā adhigamyasya akṣarasya abrahmatve bādhitā aparā ṛgveda lakṣaṇā upakrame upayasyate praśaṃsāyai plavāḥ adṛḍhāḥ rūpāḥ aṣṭādaśa avaram yeṣu etat śreyaḥ mūḍhāḥ jarām mṛtyum aparām vidyām viraktasya adhikāram parīkṣya gurum abhigacchet samidh pāṇiḥ śrotriyam brahmaiṣṭham acetasām ādīām bhavitavyam ayuktam dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ atyata sāmyea bhavitavyam sthūlāḥ sthūlāḥ dṛṣṭāta tveopāttāḥ sthūlaḥ dārṣṭātikaḥ bhūtayoiḥ abhyupagamyate tasmāt parameśvaraḥ etarau itas parameśvaraḥ bhūtayoiḥ etarau kasmāt viśiaṣṭi prakṛtam tve divyaḥ amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sabāhya abhyataraḥ ajaḥ aprāṇaḥ amaāḥ śubhraḥ etat divya viśeṣaṇam avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma pariccheda abhimāiḥ kalpayataḥ śārīrasya tasmāt aupaiṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ ucyate pradhāāt prakṛtam vyapadiśati akṣarāt paratas avyākṛtam āma bīja rūpam īśvara āśrayam upādhi sarvasmāt vikārāt tasmāt paratas vyapadiśa vivakṣitam kiṃcid svatatram tattvam abhyupagamya tasmāt ucyate kim tarhi yadi avirodhe avyākṛta vācyam parikalpyeta kalpyatām tasmāt parameśvaraḥ yoiḥ etat pratipādyate kutas parameśvaraḥ upayāsāt akṣarāt paratas etasmāt jāyate prabhṛtīām paryatāām tattvāām sargam uktvā ātmakam rūpam paśyāmaḥ agiḥ mūrdhā cakṣuṣī cadra sūryau diśaḥ śrotre vivṛtāḥ vedāḥ vāyuḥ hṛdayam viśvam padbhyām eṣa atarātmā parameśvarasya ucitam śārīrasya ayam upayāsaḥ saṃbhavati atarātma tasmāt parameśvaraḥ etarau gamyate katham yoeḥ ayam upayāsaḥ gamyate eṣaḥ prakṛti ākarṣaṇāt prakṛtyā etasmāt jāyate eṣa atarātmā vacaam bhavati upādhyāyam prakṛtya etasmāt adhīṣva eṣa veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ vacaam upādhyāya viṣayam bhavati katham guṇakasya vigrahavat rūpam saṃbhavati vivakṣayā idam ucyate vigrahavat vivakṣayā adoṣaḥ aham aham aham aham aham ahamaādaḥ ityādi aye puar upayāsaḥ etasmāt jāyate idriyāṇi kham vāyuḥ viśvasya dhāriṇī pūrvatra tattva jātam tasmāt agiḥ samidhaḥ yasya sūryaḥ evamādi sarvāḥ oṣadhayaḥ rasāḥ katham akasmāt rūpam upayasyet sṛṣṭim parisamāpya upadekṣyati puruṣaḥ idam viśvam ityādiā smṛtyoḥ trailokya śarīrasya prajāpateḥ jama upalabhāmahe hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartata agre jātaḥ patiḥ ekaḥ āsīt dādhāra pṛthivīm dyām uta imām kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema samavartata ajāyata vai śarīrī prathamaḥ vai puruṣaḥ ucyate ādikartā bhūtāām agre samavartata puruṣasya atara saṃbhavati bhūtāām adhyātmam avasthāāt asmi pakṣe puruṣaḥ idam viśvam ityādi upayāsaḥ parameśvara pratipatti hetuḥ vyākhyeyam vaiśvāaraḥ kaḥ kim am imam vaiśvāaram saṃprati adhyeṣi tam o brūhi upakramya vaiśvāaram eṣām mūrdha upadiśya āmāyate yaḥ etam prādeśa abhivimāam ātmāam vaiśvāaram upāste sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu sarveṣu ātmasu atti ha vai etasya ātmaaḥ vaiśvāarasya mūrdhā su tejāḥ viśva rūpaḥ vāyuḥ vartmā saṃdehaḥ bahulaḥ vastiḥ rayiḥ pādau uraḥ vediḥ loma ai barhiḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ āsyam āhavaīyaḥ ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim vaiśvāara śabdena jāṭhara ogī upadiśyate uta bhūtāgiḥ athavā āhosvit parameśvaraḥ kim saṃśaya kāraṇam vaiśvāaraḥ jāṭhara bhūtāgi devatāām prayogāt śārīra parameśvarayoḥ yāyyam kasya bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam jāṭhara ogiḥ kutas viśeṣeṇa kvacid prayogaḥ ayam agiḥ vaiśvāaraḥ yaḥ yamataḥ puruṣe pacyate idam adyate ityādau agi prayoga darśaāt viśvasmai agim devāḥ vaiśvāaram ketu mahām akṛṇvaḥ ityādau agi śarīrā tasyām prayoga darśaāt vaiśvāarasya sumatau syāma rājā kam evamādyāyāḥ devatāyām aiśvarya upetāyām sāmādhikaraṇyāt upakrame kaḥ kim kevala prayogāt vaśe vaiśvāara pariṇeyaḥ ucyate vaiśvāara saṃikarṣāt prādeśa viśeṣaṇasya tasmāeśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ prāptam idam ucyate vaiśvāaraḥ paramātmā bhavitum arhati kutas śabdayoḥ viśeṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ yadi etau ubhau vaiśvāara śabdau śabdau vaiśvāara sādhāraṇaḥ dvayoḥ viśeṣaḥ parameśvara tayoḥ abhyupagamyate ha etasya ātmaaḥ vaiśvāarasya mūrdhā su tejāḥ ityādiḥ atra parameśvaraḥ mūrdha viśiṣṭaḥ uvasthātara gataḥ gamyate kāraṇasya sarvābhiḥ gatābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ avasthāvat avayava sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu sarveṣu ātmasu aam atti āśrayam śrūyamāṇam parama parigrahe saṃbhavati ha pāpmāaḥ pradūyate pāpma pradāha śravaṇam kaḥ aḥ kim upakramaḥ liṅgāi parameśvaram gamayati tasmāt parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ aumāam itas parameśvara vaiśvāaraḥ yasmāt parameśvarasya agirā āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā īdṛśam trailokya ātmakam rūpam yasya agirā āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā kham ābhiḥ caraṇau kṣitiḥ sūryaḥ diśaḥ śrotram ātmai amaḥ rūpam bhūtām śrutim aumāpayat vaiśvāara parameśvara paratve aumāam gamakam hetvarthe yasmāt idam gamakam tasmāt vaiśvāaraḥ paramātmā yadi stutiḥ iyam amaḥ āsati bhūte veda vākye samyak rūpeṇa saṃbhavati dyām mūrdhāam yasya viprāḥ kham vai ābhiṃ cadra sūryau diśaḥ śrotre viddhi pādau kṣitim uciti praṇetā evaṃjātīyakā smṛtiḥ udāhartavyā utas pratiṣṭhāāt atra parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ bhavitum arhati kutas utas pratiṣṭhāāt tāvat vaiśvāara parameśvare saṃbhavati arthātare rūḍha agi eṣaḥ gir vaiśvāaraḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ bhaktam prathamam āgacchet homīyam ityādiā āhuti adhikaraṇa saṃkīrtaam etebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāṭharaḥ vaiśvāaraḥ pratyetavyaḥ pratiṣṭhāam śrūyate itas pratiṣṭhitam veda jāṭhare saṃbhavati mūrdhā su tejāḥ ityādeḥ kāraṇāt paramātmā vaiśvāaraḥ atra brūmaḥ kutas pratibhāe parameśvara viṣayaḥ viśeṣaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ jāṭhara viṣaya athavā bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati matra varṇe avagamyate yaḥ pṛthivīm dyām uta imām ātatāa rodasī atarikṣam ityādau athavā śarīrāyāḥ devatāyāḥ aiśvarya avayava bhaviṣyati tasmāt parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ atra ucyate kāraṇebhyaḥ parameśvarasya yuktam kutas parameśvara jāṭhare vaiśvāare upadiśyate mao upāsīta ityādi athavā jāṭhara vaiśvāara upādhiḥ parameśvaraḥ draṣṭavya upadiśyate mao śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ ityādi yadi parameśvaraḥ vivakṣyeta kevalaḥ jāṭhara ogiḥ vivakṣyeta mūrdhā su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣasya āgi vyapāśrayeṇa ayam viśeṣaḥ upapādayitum śakyate sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ yadi kevalaḥ jāṭharaḥ vivakṣyeta itas pratiṣṭhita kevalam vājasaeyiḥ eṣa ogiḥ vaiśvāaraḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ ha etam agim vaiśvāaram itas pratiṣṭhitam veda parameśvarasya itas pratiṣṭhita ubhayam ye puruṣavidham sūtra avayavam paṭhati eṣaḥ ṛthaḥ kevala jāṭhara parigrahe itas pratiṣṭhita kevalam puruṣavidha puruṣavidham vājasaeyiḥ puruṣavidham itas pratiṣṭhitam veda puruṣavidha adhidaivatam dyumūrdha adhyātmam prasiddham mūrdha cubuka pratiṣṭhita tvātam parigṛhyate bhūtāgeḥ mūrdhā su tejāḥ avayava kalpaam bhaviṣyati śarīrāyāḥ devatāyāḥ vaiśvarya parihartavyam ūrcyate uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ vaiśvāaraḥ bhūtāgiḥ vaiśvāaraḥ bhūtāgeḥ auṣṇya ātmakasya mūrdha kalpaā vikārasya atara devatāyāḥ aiśvarya yoge mūrdha kalpaā smbhavati akāraṇa parameśvara adhī aiśvarya saṃbhavaḥ sarveṣu pakṣeṣu sthitaḥ jaimiiḥ jāṭhara āgi pratīkaḥ jāṭhara āgi upādhikaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsyaḥ pratiṣṭhita yaurodhea idāīm parameśvara upāsa parigrahe kaścid jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ atra ucyate pratiṣṭhita vacaam puruṣavidham itas pratiṣṭhitam vede jāṭhara āgi abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate saṃśabdita katham tarhi prakṛtam mūrdha cubuka ateṣu avayaveṣu puruṣavidha kalpitam abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate puruṣavidham itas pratiṣṭhitam vede vṛkṣe śākhām pratiṣṭhitām paśyati athavā yaḥ prakṛtaḥ paramātmā adhyātmam adhidaivatam puruṣavidha upādhiḥ kevalam sākṣi rūpam abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate puruṣavidham itas pratiṣṭhitam veda paramātma parigrahe viṣayaḥ vaiśvāara vartiṣyate viśvaḥ ayam araḥ viśveṣām ayam araḥ viśve arāḥ viśvāaraḥ paramātmā viśvāaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ taddhita uaya rākṣasa vāyasa paramātma viṣayaḥ bhaviṣyati gārhapatya kalpam āhuti adhikaraṇa katham puas parameśvara parigrahe prādeśa śrutiḥ tām vyākhyātum ārabhate atimātrasya parameśvarasya prādeśa nimittam abhivyajyate kila prādeśa parimāṇaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsakāām kṛte viśeṣeṣu hṛdaya sthāeṣu viśeṣeṇa abhivyajyate parameśvare prādeśa śrutiḥ ācāryaḥ ausmṛteḥ prādeśa hṛdaya pratiṣṭhitea ayam prādeśa mātraḥ ucyate prastha mitāḥ yavāḥ prasthāḥ ucyate yadi yaveṣu gatam parimāṇam prastha saṃbadhāt vyajyate parameśvara gatam kiṃcid parimāṇam hṛdaya saṃbadhāt vyajyeta prayuktāyāḥ prādeśa saṃbhavati kathaṃcid ausmaraṇam ucyate ayam prādeśa mātraḥ prādeśa tāyai parameśvare prādeśa śrutiḥ ācāryaḥ mayate eam asmi eam parameśvaram asmi mūrdha cubuka atarāle jābālāḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ vyaktaḥ vimukte pratiṣṭhitaḥ vimuktaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ varaṇāyām āsyām madhye pratiṣṭhitaḥ kā vai varaṇā kā āsi imām āsikām sarvāṇīdriya kṛtāi pāpāi vārayati varaṇā sarvāṇīdriya kṛtāi pāpāi āśayati āsī katamat sthāam bhavati bhruvoḥ ghrāṇasya yaḥ saṃdhiḥ eṣa lokasya saṃdhiḥ bhavati tasmāt upapaā parameśvare prādeśa śrutiḥ abhivimāa śrutiḥ pratyagātma abhiprāyā pratyagātma sarvaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ abhivimīyate abhivimāaḥ abhigataḥ ayam pratyagātma vimāaḥ mā aviyogāt abhivimāaḥ abhivimimīte sarvam tasmāt parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ siddham śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ murat prathama udhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ adhikaraṇam idam śrūyate yasmin yauḥ cātarikṣam otam prāṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ tam ekam amayāḥ vimuñcatha amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ atra etat kiṃcid avagamyate kim āhosvit arthātaram saṃdihyate arthātaram kim āyatam prāptam kasmāt amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ pāravāhi setuḥ prakhyātaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pāravat śakyam abhyupagatum arthātare āyatae parigṛhyamāṇe prasiddham pradhāam parigrahītavyam āyata prasiddhaḥ vāyuḥ vāyuḥ vāva gautama sūtram vai gautama sūtreṇa ayam lokaḥ lokaḥ bhūtāi saṃdṛbdhāi bhavati vāyoḥ vidhāraṇa bhogyam prapañcam pratyāyata prāpte idam āyatam dyauḥ bhūḥ bhuvau bhuvau ādī yasya idam etat vākye dyauḥ atarikṣam maaḥ evamātmakam āyatam bhavitum arhati kutas bhavati tam ekam paramātma parigrahe samyak avakalpate ārthātara parigrahe kvacid śrūyate mūlāḥ somya imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sat āyataāḥ sat pratiṣṭhāḥ śabdena purastāt upariṣṭāt saṃkīrtyate puruṣaḥ idam viśvam tapaḥ amṛtam idam amṛtam purastāt paścāt dakṣiṇatas uttareṇa āyata āyata avat sarvam sāma ādhikaraṇyāt ātmakaḥ vṛkṣaḥ śākhā skadhaḥ mūlam āārasaḥ vicitraḥ āśaṅkā saṃbhavati tām avadhāraṇam tam ekam jāatha ātmāam etat bhavati prapañca viśiṣṭaḥ vicitraḥ vijñeyaḥ kim tarhi avidyā kṛtam prapañcam pravilāpayataḥ tam ekam āyata abhūtam ātmāam jāatha ekarasam yasmin āste devadattaḥ ayaḥ ukte devadattam devadattam vijñeya upadiśyate aṛta abhisaṃdhasya apavādaḥ śrūyate mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum āpoti yaḥ paśyati sarvam sāmāādhikaraṇyam prapañca vilāpa ekarasa pratipāda kṛtsaḥ rasa ghaaḥ vai areyam taras bāhyaḥ kṛtsaḥ aghaaḥ ekarasa setoḥ pāravat brahmaṇā ūrtha atareṇa bhavitavyam atra ucyate vidhāraṇa śrutyāḥ vivakṣyate pāravat mṛd dāru setuḥ atra mṛd dāru setuḥ abhyupagamyate vidhāraṇa vyutpatteḥ aparaḥ tam ekam etat saṃkīrtitam jñāam etat ayā vimuñcatha atra sādhaa amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ śrutyā saṃkīrtyate brahmaṇā atareṇa bhavitavyam etat ayuktam itas dyubhva āyatam muktaiḥ upasṛpyam upasṛpyam aātmasu aham asmi buddhiḥ avidyā pūjā ādau rāgaḥ paribhava ādau dveṣaḥ uccheda darśaāt bhayam mohaḥ ayam aata bhedaḥ vrātaḥ saṃtataḥ pratyakṣaḥ avidyā rāga dveṣa muktaiḥ upasṛpyam upagamyam etat prakṛtya bhavati katham bhidyate hṛdayagrathiḥ chidyate saṃśayāḥ kṣīyate karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare uktvā vidvāḥ āmarūpāt vimuktaḥ parātparam upaiti divyam brahmaṇaḥ prasiddham śāstre yadā pramucyate kāmāḥ śritāḥ martyaḥ mṛtaḥ bhavati atra evamādau prasiddham tam ekam vimuñcatha amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ vimoka pūrvakam vijñeya bhu āyataasya ucyate śrutyatare brahmaṇaḥ tam dhīraḥ vijñāya prajñām kurvīta brāhmaṇaḥ tasmāt bhu āyataam brahmaṇaḥ pratipādakaḥ vaiśeṣikaḥ hetuḥ uktaḥ vaiśeṣikaḥ hetuḥ pratipādakaḥ sāṃkhya parikalpitam pradhāam pratipattavyam kasmāt acetaasya pradhā pratipādakaḥ atra acetaasya pradhā pratipādakaḥ kaścid usti yaḥ acetaam pradhā avagamyeta viparītasya cetaasya pratipādaka utra yaḥ sarvajñaḥ ityādiḥ yadi prāṇabhṛtaḥ saṃbhavati sarvajña asaṃbhave asmāt āyata tve āśrayitavyaḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ āyata samyak saṃbhavati yoga kutas āyata tve āśrayitavyaḥ bhavati tam ekam jñātṛ bhāvea tau mumukṣu jñātā vācyam jñeyam bhu āyataam gamyate kutas bhu āyata tveā āśrayitavyaḥ prakaraṇam idam paramātmanaḥ kasmin bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati vijñā apekṣaṇāt paramātmani ātmake vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam kevale prāṇabhṛti kutas āyata tve āśrayitavyaḥ adaābhyām āyataam prakṛtya dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyau atra adae tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti tābhyām adaābhyām īśvara kṣetrajñau gṛhyete yadi īśvaraḥ vivakṣitaḥ prakṛtasya īśvarasya kṣetrajñāt vacaam avakalpate ayathā aprakṛta vacaam ākasmikam asaṃbaddham tava kṣetrajñasya īśvarāt vacaam ākasmikam prasajyeta avivakṣita kṣetrajñaḥ tve pratiśarīram upādhi saṃbaddhaḥ lokatas prasiddhaḥ āsau śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate īśvaraḥ lokataḥ śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate ākasmikam yuktam au atra etat darśitam dvā suparṇāḥ asyām ṛci īśvara kṣetrajñau ucyete yadā vyākhyāeā asyām ṛci sattva kṣetrajñau ucyete kaścid katham ghaṭa chidra pratiśarīram gṛhyamāṇaḥ bhavati pratiṣidhyate yaḥ śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ bhavati pratiṣidhyate yaḥ śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ bhavati ghaṭa chidrāṇi ghaṭa ādibhiḥ upādhibhiḥ mahā bhavati prāṇabhṛtaḥ parasmāt aya aupapatteḥ pratiṣedhaḥ opapadyate tasmāt sattva upādhi abhimāiaḥ bhvā āyataa pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt bhvā āyataam etat siddham bhūtayoi vākyasya madhye idam paṭhitam yasmin yauḥ cātarikṣam prapañca samprasādāt bhūma adhikaraṇam idam samāmaati vijijñāsitavyaḥ aam bhagavaḥ vijijñāsa āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti āyat ayat paśyati ayat śṛṇoti ayat alpam ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim āhosvit paramātmā kutas saṃśayaḥ tāvat bahutvam abhidhīyate bahoḥ bahoḥ bhūma ātatā smaraṇāt kimātmakam bahutvam ākāṅkṣāyām vai āśāyāḥ bhūyāḥ pratibhāti me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu utthāt paramātmā pratibhāti yāyyam kasya bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam kasmāt bhagavaḥ āmaḥ vāva āmaḥ bhūyasī bhagavaḥ mao vāva āma prāṇāt praśaprativacaa pravāhaḥ pravṛttaḥ prāṇāt bhagavaḥ prāṇāt adaḥ vāva prāṇāt prāṇam āma āśātebhyaḥ bhūyāṃsam vai āśāyāḥ bhūyāḥ prapañcam uktvā darśiṇaḥ ativādi ativādyasi ativādyasmi brūyāḥ apahuvīta eṣa vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati vratam ativādi aukṛṣya parityajya prāṇam paraṃparayā bhūmai avatāraya prāṇam bhūmai mayataḥ gamyate katham puas prāṇe bhūmai vyākhyāyamāe āyat paśyati etat bhūmaḥ vyākhyāyeta ucyate suṣupta avasthāyām grasteṣu karaṇeṣu darśa vyavahāraiḥ vṛtti darśaāt saṃbhavati prāṇasya āyat paśyati etat lakṣaṇam śrutiḥ śrṛṇoti paśyati ityādiā karaṇa astamaya rūpām avasthām uktvā āgayaḥ etasmin pure jāgrati tasyām avasthāyām vṛtteḥ prāṇasya jāgaraṇam bruvatī pradhāām avasthām etat bhūmaḥ yaḥ vai sukham aviruddham atra eṣa devaḥ paśyati etasmin sukham bhavati avasthāyām yaḥ vai amṛtam prāṇasya aviruddham vai amṛtam katham puas prāṇam tarati śokam vividiṣayā prakaraṇasya utthāam vivakṣitaḥ brūmaḥ ha pitā mātā bhrātā svasā ācāryaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ prāṇam am karoti vai arāḥ ābhau samarpitā asmi prāṇe sarvam samarpitam saṃbhavati vaipulya ātmikā bhūma prāṇasya tasmāt prāptam idam ucyate paramātmā bhavitum arhati kasmāt saṃprasādaḥ suṣuptam ucyate samyak prasīdati asmi bṛhadāraṇyake svapa jāgarita sthāābhyām pāṭhāt tasyām saṃprasāda avasthāyām jāgarti utra saṃprasādaḥ abhipreyate prāṇāt ūrdhvam bhūme upadiśyamāa tasmāt ūrdhvam upadiśyeta āśliṣṭam etat āmā āmaḥ āmaḥ ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam kim tarhi āmoyat arthātaram upadiṣṭam ākhyam vāva āmaḥ bhūyasī prāṇāt arthātaram ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam prāṇāt ūrdhvam upadiśyamānaḥ prāṇāt arthātarabhūtaḥ bhavitum arhati praśaḥ bhagavaḥ prāṇāt prativacam prāṇāt vāva katham prāṇāt adhi upadiśyate ucyate viṣayam ativādi ākṛṣyamāṇam paśyāmaḥ eṣa vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati āsti prāṇāt adhyupadeśaḥ atra ucyate tāvat viṣayasya ativādi tvasya etat aukarṣaṇam śakyam vaktum vādāt yaḥ satyeā ativadati ayam viṣayaḥ bhaviṣyati katham eṣa ugihotrī yaḥ satyam ukte tarhi agihotreṇa vadaam agihotriṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ ucyate eṣa vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati ukte tarhi brūmaḥ parityāga śrutyā atra pratīyate yaḥ utivadati atra vijñāasya vijñāam saṃbadhyeta śrutiḥ parityaktā vyāvṛtti tuśabdaḥ saṃgaccheta eṣa vai ativadati satyam vijijñāsitavyam prayatātara atara vivakṣām sūcayati tasmāt veda praśaṃsāyām prakṛtāyām eṣa mahābrāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ caturaḥ vedāḥ adhīte vedebhyaḥ ṛthātara bhūtaḥ catur vedaḥ praśasyate tādṛś etat draṣṭavyam bhavitavyam atara vivakṣāyāḥ śrutvā tūṣṇīṃbhūtam āradam svayam saat kumāraḥ vyutpādayati aṛta viṣayeṇa ativādi aativādi eṣa vai ativadati yaḥ satyeā ativadati satyam ucyate paramārtha satyam atarāt vyutpātitāya āradāya ham bhagavan pravṛttāya pravṛttāya vijñā sādhaa paraṃparayā upadiśati prāṇāt adhi satyam vaktavyam pratijñātam ucyate gamyate tasmāt prāṇāt adhi bhūme paramātmā bhavitum arhati vividiṣayā bhaviṣyati vivakṣitaḥ etat prāṇasya mukhyayā vṛttyā āyaḥ pathā tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu upakramya upasaṃharati mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram tamaḥ śoka kāraṇam avidyā ucyeta ātmataḥ brāhmaṇam bhaviṣyati atra bhagavaḥ sve mahimi ityādi bhūma samāpteḥ aukarṣaṇāt vaipulya ātmikā bhūma rūpatā paramātman sutarām ye śrūyate dharmāḥ paramātmani āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti darśa vyavahāra bhūmai avagamayati ayam darśa vyavahāra sarvam abhūt kam paśyet atarāt yaḥ asau avasthāyām darśa vyavahāra uktaḥ upi ātmaaḥ asaṅga vivakṣayā uktaḥ svabhāva vivakṣayā paramātma tasyām avasthāyām sukham ātmaaḥ vivakṣayā eṣaḥ usya paramaḥ āadaḥ mātrām upajīvati yaḥ vai sukham sukham sukham sukham yaḥ vai amṛtam śrūyamāṇam parama kāraṇam gamayati vikārāṇām tvasya āpekṣika atarāt mahima pratiṣṭhita dharmāḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ paramātmayā iva tasmāt paramātmā siddham atadhṛteḥ adhikaraṇam kasmin khalu otaḥ potaḥ ha uvāca etat vai gārgi brāhmaṇāḥ abhivadati sthūlam aṇu ityādi śrūyate saṃśayaḥ kim varṇa ucyate kim parameśvaraḥ samā māye ityādau varṇe prasiddhi atikramya ayukta oṃkāraḥ idam sarvam ityādau atare varṇasya upāsya tve varṇa ayukta prāpte ucyate vācyaḥ kasmāt ambarāta pṛthivyādeḥ ākāśātasya jātasya dhāraṇāt pṛthivyādeḥ samasta jātasya kāla traya vibhaktasya ūtam protam pratiṣṭhita uktvā kasmiu khalu otaḥ protaḥ aea idam avatāritam upasaṃhṛtam etasmin khalu akṣare gārgi otaḥ protaḥ iyam āta dhṛtiḥ brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati oṃkāraḥ idam sarvam pratipatti sādhaa draṣṭavyam kṣarati atva vyāpi tvābhyām etat kāryasya adhī abhyupagamyate pradhā vādiḥ upi iyam katham ambarāta brahmatva pratipattiḥ uttaram paṭhati praśāsaāt ambarāta dhṛtiḥ parameśvarasya kasmāt praśāsaāt praśāsaam śrūyate etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādi praśāsaam pārameśvaram acetaasya praśāsaam bhavati acetaāām ghaṭa kāraṇāām mṛd ādīām ghaṭa viṣayam praśāsaam aya aya kāraṇāt vācyam ambarāta dhṛtiḥ āyasya kasyacid kim idam aya ayasya ya tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ aya vyāvṛttiḥ tasyāḥ etat bhavati ayat brahmaṇā ukṣara vācyam āśaṅkyate idam ambarāta vidhāraṇam vyāvartayati śrutiḥ vai etat gārgi draṣṭṛ śrotṛ matam matṛ vijñātam vijñātṛ pradhā saṃbhavati draṣṭṛ saṃbhavati aceta draṣṭṛ āyadataḥ śrotṛ āyadataḥ matṛ śārīrasya upādhi mata ukṣara vācya upādhimat bhavati tasmāt iścayaḥ adhikaraṇam etat vai satyakāma aparam oṃkāraḥ tasmāt vidvāḥ ava prakṛtya śrūyate yaḥ puar etam mātreṇa ūm abhidhyāyīta kim asmi vākye abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate āhosvit aparam aparam ekataram aveti saṃśayaḥ aparam idam prāptam kasmāt tejasi sūrye saṃpaaḥ sāmabhiḥ uīyate lokam deśa paricchiam aśuvīta yuktam gata brahmaṇaḥ viśeṣaṇam opapadyate eṣa piṇḍa prāṇasya paratva prāpte abhidhīyate abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate kasmāt īkṣatiḥ darśaam darśa vyāpyam tve abhidhyātavyasya puruṣasya vākyaśeṣe bhavati etasmāt ghaāt parātparam puriśayam īkṣate abhidhyāyateḥ atathābhūtam vastu bhavati maoratha kalpitasya abhidhyāyati tathābhūtam vastu paramātmā ayam vyapadiṣṭaḥ gamyate abhidhyātavyaḥ pratyabhijñāyate puruṣaḥ uktaḥ īkṣaṇe parātparaḥ katham pratyabhijñāyate atra ucyate śabdau tāvat ubhayatra sādhāraṇau atra prakṛtaḥ abhidhyātavyaḥ puruṣaḥ parāmṛśyate tasmāt parātparaḥ yam īkṣitavyaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ kaḥ tarhi jīvaghaaḥ ucyate mūrtiḥ lakṣaṇaḥ ghaaḥ jīvaghaaḥ saidhava khilya yaḥ paramātmā rūpaḥ khilya upādhi kṛtaḥ viṣaya idriyebhyaḥ utra jīvaghaaḥ aparaḥ sāmabhiḥ uīyate lokam diṣṭaḥ yaḥ lokaḥ atarebhyaḥ utra ucyate jīvāām karaṇa parivṛtāām karaṇa ātmai hiraṇyagarbhe saṃghāta bhavati lokaḥ ghaaḥ tasmāt yaḥ puruṣaḥ paramātmā īkṣaṇa bhūtaḥ bhūtaḥ gamyate viśeṣaṇam paramātma parigrahe avakalpate puruṣaḥ paramātmā bhavati yasmāt kiṃcid ayaḥ kiṃcid kāṣṭhā parā gatiḥ atarāt aparam oṃkāraḥ vibhajya abhidhyātavyam bruva gamayati udaraḥ tvacā ha vai pāpmaā paramātma abhidhyātavyam sūcayati yujyate atra ucyate paramātma abhidhyāyiḥ samyak darśa utpattiḥ krama abhiprāyam etat bhaviṣyati adoṣaḥ dahara adhikaraṇam idam asmi pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma usmi atara tasmi aveṣṭavyam vāva vijijñāsitavyam ityādi vākyam samāmāyate yaḥ yam dahare hṛdaya puṇḍarīke śrutaḥ kim bhūtākāśaḥ vijñāātmā athavā paramātmā saṃśayyate kutas saṃśayaḥ pura ayam bhūtākāśe parasmin brahmaṇi kim bhūtākāśaḥ kim saṃśayaḥ puram kim āmā idam puram puram athavā brahmaṇaḥ puram puram jīvasya daharākāśa tve saṃśayaḥ bhūtākāśe rūḍha bhūtākāśaḥ dahara prāptam dahara āyata āpekṣayā dahara yau āvai ayam tāvā eṣa utarhṛdaye bāhya abhyatara bhedasya upameya dyāvāpṛthivī samāhitam avakāśa ākāśasya ekatvāt athavā jīvaḥ prāptam pura jīvasya idam puram sat puram ucyate karmaṇā upārjita bhaktyā vācya brahmaṇaḥ śarīreṇa svāmi rājñaḥ jīvaḥ prāyeṇa hṛdaye pratiṣṭhitam jīvasya idam dahara ārā agra upamita avakalpate upamita abheda vivakṣayā bhaviṣyati atra daharasya ākāśasya āveṣṭavya vijijñāsitavya śrūyate uttaram brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ atra daharākāśaḥ bhavitum arhati bhūtākāśaḥ jīvaḥ kasmāt gatebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ aveṣṭavya abhihitasya daharākāśasya tam brūyuḥ upakramya kim atra vidyate aveṣṭavyam vāva vijijñāsitavyam ākṣepa pūrvakam bhavati brūyāt yau vāva ayam tāvāeṣa utar hṛdaye ubhe yāvāpṛthivī samāhite ityādi puṇḍarīka dahara tve prāpta dahara tvasya ākāśasya aupamye dahara bhūtākāśa daharasya ākāśasya iva ṛtayati gamyate yadi bhūtākāśe rūḍhaḥ tea opapadyate bhūtākāśa śaṅkā bhavati bhavati upameya saṃbhavati saṃbhavati agatikā iyam gatiḥ kalpayitvā bhedam upameya varṇayataḥ bāhya parimāṇa upapadyeta parameśvarasya jyāyāḥ ākāśāt śrutyatarāt parimāṇa eṣa puṇḍarīkaveṣṭa aprāpta dahara ṛtti paratvāt vākyasya tāvattva pratipāda aparatvam pratipādae vākyam bhidyeta kalpita puṇḍarīka veṣṭite deśe samādhām eṣaḥ apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ vijighatsaḥ pipāsaḥ kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ apahata pāpma guṇāḥ bhūtākāśe saṃbhavati yadi jīve saṃbhavati itarebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ āśaṅkā bhavati bhavati dahara śakyam dahara śakyam yad ātmatayā jīvasya vivakṣyeta brahmaṇaḥ vivakṣyatām yuktam brahmapuram purasya upalakṣita rājñaḥ iva jīvasya idam pura deśa varti atra brūmaḥ idam brahmaṇaḥ puram sat brahmapuram ucyate tasmimukhya adhiṣṭhā etasmāt ghaāt parātparam puriśayam īkṣate vai ayam puruṣaḥ sarvāsu pūrṣu puriśayaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ athavā jīvapure asmi saṃihitam upalakṣyate sālagrāme viṣṇuḥ saṃihitaḥ citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate amutra puṇya citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate karmaṇā amata phalatvam uktvā yaḥ vrajati etān akāmān sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati daharākāśa vijñāasya ata phalatvam vada paramātma sūcayati etat daharasya ākāśasya āveṣṭavya vijijñāsitavya atra brūmaḥ yadi āveṣṭavya tve uktaḥ ayam tāvā eṣa utar hṛdaye ityādi pradarśaḥ opapadyeta etat atar varti vastu sadbhāva darśaāya pradarśyate tam brūyuḥ idam asmi brahmapure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma smi atara kim atra vidyate aveṣṭavyam vāva vijijñāsitavyam ākṣipya parihāra avasare aupamya upakrameṇa dyau pṛthivyā ādīām samāhita pradarśaāt samāhitam dyāvāpṛthivī aveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam śeṣaḥ o upapadyeta asmi kāmāḥ samāhitāḥ eṣaḥ apahata pāpmā prakṛtam dyāvāpṛthivī samādhā ādhāram ākāśam ākṛṣya yaḥ auvidya vrajati etān satyā kāmāḥ samuccaya arthe caśabde aum ādhāram āśritān kāmāḥ vijñeyāḥ śeṣaḥ tasmāt upakrame hṛdaya puṇḍarīka adhiṣṭhāḥ sthaiḥ samāhitaiḥ ādibhiḥ satyaiḥ kāmaiḥ vijñeyaḥ uktaḥ gamyate uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ parameśvaraḥ sthitam parameśvaraḥ hetubhyaḥ uttare hetavaḥ idāīm prapañcyate itas parameśvaraḥ yasmāt dahara śeṣe parameśvarasya pratipādakau śabdau bhavataḥ imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ ahar ahar gacchatyaḥ etam lokam vidati prakṛtam daharam śabdena abhidhāya viṣayā gatiḥ prajā vācyāām jīvāām abhidhīyamānā daharasya tām gamayati aharahar jīvāām suṣupta avasthāyām viṣayam śrutyatare satā somya bhavati evamādau kila gāḍham suṣuptam brahmībhūtaḥ tām gataḥ prakṛte dahare prayujyamānaḥ āśaṅkām gamayati gamayet gamayet yadi brahmaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭhī samāsa vṛttyā vyutpādyeta brahmā lokaḥ lokaḥ gamayiṣyati etat aharahar gamanam sāmāādhikaraṇya vṛtti parigrahe ahar ahar imāḥ prajāḥ lokam satyaloka ākhyam gacchati śakyam kalpayitum mahimā usya asmi hetoḥ parameśvaraḥ ayam katham prakṛtyāḥ aupamya pūrvakam tasmin prayujya apahatapāpma upadiśya tam ativṛtta prakaraṇam yaḥ setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ eṣām vidhṛtiḥ sāmādhikaraṇyāt vidhārayitā ucyate kticaḥ kartari smaraṇāt udaka saṃtāasya vidhārayitā setuḥ kṣetra saṃpadām saṃbhedāya ayam eṣām bhiāām lokāām varṇa āśrama ādīām vidhārayitā setuḥ saṃbhedāya saṃkarāya prakṛte dahare vidharaṇa lakṣaṇam mahimāam ayam mahimā parameśvaraḥ śrutyatarāt etasya vai akṣarasya gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādeḥ iścite parameśvara vākye śrūyate eṣa īśvaraḥ eṣa eṣa pālaḥ eṣa setuḥ vidharaṇaḥ eṣām āma saṃbhedāya hetoḥ parameśvaraḥ ayam itas parameśvaraḥ usmiatarākāśaḥ ucyate yatkāraṇam parameśvare prasiddhaḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ irvahitā ha vai imāi bhūtāya ākāśāt samutpadyate prayoga darśaāt jīve bhūtākāśaḥ satyām prasiddhau grahītavyaḥ yadi parameśvaraḥ parigṛhyeta jīvasya vākyaśeṣe yaḥ eṣa saṃprasādaḥ usmāt śarīrāt samutthāya upasaṃpadya sve rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate eṣaḥ ha uvāca atra saṃprasāda śrutyatare suṣupta avasthāyām avasthāvatam jīvam śakoti upasthāpayitum ārthātaram vyapāśrayasya jīvasya śarīrāt samutthāam saṃbhavati vyapāśrayāṇām vāyu ādīām ākāśāt samutthāam adṛṣṭaḥ parameśvara viṣayaḥ parameśvara samabhivyāhārāt vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ irvahitā evamādau parameśvara viṣayaḥ abhyupagataḥ viṣayaḥ bhaviṣyati tasmāt asmi atara atra jīvaḥ ucyate kasmāt jīvaḥ upādhi pariccheda abhimāī upamīyeta upādhi abhimaya māasya apahata prājāpatyāt vākyāt yaḥ apahata pāpmā apahata pāpma guṇakam aveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam pratijñāya yaḥ eṣaḥ akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyata eṣaḥ akṣi stham draṣṭāram jīvam irdiśati etam auvyākhyāsyāmi tam puas puaḥ parāmṛśya yaḥ eṣa svape carati eṣaḥ etat suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasaḥ svapam eṣaḥ jīvam avasthātara gatam vyācaṣṭe apahata pāpma etat amṛtam abhayam etat khalu ayam saṃprati am ayam aham asmi o imāi bhūtāi suṣupta avasthāyām doṣam upalabhya etam upakramya eṣa saṃprasādaḥ asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya upasaṃpadya sve rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ jīvam śarīrāt samutthitam uttamam tasmāt saṃbhavaḥ jīve pārameśvarāṇām dharmāṇām asmi jīvaḥ uktaḥ kaścid brūyāt tam brūyāt tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣa vyāvṛtti ottarasmāt vākyāt jīvasya āśaṅkā saṃbhavati kasmāt jīvaḥ vivakṣyate āvirbhūtam rūpam gatyā etat bhavati yaḥ eṣaḥ akṣiṇi akṣi lakṣitam draṣṭāram vyutthāpya etam puas puas tam vyākhyeya tve ākṛṣya svapa suṣupta upayāsa upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate pāramārthikam svarūpam rūpatayā eam jīvam vyācaṣṭe rūpeṇa upasaṃpattavyam apahata pāpma dharmakam jīvasya pāramārthikam svarūpam asi ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ etarat upādhi kalpitam yāvat sthāṇau iva buddhim dvaita lakṣaṇām avidyām aham asmi pratipadyate tāvat jīvasya yadā idriya maaḥ saṃghātāt vyutthāpya śrutyā pratibodhyate āsi idriya maaḥ saṃghātaḥ saṃsārī kim tarhi satyam caitaya asi pratibudhya asmāt abhimāāt samuttiṣṭha bhavati yaḥ ha vai paramam veda brahmā bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ pāramārthikam rūpam śarīrāt samutthāya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate katham puas svam rūpam iṣpadyate saṃbhavati kūṭasthaityasya suvarṇa ādīām dravya atara saṃparkāt abhibhūta rūpāṇām abhivyakta viśeṣāṇām kṣāra prakṣepa ādibhiḥ rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ akṣatra ādīām ahai abhibhūta prakāśāām abhibhāvaka viyoge rātrau rūpeṇa abhiṣpattiḥ ityasya keacid abhibhavaḥ saṃbhavati saṃsargi iva śrutim vijñātayaḥ jīvasya rūpam śarīrāt samutthitasya jīvasya sarvaḥ jīvaḥ paśya śrṛṇva vyavaharati ayathā vyavahāra śarīrāt samutthitasya vyavahāraḥ virudhyeta kimātmakam idam śarīrāt kim ātmikā rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ atra ucyate viveka vijñā utpatteḥ idriya maaḥ viṣaya veda upādhibhiḥ aviviktam iva jīvasya svarūpam bhavati śuddhasya sphaṭikasya svācchyam śauklyam svarūpam viveka rakta īlā upādhibhiḥ aviviktam iva bhavati pramāṇa jaita viveka svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate ucyate upādhya viviktasya jīvasya kṛtam viveka vijñāam śarīrāt samutthāam viveka vijñāa rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ kevala avagatiḥ viveka aviveka mātreṇa aśarīra matra aśarīram śarīreṣu kauteya karoti lipyate aśarīra smaraṇāt tasmāt viveka vijñā ucyate yādṛśau āvirbhāva āvirbhāvau svarūpasya saṃbhavataḥ mithyājñā kṛtaḥ parameśvarayoḥ bhedaḥ vastu kṛtaḥ asaṅga kutas etat pratipattavyam yaḥ eṣa kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ upadiśya etat amṛtam abhayam etat upadiśati yaḥ kṣiṇi prasiddhaḥ draṣṭā vibhāvyate mṛta abhaya lakṣaṇāt brahmaṇaḥ yaḥ praticchāyā ayam prajāpateḥ mṛṣāvādi dvitīye paryāye yaḥ eṣa svape carati prathama paryāya irdiṣṭāt akṣi puruṣāt draṣṭuḥ etam uvyākhyāsyāmi kiṃca aham adya svape hastiam adrākṣam tam paśyāmi pratibuddhaḥ pratyācaṣṭe draṣṭāram tam yaḥ aham svapam adrākṣam aham jāgaritam paśyāmi paryāye khalu ayam saṃprati ayam aham asmi imāi bhūtāi suṣupta avasthāyām vijñā vijñātāram viāśam apītaḥ bhavati vijñāa viāśa abhiprāyam vijñātṛ viāśa abhiprāyam vijñātuḥ vijñāteḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate viāśi caturthe paryāye etam uvyākhyāsyāmi o upakramya maghava martyam vai idam saṃprasāda uditam jīvam rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate darśaya parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ mṛta abhaya svarūpāt ayam jīvam kecid paramātma vivakṣāyām etam ākarṣaṇam etam upakrama sūcitam apahata pāpma guṇakam uvyākhyāsyāmi kalpayati etam saṃihita avalambiī viprakṛṣyeta śrutiḥ uparudhyeta paryāya atara abhihitasya etam pratijñāya caturthāt ayam ayam vyācakṣāṇasya prajāpateḥ pratāraka prasajyeta tasmāt avidyā pratyupasthāpitam apāramārthikam jaivam rūpam rāga dveṣa kaluṣitam viparītam apahata pāpma guṇakam pārameśvaram svarūpam pratipadyate rajju ādī apare pāramārthikam jaivam rūpam smadīyāḥ kecid ekatva samyagdarśa pratipakṣa bhūtāām pratiṣedhāya idam śārīrakam ārabdham ekaḥ parameśvaraḥ kūṭasthaityaḥ vijñāadhātuḥ avidyayā māyayā māyāvi ekadhā vibhāvyate āyaḥ vijñāadhātuḥ idam parameśvara vākye jīvam āśaṅkya sūtra kāraḥ āsaṃbhavāt ayam abhiprāyaḥ aśuddha buddha svabhāve kūṭasthaitye asaṅge viparītam jaivam rūpam vyomi iva tala mala parikalpitam ekatva pratipāda aparaiḥ vākyaiḥ yāya upetaiḥ dvaita vāda pratiṣedhaiḥ apaeṣyāmi jīvāt aya draḍhayati jīvasya parasmāt aya pratipipādayiṣati kim avidyā kalpitam prasiddham bhedam pravṛttāḥ vidhayaḥ virudhyate mayate pratipādyam ekatvam ityādiā varṇitaḥ asmābhiḥ virodha parihāraḥ yaḥ yam dahara vākyaśeṣe darśitaḥ yaḥ eṣa saṃprasādaḥ ityādiḥ dahare parameśvare upāsa aarthaka paryavasāyī kim tarhi parameśvara paryavasāyī katham saṃprasāda uditaḥ jīvaḥ jāgarita vyavahāre idriya pañjara adhyakṣaḥ bhūtvā śaraṇam prepsuḥ rūpāt abhimāāt samutthāya suṣupta avasthāyām śabditam upasaṃpadya vijñāavat parityajya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate upasaṃpattavyam svea rūpeṇa ayam abhiiṣpadyate eṣaḥ apahata pāpma guṇaḥ upāsyaḥ evamarthaḥ yam parameśvara vādiḥ asmi ākāśasya alpatvam śrūyamāṇam parameśvare jīvasya ārā agra upamitasya alpatvam avakalpate parihāraḥ vaktavyaḥ uktaḥ parihāraḥ parameśvare āpekṣikam alpatvam avakalpate arbhaka okaḥ e ti ce icāyya atra parihāraḥ ausaṃdhātavyaḥ sūcayati śrutyā idam alpatvam pratyuktam prasiddhe upami māayā ayam ayam tāvā eṣa utar hṛdaye aukṛteḥ aukṛti adhikaraṇam sūryaḥ bhāti vidyutaḥ bhāti kutas yam agiḥ tam sarvam bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti samāmaati yam sarvam yasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti kim dhātuḥ kaścid uta vicikitsāyām dhātuḥ tāvat prāptam kutas dhātūām sūrya ādīām bhā svabhāvakam cadra tārakā svabhāvake sūrye bhāsate prasiddham sūryeṇa sarvam idam bhāsate upi svabhāvaḥ kaścid avagamyate svabhāvakaḥ tasmāt dhātuḥ kaścid prāpte brūmaḥ ayam bhavitum arhati kasmāt aukṛteḥ aukaraṇam aukṛtiḥ etat tam bhātam aubhāti sarvam aubhāam parigrahā iva kalpate bhā rūpaḥ saṃkalpaḥ dhātum kaṃcid sūrya prasiddham sama dhātūām sūrya ādīām dhātum ayam pratyapekṣā yam pradīpaḥ pradīpaḥ iyamaḥ caturtham pādam ślokasya sūcayati bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti hetukam sūrya ādeḥ ucyamāam prājñam ātmāam gamayati devāḥ jyotiṣām āyuḥ ha upāsata imṛtam tareṇa sūrya vibhāti aprasiddham viruddham tareṇa tarasya pratighātāt athavā sūrya ādīām śloka paripaṭhitāām idam hetukam vibhāam ucyate kim tarhi sarvam idam sarvasya āma kāraka jātasya yā abhivyaktiḥ sattā aimittā sūrya sattā aimittā sarvasya jātasya abhivyaktiḥ sūryaḥ bhāti tatraśabdam āhara grahaṇam brahmavidyāyām vidyāsu adhikāraḥ abhyupagamyeta saṃbhavati katham asau ādityaḥ atra mauṣyāḥ ādityam adhyāsena upāsīra upāsakeṣu abhyupagamyamāeṣu ādityaḥ katham ayam ādityam upāsīta vasavaḥ rudrāḥ
