prepseyuḥ agiḥ pādaḥ vāyuḥ pādaḥ ādityaḥ pādaḥ diśaḥ pādaḥ vāyuḥ saṃvargaḥ ādityaḥ ādeśaḥ ityādiṣu upāsaeṣu ātmanām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati imām gautama bharadvājau ayam vai gautamaḥ yam bharadvājaḥ ityādiṣu ṛṣīṇām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati kutas idam maṇḍalam sthāam ahar rātrābhyām bambhramat avabhāsayati tasmin vacaāḥ śabdāḥ prayujyate maṇḍalasya hṛdaya ādiāḥ vigraheṇa arthi ādiāḥ vagatum śakyate mṛd aceta atva avagamāt etat matra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ vigrahavat avagamāt ayam adoṣaḥ kiṃcid svatatram pramāṇam avyabhicarita viṣayebhyaḥ pramāṇebhyaḥ lokāt prasiddhaḥ ucyate atra ādīām ayatamam pramāṇam itihāsa purāṇāām pauruṣeya pramāṇa atara tām ākāṅkṣati arthavādāḥ vigraha sadbhāve pratipadyate kasyacid arthasya pramāṇam tasmāt ādīām adhikārasya tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣam vyāvartayati ācāryaḥ adhikārasya ādīām yadi vidyāsu vyāmiśrāsu udhikārasya śuddhāyām brahmavidyāyām saṃbhavaḥ arthi sāmarthya adhikārasya kvacid etāvatā saṃbhavaḥ upodyeta mauṣyāṇām brāhmaṇa ādīām sarveṣu rājasūya adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati yaḥ utra bhaviṣyati vidyām prakṛtya bhavati darśaam śrautam adhikārasya sūcakam yaḥ yaḥ devāām pratyabudhyata abhavat ṛṣīṇām mauṣyāṇām ha ūcuḥ hata tam avicchāmaḥ yam aviṣya lokān apaḥ kāmāḥ idraḥ ha vai devāām abhipravavrāja virocaḥ asurāṇām ityādi gadharva yājñavalkya saṃvāda atra brūmaḥ viṣayāḥ vacaāḥ śabdāḥ cetaāvatam aiśvarya upetam tam tam ātmāam samarpayati matra arthavāda vyavahārāt aiśvarya āām ātmabhiḥ avasthātum iṣṭam tam tam vigraham grahītum sāmarthyam śrūyate subrahmaṇya arthavāde medhātitheḥ meṣaḥ medhātithim ha idraḥ meṣaḥ bhūtvā jahāra ādityaḥ puruṣaḥ bhūtvā upajagāma ha mṛd cetaāḥ adhiṣṭhātāraḥ abhyupagamyate mṛd abravīt āpobruvaḥ ityādi darśaāt jyodiḥ ādeḥ bhūtadhātoḥ acetaa abhyupagamyate cetaāḥ adhiṣṭhātāraḥ ātmāo matra arthavāda vyavahārāt matra arthavādayoḥ vigraha sāmarthyam atra brūmaḥ apratyayau sadbhāva asadbhāvayoḥ kāraṇam āya aya prasthitaḥ pathi patitam parṇa pratipadyate atra viṣamaḥ upayāsaḥ parṇa viṣayam pratyakṣam pravṛttam astitvam pratipadyate atra arthe rthavāde pravṛttiḥ śakyā adhyavasātum mahāvākye rtha pratyāyake pratyāyaka surāṃ pibet vākye pada traya saṃbadhāt surā pāa pratiṣedhaḥ ekaḥ ṛthaḥ avagamyate puaḥ surām pibet pada dvaya saṃbadhāt surā pāa atra ucyate viṣamaḥ upayāsaḥ yuktam surā pāa pratiṣedhe uddeśa arthavādayoḥ arthavāda sthāi avayam pratipadya kaimarthya vaśe kāmam stāvaka pratipadyate vāyavyam śvetam ālabheta kāmaḥ atra uddeśa varti vāyavya padāām vidhinā vāyuḥ vai kṣepiṣṭhā svea bhāgadheyena upadhāvati eam bhūtim gamayati maitrāyaṇī saṃhitā eṣām arthavāda gatāām padāām bhavati vāyuḥ vai ālabheta kṣepiṣṭhā devatāḥ vai ālabheta ityādi pratipadye daivatyam idam vidhim stuvati yovātara pramāṇa atara gocaraḥ bhavati pravartate pramāṇa atara viruddhaḥ ubhayam kim pramāṇa atara guṇavādaḥ āhostvit pramāṇa atara vidyamāārthavādaḥ pratīti śaraṇaiḥ vidyamāārthavādaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ guṇāuvādaḥ vidhibhiḥ idra daivatyāi havīṃṣi codayadbhiḥ apekṣitam idra ādīām rūpam rahitāḥ idra cetasyā āropayitum śakyate cetasya ārūḍhāyai tasyai tasyai devatāyai haviḥ pradātum śakyate śrāvayati yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam tām dhyāyet vaṣaṭ kariṣye svarūpam saṃbhavati arthayoḥ yādṛśam svarūpam avagatam avagatam tādṛśam pratyākhyātum yuktam itihāsa purāṇam mārgeṇa saṃbhavam atra arthavāda mūlaka prabhavati vigraha sādhayitum mūlam saṃbhavati bhavati asmākam apratyakṣam ciraṃtan pratyakṣam vyāsa ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavaharati yaḥ brūyāt pūrveṣām ādibhiḥ vyavahartum sāmarthyam vaicitryam pratiṣedhet idāīm iva sārvabhaumaḥ kṣatriyaḥ brūyāt uparudhyāt idāīm iva vyavasthā vidhāyi śāstram aarthakam kuryāt tasmāt utkarṣa vaśāt cirantan ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavajahuḥ śliṣyate smarati svādhyāyāt iṣṭadevatā saṃprayogaḥ ityādi smaryamāṇaḥ śakyate sāhasa mātreṇa pratyākhyātum śrutiḥ yoga māhātmyam prakhyāpayati samutthite ātmake yoga guṇe pravṛtte rogaḥ jarā mṛtyuḥ prāptasya ṛṣīṇām yuktam tasmāt mūlam itihāsa purāṇam prasiddhiḥ saṃbhave yuktā tasmāt matra ādīām vigrahavat avagamaḥ arthi ādīām brahmavidyāyām adhikāraḥ apaśūdrā adhikaraṇam mauṣya aiyamam apodya ādīām vidyāsu adhikāraḥ uktaḥ śūdrasya adhikāraḥ etām āśaṅkām ivartayitum idam adhikaraṇam ārabhyate śūdrasya adhikāraḥ tāvat prāptam arthi sāmarthyayoḥ tasmāt śūdraḥ yajñe avaklṛptaḥ śūdraḥ avaklṛptaḥ iṣedha karmasu kāraṇam śūdrasya agi vidyāsu adhikārasya apavādakam āhavaīya rahitā veditum śakyate bhavati śrautam śūdra adhikārasya upodbalakam saṃvarga jāaśrutim pautrāyaṇam śuśrūṣum śūdra parāmṛśati aha hāre tvā śūdra tava gobhiḥ vidura prabhṛtayaḥ tasmāt adhikriyate śūdraḥ vidyāsu prāpte brūmaḥ śūdrasya adhikāraḥ veda adhyaya ābhāvāt vidita veda veda artheṣu adhikriyate śūdrasya veda adhyayaam upaaya veda adhyayaasya upaayaasya varṇa traya viṣaya arthi sāmarthya idhikāra kāraṇam bhavati sāmarthyam laukikam kevalam kāraṇam bhavati śāstrīya ṛthe śāstrīyasya sāmarthyasya apekṣita śāstrīyasya sāmarthyasya idam śūdraḥ yajñe avaklṛptaḥ yāya avaklṛpta dyotayati yāyasya puas saṃvarga śūdra śravaṇam darśaam dyotakam bhavati atra kāmam ayam śūdra saṃvarga śūdram adhikuryāt viṣaya sarvāsu vidyāsu arthavāda kvacid ayam śūdram adhikartum utsahate śakyate ayam śūdra udhikṛta viṣaye yojayitum katham ucyate kamvaraḥ eam etat satam raikvam āttha asmāt haṃsa vākyāt śrutavataḥ jāaśruteḥ pautrāyaṇasya śuc utpede tām ṛṣiḥ raikvaḥ śūdra sūcayāṃbabhūva gamyate jātiśūdrasya katham ucyate śucam abhidudrāva śucā abhidudruve śucā raikvam abhidudrāva śūdraḥ avayava rūḍhi arthasya ayam ūsyām ākhyāyikāyām itas jātiśūdraḥ yatkāraṇam kṣatriyeṇa samabhivyāhārāt gamyate saṃvarga vākyaśeṣe caitrarathiḥ abhipratārī kṣatriyaḥ saṃkīrtyate ha śauakam kāpeyam abhipratāriṇam kākṣaseim pariviṣyamāṇau brahmacārī bibhikṣe caitrarathi abhipratāriṇaḥ kāpeya avagatavyam kāpeya citrarathasya avagataḥ vai citraratham kāpeyāḥ ayājayaḥ samāāvayāām prāyeṇa samāāvayāḥ yājakāḥ bhavati tasmāt caitrarathi rāma ekaḥ kṣatra patiḥ ajāyata kṣatra avagamāt avagatavyam kṣatriyeṇa abhipratāriṇā samāāyām saṃvarga jāa sūcayati samāāām prāyeṇa samabhivyāhārā bhavati kṣattṛ preṣaṇa aiśvarya avagatiḥ śūdrasya adhikāraḥ itas śūdrasya adhikāraḥ pradeśeṣu upaaya saṃskārāḥ parāmṛśyate tam ha upaiye adhīhi bhagavaḥ ha upasasāda parā manas anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhā brahmaiṣṭhāḥ āveṣamāṇāḥ eṣa ha vai sarvam vakṣyati ha samidh pāṇayaḥ bhagavatam pippalādam pradarśitā upaaya bhavati śūdrasya abhilapyate śūdraḥ caturthaḥ varṇaḥ ekajātiḥ jāti smaraṇāt śūdre pātakam saṃskāram arhati ādibhiḥ abhāvaiḥ dhāraṇe itas śūdrasya adhikāraḥ śūdra iḥ dhārite jābālam gautamaḥ upaetum auśāsitum pravavṛte etat abrāhmaṇaḥ vivaktum arhati samidham somya āhara tvā eṣye satyāt agāḥ adhyaya itas śūdrasya adhikāraḥ adhyaya pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati veda pratiṣedhaḥ veda adhyaya pratiṣedhaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ śūdrasya pratiṣedhaḥ tāvat ha vedam upaśrṛṇvataḥ trapu jatubhyām śrotra pratipūraṇam ha vai etat śamaśāaṃ aṃga pratiṣedhaḥ ha vai etat śamaśāam aṃga pratiṣedhaḥ ha vai etat śamaśāam aṃga pratiṣedhaḥ śūdraḥ tasmāt śūdra samīpe ādhyetavyam adhyaya pratiṣedhaḥ yasya samīpe ādhyetavyam bhavati katham aśrutam adhīyīta bhavati veda uccāraṇe jihvā chedaḥ dhāraṇe bhedaḥ arthāt pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati śūdrāya matim dadyāt yeṣām vaśāt vidura dharmavyādha prabhṛtīām jñā utpattiḥ śakyate pratiṣeddhum jñā aikātika śrāvayet caturaḥ varṇāḥ itihāsa purāṇa cāturvarṇyasya smaraṇāt veda pūrvakaḥ śūdrāṇām sthitam kampaāt kampa adhikaraṇam avasitaḥ prāsaṅgikaḥ vicāraḥ prakṛtām idāīm vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ idam vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ idam vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ idam vicāra kiṃca sarvam ejati bhayam vajram udyatam ye etat viduḥ amṛtāḥ bhavati etat vākyam dhātvartha augamāt lakṣitam vākye sarvam idam āśrayam spadate kiṃcid bhaya kāraṇam vajra śabditam udyatam vijñāāt śrūyate kaḥ asau kim bhayāakam vajram apratipatteḥ vicāre kriyamāṇe prāptam tāvat vāyuḥ vāyoḥ idam māhātmyam saṃkīrtyate katham sarvam idam vṛttau vāyau śabdite pratiṣṭhāya ejati bhayāakam vajram udyamyate vāyau vivartamāe vidyut staayitu vṛṣṭi aśaayaḥ vivartate vāyu vijñāāt idam śrutyataram vāyuḥ vyaṣṭiḥ vāyuḥ samaṣṭiḥ apa puar mṛtyum jayati yaḥ veda tasmāt vāyuḥ ayam pratipattavyaḥ prāpte brūmaḥ idam pratipattavyam kutas ālocaāt gratha bhāgayoḥ upalabhāmahe katham akasmāt atarāle pratipadyemahi pūrvatra tāvat śukram amṛtam ucyate tasimat lokāḥ śritāḥ ātyeti kaḥ saṃidhāāt sarvam ejati pratyabhijñāāt gamyate upi ayam paramātmayā iva prayuktaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam ejayitṛ idam paramātma vāyu mātrasya martyaḥ jīvati kaḥ itareṇa jīvati yasmin etau upāśritau bhayāt agiḥ tapati bhayāt tapati sūryaḥ bhayāt idraḥ vāyuḥ mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ brahmā vāyuḥ vāyukasya jagataḥ bhaya abhidhāāt saṃidhāāt bhayam vajram udyatam bhaya pratyabhijñā āirdiṣṭam gamyate vajra upi ayam bhaya sāmāyāt prayuktaḥ vajram udyatam mama śirasi ipatet yadi aham śāsaam kuryām iyam ea rāja śāsae pravartate idam c iva sūrya ādikam asmāt brahmaṇaḥ bibhyat iyam ea vyāpāre pravartate bhayāakam vajra upamitam viṣayam śrutyataram bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣā udeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agiḥ idraḥ mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ idam gamyate jñāāt tam viditvā mṛtyum eti āyaḥ pathā matravarṇāt vāyuvijñāāt kvacid abhihitam āpekṣikam vāyu ādeḥ ārta abhidhāāt atra paramātma aiścayaḥ ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt bhavyāt paśyasi vada paramātmanaḥ pṛṣṭa darśaāt adhikaraṇam eṣa saṃprasādaḥ usmāt śarīrāt samutthāya upasaṃpadya sve rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate śrūyate saṃśayyate kim viṣayatama upaham kim kim tāvat prāptam prasiddham kutas rūḍha abhidhāāt atra svārtham parityajya brahmaṇi vartate kiṃcid svārtha parityāge kāraṇam āḍīkhaṇḍe etat asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati etaiḥ raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate mumukṣoḥ abhihitā tasmāt prasiddham prāpte brūmaḥ kasmāt darśaāt prakaraṇe vaktavya tve āuvṛttiḥ yaḥ apahata pāpmā apahata pāpma guṇakasya ātmaaḥ ādau aveṣṭavya tve vijijñāsitavya tve pratijñāāt etam uvyākhyāsyāmi ausaṃdhāāt aśarīram vāva satam apriye spṛśataḥ aśarīra tāyai abhidhāāt ayatra aśarīra uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ mumukṣoḥ abhihitā asau ātyatikaḥ mokṣaḥ utkrāti saṃbadhāt ātyatike mokṣe utkrātī staḥ vakṣyāmaḥ atara atara adhikaraṇam vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ atarā amṛtam śrūyate kim kim prasiddham bhūtākāśam vicāre parigrahaḥ yuktaḥ tasmin rūḍha āma rūpaiḥ vahaṇasya avakāśa dā dvāreṇa tasmin yojayitum śakya sraṣṭṛ ādeḥ spaṣṭasya liṅgasya aśravaṇāt prāpte idam ucyate bhavitum arhati kasmāt atara atarā āma rūpābhyām arthātara ākāśam vyapadiśati brahmaṇaḥ ayaḥ āma rūpābhyām arthātaram saṃbhavati sarvasya jātasya āma rūpābhyām vyākṛta āma rūpayoḥ irvahaṇam iraṅkuśam brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi kartṛka jīvasya pratyakṣam āma viṣayam bāḍham abhedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ sraṣṭṛ abhihitam bhavati amṛtam vādasya ayam prapañcaḥ utkrātyoḥ adhikaraṇam bṛhadāraṇyake ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake katamaḥ yaḥ yam vijñā prāṇeṣu puruṣaḥ upakramya bhūyāātma viṣayaḥ prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ kim saṃsāri mātrā avākhyā aparam vākyam uta asaṃsāri pratipāda aparam viśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam saṃsāri viṣayam kutas upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām upakrame yaḥ yam vijñā amayaḥ prāṇeṣu śārīra upasaṃhāre eṣa mahā ajaḥ yaḥ yam vijñā prāṇeṣu aparityāgāt madhye prapañcaāt prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara idam vākyam śārīra mātrau ākhyā kasmāt suṣuptau utkrātau bhedea parameśvarasya suṣuptau tāvat ayam puruṣaḥ bāhyam kiṃcaa veda ātaram bhedea parameśvaram vyapadiśati puruṣaḥ veditṛ bāhya abhyatara veda aprasaṅge parameśvaraḥ sarvajñatva lakṣaṇayā prajñayā ama utkrātau ayam utsarjayāti jīvāt bhedea parameśvaram vyapadiśati jīvaḥ svāmi parameśvaraḥ tasmāt utkrātyoḥ bhedea parameśvaraḥ atra vivakṣitaḥ gamyate ādya tamadhyeṣu śārīra vākyasya atra brūmaḥ upakrame tāvat yaḥ yam vijñā prāṇeṣu saṃsāri svarūpam vivakṣitam kim tarhi saṃsāri svarūpam brahmaṇā tām vivakṣati dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva evamādi uttaragratha pravṛttiḥ saṃsāri dharmaiḥ ākaraṇa parā lakṣyate upasaṃhāre yathopakramam upasaṃharati vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ yaḥ yam vijñā amayaḥ prāṇeṣu yaḥ yam vijñā amayaḥ prāṇeṣu saṃsārī lakṣyate vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ parameśvaraḥ asmābhiḥ pratipāditaḥ yaḥ madhye prācīm diśam prasthāpitaḥ pratīcīm diśam pratiṣṭheta saṃsāri vivakṣati kim tarhi rahitatvam asaṃsāri katham etat avagamyate ūrdhvam vimokṣāya brūhi pade pade pṛcchati bhavati saṅgaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ pade pade prativakti aavāgatam puṇye aavāgatam pāpea tīrṇaḥ śokāhṛdayasya bhavati tasmāt asaṃsāri pratipāda aparam etat vākyam avagatavyam itas asaṃsāri pratipāda aparam etat vākyam avagatavyam vākye śabdāḥ asaṃsāri pratipāda aparāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva āḥ bhavati sarvasya vaśī sarvasya īśaḥ sarvasya evaṃjātīyakāḥ asaṃsāri svabhāva pratipāda aparāḥ sādhuā karmaṇā anuprāptavyam asaṃsāri svabhāva prat bhūyāḥ evaṃjātīyakāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedhaāḥ tasmāt asaṃsārī parameśvaraḥ uktaḥ avagamyate śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat prathama udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ āumāikam viyasta āumāika adhikaraṇam āumāikam aumāairūpitam pradhāam kāṭhake paṭhyate mahataḥ avyaktāt puruṣaḥ ye yatkramāḥ avyakta puruṣāḥ prasiddhāḥ pratyabhijñāyate vyaktam vyutpatti prasiddham pradhāam abhidhīyate śabdavat aśabda aupapam jagataḥ kāraṇam yāya prasiddhibhyaḥ etat etat kāṭhaka vākyam prasiddhayoḥ avyaktayoḥ astitva atra yādṛśam prasiddham svatatram kāraṇam triguṇam tādṛśam pratyabhijñāyate atra pratyabhijñāyate vyaktam yaugika sūkṣme su durlakṣye prayujyate ayam kasmin cit rūḍhaḥ yā pradhāa vādiām rūḍhiḥ pāribhāṣikī satī pratipadyate krama sāmāyāt bhavati pratyabhijñāe gām amūḍhaḥ adhyavasyati prakaraṇaiḥ ūpaṇāyām atra parikalpitam pradhāam pratīyate viyasta atra parigṛhyate kutas ādīnām rathi ratha klṛptim viddhi ratham buddhim sārathim viddhi maaḥ pragraham idriyāṇi hayāḥ āhuḥ viṣayān teṣu gocarāḥ idriya mao yuktam bhoktā āhuḥ maīṣiṇaḥ taiḥ idriya ādibhiḥ asaṃyataiḥ saṃsāram adhigacchati saṃyataiḥ adhvaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam kim adhvaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam asyām ākāṅkṣāyām tebhyaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ idriya pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam idriyebhyaḥ parāḥ arthebhyaḥ maaḥ maasaḥ parā buddhiḥ buddheḥ mahā mahataḥ avyaktāt puruṣaḥ kiṃcid kāṣṭhā parā gatiḥ ye idriya pūrvasyām prakṛtāḥ parigṛhyate idriya mao buddhayaḥ tāvat pūrvatra ye viṣayāḥ idriyebhyaḥ paratvam idriyāṇām graha viṣayāṇām atigraha viṣayebhyaḥ paratvam maaḥ viṣaya idriya vyavahārasya parā buddhiḥ buddhim āruhya bhogya jātam bhoktāram upasarpati buddheḥ mahā yaḥ ātmāam rathiam viddhi rathi upakṣiptaḥ kutas bhoktuḥ upakaraṇāt paratva svāmi upapaam athavā mahāmatiḥ brahmā pūḥ buddhiḥ khyātiḥ īśvaraḥ saṃvid citiḥ smṛtiḥ paripaṭhyate yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti yaḥ anubhūtiḥ vai vedān prahiṇoti yā prathama hiraṇyagarbhasya buddhiḥ sarvāsām buddhīām paramā pratiṣṭhā mahāātmā ucyate pūrvatra grahaṇea gṛhītā satī hiruk upadiśyate tasyāḥ asmadīyābhyaḥ buddhibhyaḥ paratva etasmin pakṣe paramātma viṣayeṇa grahaṇam draṣṭavyam paramārthataḥ paramātma vijñāātmaoḥ ekam pariśiṣyate teṣu itarāṇi idriya ādīni parama pada didarśayiṣayā samaukrāma pariśiṣyamāṇe idriya maaḥ viṣaya veda saṃyuktasya avidyāvataḥ bhoktuḥ ādīnām rūpaṇea pratyagātma avagatiḥ vivakṣitā eṣa sarveṣu gūḍha utmā prakāśate agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ vaiṣṇavasya parama padasya duravagama uktvā avagama yacchet maasī yacchet ātmai mahati chet yacchet śātaḥ ātmai etat bhavati vācam maasi saṃyacchet bāhya idriya vyāpāram utsṛjya maaḥ mātreṇa avatiṣṭheta viṣaya abhimukham darśa ea jñā uditāyām buddhau adhyavasāya svabhāvāyām dhārayet tām buddhim mahati bhoktari agryāyām buddhau iyacchet prakaraṇavati parasmin puruṣe parasyām kāṣṭhāyām pratiṣṭhāpayet apara ālocaāyām etat pariśeṣābhyām avyakta pradhāam idam idāīm āśaṅkyate katham avyakta śarīrasya yāvatā sthūla spaṣṭataram idam vyakta aspaṣṭa vacaḥ avyakta uttaram ucyate vivakṣyate sūkṣmasya avyakta yadi sthūlam idam svayam avyakta arhati ārambhakam avyakta arhati prakṛti vikāre gobhiḥ śrīṇīta matsaram śrutiḥ ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt idam vyākṛta āma vibhiam prāc avasthāyām parityakta vyākṛta āma rūpam bīja avastham avyakta yogyam adhī atvāt atra yadi idam bīja ātmakam avastham avyakta arham abhyupagamyeta śarīrasya avyakta pratijñāyeta tarhi pradhā āpadyeta jagataḥ avasthāyāḥ atra ucyate yadi vayam svatatrām kāṃcid prāc avasthām jagataḥ tveā abhyupagacchema prasañjayema pradhā akāraṇa vādam iyam asmābhiḥ prāc jagataḥ bhyupagamyate svatatrā abhyupagatavyā arthavatī arthavatī parameśvarasya sraṣṭṛ sidhyati rahitasya pravṛtti aupapatteḥ muktāām autpattiḥ kutas tasyāḥ bīja śakteḥ dāhāt avidyā ātmikā bīja śaktiḥ avyakta śabdaiḥ deśyā parameśvara āśrayā mayī mahāsuṣuptiḥ yasyām pratibodha rahitāḥ śerate saṃsāriṇaḥ jīvāḥ etat kvacid śabdaiḥ diṣṭam etasmin khalu akṣare gārgya otaḥ protaḥ kvacid uditam akṣarāt paratas kvacid sūcitam māyām prakṛtim maheśvaram matra avyaktā idam mahataḥ avyakta prabhava amahataḥ yadā hairaṇyagarbhī buddhiḥ mahā yadā jīvaḥ mahā avyakta adhī atvāt bhāvasya mahataḥ avidyā jīvasya sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ saṃtataḥ vartate avyakta gatam mahataḥ abheda upacārāt vikāre parikalpyate idriya ādīām aviśeṣe śarīrasya abheda upacārāt avyakta grahaṇam idriya ādīām śabdaiḥ gṛhīta pariśiṣṭa śarīrasya varṇayati dvividham sthūlam sthūlam idam vakṣyate atara ubhayam pūrvatra saṃkīrtitam avyakta parigṛhyate sūkṣmasya avyakta adhī jīvāt paratvam yathārtha adhī idriya vyāpārasya idriyebhyaḥ paratvam arthāām taiḥ etat vaktavyam aviśeṣeṇa dvayasya pūrvatra saṃkīrtita pariśiṣṭa tvayoḥ katham gṛhyate sthūlam āmātasya pratipattum prabhavāmaḥ āmātam āmātam avyakta padam pratipādayitum etarat vyakta arthaṃpratipatteḥ uttare āmāte ekavākyatām āpadya kaṃcid pratipādayataḥ ākāṅkṣā matareṇa ekavākyatā pratipattiḥ aviśiṣṭāyām dvayasya grāhya ākāṅkṣāyām yathākāṅkṣam ekavākyatā bādhitā bhavati kutas pratipattiḥ matavyam duḥśodha sūkṣmasya śarīrasya grahaṇam sthūlasya bībhatsa su śodha agrahaṇam kasyacid vivakṣyate atra śodha vidhāyi kiṃcid ākhyātam aa araiḥ diṣṭa kim viṣṇoḥ paramam padam idam vivakṣyate idam asmāt idam asmāt uktvā puruṣāḥ kiṃcid kiṃcid chidyate sāṃkhyaiḥ atara jñāāt vadadbhiḥ svarūpam jñātvā guṇebhyaḥ puruṣasya ataram śakyam jñātum kvacid vibhūti prāptaye jñeyam smarati idam tve ucyate pada avyakta jñātavyam upāsitavyam vākyam śakyam pratipattum tasmāt abhidhīyate asmākam viṣṇoḥ paramam padam darśayitum ayam upayāsaḥ aavadyam ce atra sāṃkhyaḥ asiddham katham śrūyate avyakta uditasya pradhāasya sparśam rūpam avyayam mahataḥ dhruvam icāyya tam mukhāt pramucyate atra yādṛśam mahataḥ smṛtau tādṛśam tasmāt pradhāam idam avyakta śabdaiḥ diṣṭam atra brūmaḥ eha paramātmā gamyate kutas prājñasya prakaraṇam vitatam vartate puruṣāḥ kiṃcid kāṣṭhā parā gatiḥ ityādi irdeśāt eṣa sarveṣu guḍha utmā prakāśate ākāṅkṣaṇāt yacchet jñāāya saṃyamasya mukha pramokṣaṇa pradhā icāyya mukhāt pramucyate sāṃkhyaiḥ iṣyate vijñāāt mukhāt pramucyate abhyupagamaḥ sarveṣu vedāteṣu prājñasya o abhilapyate upayāsaḥ pradhā avyakta vācya yasmāt asmi asmi kaṭhavallīṣu vara pradā asāmarthyāt vaktavya upayāsaḥ viṣayaḥ upayāsaḥ tāvat agim svargyam adhyeṣi mṛtyo prabrūhi tam mahyam agi viṣayaḥ praśaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā ayam etad vidyām auśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ viṣayaḥ praśaḥ ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt bhavyāt paśyasi vada paramātma viṣayaḥ ādim agim tam uvāca yā iṣṭakā yāvatīḥ agi viṣayam hata idam pravakṣyāmi guhyam maraṇam prāpya bhavati gautama prapadyate tvāya sthāṇum yathākarma yathāśrutam vyavahitam viṣayam jāyate mriyate vipaścit ityādi bahu prapañcam paramātma viṣayam pradhā viṣayaḥ praśoḥ pṛṣṭa aupayasaīya atra yaḥ yam viṣayaḥ praśaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā kim ayam dharmāt ayatra adharmāt puar aukṛṣyate kim yaḥ uyam apūrvaḥ praśaḥ utthāpyate kim ayam praśaḥ puar aukṛṣyata yadi ucyeta dvayoḥ viṣayayoḥ praśayoḥ ekatā agi viṣayaḥ viṣayaḥ dvau praśau vaktavyam apūrvaḥ praśaḥ utthāpyate ucyeta vara pradā vyatirekeṇa praśa kalpaāyām adoṣaḥ praśa vyatirekeṇa pradhā upayāsa kalpaāyām adoṣaḥ atra ucyate vayam varapradā vyatirekeṇa kaṃcid kalpayāmaḥ upakrama varapradā aciketaḥ saṃvāda rūpā pravṛttiḥ samāpteḥ lakṣyate mṛtyuḥ kila aciketase pitrā prahitāya trī varā pradadau aciketāḥ kila vareṇa pituḥ saumaasyam vavre dvitīye āgi vidyām vidyām yā iyam prete varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ yadi dharmāt apūrvaḥ praśaḥ utthāpyeta praśa kalpaāt vākyam bādhyeta praṣṭavya apūrvaḥ yam praśaḥ bhavitum arhati apūrvaḥ praśaḥ viṣayaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā jīvaḥ gocara dharmāt praśam arhati atīta ayatra dharmāt praśam arhati praśa chāyā lakṣyate pūrvasya astitva āstitva viṣaya uttarasya atīta vastu viṣaya tasmāt pratyabhijñā praśa bhedaḥ pūrvasya ākarṣaṇam prājñayoḥ ekatva bhavet praṣṭavya praśa bhedaḥ yadi ayaḥ jīvaḥ prājñāt aya tattvam asi ityādi atarebhyaḥ ayatra dharmāt praśasya prativacam jāyate mriyate vipaścit śārīra parameśvarayoḥ abhedam prasaṅge pratiṣedhaḥ bhāgī bhavati jama maraṇayoḥ saṃsparśāt śārīrasya bhavati parameśvarasya svapātam jāgaritātam ubhau mahātam vibhum ātmāam matvā dhīraḥ śocati svapa jāgarita dṛśaḥ jīvasya vibhu viśeṣaṇasya śoka vicchedam darśaya prājñāt jīvaḥ śoka vicchedaḥ agre amutra amutra mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum yaḥ paśyati dṛṣṭim ayam varam aciketaḥ vṛṇīṣva ārabhya taiḥ taiḥ kāmaiḥ aciketāḥ yadā cacāla aciketāḥ mṛtyuḥ aciketasam abhīpsiam aciketasam aciketasam aciketasam tvā kāmāḥ bahavaḥ lolupate praśasya tadīyam uvāca tam durdarśam gūḍham devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti prājñayoḥ abhedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ gamyate praśaimittām praśaṃsām mahatīm mṛtyoḥ pratyapadyata aciketāḥ yadi tam vihāya praśaṃsāataram ayam praśam upakṣipet sarvā praśaṃsā prasāritā tasmāt yā iyam prete aukarṣaṇam ayatra dharmāt praśat chāyā vailakṣaṇyam adūṣaṇam tadīyasya viśeṣasya pūrvatra vyatiriktasya ostitvam pṛṣṭam asaṃsāri yāvat avidyā tāvat gocaratvam jīvasya asi śrutyā pratyāyyate avidyāvat tve apagame kaścid viśeṣaḥ kaścid sam tamase patitām kāṃcid rajjum ahim mayamāaḥ bhītaḥ vepamāaḥ palāyate tam aparaḥ brūyāt mā bhaiṣīḥ ayam ahiḥ rajjuḥ upaśrutya kṛtam bhayam utsṛjet vepathum kāle apagama kāle vastuḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ etat draṣṭavyam jāyate mriyate evamādi bhavati sūtram avidyā kalpita yojayitavyam ekatve viṣayasya prāyaṇa avasthāyām vyatirikta astitva vicikitsaāt svabhāva aapohaāt pūrvasya paryāyasya viṣaya utprekṣyate uttarasya atyaya saṃkīrtaāt viṣaya yuktā pradhā akalpaāyām any vaiṣamyam sāṃkhyaiḥ sattā mātre prathama je prayuktaḥ tam vaidike prayoge abhidhatte buddheḥ mahā mahātam vibhum ātmāam veda aham etam mahātam evamādau prayoga hetubhyaḥ avyakta vaidike prayoge pradhāam abhidhātum arhati āsti āumāikasya śabdavat adhikaraṇam puar pradhāa vādī aśabda pradhā asiddham kasmāt matra ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām vahvīḥ prajāḥ sarūpāḥ ajaḥ ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ śete jahāti eām bhukta bhogām ajoyaḥ atra matre lohita śukla kṛṣṇa śabdaiḥ rajaḥ sattva tamāṃsi abhidhīyate lohitam rajaḥ rañja śuklam sattvam kṛṣṇam tamaḥ āvaraṇa avayava dharmaiḥ lohita śukla kṛṣṇā jāyate ajā mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ avajā chāgyām rūḍhaḥ bāḍham rūḍhiḥ āśrayitum śakyā bahvīḥ prajāḥ traiguṇya avitāḥ jaayati tām prakṛtim ajaḥ ekaḥ puruṣaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ prīyamāṇaḥ viraktaḥ jahāti eām prakṛtim bhukta bhogām apavargām parityajati mucyata tasmāt mūlā kāpilā prāpte brūmaḥ matreṇa śrutimat sāṃkhya vādasya śakyam āśrayitum ayam matraḥ svātatryeṇa kaṃcid vādam samarthayitum utsahate yayā kayācid kalpa ayā ajā saṃpāda opapatteḥ sāṃkhya abhipretaḥ avadhāraṇa arvāc bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva budhaḥ atre svātatryeṇa ayam āma asau abhipretaḥ śakyate iyatum kathaṃcid arvāc bila kalpa ajām ekām matrasya śakyate iyatum idam eṣa arvāc bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva buddhaḥ pratipattiḥ bhavati kā iyam ajā pratipattavyā atra brūmaḥ parameśvarāt pramukhā baa lakṣaṇā caturvidhasya grāmasya prakṛti bhūtā iyam ajā pratipattavyā tuśabdaḥ traya lakṣaṇā iyam ajā vijñeyā traya lakṣaṇā kasmāt parameśvarāt utpattim rohita tām rohitam rūpam tejasaḥ rūpam śuklam apām kṛṣṇam pratyabhijñāyate rohita sāmāyāt rohita ādīām śabdāām viśeṣeṣu viṣaya tvasya asaṃdigdha saṃdigdhasya vādiḥ kiṃkāraṇam upakramya apaśya śaktim pārameśvaryāḥ śakteḥ samasta vidhāyiyāḥ upakrame vagamāt vākyaśeṣe māyām prakṛtim maheśvaram yaḥ yoim yoim adhitiṣṭhati ekaḥ tasyāḥ avagamāḥ svatatrā kācid atreṇa āmāyate śakyate vaktum daivī śaktiḥ avyākṛtā ām arūpā āma rūpayoḥ matreṇa āmāyate ucyate tasyāḥ viṣayeṇa trairūpyeṇa trairūpyam katham trairūpyeṇa rūpā ajā pratipattum śakyate yāvatā tāvat tejobaeṣu aja ākṛtiḥ tejobaāām jāti jāti nimittaḥ ajā saṃbhavati uttaram paṭhati kalpa yaugikaḥ kim tarhi ajā klṛptiḥ baa lakṣaṇāyāḥ yoḥ upadiśyate yadṛcchayā kācid ajā rohita śukla kṛṣṇa varṇā bahu barkarā sarūpa barkarā tām kaścid ajaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ uśayīta kaścid eām bhukta bhogām jahyāt iyam bhūtaprakṛtiḥ varṇā bahu sarūpam lakṣaṇam jātam viduṣā kṣetrajñeā upabhujyate viduṣā parityajyate idam āśaṅkitavyam ekaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ śete ayaḥ jahāti kṣetrajña bhedaḥ pāramārthikaḥ pareṣām iṣṭaḥ iyam kṣetrajña pratipipādayiṣā kiṃtu badha vyavasthā pratipipādayiṣā eṣā prasiddham bhedam aūdya pratipādyate bhedaḥ upādhi nimittaḥ mithyājñā akalpitaḥ pāramārthikaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ gūḍhaḥ vyāpī atarātmā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ādīnām evaṃjātīyakam kalpyate idam aajāyāḥ ajā kalpyate tasmāt baeṣu ajā prayogasya adhikaraṇam parihṛte ajāmatre pratyavatiṣṭhate pratiṣṭhitaḥ tam atre viṣayā aparā śrūyate dvaya darśaāt pañcakāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā yāvataḥ saṃkhyeyā ākāṅkṣyate tāvatī sāṃkhyaiḥ saṃkhyāyate mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ ṣoḍaśakaḥ vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ prasiddhayā pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā prasiddhāām pañcaviṃśateḥ tattvāām prāptam puas śrutimat pradhā ādīām brūmaḥ pradhā ādīām śrutimat pratyāśā kartavyā kasmāt etāi pañcaviṃśatiḥ tattvāi eṣām pañcaśas pañcaśas sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ pañcaviṃśateḥ atarāle parāḥ saṃkhyāḥ dvi ādikāḥ saṃkhyāḥ ucyeta pañcaviṃśati iyam avayava dvāreṇa lakṣyate varṣāṇi vavarṣa śatakratuḥ vārṣikīm aāvṛṣṭim kathayati opapadyate ayam asmi pakṣe āśrayaṇīyā atra samastaḥ bhāṣika svareṇa pada aiścayāt prayoga atare tvā aikapadya ekasvarya vibhaktika avagamāt samasta vīpsā tea pañcaka dvaya grahaṇam saṃkhyāyāḥ ekasyāḥ saṃkhyayā parayā viśeṣaṇam pañcakāḥ upasarja puraḥ saṃkhyayā viśeṣyamāṇāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pratyeṣyate pūlyaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pūlāḥ pratīyate brūmaḥ yuktam pūlī samāhāra abhiprāya kati satyām ākāṅkṣāyām pūlyaḥ viśeṣaṇam āditas upādāāt kati asatyām ākāṅkṣāyām jaāḥ viśeṣaṇam bhavet bhavat idam viśeṣaṇam saṃkhyāyāḥ bhavet uktaḥ tasmāt pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam atirekaḥ bhavati ākāśābhyām pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyāyāḥ tāvat pratiṣṭhām yasmi saptamī sūcitasya tam tve ākarṣaṇāt puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśati avatargataḥ ādhāra ādheya yujyeta atara parigrahe tattva atirekaḥ siddhāta viruddhaḥ prasajyeta pratiṣṭhitaḥ ākāśasya pañcaviṃśata avatargatasya yāyyam atara parigrahe dūṣaṇam katham śravaṇe śrutāām pañcaviṃśati tattvāām upasaṃgrahaḥ pratīyeta jaa tattveṣu arūḍha atara upasaṃgrahe katham tarhi pañcajaāḥ ucyate diś saṃkhye saṃjñāyām smaraṇāt saṃjñāyām samāsaḥ rūḍha abhiprāyeṇa kecid vivakṣyate sāṃkhya tattva abhiprāyeṇa kati asyām ākāṅkṣāyām puaḥ prayujyate ye kecid ṛṣayaḥ ke pañcajaāḥ ucyate yasmin pañcajaāḥ uttarasmin atre svarūpaiḥ ūpaṇāya prāṇasya prāṇam uta cakṣuṣaḥ uta śrotrasya ye maasaḥ viduḥ tra gatāḥ vivakṣyate katham puas tattveṣu katham prasiddhi atikrame vaśāt grahītavyāḥ bhavati jaa bhājaḥ bhavati prāṇeṣu prayuktaḥ vai puruṣāḥ atra ha pitā ha mātā ityādi brāhmaṇam samāsa balāt samudāyasya rūḍha aviruddham katham puara prathama prayoge rūḍhiḥ śakyā āśrayitum śakyā udbhid aprasiddha samabhivyāhārāt viṣayaḥ udbhidā yajeta yūpam vedim karoti ayam pañcajaa saṃjñī ākāṅkṣī samabhivyāhṛteṣu vartiṣyate kaiścid devāḥ pitaraḥ asurāḥ rakṣāṃsi pañcajaāḥ ayaiḥ catvāraḥ varṇāḥ iṣāda pañcamāḥ parigṛhītāḥ kvacid pāñcajayayā viśā prajā prayogaḥ pañcajaa parigrahe kaścid ācāryaḥ pañcaviṃśateḥ tattvāām pratītiḥ evaṃpara vākyaśeṣāt jagāda bhaveyuḥ tāvat mādhyaṃdiāām kāṇvāām katham jaāḥ bhaveyuḥ uttaram paṭhati asatī pūryeta pūrvasmin atre svarūpaiḥ ūpaṇāya devāḥ jyotiṣām katham puar ubhayeṣām tulya idam paṭhyamāam saṃkhyayā keṣāṃcid gṛhyate mādhyaṃdiāām bhavati alābhāt kāṇvāām bhavati matre jyotiṣaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇe grahaṇa agrahaṇe tāvat prasiddhiḥ kācid pradhā aviṣayā yāya prasiddhī parihariṣyete adhikaraṇam pratipāditam brahmaṇaḥ lakṣaṇam pratipāditam viṣayam sāmāyam pratipāditam pradhā aśabda idam aparam āśaṅkyate jama kāraṇatvam brahmaṇaḥ viṣayam sāmāyam pratipādayitum śakyam kasmāt krama vaicitryāt kvacid ātman saṃbhūtaḥ ādikā āmāyate kvacid ādikā sṛjataḥ kvacid ādikā prāṇam asṛjata prāṇāt śraddhām kvacid akrameṇa imān lokāḥ asṛjata ambhaḥ marīcīḥ maramā apaḥ kvacid pūrvikā paṭhyate vai idam agre āsīt vai sat ajāyata idam agre āsīt sat āsīt samabhavat kvacid vādaiḥ ākaraṇe sat pūrvikā prakriyā pratijñāyate ha āhuḥ idam agre āsīt upakramya kutas khalu somya ha uvāca katham sat jāyeta sat somya idam agre āsīt kvacid svayam kartṛkā vyākriyā jagataḥ ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt vyākriyate vikalpasya aupapatteḥ avadhāraṇa yāyyā yāya prasiddhibhyām atara parigrahaḥ yāyyaḥ prāpte brūmaḥ prativedātam sṛjyamāeṣu krama dvārake sraṣṭari kiṃcid vigāam kutas yathābhūtaḥ vedāte sarvajñaḥ īśvaraḥ ekaḥ dvitīyaḥ vyapadiṣṭaḥ tathābhūtaḥ satyam atra tāvat viṣayeṇa bahu syām prajāyeya viṣayeṇa vikārāṇām sraṣṭuḥ abhedam abhāṣata idam sarvam asṛjata idam kim samasta sṛṣṭi nirdeśea sṛṣṭeḥ advitīyam sraṣṭāram ācaṣṭe atra lakṣaṇam vijñātam lakṣaṇam vijñāyate sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya sṛjate vai idam ekaḥ agre āsīt miṣat īkṣata lokau sṛjai evaṃjātīyakasya jātasya kvacid ādikā kvacid ādikā evaṃjātīyakam viṣayeṇa kāraṇam bhavitum arhati śakyate vaktum atiprasaṅgāt samādhāsyati ācāryaḥ viṣayam ārabhya bhavet kāryasya vigīta apratipādya ayam sṛṣṭi prapañcaḥ pratipipādayiṣitaḥ pratibaddhaḥ kaścid śrūyate kalpayitum śakyate upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām viṣayaiḥ vākyaiḥ sākam tāyāḥ sṛṣṭi prapañcasya pratipatti tām somya somya apaḥ mūlam aviccha adbhiḥ somya śuṅgea mūlam aviccha tejasā somya śuṅgea mūlam avicchaḥ mṛd dṛṣṭātaiḥ kāryasya vaditum sṛṣṭi prapañcaḥ śrāvyate gamyate saṃpradāya mṛd loha visphuliṅga ādyaiḥ yā upāyaḥ upāyaḥ bhedaḥ kathaṃca pratipatti pratibaddham śrūyate tarati śokam tam viditvā mṛtyum eti avagamam idam asi saṃsāri satyām saṃsāri puas viṣayam darśitam vai idam agre āsīt ityādi parihartavyam atra ucyate vai idam agre āsīt śrāvyate asau bhavati veda veda viduḥ vāda apavāde āstitva lakṣaṇam maya kośa paramparayā pratyagātmā aṃ dhārya kāmayate tam prakṛtam samākṛṣya prapañcām sṛṣṭim tasmāt śrāvayitvā satyam upasaṃhṛtya eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati tasmin ṛthe ślokam imam udāharati vai idam agre āsīt yadi asaiḥ ātmakam śloke ibhipreyeta udāharaṇāt asaṃbaddham vākyam āpadyeta prāyeṇa sat prasiddhaḥ vyākaraṇa utpatteḥ sat iva āsīt upacaryate eṣā idam agre āsīt atra sat āsīt samākarṣaṇāt atyata sat āsīt kim samākṛṣyeta ha āhuḥ idam agre āsīt atra śrutyatara abhiprāyeṇa ayam ekīya mata upayāsaḥ iva vikalpasya tasmāt parigṛhīta sat dārḍhyāya ayam mada mati parikalpitasya pakṣasya draṣṭavyam ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt atra iḥ adhyakṣasya jagataḥ vyākaraṇam kathyate eṣaḥ praviṣṭaḥ kha agrebhyaḥ adhyakṣasya vyākṛta iḥ adhyakṣe vyākaraṇa avalambiā samākṛṣyeta cetaasya ayam ātmaaḥ iupraveśaḥ śrūyate aupraviṣṭasya ceta paśyan śrṛṇvan śrotram yādṛśam idam adya tve āma rūpābhyām vyākriyamāṇam sādhyakṣam vyākriyate ādisarge gamyate viparīta kalpa śrutyataram āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi sādhyakṣām jagataḥ vyākriyām vyākriyatam kartari lakāraḥ parameśvare vyākartari saukaryam draṣṭavyaḥ lūyate kedāraḥ svayam evā pūrṇake lavitari eṣa lakāraḥ ūrtha ākṣiptam ataram draṣṭavyaḥ gamyate grāmaḥ bālāki adhikaraṇam kauṣītaki brāhmaṇe bālāki ajātaśatru saṃvāde śrūyate yaḥ vai bālākaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām yasya etat vai veditavyaḥ kim jīvaḥ veditavya tveā upadiśyate uta mukhyaḥ uta paramātmā viśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam kutas yasya etat parispada lakṣaṇasya karmaṇaḥ vākyaśeṣe ekadhā bhavati mukhye prāṇe ye āditye puruṣaḥ dramasi puruṣaḥ evamādayaḥ puruṣāḥ bhavati ātmaām katamaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ tyad atara jīvaḥ ayam veditavya upadiśyate adharma lakṣaṇam śakyate śrāvayitum yasya etat upi upakaraṇa bhūtāām eteṣām puruṣāṇām vākyaśeṣe avagamyate yatkāraṇam veditavya upayastasya puruṣāṇām veda āya upetam bālākim bubodhayiṣuḥ ajātaśatruḥ suptam āmatrya āmatraṇa aśravaṇāt ādīnām pratibodhya yaṣṭi ghāta utthāpaāt vyatiriktam jīvam bhoktāram pratibodhayati parastāt avagamyate śreṣṭhī svaiḥ bhuṅkte svāḥ bhuñjati eṣa etaiḥ ātmabhiḥ bhuṅkte etam ātmāam bhuñjati jīvasya upapaam tasmāt prāṇayoḥ ayataraḥ grahaṇīyaḥ parameśvaraḥ avagamāt prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ ayam eteṣām puruṣāṇām kasmāt upakrama bālākiḥ ajātaśatruṇā bravāṇi saṃvaditum upacakrame katicid adhikaraṇā puruṣāḥ amukhya bhājaḥ uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva tam ajātaśatruḥ mṛṣā vai khalu mā saṃvadiṣṭhāḥ bravāṇi amukhya vādi apodya kartāram ayam veditavya upacikṣepa yadi amukhya upakramaḥ bādhyeta tasmāt parameśvaraḥ ayam bhavitum arhati eteṣām puruṣāṇām parameśvarāt ayasya svātatryeṇa avakalpate yasya etat ayam parispada lakṣaṇasya adharma lakṣaṇasya karmaṇaḥ irdeśaḥ tayoḥ ayatarasya aprakṛta asaṃśabdita puruṣāṇām ayam irdeśaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām irdiṣṭa viṣayasya karoti arthasya phalasya ayam irdeśaḥ tayoḥ upātta pāriśeṣyāt saṃihitam āma etat irdiśyate kriyate aprakṛtam asaṃśabditam satyam etat saṃidhāea saṃihita vastu mātrasya ayam irdeśaḥ gamyate viśiṣṭasya pūrvatra deśa bhūtāām puruṣāṇām upādāāt aviśeṣitam upādīyate gamyate etat bhavati yaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām deśa bhūtāām viśeṣeṇa yasya kṛtsam aviśeṣitam deśa avacchia vyāvṛtti ye brahmatva abhimatāḥ puruṣāḥ kīrtitāḥ abrahmatva khyāpaāya gatāt tayoḥ ayatarasya grahaṇam yāyyam parameśvarasya parihartavyam atra ucyate parihṛtam etat opāsā atra trividham atra upāsaam prasajyeta upāsaam upāsaam upāsaam upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām viṣaya vākyasya avagamyate upakramasya tāvat viṣaya darśitam upasaṃhārasya bhūtāām śraiṣṭhyam svārājyam ādhipatyam paryeti yaḥ veda erṇayeta idam vākyam irṇīyeta yasya etat ityasya viṣaya tasmāt atra śaṅkā puar utpadyamāā iva ṛtyate viṣayaḥ somya maaḥ atra upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ viṣaya abheda abhiprāyeṇa yojayitavyam jaimiiḥ atra vivaditavyam pradhāam idam vākyam pradhāam pratipatti vākye jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ kasmāt vyatirikte jīve pratibodhite puar vyatirikta viṣayaḥ kva eṣa etat bālāke puruṣaḥ ūśayiṣṭa kva etat abhūt kutas etat āgāt yadā suptaḥ svapam paśyati asmi ekadhā bhavati ityādi etasmāt yathāyataam vipratiṣṭhate prāṇebhyaḥ devāḥ devebhyaḥ lokāḥ kāle brahmaṇā jīvaḥ ekatām gacchati parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ ādikam jāyate tasmāt jīvasya svāpaḥ upādhi jaita vijñā rahitam svarūpam bhraṃśa rūpam utra paramātmā veditavya śrāvitaḥ gamyate bālākya jātaśatru saṃvāde spaṣṭam vyatiriktam yaḥ eṣa vijñā puruṣaḥ kva eṣa abhūt kutas etat āgāt yaḥ eṣa vijñā puruṣaḥ kva eṣa abhūt kutas etat āgāt yaḥ eṣa utar hṛdaye tasmin śete paramātmai prayuktaḥ smi atara atra vyuccarati upādhimatām āmayataḥ vyuccaraṇam āmaataḥ paramātmā aam tve āmaati gamyate prāṇaiḥ ākaraṇasya vyatirikta abhyuccayaḥ vākyāvayāt vākyāvaya adhikaraṇam brṛhadāraṇyake maitreyī brāhmaṇe abhidhīyate vai are kāmāya upakramya vai are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ vai are darśaea matyā vijñāea idam sarvam viditam etat vicikitsyate kim vijñā ayam draṣṭavya śrotavya rūpeṇa upadiśyate āhosvit paramātmā kutas bhoktrā vijñā pratibhāti bhoktrā vijñā pratibhāti vijñā paramātma kim tāvat prāptam vijñā kasmāt upakrama jāyā vitta ādikam bhogya sarvam priyam bhavati saṃsūcitam bhoktāram ātmāam upakramya idam ātmao madhye idam aatam apāram pretya prakṛtasya mahataḥ draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ idam draṣṭavya vijñātāram are bhogya jātasya aupacārikam draṣṭavyam prāpte brūmaḥ paramātma ayam kasmāt avayāt vākyam idam paurvāparyeṇa avekṣyamāṇam paramātmā aam lakṣyate katham upapādyate tvasya āśāsti yājñavalkyāt upaśrutya syām kim aham kuryām bhagavā aveda me brūhi āśāsāāyai maitreyyai yājñavalkyaḥ vijñāam upadiśati ayatra paramātma vijñāāt vādāḥ vijñāam ucyamāam etat aupacārikam āśrayitum śakyam kāraṇam vijñāam upapādayati tam parādāt yaḥ veda ityādiā yaḥ svātatryeṇa labdha sadbhāvam paśyati tam mithyādarśiam mithyādṛṣṭam kṣatra ādikam parākaroti dṛṣṭim apodya idam sarvam ayam sarvasya vastu jātasya vyatirekam avatārayati dudubhi dṛṣṭātaiḥ tam vyatirekam draḍhayati mahataḥ prakṛtasya āma prapañca kāraṇatām vyācakṣāṇaḥ gamayati ekāyaa prakriyāyām viṣayasya idriyasya ataḥkaraṇasya prapañcasya kṛtsam aghaam vyācakṣāṇaḥ gamayati tasmāt paramātmaaḥ ayam darśa gamyate puar saṃsūcita vijñā ātmaaḥ ayam darśa atra brūmaḥ atra vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati idam sarvam ayam tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etat saṃsūcitasya draṣṭavya saṃkīrtaam yadi vijñāātmā paramātma oyaḥ vijñāātmā vijñāyate pratijñātam hīyeta tasmāt siddhi vijñāātma paramātmaoḥ abheda aṃśe upakramaṇam ācāryaḥ evambhāvāt idriya maaḥ saṃghāta upādhi saṃparkāt kaluṣībhūtasya saṃghātāt utkramiṣyataḥ paramātma aikya idam abhedena upakramaṇam ācāryaḥ mayate śrutiḥ bhavati eṣa saṃprasādaḥ śarīrāt samutthāya upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate kvacid āśrayam āma rūpam jñāpayati adyaḥ samudre staṃgacchati āma rūpe vihāya vidvāḥ āma rūpāt vimuktaḥ upaiti divyam adyaḥ āśrayam āma rūpam vihāya samudram upayati jīvaḥ āśrayam āma rūpam vihāya upaiti pratīyate dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ tulya tāyai kāśakṛtsaḥ idam abhede upakramaṇam kāśakṛtsaḥ ācāryaḥ brāhmaṇam āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi evaṃjātīyakam avasthāam rūpāṇi vicitya kṛtvā abhivada āste evaṃjātīyakaḥ prabhṛtīām sṛṣṭau jīvasya śrutāḥ parasmāt oyaḥ vikāraḥ jīvaḥ kāśakṛtsasya ācāryasya avikṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ jīvaḥ āyaḥ matam āśmarathyasya yadi jīvasya parasmāt aaya abhipretam abhidhāāt kiyā abhipretaḥ gamyate auḍulomi pakṣe spaṣṭam tara apekṣau abhedau gamyete kāśakṛtsīyam matam ausārī gamyate tattvam asi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ avakalpate tve vikārasya prakṛti saṃbadhe pralaya prasaṅgāḥ tajjñāāt avakalpeta āśrayasya āma rūpasya upādhi āśrayam āma rūpam jīve upacaryate utpattiḥ jīvasya kvacid śrāvyamāṇā upādhi āśrayā veditavyā prakṛtasya mahataḥ draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ idam draṣṭavya iyam sūtrī yojayitavyā idam atra pratijñātam vidite sarvam idam viditam bhavati idam sarvam ayam upapāditam sarvasya āma prapañcasya prasava pralaya dudubhi dṛṣṭātaiḥ kāraṇayoḥ tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etat mahataḥ bhūtebhyaḥ kathitam ācāryaḥ abhede vijñāam pratijñātam avakalpate utkramiṣyataḥ evaṃbhāvāt utkramiṣyataḥ aikya idam abheda abhidhāam ācāryaḥ mayate kāśakṛtsaḥ idam abheda abhidhāam kāśakṛtsaḥ ācāryaḥ mayate etat etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya pretya katham etat abhidhāam etat uccheda abhiprāyam atra mā bhagavā amūmuha pretya paryauyujya svayam śrutyā arthātarasya darśita are ham moham bravīmi are yam ucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsargaḥ bhavati etat bhavati kūṭasthaityaḥ ayam mātrābhiḥ idriya lakṣaṇābhiḥ avidyā kṛtābhiḥ saṃsargaḥ bhavati saṃsarga kṛtasya vijñāasya pretya vijñātāram are śabdeā upasaṃhārāt vijñāātmaaḥ idam draṣṭavyam pariharaṇīyam dvaitam iva bhavati itaram paśyati ārabhya avidyā viṣaye darśa lakṣaṇam vijñāam prapañcya sarvam abhūt kam paśyet ādiā viṣaye darśa lakṣaṇasya vijñāasya abhidadhāti viṣaya ātmāam vijāīyāt āśaṅkya vijñātāram are vijāīyāt vijñā upapāda vākyasya vijñāa dhātuḥ kevalaḥ gatyā gamyate darśitam purastāt kāśakṛtsīyasya pakṣasya śrutimat vijñā paramātmaoḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma racita upādhi nimittaḥ bhedaḥ avidyā pāramārthikaḥ eṣaḥ rthaḥ sarvaiḥ vedātavādibhiḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam idam sarvam brahmā idam sarvam idam sarvam ayam draṣṭā draṣṭṛ evaṃrūpābhyaḥ śrutibhyaḥ smṛtibhyaḥ vāsudevaḥ sarvam kṣetrajñam mām viddhi kṣetreṣu bhārata samam sarveṣu tiṣṭhatam parameśvaram evaṃrūpābhyaḥ darśa apavādāt ayaḥ sau ayaḥ ham asmi veda paśuḥ mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum yaḥ paśyati evaṃjātīyakāt vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ vikriyā ayathā mumukṣūṇām vijñāam ākāṅkṣā aivartakam viṣayam iṣyate kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ aupaśyataḥ sthita prajña kṣetrajña viṣaye samyak darśae kṣetrajñaḥ paramātmā āma kṣetrajñaḥ yam paramātmā paramātmā ayam kṣetrajñāt evaṃjātīyakaḥ viṣayaḥ yam ekaḥ ayam bahudhā abhidhīyate satyam jñāam yaḥ veda ihitam guhāyām kāṃcid ekām adhikṛtya etat brahmaṇaḥ yaḥ guhāyām sṛṣṭvā auprāviśat sraṣṭuḥ praveśa ye kurvati śreyaḥ uddhāram samyak darśam bādhate kṛtakam aityam mokṣam kalpayati saṃgacchate dṛṣṭātā prakṛti adhikaraṇam abhyudaya dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ iḥśreyasa jijñāsyam lakṣitam lakṣaṇam ghaṭa rucaka ādīām mṛd suvarṇa prakṛti tve kulāla suvarṇakāra vaimitta tve bhavati vimarśaḥ kimātmakam puar brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvam imittakāraṇam tāvat kevalam pratibhāti kasmāt īkṣā īkṣā pūrvakam brahmaṇaḥ avagamyate īkṣāṃcakre prāṇam asṛjata ityādi śrutibhyaḥ īkṣā pūrvakam imittakāraṇeṣu kulāla dṛṣṭā kartari yuktaḥ saṃkramayitum īśvara īśvarāṇām imitta kevalam pratīyate parameśvarasya imitta yuktam pratipattum idam sāvayavam acetaam kāraṇe bhavitavyam kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya darśaāt evaṃlakṣaṇam avagamyate iṣkalam iṣkriyam śātam iravadyam irañjaam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ pāriśeṣyāt brahmaṇaḥ upādāakāraṇam aśuddhi guṇakam prasiddham abhyupagatavyam kāraṇatva imitta mātre paryavasāāt prāpte brūmaḥ upādāakāraṇam abhyupagatavyam imitta kāraṇam kevalam imitta kāraṇam kasmāt dṛṣṭātā dṛṣṭātau śrautau tāvat uta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ ye aśrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam vijñātea sarvam ayat avijñātam vijñātam bhavati pratīyate upādā vijñāe saṃbhavati upādā vyatirekāt kāryasya imitta kāryasya takṣṇaḥ prāsāda darśaāt somya sarvam mṛ mayam vijñātam vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam mṛttikā satyam upādā akāraṇa gocaraḥ sarvam loha mayam vijñātam sarvam kārṣṇāyasam vijñātam bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavati dṛṣṭātaḥ khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam dudubheḥ hayamāasya bāhyān śabdān śakuyāt grahaṇāya dudubheḥ dudubhyā ghātasya gṛhītaḥ dṛṣṭātaḥ yathāsaṃbhavam dṛṣṭātau prakṛti sādhaau pratyetavyau iyam pañcamī imāi bhūtāi jāyate atra smaraṇāt prakṛti lakṣaṇe apādāe draṣṭavyāḥ imitta adhiṣṭhātratara adhigatavyam mṛd suvarṇa ādikam upādā akāraṇam kulāla suvarṇakāra adhiṣṭhātṛ pravartate brahmaṇaḥ upādā akāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ upādā akāraṇasya utpatteḥ ekam advitīyam adhiṣṭhātṛ atara veditavyaḥ adhiṣṭhātari vijñānasya pratijñādṛṣṭāta tasmāt adhiṣṭhātṛ atara ātmaaḥ upādāātara prakṛti kutas ātmaaḥ prakṛti tve ātmaaḥ prakṛti tve gamayati kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya pūrvikāyāḥ svātatrya gamyate bahu syām pratyagātma viṣaya bahu bhava gamyate prakṛti tvasya ayam abhyuccayaḥ itas kāraṇam kāraṇam upādāya ubhau prabhava pralayau āmāyete ha vai imāi bhūtāya ākāśāt samutpadyate ākāśam pratyastam yati yasmāt prabhavati yasmin pralīyate upādāam prasiddham vrīhi yava ādīām sūcayati ākāśāt asta kāryasya itas yatkāraṇam prakriyāyām am svayam akuruta ātman am svayam akuruta katham puas siddhasya vyavasthitasya kriyamāṇa śakyam saṃpādayitum brūmaḥ siddhaḥ viśeṣeṇa pariṇamayāmāsa am pariṇāmaḥ mṛd ādyāsu prakṛtiṣu upalabdhaḥ svayam pratīyate sūtram eṣa ṛthaḥ itas yatkāraṇam brahmaṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ sat tyad abhavaiḥ eti itas yatkāraṇam yoiḥ paṭhyate kartāram īśam brahmayoim bhūtayoim paripaśyati dhīrāḥ yoi prakṛti vacaḥ samadhigataḥ strī yoeḥ avayava dvāreṇa garbham upādā yoi atra prakṛtivacaatā parigṛhyate ūrṇaābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate evaṃjātīyakāt prakṛti brahmaṇaḥ prasiddham puar idam īkṣā pūrvakam imitta kāraṇeṣu kulāla pratyucyate bhavitavyam ayam aumā agamyaḥ ṛthaḥ gamya arthasya bhavitavyam īkṣituḥ īśvarasya prakṛti pratipādayati avocāma puas etat sarvam vistareṇa prativakṣyāmaḥ vyākhyā adhikaraṇam āśabdam ārabhya pradhā sūtraiḥ puas puas āśaṅkyaḥ irākṛtaḥ pakṣasya upodbalakāi kāicid ābhāsāi mada matī bhāti āaya pratyāsaḥ vedāta vādasya devala prabhṛtibhiḥ kaiścid dharmasūtra kāraiḥ gratheṣu āśritaḥ pratiṣedhe tīva kṛtaḥ āṇu kāraṇavāda pratiṣedhe kāraṇavāda pakṣasya pratipakṣa pratiṣeddhavyāḥ upodbalakam vaidikam kiṃcid mada matī bhāyāt ṇu kāraṇavādāḥ veditavyāḥ pradhā aśabda virodhi pada abhyāsaḥ dhyāya parisamāptim dyotayati śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ murat dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ avakāśa āya avakāśa adhikaraṇam sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam ayuktam kutas avakāśa smṛtiḥ ākhyā parama ṛṣi praṇītā parigṛhītāḥ ayāḥ ausāriṇyaḥ smṛtayaḥ avakāśāḥ prasajyera tāsu cetaam pradhāam svatatram jagataḥ kāraṇam mava smṛtayaḥ tāvat samarpayatyaḥ avakāśā bhavati varṇasya asmi kāle īdṛśaḥ ācāraḥ ittham ittham samāvarta ittham dharmacāriṇī saṃyogaḥ arthān catur varṇa āśrama dharmāḥ vidadhati kāpila smṛtīām auṣṭheye viṣaye avakāśaḥ sādhaam samyak darśaam adhikṛtya praṇītāḥ yadi avakāśāḥ syuḥ āarthakyam āsām prasajyeta vyākhyātavyāḥ katham puar hetubhyaḥ brahmā sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam avadhāritaḥ ākṣipyate bhavet ayam ākṣepaḥ svatatra prajñāām paratatra prajñāḥ prāyeṇa svātatryeṇa avadhārayitum śakuvataḥ prakhyāta praṇetṛkāsu smṛtiṣu avalambera pratipitsera asmad kṛte vyākhyāe viśvasyuḥ bahu māāt smṛtīām praṇetṛṣu kapila prabhṛtīām ārṣam jñāam pratihatam śrutiḥ bhavati ṛṣim prasūtam kapilam yaḥ tam agre bibharti jāyamāam paśyet eṣām matam ayathārtham śakyam saṃbhāvayitum avaṣṭambhe ṛtham pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmāt vyākhyeyāḥ ākṣepaḥ samādhiḥ āya smṛtya avakāśa yadi avakāśa prasaṅge īśvara ākṣipyeta ayāḥ smṛtayaḥ avakāśāḥ prasajyera udāhariṣyāmaḥ yad avijñeyam prakṛtya atarātmā bhūtāām kṣetrajñaḥ kathyate uktvā tasmāt triguṇam dvijasattama puruṣe brahmaiḥ guṇe saṃpralīyate saṃkṣepam imam śrṛṇudhvam ārāyaṇaḥ sarvam idam purāṇaḥ sarga kāle karoti sargam saṃhāra kāle atti purāṇe bhagavadgītāsu aham kṛtsasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ prakṛtyā āpastambaḥ paṭhati tasmāt kāyāḥ prabhavati mūlam śāśvatikaḥ ityaḥ aekaśas smṛtiṣu īśvaraḥ prakāśyate bale uttaram pravakṣyāmi darśitam śrutīām īśvara vādam tātparyam vipratipattau smṛtīām kartavye yatara parigrahe yatara parityāge ausāriṇyaḥ smṛtayaḥ pramāṇam apekṣyāḥ itarāḥ pramāṇa lakṣaṇe virodhe aapekṣam atareṇa kaścid upalabhate śakyam saṃbhāvayitum imitta śakyam kapila ādīām siddhāām apratihata jñāa dharmaḥ codaā lakṣaṇaḥ siddhāyāḥ codaāyāḥ śakyate siddha vyapāśraya kalpaāyām bahu siddhāām pradarśitā prakāreṇa vipratipattau satyām vyapāśrayāt ayaḥ irṇaya kāraṇam paratatra prajñasya ākasmāt viṣayaḥ pakṣapātaḥ yuktaḥ kasyacid kvacid pakṣapāte vaiśvarūpyeṇa tattva avyavasthā aprasaṅgāt tasmāt vipratipatti upayāse mārge saṃgrahaṇīyā yā śrutiḥ kapilasya jñā atiśayam pradarśayatī pradarśitā viruddham kāpilam matam śraddhātum śakyam kapilam sāma āya ayasya kapilasya sagara putrāṇām prataptuḥ smaraṇāt prāpti rahitasya sādhaka bhavati āyā maoḥ māhātmyam prakhyāpayatī śrutiḥ vai kiṃca mauḥ avadat bheṣajam ātmāam bhūtāi ātmai saṃpaśyaḥ yājī vai svārājyam adhigacchati darśaam praśaṃsatā kāpilam matam idyate gamyate kapilaḥ mahābhārate bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ uta aho vicārya bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ rāja sāṃkhya yoga vicāriṇām pakṣam upayasya bahūām puruṣāṇām ekā ucyate tam viśvam ākhyāsyāmi upakramya tava ye āye dehi saṃjñitāḥ sākṣi bhūtaḥ grāhyaḥ kaścid kvacid viśvamūrdhā viśva bhujaḥ viśva akṣiāsikaḥ ekaḥ carati svaira cārī yathāsukham ātmatā śrutiḥ ātmatāyām bhavati bhūtāni abhūt kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ aupaśyataḥ evaṃvidhāḥ siddham kalpaayā kāpilasya tatrasya kevalam prakṛti kalpaayā vedasya svārthe prāmāṇyam raveḥ iva viṣaye vacasām atara vaktṛ vyavahitam viprakarṣaḥ tasmāt veda viruddhe viṣaye kutas avakāśa aupalabdheḥ pradhā itarāṇi smṛtau kalpitāi ādīi vede idriyāṇi tāvat veda śakyate smartum veda ādīām ṣaṣṭhasya iva idriya arthasya smṛtiḥ avakalpate kvacid tatparam iva śravaṇam avabhāsate atatparam āumāikam atra aprāmāṇyāt aprāmāṇyam yuktam abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt avaṣṭambham ārabhya umathiṣyati yoga pratyukti adhikaraṇam yoga smṛtiḥ pratyākhyātā draṣṭavyā atidiśati virodhe svatatram kāraṇam ādīi kāryāṇi veda prasiddhāi kalpyate pūrveṇa etat gatam kimartham puar atidiśyate atra abhyadhikā āśaṅkā samyak darśa ābhyupāyaḥ veda vihitaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ sthāpya samam śvetāśvatara upaiṣadi liṅgāi vaidikāi yoga viṣayāṇi sahasraśas tām mayate sthirām idriya dhāraṇām kaṭhaḥ vidyām etām yoga vidhim kṛtsam kaṭhaḥ yoga śāstre darśa abhyupāyaḥ aṅgīkriyate deśa aṣṭaka yoga smṛtiḥ bhaviṣyati iyam adhikā śaṅkā atideśe deśa saṃpratipattau deśa vipratipatteḥ uktāyāḥ satīṣu viṣayāsu bahvīṣu smṛtiṣu sāṃkhya yoga smṛtyoḥ irā karaṇe kṛtaḥ sāṃkhya yogau prakhyātau śiṣṭaiḥ parigṛhītau liṅge śraute upabṛṃhitau kāraṇam jñātvā devam mucyate pāśaiḥ irā vedaiḥ apekṣeṇa yoga mārgeṇa iḥśreyasam adhigamyate śrutiḥ vaidikāt vijñāāt ayaḥ iḥśreyasa sādhaam vārayati tam viditvā mṛtyum eti āyaḥ pathā vidyate dvaitiḥ sāṃkhyāḥ yogāḥ darśiḥ kāraṇam vaidikam jñāam dhyāam sāṃkhya yoga abhilapyete pratyāsatteḥ avagatavyam virudhyete sāṃkhya yoga smṛtyoḥ sāvakāśa saṅgaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ evamādi prasiddham puruṣasya viśuddha sāṃkhyaiḥ abhyupagamyate yaugaiḥ parivrāj vivarṇa vāsāḥ parigrahaḥ evamādi prasiddham smaraṇāi upapattibhyām tattva jñāāya upakurvati upakurvatu tattva jñāam maute tam bṛhatam tam aupaiṣadam pracchāmi evamādi śrutibhyaḥ avilakṣaṇa adhikaraṇam jagataḥ imitta kāraṇam yasya pakṣasya ākṣepaḥ imittaḥ parihṛtaḥ aimittaḥ idāīm ākṣepaḥ parihriyate kutas asmi avadhārite āgama arthe aimittasya ākṣepasya avakāśaḥ dharme iva brahmaṇi āgamaḥ bhavitum arhati bhavet ayam yadi āgama prameyaḥ yam auṣṭheya rūpaḥ iva dharmaḥ avagamyate pramāṇa atarāṇām avakāśaḥ paraspara virodhe satī vaśe itarā īyate pramāṇa atara virodhe vaśe śrutiḥ īyeta sādharmyeṇa adṛṣṭam samarpayatī yuktiḥ aubhavasya saṃikṛṣyate viprakṛṣyate śrutiḥ aitihya mātreṇa abhidhāāt avidyāyāḥ sādhaam iṣyate śrutiḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ vyatirekeṇa vidadhatī tarkam atra ādartavyam aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ kriyate jagataḥ kāraṇam kasmāt vikārasya prakṛtyāḥ idam tveā abhipreyamāṇam vilakṣaṇam acetaam vilakṣaṇam śuddham śrūyate tve prakṛti rucaka vikārāḥ mṛd prakṛtikā bhavati śarāva suvarṇa prakṛtikāḥ mṛdā mṛdavitā vikārāḥ prakriyate suvarṇāvitāḥ idam acetaam dukha moha āvitam sat acetaasya duḥkha moha ātmakasya kāraṇasya bhavitum arhati vilakṣaṇasya brahmaṇaḥ avagatavyam idam duḥkha moha pratīyate prīti paritāpa viṣāda svarga araka uccāvaca prapañca acetaam idam upakaraṇa upagamāt sāmye upakārya upakāraka bhavati pradīpau parasparasya upakurutaḥ au cetaam kāraṇam bhoktuḥ upakariṣyati svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ cetaa aṃśasya cetaam pratyupakāraka yaḥ cetaasya parigrahaḥ acetaa bhāgaḥ ayasya cetaasya upakaroti svayam cetaaḥ cetaātarasya upakaroti apakaroti akartāraḥ cetaāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ tasmāt acetaam kāraṇam kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīām cetaa tve kiṃcid pramāṇam prasiddhaḥ ayam ceta tasmāt tvāā idam prakṛtikam yaḥ kaścid ācakṣīta śrutyā jagataḥ ceta prakṛtika tām bale samastam cetaam avagamiṣyāmi prakṛti rūpasya caitayasya pariṇāma bhaviṣyati spaṣṭa caitayānām svāpa mūrchā avasthāsu caitayam vibhāvyate kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīām caitayam vibhāvayiṣyate etasmāt vibhāvita vibhāvita kṛtāt abhāvābhyām kāraṇānām ātmaām virotsyate pārthiva aviśeṣe paraspara upakāri bhavati bhaviṣyati pravibhāga prasiddhiḥ virotsyate kathaṃcid cetaa acetaa lakṣaṇam parihriyeta śuddhi aśuddhi lakṣaṇam parihartum śakyate idam samastasya cetaa cetaa prakṛtika śaraṇa kevalayā utprekṣeta virudhyate avagamyate prakṛti kathayati vijñāam kasyacid vibhāgasya acetaa tām śrāvayan cetaāt brahmaṇaḥ vilakṣaṇam acetaam śrāvayati cetaa kvacid acetaa abhimatāām idriyāṇām śrūyate mṛd abravīt āpobruvaḥ aikṣata aikṣata evamādyā viṣayā cetaa śrutiḥ idriya viṣayāḥ heme ahaṃśreyase vivadamāāḥ jagmuḥ ha vācam ūcuḥ udgāya evamādya idriya viṣayā uttaram paṭhati abhimāi augatibhyām tuśabdaḥ āśaṅkām khalu mṛd abravīt evaṃjātīyakayā śrutyā idriyāṇām cetaa bhimāi eṣaḥ mṛd abhimāiyaḥ abhimāiyaḥ cetaādevatāḥ vada asaṃvada cetaociteṣu vyavahāreṣu idriya kasmāt augatibhyām viśeṣaḥ bhoktṛṇām idriyāṇām cetaā cetaa pravibhāga lakṣaṇaḥ prāc abhihitaḥ cetaa tāyām asau opapadyeta kauṣītakiaḥ saṃvāde viśiṣati etāḥ ha vai devatāḥ ahaṃśreyase vivadamānāḥ vai etāḥ sarvāḥ devatāḥ prāṇe iḥśreyasam viditvā augatāḥ abhimāiyaḥ cetaāḥ devatāḥ matra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa uvagamyate agiḥ bhūtvā mukham prāviśat evamādikā śrutiḥ karaṇeṣu augrāhikām devatām augatām saṃvāda vākyaśeṣe ha prajāpatim pitaram etya ūcuḥ śreṣṭha tvaiḥ dhāraṇāya prajāpati gamaam vacaāt ekaika utkramaṇa āvayavyatirekābhyām śraiṣṭhya pratipattiḥ bali haraṇam evaṃjātīyakaḥ usmad iva draḍhayati aikṣata parasyāḥ devatāyāḥ adhiṣṭhātryāḥ vikāreṣu augatāyāḥ iyam īkṣā draṣṭavyam tasmāt vilakṣaṇam idam brahmaṇaḥ prakṛtikam ākṣipte pratividhatte tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati idam prakṛtikam prasiddhebhyaḥ utpattiḥ prasiddhebhyaḥ gomaya vṛścika ādīām śarīrāṇi acetaāām keśa akha ādīām kāraṇāi acetaāi vṛścika śarīrāṇi acetaāām gomaya ādīām kāryāṇi ucyate kiṃcid acetaam upagacchati kiṃcid eti vailakṣaṇyam mahān ayam pāriṇāmikaḥ svabhāva viprakarṣaḥ ādīām keśa akha ādīām gomaya ādīām vṛścika ādīām atyata sārūpye prakṛti pralīyeta ucyeta kaścid pārthiva svabhāvaḥ ādīām keśa akha gomaya ādīām vṛścika brahmaṇaḥ tarhi sattā lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ prakṛtika jagataḥ dūṣayatā kim aśeṣasya svabhāvasya āauvartaam abhipreyate uta yasya kasyacid vaktavyam vikalpe samasta prakṛti uccheda atiśaye prakṛti bhavati dvitīye asiddha sattā lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ atā kim abrahma prakṛtikam vādiam pratyudāhriyeta samastasya vastu jātasya prakṛtika āgama prasiddhaḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam āgama tātparyasya prasādhita brahmaṇi pramāṇa ātarāṇi saṃbhaveyuḥ maoratha ayam pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ āgama samadhigamyaḥ ayam śrutiḥ su jñāāya preṣṭhaḥ kaḥ addhā veda kaḥ pravocat iyam visṛṣṭiḥ yata ābabhūva ṛcau īśvarāṇām durbodhatām kāraṇasya smṛtiḥ bhavati acityāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ tān tarkeṇa yojayet avyaktaḥ yam acityaḥ yam avikāryaḥ yam ucyate me viduḥ sura gaṇāḥ prabhavam mahā ṛṣayaḥ aham devāām mahā ṛṣīṇām sarvaśas evaṃjātīyakāḥ vyatirekeṇa maaam vidadhat tarkam ādartavyam miṣeṇa śuṣka tarkasya atra ātmalābhaḥ saṃbhavati atra tarkaḥ ubhava tve āśrīyate vyabhicārāt avāgata saṃprasāde sat prapañcasya prabhava avyatirekaḥ evaṃjātīyakaḥ apratiṣṭhāāt kevalasya tarkasya vipralambhaka darśayiṣyati samastasya jagataḥ cetaa tām utprekṣeta cetaā ceta vibhāga śravaṇam caitayasya śakyate yojayitum idam vibhāga śravaṇam yujyate katham parama kāraṇasya atra samasta ātmaā śrāvyate vijñāam bhavat opapadyate acetaasya opapadyate pratyukta tvasya śrutyā kāraṇam grahītavyam bhavati ce yadi cetaam śuddham viparītasya acetaasya aśuddhasya ādimataḥ kāryasya kāraṇam iṣyeta tarhi utpatteḥ prasajyeta aiṣṭam etat satkārya vādi astava eṣa idam pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhyam ayam pratiṣedhaḥ utpatteḥ sattvam kāryasya pratiṣeddhum katham idāīm idam sat utpatteḥ gamyate svatatram sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ sarvam vedaḥ ityādi ātmaā sattvam kāryasya prāc utpatteḥ aviśiṣṭam jagataḥ kāraṇam bāḍham prāc utpatteḥ idāīm śakyate vaktum utpatteḥ asatkāryam vistareṇa etat āaya vāde vakṣyāmaḥ atra yadi kāraṇakam abhyupagamyeta itau pralaye pratisaṃsṛjyamāam avibhāgam āpadyamāam kāraṇam dūṣayet itau kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ kāryasya iva aśuddhi sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam idam aupaiṣadam samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ puar utpattau iyam akāraṇa bhogya vibhāgena utpattiḥ bhoktṛṇām brahmaṇā avibhāgam gatāām pralaye puar utpattau abhyupagamyamāāyām muktāām puar idam vibhaktam brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta apītiḥ saṃbhavati vyatiriktam saṃbhavati atra ucyate dṛṣṭāta kiṃcid asāmañjasyam tāvat abhihitam kāraṇam gacchat kāraṇam dūṣayet dūṣaṇam kasmāt dṛṣṭāta dṛṣṭātāḥ kāraṇam apigacchat kāraṇam ātmīyea dharmeṇa dūṣayati śarāva mṛd prakṛtikāḥ vikārāḥ vibhāga avasthāyām uccāvaca madhyama prabhedāḥ puas prakṛtim apigacchataḥ tām ātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati rucaka suvarṇa vikārāḥ puas suvarṇam ātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati vikāraḥ caturvidhaḥ grāmaḥ dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati tvad pakṣasya kaścid dṛṣṭātosti apītiḥ saṃbhavet yadi kāraṇe svadharmeṇa avatiṣṭheta kāraṇayoḥ kāryasya ātmatvam kāraṇasya ātmatvam atra vakṣyāmaḥ alpam idam ucyate dharmeṇa kāraṇam saṃsṛjet sthitau kāraṇayoḥ aaya idam sarvam ayam idam sarvam idam amṛtam purastāt sarvam khalu idam evamādyābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa triṣu kāleṣu kāryasya śrāvyate yaḥ parihāraḥ kāryasya dharmāṇām avidyā adhyāropita taiḥ kāraṇam saṃsṛjyate itau samaḥ ayam aparaḥ dṛṣṭātaḥ svayam prasāritayā māyayā māyāvī triṣu kāleṣu saṃspṛśyate avastu paramātmā māyayā saṃspṛśyate svapadṛś ekaḥ svapa darśa māyayā saṃspṛśyate prabodha saṃprasādayoḥ avāgata traya sākṣī ekaḥ vyabhicārī trayeṇa vyabhicāriṇā saṃspṛśyate etat paramātma vasthā traya avabhāsaam rajjvā iva sarpa atra vedātārtha saṃpradāya vidbhiḥ ācāryaiḥ māyayā suptaḥ yadā jīvaḥ prabudhyate ajam aidram svapam advaitam budhyate kāraṇasya kāryasya iva sthaulya etat ayuktam puar etat samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ iyam akāraṇam ayam adoṣaḥ āta ādau satyām svābhāvikyām avibhāga prāptau mithyā jñā apodita puar prabodhe bhavati bhaviṣyati śrutiḥ atra bhavati imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ saṃpadya viduḥ saṃpadyāmahe vyāghraḥ siṃhaḥ vṛkaḥ varāhaḥ kīṭaḥ pataṅgaḥ daṃśaḥ maśakaḥ bhavati bhavati avibhāge mithyājñā apratibaddhaḥ vibhāga vyavahāraḥ svapa avyāhataḥ sthitau mithyājñā pratibaddhā muktāām muktāām puar yaḥ utprekṣitaḥ idam vibhaktam brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta upi pratiṣiddhaḥ tasmāt idam aupaiṣadam darśaam pakṣe sādhāraṇāḥ doṣāḥ prāduḥṣyuḥ katham ucyate tāvat abhihitam tvā idam prakṛtikam pradhā aprakṛtikatāyām etat hīāt ādimataḥ jagataḥ samaḥ utpatteḥ asatkārya vāda kāryasya avibhāga samaḥ mṛdita viśeṣeṣu vikāreṣu avibhāga tām gateṣu idam puruṣasya upādāam idam pralayāt pratipuruṣam ye iyatā bhedāḥ puar utpattau śakyate sāmyām uktāām kecid bhedāḥ itau avibhāgam āpadyate ye āpadyate doṣāḥ tvāḥ pakṣe codayitavyā bhavati adoṣa tām eṣām draḍhayati āśrayitavya apratiṣṭhāāt ayathā umā iyam avimokṣa itas āgama gamye rthe tarkeṇa pratyavasthātavyam yasmai tarkāḥ apratiṣṭhitāḥ bhavati utprekṣāyāḥ kaiḥ cit abhiyuktaiḥ yateḥ utprekṣitāḥ tarkāḥ abhiyuktataraiḥ taiḥ utprekṣitāḥ satas yaiḥ ābhāsyate pratiṣṭhita tarkāṇām śakyam āśrayitum vairūpyāt kasyacid māhātmyasya kapilasya ayasya saṃmataḥ tarkaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ āśrīyeta apratiṣṭhita māhātmya abhimatāām tīrthakarāṇām kapila kaṇabhuj prabhṛtīām paraspara vipratipatti darśaāt ucyeta ayathā vayam aumāsyāmahe pratiṣṭhā bhaviṣyati pratiṣṭhitaḥ tarkaḥ śakyate vaktum etat tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tarkeṇa pratiṣṭhāpyate keṣāṃcid tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita darśaeāyeṣām apratiṣṭhāyām lokavyavahāra uccheda duḥkha prāpti parihārāya lokaḥ vipratipattau samyak arthaiḥ dhāraṇam tarkeṇa kriyate mauḥ kriyate mauḥ pratyakṣam aumāam śāstram vividha āgamam trayam su viditam śuddhim abhīpsatā ārṣam upadeśam yaḥ tarkeṇa ausaṃdhatte vedaḥ etaraḥ bruva ayam tarkasya alaṃkāraḥ sāvadya parityāge sāvadya parityāge tarkaḥ pratipattavyaḥ bhavati pūrvajaḥ mūḍhaḥ āsīt bhavitavyam kiṃcid pramāṇam tasmāt apratiṣṭhā avimokṣa yadi kvacid viṣaye tarkasya pratiṣṭhita upalakṣyate prakṛte tāvat viṣaye prasajyate apratiṣṭhita tarkasya idam gambhīram yāthātmyam āgamam atareṇa utprekṣitum śakyam ayam pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ avocāma mokṣaḥ vādiām abhyupagamaḥ rūpam vastu rūpeṇa avasthitaḥ yaḥ ṛthaḥ paramārthaḥ viṣayam samyak jñāam ucyate agiḥ uṣṇaḥ samyak jñāe puruṣāṇām vipratipattiḥ jñāāām prasiddhā vipratipattiḥ keacid tārkikeṇa idam pratiṣṭhāpitam apareṇa vyutthāpyate pratiṣṭhāpitam vyutthāpyate prasiddham katham avasthita viṣayam prabhavam samyak jñāam bhavet pradhāa vādī vidām uttamaḥ sarvaiḥ tārkikaiḥ parigṛhītaḥ tadīyam matam samyak jñāam pratipadyemahi śakyate tīta āāgata vartamāāḥ tārkikāḥ ekasmi deśe kāle samāhartum rūpā viṣayā samyak matiḥ vedasya itya tve vijñā tve vyavasthita viṣaya sarvaiḥ tārkikaiḥ apahotum aśakyam siddham aupaiṣadasya jñā samyak jñā samyak jñā aupapatteḥ avimokṣaḥ prasajyeta āgama vaśea jagataḥ kāraṇam sthitam aparigrahāḥ aparigraha adhikaraṇam vaidikasya darśaasya pratyāsa gurutara bala upeta vedāusāribhiḥ kaiścid śiṣṭaiḥ parigṛhīta pradhā vādam tāvat vyapāśritya yaḥ aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ parihṛtaḥ idāīm aṇu vāda vyapāśrayeṇa kaiścid mada matibhiḥ aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ āśaṅkyate aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ āśaṅkyate parigṛhyate aparigrahāḥ śiṣṭāām aparigrahāḥ aparigrahāḥ prakṛtea śiṣṭaiḥ mauvyāsa prabhṛtibhiḥ ye ṇu vādāḥ irākṛtāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ tulya irākaraṇa kāraṇasya atra āśaṅkitavyam kiṃcid atra parama gambhīrasya kāraṇasya avagāhya tarkasya pratiṣṭhita ayathā vimokṣaḥ āgama evaṃjātīyakam irā karaṇa kāraṇam āpatti adhikaraṇam ayathā yadi śrutiḥ pramāṇam viṣaye bhavati pramāṇa atareṇa viṣaya apahāre bhavitum arhati matra arthavādau viṣayāt adharmayoḥ kim yadi idam ayuktam pramāṇa atara bādhaam katham puas pramāṇa atara prasiddhaḥ rthaḥ śrutyā bādhyate atra ucyate prasiddhaḥ ayam bhogya bhoktā bhogyāḥ viṣayāḥ bhoktā devadattaḥ bhogyaḥ vibhāgasya prasajyeta yadi bhoktā bhogya āpadyeta bhogyam āpadyeta tayoḥ parama kāraṇāt brahmaṇaḥ aya prasajyeta prasiddhasya vibhāgasya yuktam adyatve bhogyayoḥ atīta aāgatayoḥ kalpayitavyaḥ tasmāt prasiddhasya bhogya vibhāgasya ayuktam idam kāraṇatā avadhāraṇam kaścid codayet tam brūyāt ayam asmad pakṣe samudrāt udaka ātman aya tve vikārāṇām asaṃśleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ vyavahāraḥ samudrāt udaka ātman aya tve vikārāṇām bhavati bhāvāām pattau bhavati bhogyayoḥ parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ ya bhaviṣyati yadi bhoktā brahmaṇaḥ vikāraḥ sṛṣṭvā auprāviśat sraṣṭuḥ avikṛtasya upādhi imittaḥ ākāśasya iva ghaṭa upādhi imittaḥ parama kāraṇāt brahmaṇaḥ aya tve bhogya lakṣaṇaḥ aaya adhikaraṇam abhyupagamya imam vyāvahārikam bhogya lakṣaṇam vibhāgam parihāraḥ bhihitaḥ ayam paramārthataḥ yasmāt tayoḥ kāraṇayoḥ aaya avagamyate ādikam bahu prapañcam kāraṇam tasmāt kāraṇāt paramārthataḥ aya vyatirekeṇa kāryasya avagamyate kutas tāvat vijñāam pratijñāya ucyate somya ekea sarvam mṛ mayam vijñātam vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam mṛttikā satyam etat bhavati sarvam mṛd mayam ghaṭa śarāva udañca ādikam mṛd vijñātam bhavet vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam vācā kevalam ārabhyate vikāraḥ ghaṭaḥ śarāvaḥ kaścid āmadheya etat aṛtam mṛttikā satyam eṣa brahmaṇaḥ śrutāt vācā dārṣṭātike vyatirekeṇa jātasya gamyate tām uktvā ba kāryāṇām ba vyatirekeṇa apāgāt ageḥ agi vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam trīṇi rūpāṇi satyam aitadātmyam idam sarvam satyam asi idam sarvam ayam idam sarvam idam sarvam evamādi ekatva pratipāda aparam udāhartavyam tasmāt ghaṭa karaka ākāśāām mahā ākāśāt mṛgatṛṣṇikā udaka ādīām ūṣara aṣṭa svarūpeṇa aupākhya bhogya prapañca jātasya vyatirekeṇa draṣṭavyam śākhaḥ ekatvam ubhayam satyam vṛkṣaḥ ekatvam śākhāḥ āātvam samudra aikatvam phea taraṅga āātvam mṛd aikatvam ghaṭa śarāva āātvam ekatva aṃśea vyavahāraḥ setsyati karmakāṇḍa āśrayau laukika vaidika vyavahārau setsyataḥ mṛd dṛṣṭātā aurūpā bhaviṣyati aivam mṛttikā satyam prakṛti mātrasya dṛṣṭāte vācā jātasya aṛta abhidhāāt dārṣṭātike aitadātmyam idam sarvam satyam parama kāraṇasya asi śvetaketo śārīrasya svayam prasiddham etat śārīrasya ātmatvam upadiśyate yata atara prasādhyam idam śāstrīyam ātmatvam svābhāvikasya śārīra tvasya bādhakam rajju buddhayaḥ iva sarpa buddhīām bādhite śārīra tve āśrayaḥ samastaḥ svābhāvikaḥ vyavahāraḥ bādhitaḥ bhavati prasiddhaye brahmaṇaḥ kalpyeta sarvam abhūt kaḥ kam paśyet ityādiā ātmatva darśiam samastasya kāraka lakṣaṇasya vyavahārasya ayam vyavahāra abhidhīyate yuktam vaktum asi aṛta abhisaṃdhasya abhisaṃdhasya mokṣam darśaya ekatvam ekam pāramārthikam mithyājñā avijṛmbhitam satyatāyām katham vyavahāra gocaraḥ jatuḥ aṛta abhisaṃdhaḥ ucyate mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum āpa yaḥ paśyati dṛṣṭim apavada etat asmi mokṣaḥ samyak jñāā apaodyasya kasyacid mithyājñāasya tveā satyatāyām katham ucyate ekatva ekātā āātva ādīi laukikāi pramāṇāi vyāhayeraa sthāṇu iva śāstram vyāhayeta śāstrasya śiṣya śāsitṛ vyāghātaḥ katham śāstreṇa pratipāditasya ekatvasya upapadyeta atrā ucyate eṣa vyavahārāṇām ātmatā vijñāāt bodhāt yāvat ekatva pratipattiḥ tāvat pramāṇa prameya lakṣaṇeṣu vikāreṣu aṛta buddhiḥ kasyacid utpadyate vikārāḥ aham mama avidyayā ātmīyea bhāvea sarvaḥ jatuḥ pratipadyate svābhāvikīm ātmatām hitvā tasmāt ātmatā prabodhāt sarvaḥ laukikaḥ vaidikaḥ vyavahāraḥ suptasya prākṛtasya svape uccāvacāḥ abhimatam bhavati prabodhāt ābhāsa abhiprāyaḥ kāle bhavati katham satyasya ātmatvasya pratipattiḥ upapadyeta rajju sarpeṇa daṣṭaḥ mriyate mṛgatṛṣṇikā ambhasā kriyate eṣa śaṅkā viṣa maraṇa svapa darśa avasthasya sarpa daṃśa odaka sāā darśaāt aṛtam brūyāt brūmaḥ yadi svapa darśa avasthasya sarpa daṃśa odaka sāā aṛtam avagatiḥ satyam pratibuddhasya svapāt utthitaḥ sarpa daṃśa odaka mithyā avagatim mithyā kaścid dūṣitaḥ veditavyaḥ śrutiḥ yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu striyam svapeṣu paśyati samṛddhim satyāyāḥ samṛddheḥ prāptim darśaeṣu satyāyāḥ samṛddheḥ prāptim darśaeṣu keṣucid ariṣṭeṣu jāteṣu ciram iva jīviṣyati vidyāt uktvā yaḥ svape kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa datam paśyati śā ityādiā maraṇam prasiddham idam sādhu āgamaḥ īdṛśeā asādhu āgamaḥ akāra pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā rekhā ṛta atyam idam pramāṇam tvasya pratipādakam kiṃcid ākāṅkṣyam yajeta ukte kim katham ākāṅkṣyate asi aham asmi ukte kiṃcid ākāṅkṣyam viṣaya avagateḥ avaśiṣyamāṇe rthe ākāṅkṣā ekatva vyatirekeṇa avaśiṣyamāṇaḥ yaḥ rthaḥ yaḥ ākāṅkṣyeta iyam avagatiḥ utpadyate śakyam vaktum ityādi śrutibhyaḥ avagati sādhaāām ādīām iyam iyam avagatiḥ arthikā bhrātiḥ śakyam vaktum avidyā vṛtti darśaāt bādhaka jñāātara avagateḥ avyāhataḥ sarvaḥ aṛta vyavahāraḥ laukikaḥ vaidikaḥ avocāma tasmāt pramāṇea pratipādite tve samastasya vyavahārasya bādhita mṛd ata praṇayaāt pariṇāma śāstrasya abhimatam gamyate mṛd rthāḥ samadhigatāḥ ucyate vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ bhayaḥ eṣaḥ eti eti sthūlam aṇu ityādyābhyaḥ vikriyā śrutibhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ kūṭastha avagamāt brahmaṇaḥ pariṇāma rahita śakyam pratipattum kūṭasthasya kūṭasthasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati kūṭastham ityam vikriyā avocāma brahmaṇaḥ darśaam sādhaam ākāra pariṇāmi darśaam svatatram kasmaicid phalāya abhipreyate pramāṇa kūṭastha vijñāāt śāstram eṣaḥ eti eti upakramya abhayam vai jaaka si evaṃjātīyakam etat siddham bhavati prakaraṇe rahita darśaāt siddhau satyām aphalam śrūyate brahmaṇaḥ ākāra pariṇāmi viiyujyate phalavat saṃidhau aphalam aṅgam itivat svatatram phalāya kalpyate pariṇāmavat vijñāāt pariṇāmavat ātmaaḥ vaktum yuktam kūṭastha aitya mokṣasya ekatva aikātyāt īśitṛ īśitavya īśvara avidyā āma bīja vyākaraṇa sarvajñatvasya tasmāt vai etasmāt saṃbhūtaḥ ityādi vākyebhyaḥ aśuddha buddha svarūpāt sarvajñāt śakteḥ īśvarāt eṣaḥ rthaḥ pratijñātaḥ rthaḥ ucyate katham ocyate atyatam ekatvam advitīya bruvatā śṛṇu ocyate sarvajñasya īśvarasya bhūte iva avidyā kalpite āma rūpe tattva ayatvābhyām airvacaīye prapañca bīja bhūte sarvajñasya īśvarasya śaktiḥ smṛtyoḥ abhilapyete tābhyām ayaḥ sarvajñaḥ īśvaraḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ atarā āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya ekam bījam bahudhā yaḥ karoti ityādi śrutibhyaḥ avidyā āma upādhi aurodhi īśvaraḥ bhavati vyom iva ghaṭa karaka upādhi aurodhi svātma bhūtāḥ ghaṭa sthāīyāḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma karaṇa saṃghāta aurodhiḥ pratīṣṭe vyavahāra viṣaye avidyā upādhi pariccheda īśvarasya īśvara sarvajña paramārthataḥ apāsta upādhi svarūpe ātmai īśitṛ īśitavya sarvajña vyavahāraḥ āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti āyat sarvam abhūt kaḥ kam paśyet paramārtha avasthāyām gṛhṇāti atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti evaṃjātīyakāyām virodha pratītau āśrayaṇam virodha parihāra kāraṇam bhavati āśrayaṇe virodha parihāraḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt durghaṭam etat eṣa avidyā kalpita avidyā kalpitea bhedea avayavam vastu timira upahata iva cadramāḥ bhavati avidyā kalpitea āma lakṣaṇea vyākṛta avyākṛta ātmake tattva airvacaīye pariṇāma vyavahāra āspada pratipadyate pāramārthike rūpeṇa vyavahāra atītam apariṇatam avatiṣṭhate vācā avidyā kalpitasya āma bhedasya brahmaṇaḥ kupyati iyam pariṇāma śrutiḥ pariṇāma pratipāda aavagamāt vyavahāra hīa pratipāda eṣā avagamāt eṣaḥ eti eti upakramya abhayam vai jaaka prāptaḥ asi tasmāt asmad pakṣe kaścid atra vivaditavyam katham brahmaṇi paṭhyate rathāḥ ratha yogāḥ bhavati sṛjate ityādiā māyāvya hasti sṛṣṭayaḥ brahmaṇi bhaviṣyati pareṣām eṣa samāaḥ paricchiam hīam pradhāam avayavasya ādimataḥ kāryasya kāraṇam pakṣaḥ iḥ iḥ avayava pradhā iḥ avayava abhyupagama taiḥ iḥ avayavam abhyupagamyate sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi trayaḥ guṇāḥ taiḥ avayavaiḥ avayavam aivaṃjātīyake avayava tve prakṛtaḥ parihartum pāryate sattva rajaḥ tamasām ekaikasya ekaikam dvaya gṛhītam sajātīyasya prapañcasya prasaṅgasya apratiṣṭhāāt sāvayavatvam aitya śaktayaḥ vaicitrya sūcitāḥ avayavāḥ abhiprāyaḥ aviśiṣṭāḥ aṇu vādiḥ aṇvatareṇa saṃyujyamānaḥ yadi saṃyujyeta aṇu saṃyujyeta iḥ avayava abhyupagama pakṣe eṣa samāa pakṣe upakṣeptavyaḥ bhavati parihṛtaḥ pakṣe darśaāt upeta adhikaraṇam brahmaṇaḥ vicitra vicitraḥ prapañcaḥ puas katham avagamyate vicitra yuktam ucyate darśaāt yuktā parā abhyupagatavyam kutas darśaāt śrutiḥ parasyāḥ devatāyāḥ karmā kāmaḥ rasaḥ sarvam idam abhyāttaḥ ādaraḥ kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ evaṃjātīyakāḥ tvā etat vikaraṇām parām devatām śāstram acakṣuṣkam aśrotram avāgamaāḥ evaṃjātīyakam katham yuktā satī prabhavet cetaāḥ yuktāḥ ādhyātmika karaṇa saṃpaāḥ prabhavataḥ vijñāyate katham eti eti viśeṣāyāḥ devatāyāḥ saṃbhavet atra vaktavyam purastāt avagāhyam idam gambhīram avagāhyam sāmarthyam bhavitavyam bhavitavyam viśeṣasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati etat avidyā kalpita upayāseā śāstram pāṇi pādaḥ grahītā paśyati śrṛṇoti karṇaḥ karaṇasya brahmaṇaḥ sāmarthya prayoja avat prayoja avat adhikaraṇam ayathā puas ceta akartṛ jagataḥ ākṣipati khalu cetaaḥ paramātmā idam bimbam viracayitum arhati kutas prayoja avat pravṛttīām cetao kārī puruṣaḥ mada upakramām tāvat pravṛttim prayoja āupayogiīm ārabhamāṇaḥ kim uta gurutara saṃrambhām bhavati prasiddhi auvādiī śrutiḥ vai are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati gurutara saṃrambhā iyam pravṛttiḥ uccāvaca prapañcam bimbam viracayitavyam yadi iyam pravṛttiḥ cetaasya paramātmaaḥ prayoja upayogiī parikalpyeta paritṛpta paramātmaaḥ śrūyamāṇam bādhyeta prayoja pravṛtti aparādhāt atareṇa prayojaam pravartamāaḥ paramātmā pravartiṣyate ucyeta sarvajña paramātmanaḥ śrūyamāṇam bādhyeta tasmāt aśliṣṭā cetaāt tuśabde ākṣepam pariharati kasyacid āpta eṣaṇasya rājñaḥ rāja amātyasya vyatiriktam kiṃcid kevalam rūpāḥ pravṛttayaḥ krīḍā vihāreṣu bhavati ucchvāsa praśvāsa abhisaṃdhāya bāhyam kiṃcid svabhāvāt saṃbhavati īśvarasya kiṃcid svabhāvāt kevalam rūpā pravṛttiḥ bhaviṣyati īśvarasya śrutitaḥ saṃbhavati svabhāvaḥ paryauyoktum śakyate yadi asmākam iyam gurutara saṃrambhā iva ābhāti parameśvarasya kevalā iyam aparimita yadi līlāsu kiṃcid utprekṣyeta kiṃcid utprekṣitum śakyate āpta āpī apravṛttiḥ sṛṣṭi sarvajña iyam paramārtha viṣayā sṛṣṭi śrutiḥ avidyā kalpita āma vyavahāra gocara pratipāda apara etat vismartavyam aairghṛṇye airghṛṇya adhikaraṇam jama īśvarasya ākṣipyate pratijñātasya arthasya dṛḍhīkaraṇāya eśvaraḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam kutas airghṛṇya kāṃścid atyata bhājaḥ karoti ādī kāṃścid atyata duḥkha bhājaḥ paśu ādī madhyama bhājaḥ mauṣya ādī viṣamām sṛṣṭim irmimāṇasya īśvarasya rāga dveṣa avadhārita svaccha īśvara svabhāva vilopaḥ prasajyeta khala jaaiḥ jugupsitam krūra duḥkha yoga vidhāāt prajā upasaṃhārāt prasajyeta tasmāt airghṛṇya prasaṅgāḥ eśvaraḥ kāraṇam prāpte brūmaḥ aairghṛṇye eśvarasya prasajyete kasmāt yadi irapekṣaḥ kevalaḥ īśvaraḥ viṣamām sṛṣṭim syātām etau doṣau vaiṣamyam airghṛṇyam ir apekṣasya irmātṛ īśvaraḥ viṣamām sṛṣṭim irmimīte kim apekṣate adharmau apekṣate vadāmaḥ viṣamā ayam īśvarasya aparādhaḥ īśvaraḥ parjaya draṣṭavyaḥ parjayaḥ vrīhi yava sṛṣṭau sādhāraṇam kāraṇam bhavati vrīhi yava vaiṣamye bīja gatāi sādhāraṇāi sāmarthyāi bhavati īśvaraḥ mauṣya sṛṣṭau sādhāraṇam kāraṇam bhavati mauṣya vaiṣamye asādhāraṇāi karmāṇi kāraṇāi bhavati īśvaraḥ airghṛṇyābhyām duṣyati katham avagamyate saṃsāram saṃsāram irmimīta śrutiḥ eṣa sādhu kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ uiīṣate eṣaḥ asādhu kārayati tam yam adhas iīṣate puṇyaḥ vai karmaṇā pāpaḥ smṛtiḥ prāṇi īśvarasya āugrahītṛ igrahītṛ ye mām prapadyate tān bhajāmi aham / evaṃjātīyakāḥ ce sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam sṛṣṭeḥ avibhāga avadhāraṇā viṣamā sṛṣṭi kālam vibhāga prasajyeta vibhāgāt ūrdhvam īśvaraḥ pravartatām vibhāgāt vaicitrya aimittasya karmaṇaḥ tulyā ādyā eṣa saṃsārasya bhavet eṣa yadi ādimā ayam saṃsāraḥ aādau saṃsāre bīja aṅkura karmaṇaḥ sarga vaiṣamyasya pravṛttiḥ virudhyate katham avagamyate eṣa saṃsāraḥ uttaram paṭhati saṃsārasya tve saṃsārasya akasmāt udbhūteḥ duḥkha udbhūti akṛta abhyāgama vipraṇāśa duḥkha vaiṣamyasya īśvaraḥ hetuḥ avidyā kevalā vaiṣamyasya kāraṇam rāga kleśa vāsa ākṣipta adhikaraṇam jagataḥ kāraṇam asmi avadhārite veda arthe paraiḥ upakṣiptā ādī doṣā paryahārṣīt ācāryaḥ idāīm parapakṣa pradhāam prakaraṇam prāripsamāṇaḥ parigraha pradhāam prakaraṇam upasaṃharati yasmāt bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ yadi idam śāstram pravṛttam kevalābhiḥ yuktibhiḥ kaṃcid siddhātam sādhayitum pakṣaiḥ ākaraṇea dveṣa karaṇea bāḍham sāṃkhya tatrāṇi pravṛttāy upalabhya bhavet samyak darśaāya upādeyāi sarvajña bhāṣita śraddhā asāra upapādaāya prayatyate āśabdam pūrvatra sāṃkhya pratikṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ kim ucyate sāṃkhya udāhṛtya āuguṇyena yojayataḥ vyācakṣate samyak vyākhyāam kṛtam vākyaiḥ svatatraḥ yukti pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate eṣa viśeṣaḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ghaṭa śarāva bhedāḥ mṛd avīyamāāḥ mṛd sāmāya utpādaḥ eteṣām svabhāvaḥ bhyupagatavyaḥ calam vṛttam abhyupagamaḥ tasmāt avasthāyām yogyāḥ guṇāḥ avatiṣṭhate pradhā uktāḥ doṣāḥ avasthāḥ śaktim ekam vaiṣamyam bhajera imitta sarvadā vaiṣamyam bhajera aarthakam auṣṇya dharmasya pradīpasya avasthasya tābhyām yaḥ jala taraṅga vīcī phe upayāsaḥ jala vīci viśeṣāḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāva rūpeṇa vīci ādibhiḥ eḥ mokṣaḥ prasiddhaḥ ayam tapya tāpakayoḥ jātyatara arthī lakṣyete yadi arthiḥ yasya arthiḥ yad viṣayam arthi asiddhaḥ viṣayam arthi ātmaaḥ pradīpasya asiddhaḥ viṣayam arthi bhavati aprāpte īrthi arthasya yadi svārtha etat saṃbadhi śabdau etau arthī dvayoḥ saṃbadhioḥ aikasya tasmāt bhiau etau arthiau arthiau arthioukūlaḥ pratikūlaḥ aarthaḥ tābhyām ekaḥ paryāyeṇa ubhābhyām saṃbadhyate arthasya alpīyaḥ aarthasya ubhau arthau aarthaḥ tāpakaḥ ucyate tapyaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ ekaḥ paryāyeṇa ubhābhyām saṃbadhyate tayoḥ tapya tāpakayoḥ ātmatāyām upapattiḥ jāti atara saṃyoga parihārāt kadācid upapattiḥ atra ucyate ekatvāt tapya tāpaka aupapatteḥ bhavet eṣa yadi tāyām tapya tāpakau viṣaya viṣayi pratipadyeyātām etat ekatvāt agir ekaḥ svam aam dahati prakāśayati auṣṇya pariṇāmi tve kim kūṭasthe brahmaṇi tapya tāpaka saṃbhavet kva ayam tapya tāpaka ucyate kim paśyasi bhūtaḥ jīvat dehaḥ tapyaḥ tāpakaḥ savitā duḥkham cetayituḥ dehasya yadi dehasya taptiḥ āśe svayam aśyati ucyate kevalasya taptiḥ dṛṣṭā tvayā taptiḥ āma vikriyā cetayituḥ kevalasya iṣyate cetaayoḥ saṃhata aśuddhi tapteḥ taptim abhyupagacchasi katham tava tapya tāpaka sattvam tapyam tāpakam rajaḥ tābhyām cetaasya saṃhata aupapatteḥ sattva aurodhi cetaaḥ tapyate iva paramārthataḥ tarhi tapyate āpatati iva prayogāt tapyate doṣāya ḍuṇḍubhaḥ sarpaḥ iva etāvatā viṣaḥ bhavati sarpaḥ ḍuṇḍubha sarpaḥ iva etāvatā irviṣaḥ bhavati avidyā kṛtaḥ yam tapya tāpaka as pāramārthikaḥ abhyupagatavyam mama kiṃcid duṣyati pāramārthikam tapya abhyupagacchasi tava sutarām aiḥ mokṣaḥ prasajyeta ityatva tāpakasya tapya tāpaka śaktyoḥ ityatve saimitta saṃyoga tapteḥ saṃyoga aimitta ādarśa ai vṛttau ātyatikaḥ saṃyoga uparamaḥ ātyatikaḥ mokṣaḥ adarśaasya tamasaḥ ityatva guṇāām udbhava abhibhavayoḥ aiyata aiyataḥ saṃyoga aimitta uparamaḥ viyogasya aiyata sāṃkhyasya aiḥ uparihāryaḥ aupaiṣadasya ekatva viṣaya viṣayi aupapatteḥ bhedasya vācā vyavahāre tapya tāpaka codayitavyaḥ parihartavyaḥ bhavati pradhā irākṛtaḥ paramāṇu idāīm irākartavyaḥ ādau tāvat utprekṣyate pratisamādhīyate ayam vaiśeṣikāṇām abhyupagamaḥ dravya samavāyiḥ guṇāḥ dravye ātaram ārabhate śuklebhyaḥ tatubhyaḥ śuklasya paṭasya prasava darśaāt viparyaya darśaāt tasmāt cetaasya brahmaṇaḥ tve abhyupagamyamāe jagati samaveyāt adarśaāt cetaam kāraṇam bhavitum arhati imam abhyupagamam tadīyayā prakriyayā vyabhicārayati dīrghavat adhikaraṇam eṣā prakriyā paramāṇavaḥ kila kaṃcid kālam aārabdha kāryāḥ yathāyogam ādimataḥ pārimāṇḍalya parimāṇāḥ tiṣṭhati paścāt puraḥsarāḥ saṃyoga sacivāḥ dvyaṇuka kṛtsam jātam ārabhate guṇāḥ guṇātaram yadā dvau paramāṇū dvyaṇukam ārabhete paramāṇu gatāḥ viśeṣāḥ śukla dvyaṇuke śukla aparāḥ ārabhate paramāṇu viśeṣaḥ pārimāṇḍalyam dvyaṇuke pārimāṇḍalyam aparam ārabhate dvyaṇukasya parimāṇa atara yoga aṇu tve parimāṇe varṇayati yadā dve dvyaṇuke catur aṇukam ārabhete śukla ādīām ārambhaka aṇu tve dvyaṇuka samavāyī caturaṇukasya parimāṇa yoga yadā bahavaḥ paramāṇavaḥ dvyaṇukāi dvyaṇuka sahitaḥ paramāṇuḥ ārabhate paramāṇoḥ parimaṇḍalāt oṇu hrasvam dvyaṇukam svabhāvāt pārimāṇḍalya ādīām aārambhaka draṣṭavyam saṃyogāt dravya ādīām vilakṣaṇāām darśaāt sama ajātīya vyabhicāraḥ dravye prakṛte udāharaṇam ayuktam dṛṣṭātea ārambha mātrasya dravyasya dravyam evā udāhartavyam guṇasya guṇaḥ evā hetuḥ sūtrakāraḥ bhavatām dravyasya guṇam udājahāra apratyakṣāṇām apratyakṣa saṃyogasya ātmakam vidyate pratyakṣam pāñcabhautikam etat bhavati guṇaḥ saṃyogaḥ dravyam atra utpattiḥ prapañcitā etat gatam eti brūmaḥ sāṃkhyam pratyuktam etat vaiśeṣikam kṛtaḥ aparigrahāḥ satyam etat ayam vaiśeṣika parīkṣā ārambhe prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ paramāṇu akāraṇa adhikaraṇam idāīm paramāṇu vādam irākaroti ittham samuttiṣṭhati ādīi avayavāi dravyāṇi svāugataiḥ saṃyoga sacivaiḥ dravyaiḥ ārabhyamāṇāi dṛṣṭāi yāvat kiṃcid avayavam sarvam svāugataiḥ saṃyoga sacivaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ dravyaiḥ ārabdham gamyate ayam avayava avayavi paramāṇuḥ sarvam idam giri samudra ādikam avayavam avaya kāryeṇa bhavitavyam jagataḥ kāraṇam kaṇabhuj abhiprāyaḥ catvāri bhūtāi avayavāi upalabhya caturvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ parikalpyate paratas vibhāga ādīām paramāṇu paryata bhavati pralaya kālaḥ sarga kāle vāyavīyeṣu aṇuṣu utpadyate āśrayam aṇum aṇvatareṇa saṃyuakti dvi aṇuka vāyuḥ utpadyate agiḥ idriyam sarvam idam aṇubhyaḥ saṃbhavati aṇu gatebhyaḥ saṃbhavati kāṇādāḥ idam abhidhīyate vibhāga avasthāām tāvat aṇūām saṃyogaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ karmavatām saṃyoga darśaāt karmaṇaḥ nimittam kim abhyupagatavyam imitta aṇuṣu ādyam yadi prayata abhighāta kim karmaṇaḥ imittam abhyupagamyeta aṇuṣu ādyam tasyām avasthāyām guṇaḥ prayataḥ saṃbhavati pratiṣṭhe saṃyoge guṇaḥ prayataḥ jāyate saṃyoge
