hetukaḥ prakāraḥ samudāyaḥ pareṣām abhipretaḥ aṇu hetukaḥ bhautika saṃhati rūpaḥ skadha hetukaḥ bhipreyamāṇe samudāya samudāya aupapattiḥ kutas samudāyiām citta abhijvalaasya samudāya siddhi adhī atvāt kasyacid bhoktuḥ praśāsituḥ sthirasya saṃhatuḥ i r pravṛtti pravṛtti auparama āśayasya aya aya tvābhyām airūpya kṣaṇika iḥ pravṛtti aupapatteḥ tasmāt samudāya aupapattiḥ samudāya aupapattau āśrayā lokayātrā lupyeta ce aimitta yadi bhoktā praśāsitā kaścid saṃhatā sthiraḥ abhyupagamyate avidyā ādīām lokayātrā tasyām upapadyamāāyām kiṃcid aparam apekṣitavyam avidyā avidyā saṃskāraḥ vijñāam rūpam ṣaṣ sparśaḥ tṛṣṇā bhavaḥ jātiḥ jarā maraṇam śokaḥ paridevaā duḥkham evaṃjātīyakāḥ hetukāḥ saugate samaye kvacid saṃkṣiptāḥ irdiṣṭāḥ kvacid ayam pratyākhyeyaḥ avidyā kalāpe ghaṭīyatra aiśam āvartamāne ākṣiptaḥ saṃghātaḥ kasmāt aimitta bhavet saṃghātaḥ yadi saṃghātasya imittam avagamyeta avagamyate tve avidyā ādīām uttarasya aimittam bhavat bhavet saṃghāta utpatteḥ imittam saṃbhavati avidyā ādibhiḥ arthāt ākṣipyate saṃghātaḥ atra ucyate yadi tāvat ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā saṃghātam labhamāā apekṣate saṃghātam saṃghātasya kiṃci imittam vaktavyam ityeṣu aṇuṣu āśrayi bhoktṛṣu satsu vaiśeṣika parīkṣāyām kim kṣaṇikeṣu aṇuṣu rahiteṣu āśrayi śūyeṣu saṃbhavet ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā saṃghātasya imittam katham tam āśritya ātmāam imittam syuḥ saṃghātāḥ ādau saṃsāre saṃtatya āvartate āśrayāḥ avidyā saṃghātāt sadṛśam utpadyeta sadṛśam visadṛśam utpadyeta iyama mauṣya pudgalasya tiryagyoiāraka prāpti aiyama mauṣya pudgalaḥ kadācid aiyama mauṣya pudgalaḥ kadācid hastī bhūtvā devaḥ mauṣyaḥ bhavet prāpuyāt ubhayam abhyupagama viruddham yad saṃghātaḥ jīvaḥ sthiraḥ bhoktā tava abhyupagamaḥ bhogaḥ prārthaīyaḥ mokṣaḥ mumukṣuṇā bhavitavyam prārthyeta ubhayam bhavitavyam avasthāyi tve kṣaṇika abhyupagama tasmāt avidyā ādīām yadi bhavet bhavatu saṃghātaḥ sidhyet abhiprāyaḥ airodhāt etat avidyā ādīām saṃghāta aimitta saṃbhavati idam idāīm upapādyate kṣaṇabhaṅga vādiḥ yam abhyupagamaḥ uttarasmi kṣaṇe utpadyamāe pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ irudhyate abhyupagacchatā kṣaṇayoḥ śakyate saṃpādayitum irudhyamāasya iruddhasya kṣaṇasya grasta kṣaṇa aupapatteḥ bhūtaḥ kṣaṇaḥ kṣaṇasya hetuḥ abhiprāyaḥ opapadyate kalpaāyām vyāpāraḥ abhiprāyaḥ svabhāva uparaktasya phalasya svabhāva uparāga svabhāvasya kāla avasthāyi tve kṣaṇa bhaṅga abhyupagama tyāga svabhāva uparāgeṇa abhyupagacchataḥ prāpteḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ utpāda erodhau vastuaḥ svarūpam syātām avasthātaram vastvataram yadi tāvat vastuaḥ svarūpam evā utpāda erodhau syātām vastu utpāda erodha śabdau paryāyāḥ prāpuyuḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ mayā itas utpāda erodha abhilapyete vastuaḥ kṣaṇika abhyupagama hāiḥ atyata vyatiriktau evā utpāda airodhau vastuaḥ syātām mahiṣa vastu utpāda airodhābhyām saṃspṛṣṭam vastuaḥ śāśvata yadi utpāda airodhau syātām draṣṭṛ dharmau tau vastu dharmau vastuaḥ śāśvata tasmāt asaṃgatam saugatam matam ayathā kṣaṇabhaṅga vāde uttarasya kṣaṇasya hetuḥ bhavati hetau utpattim brūyāt citta caittāḥ utpadyate iyam hīyeta iḥ hetukāyām utpattau apratibadhāt sarvam utpadyeta kṣaṇa utpattiḥ yāvat tāvat avatiṣṭhate kṣaṇe brūyāt phalayoḥ kṣaṇikāḥ saṃskārāḥ iyam uparudhyeta irodha vaiāśikāḥ kalpayati bodhyam trayāt ayat saṃskṛtam kṣaṇikam trayam irodhau ākāśam trayam etat avastu pūrvakaḥ kila bhāṣyate viparītaḥ upratisaṃkhyā irodhaḥ āvaraṇa ākāśam ākāśam parastāt pratyākhyāsyati irodha dvayam idāīm pratyācaṣṭe irodhayoḥ kasmāt etau irodhau saṃtā gocarau syātām gocarau tāvat saṃtā gocarau saṃbhavataḥ sarveṣu saṃtā eṣu saṃtā vicchedasya gocarau saṃbhavataḥ bhāvāām viāśaḥ saṃbhavati sarvāsu avasthāsu aspaṣṭa pratyabhijñāsu avasthāsu tasmāt parikalpitasya irodha dvayasya upapattiḥ yaḥ yam avidyā irodhaḥ irodha pātī parikalpitaḥ samyak jñāāt parikarāt svayam pūrvasmin vikalpe uttarasmin mārga āarthakya idam abhipretam ākāśam irupākhyam irodha dvayasya irupākhya purastāt irākṛtam ākāśasya idāīm irākriyate ayuktaḥ irupākhya abhyupagamaḥ irodhayoḥ iva vastu āgama prāmāṇyāt tāvat anubhūtiḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ākāśasya vastu prasiddhiḥ aumeya vaktavyam guṇānām vastu darśaāt āvaraṇa ākāśam icchatām ekasmi suparṇe patati āvaraṇasya suparṇa atarasya utpitsataḥ avakāśa āvaraṇa patiṣyati viśeṣyate tarhi vastu ākāśam āvaraṇa āvaraṇa saugatasya abhyupagama prasajyeta saugate samaye bhagava kiṃsaṃiśrayā asmi vāyuḥ kiṃsaṃiśrayaḥ bhavati vāyuḥ saṃiśrayaḥ ākāśasya vastu tve tasmāt ayuktam ākāśasya vastu irodha dvayam ākāśam trayam etaiḥ upākhyam avastu vipratiṣiddham saṃbhavati vastu dharmi vyavahārasya dharmi ghaṭa vastu vaiāśikaḥ sarvasya vastuaḥ kṣaṇikatām abhyupaye upalabdhuḥ kṣaṇikatām abhyupeyāt saṃbhavati ausmṛteḥ aubhavam smaraṇam ausmṛtiḥ kartṛkā satī saṃbhavati atara viṣaye atarasya adarśaāt katham aham adā udrākṣam idam idāīm paśyāmi pratyayaḥ darśa smaraṇayoḥ pratyabhijñā pratyayaḥ sarvasya lokasya prasiddhaḥ aham adā udrākṣam idam paśyāmi yadi tayoḥ aham smarāmi adrākṣīt ayaḥ pratīyāt pratyeti kaścid pratyayaḥ darśa smaraṇayoḥ bhiam kartāram lokaḥ uvagacchati smarāmi aham asau adā udrākṣīt aham adā udrākṣam darśa smaraṇayoḥ vaiāśikaḥ upi ātmāam ekam kartāram avagacchati pratipattim pratyabhijāa kartṛkām uttamāt ucchvāsāt atītāḥ pratipattīḥ kartṛkāḥ katham kṣaṇabhaṅga vādī vaiāśikaḥ āpatrapeta yadi brūyāt sādṛśyāt etat saṃpatsyate tam pratibrūyāt idam sadṛśam dvaya āyatta sādṛśyasya kṣaṇabhaṅga vādiḥ sadṛśayoḥ dvayoḥ vastuoḥ grahītuḥ sādṛśya nimittam mithyā pralāpaḥ kṣaṇayoḥ sādṛśyasya grahītā ekaḥ kṣaṇa dvaya avasthāāt kṣaṇika pīḍyeta sadṛśam ātaram idam kṣaṇa dvaya grahaṇa aimittam kṣaṇa dvaya grahaṇa aimittam idam sādṛśya viṣayam sadṛśam prayogaḥ arthakaḥ sādṛśyam prayogaḥ prāpuyāt yadā prasiddhaḥ padārthaḥ parīkṣakaiḥ parigṛhyate ubhayam ucyamāam parīkṣakāṇām saṃtāam ārohati eṣa ṛthaḥ vaktavyam ucyamāam bahu pralāpi kevalam prakhyāpayet ayam sādṛśyāt saṃvyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ avagamāt sadṛśa aavagamāt bhavet kadācid bāhya vastui vipralambha idam sadṛśam saṃdehaḥ upalabdhari saṃdehaḥ as kadācid bhavati aham syām sadṛśaḥ yaḥ aham pūrvedyus adrākṣam aham adya smarāmi tasmāt aupapaḥ vaiāśika samayaḥ āsatas itas aupapaaḥ vaiāśika samayaḥ sthiram auyāyi kāraṇam abhyupagacchatām utpattiḥ etat āpadyeta utpattim prādurbhāvāt viaṣṭāt kila bījāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate viaṣṭāt kṣīrāt dadhi mṛd piṇḍāt ghaṭaḥ kūṭasthāt kāraṇāt utpadyeta sarvam sarvatas utpadyeta tasmāt grastebhyaḥ bīja utpattiḥ idam ucyate āsataḥ utpadyate yadi utpadyeta abhyupagamaḥ arthakaḥ bīja ādīām upamṛditāām yaḥ abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇa ādīām kaścid viśeṣaḥ bījāt aṅkuraḥ jāyate kṣīrāt dadhi evaṃjātīyakaḥ abhyupagamaḥ ṛthavāsyāt abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇa aṅkura abhyupagamyate mṛd vikārāḥ bhāvāḥ lokaḥ pratyeti atareṇa kasyacid kūṭasthasya vastuaḥ aupapatteḥ utpattiḥ bhavitum arhati duruktam sthira svabhāvāām suvarṇa ādīām pratyabhijñāyamāām rucaka darśaāt yeṣu bīja upamardaḥ lakṣyate teṣu āsau avasthāyāḥ kāraṇam abhyupagamyate bīja avayavāām aṅkura tasmāt asadbhyaḥ śaśaviṣāṇa sat adarśaāt sadbhyaḥ suvarṇa sat darśaāt aupapaḥ abhyupagamaḥ caturbhiḥ citta caittāḥ utpadyate paramāṇubhyaḥ bhautika lakṣaṇaḥ samudāyaḥ utpadyate abhyupagamya puara utpattim kalpayadbhiḥ abhyupagamam vaiāśikaiḥ lokaḥ ākulīkriyate yadi utpattiḥ abhyupagamyeta abhāvasya abhyupagamyate keacid tasmāt aupapaoyam abhyupagamaḥ ābhāvaḥ ābhāva adhikaraṇam bāhya vādam āśritya samudāya aprāpti dūṣaṇeṣu udbhāviteṣu vijñāa vādī bauddhaḥ idāīm pratyavatiṣṭhate keṣāṃcid kila bāhye ālakṣya bāhya vāda prakriyā iyam viracitā āsau sugata abhiprāyaḥ vijñāaikaskadhavādaḥ abhipretaḥ tasmin vijñāa vāde rūpeṇa ātasthe pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ sarvaḥ bāhya arthe āroham atareṇa pramāṇa vyavahāra avatārāt katham avagamyate atasthaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ bāhyaḥ ṛthaḥ paramāṇavaḥ syuḥ samūhāḥ stambha syuḥ tāvat paramāṇavaḥ stambha paricchedyāḥ bhavitum arhati paramāṇu ābhāsa jñā samūhāḥ stambha aśakya jāti ādī pratyācakṣīta aubhava mātreṇa jñāasya jāyamāasya viṣayam pakṣapātaḥ stambha jñāam kuḍya jñāam ghaṭa jñāam jñāam asau jñāa gata atareṇa avaśyam viṣaya sārūpyam jñāasya aṅgīkartavyam aṅgīkṛte viṣaya ākārasya svabhāva viveke yuktam pratibadha tasmāt svapa idam draṣṭavyam svapa marīci udaka gadharva agara pratyayā grāhya grāhaka ākārā bhavati jāgarita gocarā stambha pratyayā bhavitum arhati avagamyate katham bāhya arthe vaicitryam ādau saṃsāre bīja aṅkura vaicitryam vipratiṣidhyate avayavi atirekābhyām vāsa āimittam jñā avaicitryam avagamyate svapa atareṇa vāsa āimittasya jñā avaicitryasya ubhābhyām āvābhyām abhyupagamyamāa atareṇa nimittasya jñā vaicitryasya mayā tasmāt bāhya arthasya prāpte brūmaḥ ābhāvaḥ khalu bāhyasya arthasya adhyavasātum śakyate kasmāt bāhyaḥ ṛthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyam ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ upalabhyamāasya bhavitum arhati kaścid sādhyāyām tṛptau svayam brūyāt aham bhuñje tṛpyāmi idriya saṃikarṣeṇa svayam upalabhamāa bāhyam aham upalabhe bruva katham upādeya vacaḥ au aham bravīmi kaṃcid upalabhe kim vyatiriktam opalabhe bravīmi bāḍham bravīṣi iraṅkuśa tuṇḍasya yukti upetam bravīṣi balāt arthasya abhyupagatavyaḥ kaścid upalabdhim stambhaḥ kuḍyam upalabhate viṣaya tve stambha kuḍya ādī laukikāḥ upalabhate laukikāḥ upalabhate pratyācakṣāṇāḥ bāhyam avabhāsate prasiddhām avabhāsamāām saṃvidam pratyākhyātu kāmāḥ bāhyam vatkāram kurvati itarathā kasmāt brūyuḥ viṣṇu mitraḥ vadhyā avabhāsate kaścid ācakṣīta tasmāt aubhavam tattvam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ avabhāsate yuktam abhyupagatum avabhāsate bāhyasya arthasya avabhāsate adhyavasitam sādhuḥ adhyavasāyaḥ pramāṇa pravṛtti apravṛtti pūrvakau saṃbhava asaṃbhavau avadhāryete saṃbhava asaṃbhava pūrvake pramāṇa pravṛtti apravṛttī ādīām pramāṇeā saṃbhavati keacid pramāṇena saṃbhavati yathāsvam sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ katham avyatireka vikalpaiḥ saṃbhavati ucyeta viṣaya sārūpyāt viṣaya āśaḥ bhavati viṣaye viṣaya sārūpya aupapatteḥ viṣayasya viṣayayoḥ upāya upeya hetukaḥ abheda hetukaḥ abhyupagatavyam ghaṭa jñāam jñāam viśeṣaṇayoḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣyasya jñāasya śuklaḥ gauḥ kṛṣṇaḥ gauḥ śauklya kārṣṇyayoḥ bhedaḥ go tvasya dvābhyām bhedaḥ siddhaḥ bhavati ekasmāt dvayoḥ tasmāt bhedaḥ ghaṭa darśaam ghaṭa smaraṇam atra pratipattavyam atra viśeṣyayoḥ darśa smaraṇayoḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇasya ghaṭasya kṣīragadhaḥ kṣīra rasaḥ viśeṣyayoḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇasya kṣīrasya dvayoḥ vijñāayoḥ upakṣīṇayoḥ grāhya grāhaka aupapattiḥ vijñā abheda kṣaṇika sāmāya vāsya vāsaka avidyā upaplava sat badha pratijñāḥ gatāḥ hīyera kiṃca ayat vijñāam vijñāam abhyupagacchatā bāhya stambhaḥ kuḍyam evaṃjātīyakaḥ kasmai vaktavyam bāhyaḥ udbhūyate yuktam abhyupagatum svayam bāhyaḥ atyata viruddhām svātmaiḥ kriyām abhyupagacchasi dahati itivat aviruddham prasiddham ecchasi aho pāṇḍityam darśitam vyatiriktam svayam au vijñāasya vyatirikta grāhya tve grāhyam avabhāsa jñāasya jñā ātaram kalpayataḥ sama avabhāsya avabhāsaka aupapatteḥ kalpa āarthakyam ubhayam vijñā grahaṇa mātre vijñā sākṣiṇaḥ grahaṇa ākāṅkṣā utpādāt aavasthā śaṅkā sākṣi pratyayayoḥ svabhāva vaiṣamyāt upalabdhṛ upalabhya svayaṃsiddhasya sākṣiṇā pratyākhyeya kiṃca ayat vijñāam avabhāsa kātaraiḥ svayam prathate bruvatā pramāṇa gamyam vijñāam bāḍham aubhava vijñāasya iṣṭaḥ aḥ pakṣaḥ tvayā sādhaasya prathaa darśaāt vijñāasya avabhāsya avagatari avagamyate sākṣiṇā uvagatuḥ svayaṃsiddha tām upakṣipatā svayam prathate vijñāam eṣaḥ mama pakṣaḥ tvayā vācoyuktyatareṇa āśritaḥ vijñā pradhvaṃsa viśeṣavat vijñā vyatirikta avagamya asmābhiḥ prasādhitam pa jāgarita gocarāḥ stambha pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ prativaktavyam atra ucyate svapa pratyayā bhavitum arhati kasmāt vaidharmyam bhavati svapa jāgaritayoḥ kim puar vaidharmyam bādhā bādhau brūmaḥ bādhyate svapa upalabdham vastu pratibuddhasya mithyā mayā upalabdhaḥ mahā jaa samāgamaḥ mama mahā jaa samāgamaḥ me babhūva bhrātiḥ udbabhūva bhavati yathāyatham jāgarita upalabdham vastu stambha ādikam kasyāṃcid avasthāyām bādhyate smṛtiḥ eṣā upalabdhiḥ upalabdhyoḥ pratyakṣam ataram viprayoga saṃprayoga ātmakam iṣṭam putram smarāmi opalabhe upalabdhum icchāmi śakyate vaktum mithyā jāgarita upalabdhiḥ svapa ataram svayamaubhava aubhava apalāpaḥ kartum aubhava virodha jāgarita pratyayāām vaktum aśakuvatā svapa sādharmyāt vaktum iṣyate yaḥ yasya svatas saṃbhavati yasya sādharmyāt saṃbhaviṣyati udaka sādharmyāt śītaḥ bhaviṣyati darśitam vaidharmyam svapa jāgaritayoḥ jñā vaicitryam prativaktavyam atra ucyate tvad pakṣe bāhyāām arthāām nimittāḥ pratyartham bhavati artheṣu kiṃimittāḥ bhaveyuḥ upalabdhyā vāsas viā vāsas upagamāt upalabdhyā vāsas sadbhāvam avayavyatirekau pratiṣṭhāpayataḥ viśeṣāḥ saṃskārāḥ āśrayam atareṇa avakalpate tava vāsa āśrayaḥ kaścid kṣaṇika ālayavijñāam parikalpitam kṣaṇika aavasthita svarūpam sat bhavitum arhati kūṭasthe darśii deśa kāla aimitta vāsa ādhī pratisaṃdhā vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati sthira tve vijñāa vāde kṣaṇika abhyupagamasya bāhya vāde dūṣaṇāy udbhāvitāi airodhāt evamādīi etau dvau vaiāśika pakṣau bāhya vādi pakṣaḥ kāle utpādayitum yatate stimitam tiṣṭhati teāyatvam avasīyate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ākāśayoḥ abheda upacāra sarvam utpadyamāam vyatirikta deśa kālam utpadyate brahmaṇā vyatirikta deśa kālam ākāśam bhavati brahmaṇā kāryeṇa vijñātam ākāśam bhavati kṣīra pūrṇe ghaṭe katicid abbidavaḥ prakṣiptāḥ satas kṣīra grahaṇe gṛhītā bhavati kṣīra ap bidu grahaṇam pariśiṣyate brahmaṇā kāryaiḥ vyatirikta deśa kāla gṛhītam abhaḥ bhavati tasmāt abhasaḥ saṃbhava śravaṇam prāpte idam hāiḥ bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam kasmin bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati evaṃrūpā vijñāyate tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ yadi kṛtsasya vastu jātasya vijñeyāt brahmaṇaḥ vyatireke sarvam vijñāyate iyam hīyeta avyatirekaḥ yadi kṛtsam vastu jātam ekasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpadyeta prakṛti avyatireka avagamyate bhavati pratijñāya mṛd dṛṣṭātaiḥ abheda pratipāda aparaiḥ eṣā samarthyate sādhaāya uttare śabdāḥ sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam aikṣata sṛjate jātam brahmaṇaḥ pradarśya vyatirekam pradarśayati aitadātmyam id sarvam ārabhya prapāṭhaka parisamāpteḥ yadi ākāśam brahmaṇi vijñāte ākāśam vijñāyeta hāiḥ hāyāḥ vedasya prāmāṇyam yuktam kartum śabdāḥ tea tea tām pratijñām jñāpayati idam sarvam ayam idam amṛtam purastāt evamādayaḥ tasmāt jvala gagaam utpadyate utpadyate ayuktam viṣaya atarasya darśita tasmāt vai etasmāt saṃbhūtaḥ satyam darśitam viruddham sṛjate śrutyatareṇa ekavākya śrutīām bhavatu ekavākya aviruddhāām uktaḥ sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaya dvayoḥ prathama ja eṣa sargasya taittirīyake tasmāt vai etasmāt saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ aśakyā iyam śrutiḥ ayathā pariṇetum śakyā pariṇetum chādogya śrutiḥ ākāśam sṛṣṭvā sṛjate iyam śrutiḥ satī atara prasiddhām ākāśasya utpattim vārayitum vākyasya dvaya sraṣṭā ekaḥ ekam sraṣṭavyam sṛjet ekavākya kalpaāyām saṃbhavatyām viruddha tve śrutiḥ hātavyā asmābhiḥ sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaya saṃbandhaḥ abhipreyate sraṣṭavya atara sarvam khalu idam jalāḥ atra sarvasya vastu jātasya ja śrūyamāṇam atara vihitam pramukham kramam vārayati tejasaḥ ja śrūyamāṇam śrutyatara vihitam abhaḥ pramukham kramam vārayitum arhati vidhā etat vākyam upāsīta sṛjate etat sṛṣṭi vākyam tasmāt atra yathāśruti kramaḥ grahītavyaḥ ucyate padārthaḥ parityaktavyaḥ bhavati padārtha kramasya sṛjate atra kramasya vācakaḥ kaścid arthāt kramaḥ gamyate vāyoḥ agiḥ atara prasiddhea samuccayau tejasoḥ prathama ja viṣayau asaṃbhava aabhyupagamābhyām tasmāt śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ chādogye utpattau upasaṃkhyātavyam kim saṃgṛhyate ākāśasya sarveṇa āaya deśa kāla brahmaṇā kāryaiḥ viditam bhavati hīyate ekam advitīyam bhavati kṣīrodaka abhasoḥ avyatireka atra ucyate vijñāam etavyam mṛd dṛṣṭāta praṇayaāt prakṛti idam vijñāam etavyam gamyate vijñāam samyak vijñāam kṣīra jñā gṛhītasya udakasya samyak vijñā gṛhīta vedasya puruṣāṇām iva alīka vañca ādibhiḥ avadhāraṇam avadhāraṇā iyam ekam advitīyam śrutiḥ pīḍyeta idam vastu deśa viṣayam yāyyam mṛd bhavati śvetaketo yau somya idam bhavati śvetaketo yau somya idam tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ tasmāt aśeṣa vastu viṣayam idam vijñāam sarvasya kāryatā upayasyata draṣṭavyam puar etat gaga śrutiḥ atra brūmaḥ tuśabda ūsaṃbhava āśaṅkā vyāvṛtti khalu utpattau asaṃbhava āśaṅkā kartavyā yāvat kiṃcid jātam ghaṭa ghaṭikā udañca kaṭaka keyūra sūcī ārācaistriṃśa lakṣyate avikṛtam kiṃcid kutaścid vibhaktam ākāśasya avagamyate tasmāt vikāraḥ bhavitum arhati diś kāla maaḥ paramāṇu ādīām vibhaktaḥ ghaṭa saṃbhūtaḥ yadi vikāraḥ tasmāt sarvam tve śūyavādaḥ prasajyeta irā karaṇa śaṅkā upapattiḥ āgatukaḥ kasyacid svayam siddha pramāṇam sidhyati upādīyate padārthāḥ pramāṇaiḥ apekṣāḥ svayam siddhāḥ keacid abhyupagamyate pramāṇa vyavahāra pramāṇa vyavahārāt sidhyati īdṛśasya saṃbhavati āgatukam vastu irākriyate svarūpam yaḥ irākartā svarūpam ageḥ auṣṇyam agiā irākriyate aham idāīm vartamāam vastu aham atītam atītataram ajñāsiṣam aham āgatam aāgatataram jñāsyāmi atīta āgata vartamā yathābhavati jñātavye sarvadā vartamā asvabhāva bhasmībhavati dehe ucchedaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyam apratyākhyeya svabhāva akārya aḥ ākāśasya dravyam pratyucyate tāvat samā ajātīyam ārabhate saṃyogāām samā ajātīya dravya imitta kāraṇāām turī vema ādīām etat samavāyi viṣaye atara viṣayaḥ aaikātikam sūtra go vālaiḥ jātīyaiḥ ekā rajjuḥ sūtraiḥ ūrṇā ādibhiḥ sattva dravya sama jātīya tve sarvasya sarveṇa sama jātīyaka āpya ekam ārabhate aikam aṇu maasoḥ ādya ārambha ekaikaḥ paramāṇuḥ maaḥ ādyam ārabhate aṇu maasoḥ ādyam ārabhate aṇu maasoḥ ādyam ārabhate aṇu maas ādyam ārabhate aṇu maas ādyam ārabhate aṇu maas ādyam ārabhate aṇu maas ādyam bīja kvacid ekam pariṇamate kṣīra dadhi bhāvea ākāśasya utpattau kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyate ayuktam viśeṣeṇa abhaḥ idāīm adhyavasīyate viśeṣaḥ utpatteḥ āsīt gamyate sthūla ādibhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ svabhāvavat asthūlam aaṇu ityādi śrutibhyaḥ svabhāve svabhāvavat aākāśam avagamyate tasmāt utpatteḥ aākāśam sthitam ākāśasya aja virodhe asaṃbhava aumāasya ābhāsa aumāasya darśita aityam ākāśam aitya ghaṭa ityādi prayoga ātmaya aikātikam aitya asiddheḥ vibhu asiddha etat śrutiḥ tāvat viyati amṛtāḥ divaukasaḥ draṣṭavyā pralayayoḥ upapādita gataḥ ityaḥ kriyate sama tvāya iṣuḥ iva savitā dhāvati kṣipra tvāya ucyate iṣu tulya tvāya atatva aśrutiḥ vyākhyātā jyāyāḥ ākāśāt ityādi śrutibhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt ākāśasya parimāṇa pratimā brahmaṇaḥ yeṣām ādīām ārta tapasi ākāśasya jama gauṇa etat saṃbhava śrutyā aumāābhyām parihṛtam tasmāt siddham mātariśva adhikaraṇam atideśaḥ yam vyākhyāea āśrayaḥ vāyuḥ yathāyogam pakṣāḥ racayitavyāḥ vāyuḥ utpadyate chadogāām prakaraṇe āmāam ekaḥ pakṣaḥ taittirīyāṇām prakaraṇe ākāśāt vāyuḥ ataram śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhe vāyoḥ śrutiḥ aparaḥ abhiprāyaḥ eṣā astamitā vāyuḥ astamaya yāvat vikāram vibhāga utpadyate vāyuḥ siddhātaḥ astamaya upara viṣayaḥ āpekṣikaḥ śravaṇam vāyoḥ ākāśasya tulyayoḥ prakaraṇe aśravaṇayoḥ ekam adhikaraṇam viṣayam kim atideśe viśeṣaḥ ucyate satyam etat mada āśaṅkā aivṛtti yam atideśaḥ kriyate saṃvarga upāsyata vāyoḥ mahābhāga astamaya bhavati kasyacid asambhavaḥ satas asaṃbhava adhikaraṇam utpattim upaśrutya brahmaṇaḥ bhavet kutaścid utpattiḥ kasyacid matiḥ vikārebhyaḥ uttareṣām vikārāṇām utpattim upaśrutya ākāśasya vikārāt brahmaṇaḥ utpattiḥ kaścid mayeta tām āśaṅkām apaetum idam sūtram khalu brahmaṇaḥ sat ātmakasya kutaścid ayataḥ saṃbhavaḥ utpattiḥ āśaṅkitavyā kasmāt aupapatteḥ samātram samātrāt utpattiḥ pradarśitā brahmaṇaḥ vaiṣamyam vikārebhyaḥ atara darśaāt brahmaṇaḥ bhavitum arhati mūlaprakṛtyā yā mūlaprakṛtiḥ abhyupagamyate chādogye tejasaḥ śrāvitam taittirīyake vāyu vipratipattau satyām prāptam tāvat brahmayoikam kutas devaḥ upakramya sṛjataḥ sarvavijñāa pratijñāyāḥ prabhava tve sarvasya jalāḥ etasmāt jāyate upakramya śrutyatare sarvasya aviśeṣeṇa ja taittirīyake tapaḥ taptvā idam bhaviṣyati brūmaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātman saṃbhūtaḥ purastāt pañcamībhiḥ deśāt saṃbhavateḥ parastāt adhikāre pṛthivyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ apādāa pañcamī darśaāt vāyoḥ agiḥ apādāa pañcamī eṣā gamyate vāyoḥ kalpyate ja tejasaḥ virudhyate tasyāḥ śrṛtam tasyāḥ dadhi tasyāḥ āmikṣā ityādi brahmaṇaḥ īśvara smaraṇam bhavati buddhiḥ jñā asaṃmohaḥ bhavati bhāvāḥ bhūtāām mattaḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ yadi kāraṇebhyaḥ pratyakṣam bhavataḥ sarvasya jātasya praṇāḍyā īśvara vaṃśya śrutayaḥ tāsām ayathā sat vaṃśya apekṣate as vaṃśya apekṣate avyavahita jaya tejasaḥ jāyate kasmāt aposṛjata ageḥ apaḥ saṃśayaḥ tejasaḥ sṛṣṭim vyākhyāya pṛthivyāḥ vyākhyāsya apotariyām sūtrayāṃbabhūva atarebhyaḥ adhikaraṇam aikṣata bahvyaḥ syāma prajāyemahi aam asṛjata śrūyate saṃśayaḥ kim vrīhi yava abhyavahāryam vai oda ucyate kim prāptam tāvat vrīhi yava oda parigrahītavyam aa prasiddhaḥ vākyaśeṣaḥ etam upodbalayati tasmāt kva varṣati bhūyiṣṭham aam bhavati vrīhi yava varṣaṇe bahu bhavati prāpte brūmaḥ iyam vivakṣyate kasmāt rūpāt atarāt adhikāraḥ tāvat sṛjata apaḥ sṛjata mahābhūta viṣayaḥ vartate krama prāptām pṛthivīm mahābhūtam vilaṅghya ākasmāt vrīhi parigrahaḥ yāyyaḥ rūpam śeṣe auguṇam kṛṣṇam oda ādeḥ abhyavahāryasya kṛṣṇa tvaiyamaḥ vrīhi ādīām pṛthivyāḥ kṛṣṇa tvaiyamaḥ pāṇḍurasya aṅgāra rohitasya kṣetrasya darśaāt ayam bāhulya bhūyiṣṭham pṛthivyāḥ kṛṣṇam rūpam śvetarohite paurāṇikāḥ chāyām śarvarīm upadiśati kṛṣṇa ābhāsā kṛṣṇam rūpam pṛthivyāḥ śliṣyate śrutyataram adabhyaḥ bhavati apām śaraḥ āsīt samahayata abhavat pṛthivyāḥ vrīhi ādeḥ utpattim pṛthivyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ oṣadhībhyaḥ am pṛthivyāḥ pratipādakeṣu satsu kutas vrīhi pratipattiḥ prasiddhiḥ ādibhiḥ bādhyate dvāreṇa pṛthivyāḥ adbhyaḥ prabhava sūcayati draṣṭavyam tasmāt pṛthivīyam adhikaraṇam kim imāi ādīi bhūtāi svayam vikārān sṛjati āhosvit parameśvaraḥ tam tam vikāram sṛjati saṃdehe prāptam tāvat svayam sṛjati kutas ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ ityādi svātatrya au acetaāām svatatrāṇām pravṛttiḥ pratiṣiddhā eṣa aikṣata aikṣata bhūtāām cetas atva prāpte abhidhīyate parameśvaraḥ avatiṣṭhamānaḥ abhidhyāya tam tam vikāram sṛjati kutas śāstram yaḥ pṛthivyām pṛthivyāḥ ataraḥ yam veda yasya yaḥ pṛthivīm ataraḥ yamayati evaṃjātīyakam sādhyakṣāṇām bhūtāām pravṛttim ukāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya prastutya sat tyad abhavat am svayam akuruta īkṣaṇa śravaṇam ap tejasoḥ parameśvara āveśa vaśāt draṣṭavyam draṣṭā īkṣitratara īkṣituḥ aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya atra krama ūtaḥ viparyaya adhikaraṇam bhūtāām kramaḥ cititaḥ idāīm kramaḥ cityate apyayaḥ uta athavā trayaḥ pralayāḥ bhūtāām āyattāḥ śrūyate vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate yea tve karaṇāām somya mayī evaṃjātīyakam kvacid bhūtāām karaṇāām etavyaḥ abhautikāi karaṇāi kramaḥ karaṇaiḥ viśiṣyate prathamam karaṇāt utpadyate caramam prathamam bhūtāt utpadyate caramam karaṇāi ātharvaṇe bhūtāām kramaḥ ucyate kramāt karaṇa kramaḥ prajāpatiḥ vai idam agre āsīt amaikṣata maosṛjata tamaḥ āsīt amaikṣata vācam asṛjata ityādi tasmāt kramasya bhaṅgaḥ vyapāśraya adhikaraṇam staḥ jīvasya pralayau jātaḥ devadattaḥ mṛtaḥ devadattaḥ evaṃjātīyakāt laukika jātakarma vidhāāt kasyacid bhrātiḥ tāmapaudāmaḥ jīvasya pralayau staḥ jīve jīve atara gata prāpti parihāra arthau pratiṣedhau aarthakau syātām śrūyate apetam vāva kila idam mriyate jīvaḥ mriyate jama maraṇa jīvasya darśitaḥ satyam darśitaḥ eṣa jīvasya jama maraṇa kimāśrayaḥ mukhyaḥ yad ucyate sthāvara jaṅgama viṣayau jama maraṇa śabdau āi jāyate mriyate viṣayau jama maraṇa śabdau mukhyau satau sthe ātmayupacaryete prādurbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ satoḥ jama maraṇa śabdau bhavataḥ āsatoḥ jātaḥ mṛtaḥ kecid lakṣyate vai ayam puruṣaḥ jāyamāaḥ abhisaṃpadyamāaḥ utkrāma mriyamāṇaḥ saṃyoga viyoga aimittau jama maraṇa śabdau jātakarma vidhāam prādurbhāva draṣṭavyam prādurbhāvasya jīvasya parasmāt utpattiḥ ādīām iva āsti etat uttareṇa sūtreṇa vakṣyati āśrayau tāvat jīvasya sthūlau pralayau staḥ etad aea sūtreṇa avocat atvāt adhikaraṇam ākhyaḥ idriya pañjara adhyakṣaḥ saṃbadhī kim utpadyate brahmaṇaḥ āhosvit utpadyate vipratipatteḥ viśayaḥ kāsucid śrutiṣu parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpattiḥ āmāyate kāsucid avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ vijñāyate utpattiḥ āmāyate prāptam tāvat utpadyate jīvaḥ kutas iyam sarvasya vastu jātasya prabhava tve oparudhyeta tattva atara tve jīvasya iyam uparudhyeta vikṛtaḥ paramātmā jīvaḥ śakyate vijñātum apahata pāpma dharmakaḥ paramātmā viparītaḥ jīvaḥ vibhāgāt yāvā pravibhaktaḥ sarvaḥ vikāraḥ ādeḥ utpattiḥ samadhigatā jīvātmā puṇya apuṇya karmā duḥkha yuj pratiśarīram pravibhaktaḥ prapañca avasare utpattiḥ bhavitum arhati āgeḥ kṣudrāḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vyuccarati asmāt ādeḥ bhogya jātasya sṛṣṭim śiṣṭvā vyuccarati bhoktṛṇām sṛṣṭim su dīptāt pāvakāt visphuliṅgāḥ sahasraśas prabhavate sarūpāḥ akṣarāt vividhāḥ somya bhāvāḥ prajāyate apiyati pralayau ucyete sarūpa vacaāt bhavati caitaya kvacid aśravaṇam ayatra vārayitum arhati atara gatasya aviruddhasya adhikasya arthasya upasaṃhartavya praveśa śrutiḥ āpattyā vyākhyātavyā aam svayam akuruta ityādi tasmāt utpadyate jīvaḥ prāpte brūmaḥ jīvaḥ utpadyate kasmāt prakaraṇe śravaṇam bhūyaḥsu pradeśeṣu kvacid aśravaṇam ayatra vārayati satyam utpattiḥ tvasya saṃbhavati vadāmaḥ kasmāt itya caśabdāt aja itya śrutibhyaḥ uvagamyate aja avikāri avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ evaṃrūpasya utpattiḥ kāḥ śrutayaḥ jīvaḥ mriyate vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ajaroma romṛta ubhayaḥ jāyate mriyate vipaścit ajaḥ ityaḥ śāśvataḥ yam purāṇaḥ sṛṣṭvā auprāviśat āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi eṣaḥ praviṣṭaḥ akha agrebhyaḥ asi aham asmi ayam aubhūḥ evamādyāḥ satyaḥ jīvasya utpattim pratibadhati pravibhakta vikāraḥ utpadyate atra ucyate pravibhāgaḥ svatas ekaḥ devaḥ gūḍhaḥ vyāpī acaitaya tve supta mūrchita graha āviṣṭāām caitayam pṛṣṭāḥ kiṃcid vayam cetayemahi jalpati svasthāḥ cetayamānāḥ kādācitka caitaya āgatuka caitayaḥ prāpte abhidhīyate caitayaḥ yam yasmāt otpadyate avikṛtam upādhi saṃparkāt avatiṣṭhate brahmaṇaḥ caitaya āmātam satyam jñāamaatam kṛtsaḥ ityādiṣu śrutiṣu jīvaḥ tasmāt jīvasya gamyate vijñā amaya prakriyāyām śrutayaḥ bhavati suptaḥ supta abhicākaśīti pariccheda gadhāya ghrāṇam ityādi supta cetayataḥ śrutyā parihāraḥ abhihitaḥ suṣuptam prakṛtya vai paśyati draṣṭuḥ viparilopaḥ dvitīyam vibhaktam paśyet ityādiā etat bhavati viṣaya iyam acetayamāatā mahā parimāṇaḥ utpadyate ayam jīvaḥ āpatati kutas jīvasya parimāṇa citā avatāraḥ ucyate satyam etat jīvasya paricchedam prāpayati kvacid aṇu parimāṇa sarvasya ākula upapāda ayam ārambhaḥ prāptam tāvat jīvaḥ utkrātiḥ tāvat yadā asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati etaiḥ sarvaiḥ utkrāmati gatiḥ ye vai ke asmāt lokāt prayati cadramasam gacchati āgatiḥ tasmāt lokāt puar aiti asmai lokāya karmaṇe āsām tāvat jīvaḥ vibhoḥ gamyate utkrātiḥ kadācid acalataḥ svāmi aivṛtti svāmi aivṛttyā kṣayeṇa avakalpeta uttare āgatī ācalataḥ saṃbhavataḥ tayoḥ bhavati gameḥ amadhyama parimāṇasya āgatī aṇu tve saṃbhavataḥ satyoḥ āgatyoḥ utkrātiḥ apasṛptiḥ dehāt pratīyate dehāt āgatī syātām pradeśāām utkrātau cakṣuṣṭoma mūrdhaḥ vāyebhyaḥ śaīra deśebhyaḥ etāḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadai hṛdayam avavakrāmati śukram ādāya puaraiti atare śārīrasya āgatī bhavataḥ tasmāt aṇu āṇuḥ āṇuḥ ayam kasmāt aṇu viparīta parimāṇa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ yaḥ yam vijñā prāṇeṣu gataḥ satyam satyam evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ oṇu tve vipratiṣidhyeta eṣa kasmāt mātraḥ avaraḥ vaṇu tve deśa sthasya sakala gata upalabdhiḥ virudhyate śaitya upalabdhiḥ idāgha samaye sakala paritāpa upalabdhiḥ uttaram paṭhati cadaa deśa saṃbaddhaḥ sakala vyāpiam āhlādam karoti deśa sthaḥ sakala vyāpiīm upalabdhim kariṣyati tvac saṃbadhāt sakala gatā virudhyate tvac ātmaoḥ saṃbadhaḥ kṛtsāyām tvaci vartate tvac kṛtsa vyāpi atra cadaa ayuktam dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ atulya siddhe deśa tve bhavati pratyakṣam cadaasya deśa sakala āhlādam ātmaaḥ sakala pratyakṣam aikadeśavartitvam aumeyam ucyeta sakala gatāḥ kim vibhoḥ abhasaḥ iva āhosvit cada abidoḥ iva aṇoḥ deśa sthasya avabodhaḥ tāvat ayam upādhi saṃbadhaḥ śāmyati veda aham etam mahātam varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tam viditvā mṛtyum eti āyaḥ pathā suṣupta pralayayoḥ śakyate suṣupta pralayayoḥ śakyate suṣupta pralayayoḥ buddhiḥ ataḥkaraṇam avaśyam abhyupagatavyam ayathā aupalabdhi idriya viṣayāṇām sādhaāām ityam upalabdhiḥ prasajyeta samavadhāe prasajyeta athavā idriyasya pratibadhaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ ātmaaḥ pratibadhaḥ saṃbhavati avikriya āpi idriyasya kṣaṇayoḥ apratibaddha śaktikasya satā ukasmāt śaktiḥ pratibadhyeta tasmāt śrutiḥ ayatramaāḥ abhūvam ādarśam ayatramaāḥ abhūvam āśrauṣam maasā paśyati kasmāt yajeta juhuyāt dadyāt evaṃvidham śāstram itas jīvasya prakriyāyām vihāram upadiśati īyate mṛtaḥ kāmam sve parivartate upādāāt itas prakriyāyām karaṇāām upādāam saṃkīrtayati eṣām prāṇāām vijñāea vijñāam ādāya gṛhītvā itas jīvasya laukikīṣu vaidikīṣu kriyāsu vyapadiśati śāstram yajñam taute karmāṇi vijñāa buddhau samadhigataḥ katham aea jīvasya ucyate jīvasya eṣa buddheḥ jīvasya vivakṣāyām bhuñje aham pibāmi tasyāḥ yuktāyāḥ kāri ayat kalpayitavyam śaktā upi upādāya kriyāsu pravartamāaḥ mātre vivādaḥ vastu bhedaḥ kaścid karaṇa vyatiriktasya ayam samādhiḥ upadiṣṭaḥ vai are draṣṭavyaḥ saṃparka kṛtam śramam śyeasya iva viparipatataḥ śrāvayitvā suṣuptau saṃpariṣvaktasya śrāvayati vai etat āpta kāmam kāmam akāmam rūpam śokātaram ārabhya eṣā paramā gatiḥ eṣā paramā saṃpad eṣā usya paramaḥ lokaḥ eṣā usya parama upasaṃhārāt etat ācāryaḥ ubhayathāḥ arthe ayam caḥ paṭhitaḥ matavyam svābhāvikam ageḥ iva auṣṇyam takṣā vāsi karaṇa hastaḥ duḥkhī bhavati gṛham prāptaḥ vimukta vāsi karaṇaḥ svasthaḥ irvṛtaḥ irvyāpāraḥ sukhī bhavati avidyā pratyupasthāpita dvaita saṃpṛktaḥ svapa jāgarita avasthayoḥ duḥkhī bhavati svam praviśya sukhī bhavati saṃprasāda avasthāyām avasthāyām avidyā dhvātam pradīpea vidhūya sukhī bhavati dṛṣṭātaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ takṣā viśiṣṭeṣu takṣaṇa vyāpāreṣu karaṇāi bhavati śarīreṇa akartā ayam vyāpāreṣu karaṇāi bhavati takṣṇaḥ iva avayavāḥ yaiḥ ādibhiḥ iva takṣā upādadīta yasya id ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ svābhāvikam ātmaaḥ śāstram tāvat yathāprāptam upādāya kartavya upadiśati pratipādayati svābhāvikam ātmatva avocāma tasmāt avidyā kṛtam upādāya śāstram pravartiṣyate vijñāātmā puruṣaḥ evaṃjātīyakam śāstram auvāda yathāprāptam avidyā kṛtam parihṛte tayoḥ saṃdhye prasupteṣu karaṇeṣu sve parivartate vihāraḥ upadiśyamāaḥ kevalasya āvahati upādāe eṣām prāṇāām ādāya karaṇeṣu karaṇa vibhaktī śrūyamāṇe kevalasya gamayataḥ atra ucyate tāvat karaṇa viramaṇam dhīḥ svapaḥ bhūtvā imam lokam atikrāmati saṃbadha smarati idriyāṇām uparame yadi sevate viṣayāḥ vidyāt svapa darśam vṛttayaḥ śrutiḥ svape tasmāt samaāḥ svapte viharati vihāraḥ tatratyaḥ vāsa āmayaḥ pāramārthikaḥ śrutiḥ svapa vyāpāram varṇayati uta iva strībhiḥ jakṣat uta iva laukikāḥ svapam kathayati ārukṣam iva giri śrṛṅgam adrākṣam iva vaarājim yadi karaṇeṣu karaṇa vibhakti nirdeśaḥ saṃpṛktasya ātmaaḥ draṣṭavyam kevale asaṃbhavasya darśita bhavati prakārā vivakṣā yudhyate yodhaiḥ rājā yudhyate asmi karaṇa uparama vivakṣyate svātatryam kasyacid abuddhi pūrvakasya svāpe karaṇa uparam yasya ayam darśitaḥ vijñāam yajñam taute buddheḥ prāpayati vijñāa maoataram pāṭhāt śraddhā śraddhā avayava saṃkīrtaāt śraddhā ādīām vijñāam devāḥ jyeṣṭham upāsate jyeṣṭha tvasya prathama ja tvasya buddhau eṣa cittasya uttarottara kramaḥ yajñaḥ śrutyatare yajñasya sādhya buddheḥ karaṇāām bhavati kārakāṇām vyāpāreṣu tvasya avaśyaṃbhāvi eṣām karaṇāām karaṇa tasyām ahaṃkāra pūrvakam opalabdhuḥ bhavitum arhati ahaṃkārasya upalabhyamāa karaṇa atara kalpa buddheḥ karaṇa parihṛtaḥ yathāprāptam upādāya vidhāāt tasmāt upādhi nimittam sthitam idam avidyā avasthāyām jīvasya abhihitam kim īśvaram bhavati āhosvit īśvara bhavati vicāraṇā prāptam tāvat eśvaram apekṣate jīvaḥ tve kasmāt prayoja ābhāvāt ayam jīvaḥ svayam rāga dveṣa prayuktaḥ kim īśvaraḥ kariṣyati kim īśvaraḥ kariṣyati kṛṣi ādikāsu kriyāsu aaḍuha īśvara upara upekṣitavyaḥ kleśa ātmake tve īśvarasya airghṛṇyam prasajyeta viṣama eṣām vidadhataḥ vaiṣamyam aairghṛṇye satyam īśvarasya saṃbhave īśvarasya saṃbhavati adharmayoḥ tayoḥ sadbhāvaḥ jīvasya tve īśvara kiṃviṣayam īśvarasya ucyeta akṛta abhyāgamaḥ jīvasya prasajyeta tasmāt svatas etām prāptim tuśabdena vyāvartya pratijāīte avidyā avasthāyām karaṇa saṃghāta aviveka jīvasya avidyā timira ādhasya parasmāt adhyakṣāt adhivāsāt sākṣiṇaḥ cetayituḥ īśvarāt aujñayā lakṣaṇasya saṃsārasya bhavitum arhati kutas yadi prayuktaḥ sāmagrī saṃpaaḥ jīvaḥ yadi kṛṣi karmasu eśvara prasiddham sarvāsu pravṛttiṣu īśvaraḥ avasīyate śrutiḥ bhavati eṣa sādhu kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ uiīṣate eṣa asādhu kārayati tam yam adhas yaḥ ātmai yamayati evaṃjātīyakāḥ īśvarasya kārayitṛ tve airghṛṇye syātām akṛta abhyāgamaḥ jīvasya ucyata prayata tuśabdaḥ codita vyāvarta kṛtaḥ yaḥ prayataḥ jīvasya adharma lakṣaṇaḥ eam īśvaraḥ kārayati coditāḥ doṣāḥ prasajyate adharma phalāi viṣamam vibhajet parjaya imitta mātreṇa guccha gulma ādīām vrīhi yava ādīām asādhāraṇebhyaḥ bījebhyaḥ jāyamāāām sādhāraṇam imittam bhavati parjayaḥ parjaye rasa puṣpa palāśa vaiṣamyam jāyate bījeṣu prayata īśvaraḥ śubha aśubham vidadhyāt śliṣyate prayata jīvasya parāyatte tve eṣa parāyatte tve karoti jīvaḥ kurvatam tam īśvaraḥ kārayati prayatam idāīm kārayati pūrvataram prayatam akārayat saṃsārasya aavadyam katham prayata īśvaraḥ svarga kāmaḥ yajeta brāhmaṇaḥ hatavyaḥ evaṃjātīyakasya vihitasya pratiṣiddhasya avaiyarthyam bhavati ayathā aarthakam īśvaraḥ atyata paratatra jīvasya kāriṇam saṃsṛjet kāriṇam prāmāṇyam vedasya astam iyāt īśvarasya atyatā aapekṣa tve laukikasya puruṣakārasya vaiyarthyam deśa kālaimittāām ukta evaṃjātīyakam jātam grahaṇena dāśakitavādi dāśakitavādi īśvarayoḥ upakārya upakāraka uktaḥ saṃbaddhayoḥ svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ agi visphuliṅgayoḥ īśvarayoḥ upakārya upakāraka kim āhosvit agi visphuliṅga asyām vicikitsāyām aiyamaḥ athavā svāmi bhṛtya prakāreṣu īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvasya tadvidhaḥ jīvaḥ īśvarasya bhavitum arhati āgeḥ visphuliṅgaḥ iva iḥ avayavasya mukhyaḥ oṃśaḥ saṃbhavati kasmāt puaḥ iḥ avayava bhavati iṣṭavyaḥ vijijñāsitavyaḥ etam viditvā muiḥ bhavati yaḥ ātmai tiṣṭha amataraḥ yamayati evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhedaiḥ deśaḥ āsati yujyate ayam sutarām svāmi bhṛtya sārūpye yujyate ayathā kevalāt aṃśa pratipattiḥ kim tarhi ayathā pratipādakaḥ kitava brahmaṇaḥ āmaatya ātharvaṇikāḥ brahmasūkte dāśāḥ dāsāḥ kitavāḥ dāśāḥ ye kaivartāḥ prasiddhāḥ ye amīdāsāḥ ye aye kitavāḥ dyūta kṛtaḥ brahmā āma karaṇa saṃghāta praviṣṭāām jīvāām brahmatvam prakriyāyām ayam prapañcyate strī pumān asi kumāraḥ uta kumārī jīrṇaḥ jātaḥ bhavati viśvatomukhaḥ rūpāṇi vicitya āyotaḥ draṣṭā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ arthasya caitayam aviśiṣṭam īśvarayoḥ agi visphuliṅgayoḥ auṣṇyam abheda avagamābhyām aṃśa avagamaḥ kutas aṃśa avagamaḥ matravarṇāt matravarṇaḥ etam avagamayati tāvā mahimā jyāyāḥ puruṣaḥ pādaḥ usya sarvā pādasya amṛtam divi atra sthāvara jaṅgamāi irdiśati tīrthebhyaḥ prayogāt pādaḥ bhāgaḥ aarthātaram tasmāt aṃśa avagamaḥ kutas aṃśa avagamaḥ īśvaragītāsu īśvara aṃśa jīvasya mama bhūtaḥ tasmāt aṃśa avagamaḥ svāmi bhṛtya īśitṛ īśitavya prasiddhaḥ yadi eṣā prasiddhiḥ śāstrāt atra aṃśa aṃśi īśitṛ īśitavya iścīyate praśāsti kiṃcid vipratiṣidhyate atra jīvasya īśvara aṃśa duḥkhi devadattasya duḥkhi prāptāām mahattaram duḥkham prāpuyāt varam avasthaḥ saṃsāraḥ samyak darśa āarthakya atra ucyate prakāśāt iva jīvaḥ duḥkham ubhavati īśvaraḥ ubhavati pratijāīmahe jīvaḥ avidyā veśa vaśāt iva gatvā duḥkhī aham avidyayā kṛtam duḥkha upabhogam parameśvarasya duḥkha abhimāaḥ jīvasya duḥkha abhimāaḥ pāramārthikaḥ gata dāha cheda nimittam duḥkham abhimā abhrātyā ubhavati mitra gocaram duḥkham aham putraḥ aham mitram mitra etat avagamyate mithyā abhimā bhrama maimittaḥ duḥkha āubhavaḥ darśaāt avagamyate mitra ādimatsu bahuṣu upaviṣṭeṣu itareṣu putraḥ mṛtaḥ mitram mṛtam āghoṣite yeṣām mitra ādimattva abhimāaḥ taimittam duḥkham utpadyate parivrājaka ādīām laukikasya puṃsaḥ samyak daśā kim uta tasmāt samyak darśa āarthakya sauraḥ ādramasaḥ vyāpya avatiṣṭhamāaḥ teṣu ṛju vakra pratipadyamāeṣu paramārthataḥ pratipadyate ghaṭa gacchatsu gaccha vibhāvyamānaḥ paramārthataḥ pratipadyate ghaṭa gacchatsu gaccha vibhāvyamānaḥ paramārthataḥ pratipadyate ghaṭa gacchatsu gaccha paramārthataḥ gacchati uda śarāva kampaāt gate sūrya pratibimbe gate sūrya pratibimbe avidyā pratyupasthāpite upahite ākhye aṃśe īśvaraḥ duḥkhāyate jīvasya duḥkha avidyā nimittā vyudāsea jīvasya pratipādayati tattvam asi evamādayaḥ tasmāā duḥkhea paramātmanaḥ duḥkhi smarati smarati vyāsa jaivea paramātmā duḥkhāyate yaḥ paramātmā irguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ lipyate phalaiḥ padma patram iva ambhasā aparaḥ yaḥ asau yujyate saptadaśakena yujyate caśabdāt vākyaśeṣaḥ tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam abhicākaśīti ekaḥ atarātmā lipyate duḥkhea bāhyaḥ atra yadi tarhi ekaḥ katham aujñā syātām laukikau vaidikau jīvaḥ īśvarasya aujñā āśrayau avyatikīrṇau upapadyete kim atra codyate ucyate aitadevam aṃśa jīvasya abheda vādiyaḥ śrutayaḥ pratipādayati sṛṣṭvā auprāviśat draṣṭā mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum āpoti yaḥ paśyati tattvam asi aham asmi evaṃjātīyakāḥ abheda avagamābhyām aṃśa sidhyati etat yadi ubhau abhedau pratipipādayiṣitau syātām abhedaḥ atra ātmatva svabhāva prāptaḥ bhedaḥ uūdyate brahmaṇaḥ mukhyaḥ oṃśaḥ jīvaḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt ekaḥ bhūtāām atarātmā bhāvena avasthitaḥ vaktavyā aujñāparihāra upapattiḥ tām brūmaḥ aujñāparihārau ṛtau bhāryām upeyāt aujñā opagacchet parihāraḥ agīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet aujñā viparīta utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā aham gacchāmi aham āgacchāmi aham adhas aham aadhas aham mūḍhaḥ aham amūḍhaḥ ātmikā asyāḥ samyak darśaāt pratatā eṣā bhrātiḥ jatuṣu avidyā upādhi saṃbadha kṛtāt aikātmya aujñāparihārau avakalpete samyagdarśiṇaḥ tarhi aujñāparihāra āarthakyam prāptam kṛtārtha iyojya aupapatteḥ upādeyayoḥ iyojyaḥ atiriktam heyam upādeyam vastu apaśya katham darśiḥ iyojya saṃhata abhimāāt satyam asaṃhata paśyataḥ asaṃhata darśiḥ kasyacid iyogaḥ kim uta aikātmya darśiḥ iyoga samyak darśiḥ yatheṣṭa ceṣṭā abhimāasya pravartaka abhimāa samyak darśiḥ jyotiṣaḥ ekatve agiḥ kravyād parihriyate etaraḥ savituḥ amedhya deśa saṃbaddhaḥ parihriyate etaraḥ śuci bhūmiṣṭhaḥ bhaumāḥ pradeśāḥ vajra vaiḍūrya upādīyate bhaumāḥ ara kalebara parihriyate mūtra purīṣam gavām pavitra parigṛhyate jātyatare parivarjyate asatateḥ avyatikaraḥ syātām yaḥ ayam aikātmya vyatikīryeta svāmi saṃtateḥ bhoktuḥ ātmaḥ saṃtataḥ sarvaiḥ śarīraiḥ jīvaḥ upādhi asaṃtāāt bhaviṣyati eṣa jīvaḥ o jala pratipattavyaḥ vastvataram aikasmin jalasūryake jalasūryakātaram kampate aikasmin jīve jīvātarasya saṃbadhaḥ avyatikaraḥ phalayoḥ ābhāsasya avidyā āśrayasya saṃsārasya avidyā upapattiḥ pāramārthikasya bhāvasya upapattiḥ yeṣām bahavaḥ ātmāaḥ gatāḥ eṣa katham bahavaḥ vibhavaḥ aḥ caitaya svarūpāḥ iḥ guṇāḥ iḥ atiśayāḥ sādhāraṇam apavarga sāṃkhyāḥ bahu tve vibhu tve ghaṭa kuḍya samāḥ dravya svarūpāḥ svatas acetaāḥ upakaraṇāi maāṃsi dravyāṇām saṃyogāt icchā vaiśeṣikāḥ guṇāḥ utpadyate vyatirekeṇa ātmasu samavayati saṃsāraḥ mokṣaḥ kāṇādāḥ tāvat caitaya ātmanām saṃidhā ādya duḥkha saṃbadhe duḥkha saṃbadhaḥ etat pradhā apravṛtteḥ kaivalya vyavasthā bhaviṣyati ayathā vibhūti khyāpa pradhā apravṛttiḥ aiḥ mokṣaḥ prasajyeta vyavasthā śakyā vijñātum upapattyā kayācid vyavasthā ucyeta asatyām vyavasthā kāṇādāām yadā saṃyujyate ataraiḥ ātarīyakaḥ saṃyogaḥ ātmaaḥ duḥkha yoge ātmaām duḥkhi prasajyeta etat aimittaḥ iyamaḥ bhaviṣyati etya aiyamāt bahuṣu ātmasu gateṣu pratiśarīram bāhya abhyatara aviśeṣeṇa saṃihiteṣu adharma lakṣaṇam adṛṣṭam upārjyate sāṃkhyāām tāvat samavāyi pradhā avarti pradhā sādhāraṇyā pratyātmam duḥkha upabhogasya kāṇādāām eṣaḥ etat aham idam idam idam pariharāṇi ittham prayatai ittham karavāṇi evaṃvidhāḥ abhisaṃdhyā pratyātmam pravartamāāḥ adṛṣṭasya ātmanām svāmi svāmi iyaṃsyati etya abhisadhyā saṃidhau kriyamāṇāām iyam ahetu aupapatteḥ ukta auṣaṅgaḥ pradeśāt ce ātarbhāvāt ucyeta vibhu tve saṃyogaḥ pradeśe bhaviṣyati kṛtā vyavasthā abhisaṃdhyā ādīām adṛṣṭasya duḥkhayoḥ bhaviṣyati opapadyate kasmāt atarbhāvāt vibhu sarvaḥ śarīreṣu vaiśeṣikaiḥ ātmaaḥ pradeśaḥ kalpayitum śakyaḥ ayam pradeśaḥ pāramārthikam saṃidhau ātmaaḥ etareṣām iyatum śakyam dvayoḥ ātmaoḥ dvayoḥ ātmaoḥ kadācid samāa pradeśasya dvayoḥ ātmaoḥ adṛṣṭasya devadattaḥ yasmin pradeśe duḥkham tasmāt pradeśāt apakrāte yajñadatta tam pradeśam itareṇa duḥkha aubhavaḥ yadi devadatta yajñadattayoḥ svarga aupabhoga vādiḥ brāhmaṇa pradeśeṣu aiṣpatteḥ atara varti svarga upabhogasya aupapattiḥ vada tāvat ke bahavaḥ samāadeśāḥ dharmi aṃśeā vaśāt upapattiḥ ādīām vibhu vādinoḥ siddham kāryatva tasmāt ekatva pakṣe siddham śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ adhikaraṇam katham āulomyam ābhāvāt bahutva vādi dūṣaṇam prakṛtam saṃbhavati sādṛśya sādṛśye am siṃhaḥ balavarmā pratipāda yadi ucyeta adṛṣṭasya saṃidhau utpadyamāasya aiyata prāṇāām pratyaiyata bhavet upamīyera siddhāta jīvasya autpattiḥ ākhyātā prāṇāām utpattiḥ ācikhyāsitā tasmāt asaṃbaddham iva pratibhāti atra vādi jātam udāharaṇam etasmāt lokāḥ devāḥ bhūtāi vyuccarati evaṃjātīyakam parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpadyate etasmāt jāyate maaḥ idriyāṇi kham vāyuḥ viśvasya dhāriṇī evamādiṣu kha prāṇāām utpattiḥ draṣṭavyam athavā evamādiṣu brahmaṇaḥ vikārāḥ samadhigatāḥ brahmaṇaḥ vikārāḥ yojayitavyam kaḥ puar prāṇāām tve hetuḥ keṣucid pradeśeṣu prāṇāām utpattiḥ śrūyate ayuktam atareṣu kvacid aśravaṇam ayatra iva ārayitum utsahate tasmāt utpadyate sūktam puaruktam utpatteḥ sadbhāva āām śrutiḥ pratyāha gauṇyāḥ āām śrutiḥ saṃbhavati āām śrutiḥ saṃbhavati bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati vijñāam pratijñāya etasmāt jāyate ityādi ādeḥ samastasya jagataḥ tve prakṛti vyatirekeṇa sidhyati gauṇyām prāṇāām śrutau iyam hīyeta pratijñāta upasaṃharati puruṣaḥ idam viśvam tapaḥ amṛtam idam viśvam idam variṣṭham vai are darśayā śravaṇea matyā vijñāea idam sarvam viditam evaṃjātīyakāsu śrutiṣu eṣā yojayitavyā katham puas utpatteḥ prāṇāām sadbhāva śravaṇam aita mūlaprakṛti viṣayam aprāṇaḥ amaāḥ śubhraḥ akṣarāt paratas mūlaprakṛteḥ samasta rahita avātara prakṛti viṣayam etat utpatteḥ prāṇāām sadbhāva avadhāraṇam draṣṭavyam vyākṛta viṣayāṇām bhūyasīām avasthāām smṛtyoḥ prakṛti adhikaraṇe pūrvapakṣa sūtra jama śrutiḥ hāyā siddhātaḥ abhihitaḥ siddhāta sūtra gauṇyāḥ jama jama śrutiḥ vyācakṣāṇaiḥ itas ādīām iva prāṇāām mukhyā jama śrutiḥ jāyate ekam jama padam prāṇeṣu sat uttareṣu auvartate etasmāt jāyate atra mukhyam jama pratiṣṭhāpitam sāma āyāt prāṇeṣu mukhyam jama bhavitum arhati prakaraṇe vākye ekaḥ sakṛt uccaritaḥ bahubhiḥ kvacid mukhyaḥ kvacid adhyavasātum śakyam vairūpya prāṇam asṛjata prāṇāt śraddhām atra prāṇeṣu śrutaḥ sṛjatiḥ pareṣu utpattimatsu śraddhā auṣajyate paścāt śrutaḥ vacaḥ pūrvaiḥ saṃbadhyate eṣaḥ yāyaḥ vyuccarati ayam ate paṭhitaḥ vyuccarati pūrvaiḥ ādibhiḥ saṃbadhyate yadi sṛjate etasmin prakaraṇe prāṇāām utpattiḥ paṭhyate baāām bhūtāām sāmāyāt prāṇāām prabhava siddham bhavati prakaraṇe baa aa mayam somya mayī yadi tau amukhyam eṣām maya vartate prabhava kartṛkāyām āma vyākriyāyām yeāśrutam bhavati aitadātmyam idam sarvam upasaṃhārāt atara prapañca gamyate tasmāt prāṇāām adhi adhikaraṇam viṣayaḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ prāṇānām parihṛtaḥ viṣayaḥ idāīm parihriyate mukhyam prāṇam upariṣṭāt vakṣyati saṃprati kati saṃpradhārayati vipratipatteḥ atra viśayaḥ kvacid saṃkīrtyate prabhavati tasmāt kvacid aṣṭau guṇe saṃkīrtyate aṣṭau grahāḥ aṣṭau atigrahāḥ kvacid vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ dvau avāñcau kvacid daśa ava vai puruṣe ābhiḥ daśamī kvacid ekādaśa daśa puruṣe ekādaśaḥ kvacid atra kvacid trayodaśa draṣṭavyam atra iyattām śrutayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam kutas tāvatā uvagamyate prabhavati tasmāt evaṃvidhāsu śrutiṣu viśeṣitāḥ vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ atra guhā āśayāḥ ihitāḥ vīpsā śrūyate saptabhyā utiriktā prāṇā āgamayati eṣa abhiprāyā iyam vīpsā pratipuruṣam tattva abhiprāyā ayeye prāṇā prāṇeṣu udāhṛtā katham syuḥ satyam udāhṛtā ayatamā adhyavasātavyā vṛtti saṃkhyātara śravaṇam atra ucyate sthita itas apare saptabhyā utiriktāḥ śrūyate hastaḥ vai grahaḥ karmaṇā atigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ hastābhyām karoti evamādyāsu śrutiṣu atireke atarbhāvāt śakyate saṃbhāvayitum hīā vipratipattau adhikā saṃgrāhyā bhavati tasyām hīā atarbhavati hīāyām adhikā matavyam stoka kalpa aāurodhāt syuḥ aurodhāt ekādaśā syuḥ udāhṛtā śrutiḥ daśa puruṣe ekādaśaḥ atra ataḥkaraṇam parigṛhyate karaṇa au ekādaśa adhike trayodaśa tve udāhṛte satyam udāhṛte ekādaśabhyaḥ jātebhyaḥ dhikam jātam yad kalpyeta sparśa rasa gadha viṣayāḥ bhedāḥ buddhīdriyāṇi bhedāḥ karmedriyāṇi viṣayam traikālya vṛtti maas ekam aekavṛttikam vṛtti kvacid bhia buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ cittam śrutiḥ ādyāḥ āāvidhāḥ vṛttīḥ aukramya etat sarvam me catvāraḥ abhimatāḥ syuḥ sthā catvāraḥ gaṇyate dve śrotre dve cakṣuṣī dve āsike ekā tāvatām vṛtti bhedāḥ śakyate vaktum vṛttīām atyata vijātīya vai puruṣe ābhiḥ daśamī atra chidra abhiprāyeṇa daśa ucyate tattva abhiprāyeṇa ābhiḥ daśamī vacaāt kaścit prasiddhaḥ mukhyasya prāṇasya bhavati ābhiḥ ekam ābhiḥ daśamī ucyate kvacid upāsa katicid gaṇyate kvacid pradarśa vicitre kva kim vivektavyam viṣayam pramāṇam sthitam iyam aparā sūtra dvaya yojaā syuḥ gatiḥ śrūyate tam utkrāmatam utkrāmati prāṇam aūtkrāmati atra utra paṭhyate katham saptāām gatiḥ pratijñāyate tvac paryatāḥ viśeṣitāḥ prakṛtāḥ cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ parāṅ paryāvartate ithārūpa bhavati ekībhavati paśyati āhuḥ evamādi gāmī bhavati brāhmaṇāḥ bhojayitavyāḥ ye imatritāḥ prakṛtāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ śabdena ucyate ye prakṛtāḥ śabdena ucyate katham tattva vṛtti tasmāt prāpte brūmaḥ apare saptabhyā utiriktāḥ pratīyate hastaḥ vai grahaḥ ityādi śrutiṣu graha gṛhyate badhyate kṣetrajñaḥ graha saṃjñakea kṣetrajñaḥ badhyate atareṣu tulya badhaasya tasmāt atara saṃcāri idam graha saṃjñakam arthāt bhavati smṛtiḥ liṅgea ādyea yujyate baddhasya vai badhaḥ mokṣaḥ muktasya mokṣāt aviyogam ātharvaṇe draṣṭavyam atra tulyavat idriyāṇi hastau ādātavyam upasthaḥ pāyuḥ visarjayitavyam pādau gatavyam daśa puruṣe ekādaśaḥ yadā asmāt amartyāt utkrāmati rodayati ekādaśāām prāṇāām utkrātim vaśe saptasu avasthāpayitum śakyate brāhmaṇāḥ bhojayitavyāḥ atra brāhmaṇāām grahaṇam yāyyam bhoja āśritā kiṃcid saṃkocae kāraṇam tasmāt atra aśeṣāṇām prāṇāām parigrahaḥ pradarśa tasmāt ekādaśa śabdataḥ kāryataḥ siddham aṇu adhikaraṇam prāṇāām prakṛtāḥ pratipattavyāḥ aṇu eṣām saukṣmya paricchedau paramāṇu tulya sūkṣmāḥ sthūlāḥ syuḥ maraṇa kāle bilāt ahiḥ iva upalabhyera mriyamāṇasya pārśva sthaiḥ paricchiāḥ gatāḥ syuḥ utkrāti āgati vyākopaḥ jīvasya sidhyet sarvagatāām vṛtti lābhaḥ deśe vṛtti mātrasya karaṇa sādhaam karaṇa mātre vivādaḥ tasmāt sūkṣmāḥ adhyavasyāmaḥ śraiṣṭhya adhikaraṇam mukhyaḥ vikāraḥ atidiśati aviśeṣeṇa prāṇāām ākhyātam etasmāt jāyate maaḥ idriyāṇi idriya maaḥ vyatirekeṇa prāṇasya prāṇam asṛjata ityādi śravaṇebhyaḥ kimarthaḥ āśaṅkā vāraṇa āsadāsīye pradhāe sūkte matra varṇaḥ bhavati mṛtyuḥ āsīt amṛtam tarhi rātryā aha āsīt praketaḥ āīt avātam svadhayā ekam kiṃca āsa upādāāt utpatteḥ satam iva prāṇam sūcayati tasmāt ajaḥ jāyate kasyacid matiḥ tām atideśe apaudati āīt utpatteḥ sadbhāvam sūcayati avātam aprāṇaḥ amaāḥ śubhraḥ mūlaprakṛteḥ samasta rahita tvasya darśita tasmāt sadbhāva pradarśa ayam āīt mukhyam prāṇam abhidadhāti vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śukra aiṣeka kālāt ārabhya vṛtti lābhāt tadāīm vṛtti lābhaḥ saṃbhavet śrotra ādīām jyeṣṭha ādhikyāt vai śakṣyāmaḥ tvat ṛte jīvitum vāyu vāyu adhikaraṇam puarmukhyaḥ kiṃsvarūpaḥ idāīm jijñāsyate prāptam tāvat vāyuḥ śrūyate yaḥ vāyuḥ eṣa vāyuḥ pañcavidhaḥ upāaḥ vyāaḥ udāaḥ samāaḥ athavā ātarīya abhiprāyāt samasta karaṇa prāptam ātarīyāḥ sāmāyā karaṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ atra ucyate vāyuḥ karaṇa vyāpāraḥ kutas vāyoḥ tāvat prāṇasya bhavati brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ bhāti tapati vāyuḥ vāyoḥ upadiśyeta karaṇa vṛtteḥ bhavati vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ karaṇa vyāpāraḥ karaṇebhyaḥ upadiśyeta etasmāt jāyate idriyāṇi kham vāyuḥ evamādayaḥ vāyoḥ karaṇebhyaḥ prāṇasya samastāām karaṇāām ekā saṃbhavati vṛtti samudāyasya akāraka etat bhaviṣyati pañjara varti anuprāṇi ekādaśa pakṣiṇaḥ pratiiyata vyāpārāḥ saṃbhūya ekam pañjaram cālayati śarīravartin ekādaśa pratiiyata vṛttayaḥ saṃbhūya ekām ākhyām vṛttim pratilapsyate ucyate yuktam pratyeka vṛttibhiḥ avātara vyāpāraiḥ pañjara cāla āurūpaiḥ upetāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃbhūya ekam pañjaram cālayeyuḥ avātara upetāḥ saṃbhūya prāṇyuḥ yuktam pramāṇa atyata vijātīya prāṇasya śreṣṭha yuddha ūṣaṇam upagamaḥ tam ādīām karaṇa vṛtti mātre iva kalpate tasmāt ayaḥ vāyu kriyābhyām katham tarhi iyam śrutiḥ yaḥ vāyuḥ ucyate vāyuḥ ayam vyūhaḥ bhaṇyate abheda śrutī ubhe abheda śrutī virudhyete etat tarhi asmi svātatryam śreṣṭha upagamāt tam ekavidhā vibhūtiḥ prāṇasya śrāvyate supteṣu ekaḥ jāgarti ekaḥ mṛtyoḥ saṃvargaḥ ādī saṃvṛṅkte mātā iva putrāḥ tasmāt prāṇasya svātatrya tam pariharati tuśabdaḥ prāṇasya svātatryam vyāvartayati rāja prakṛti jīvasya upakaraṇāi svatatrāṇi mukhyaḥ rāja matri jīvasya upakaraṇa bhūtaḥ svatatraḥ kutas taiḥ ādibhiḥ śiṣyate saṃvāda yuktam bṛhat rathaṃtara saṃhata acetaa ādī prāṇasya svātatryaiḥ ākaraṇa hetū etat yadi prāṇasya jīvam karaṇa abhyupagamyeta viṣaya ātaram prasajyeta āloca ādibhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ yathāsvam jīvam karaṇa bhavati ekādaśa jātāi parigaṇitāi yad ekādaśa saṃgṛhītāḥ dvādaśam aparam jātam avagamyate yad ayam dvādaśaḥ pratijñāyate uttaram paṭhati tāvat viṣaya atara prāṇasya prāṇasya viṣaya paricchede karaṇa abhyupagamyate etāvatā kasmāt śrutiḥ prāṇasya vaiśeṣikam saṃvāda ha aham śreyasi vyūdire upakramya yasmin iva utkrāte pāpiṣṭhataram iva dṛśyeta vaḥ upayasya vṛtti hīam yathāpūrvam darśayitvā uccikramiṣāyām śaithilya āpattim pāta prasaṅgam darśayatī śrutiḥ aimittām idriya tau ariṣṭhaḥ uvāca mā moham āpat aham etat pañcadhā am pravibhajya etat bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi etam śrutiḥ iau kulāyam supteṣu aimittām rakṣām yasmāt kasmāt aṅgāt utkrāmati śuṣyati aśāti pibati aimittām idriya puṣṭim kasmin aham utkrātaḥ utkrātaḥ bhaviṣyāmi kasmin pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi prāṇam asṛjata aimitte jīvasya utkrāti pratiṣṭhe maaḥ itas mukhyasya prāṇasya vaiśeṣikam yatkāraṇam ayam śrutiṣu upāaḥ vyāaḥ udāaḥ samāaḥ vṛtti bhedaḥ ayam prāc ucchvāsa karmā apāaḥ avāc riśvāsa karmā vyāaḥ tayoḥ saṃdhau vīryavat hetuḥ udāaḥ ūrdhva utkrāti hetuḥ samāaḥ samam sarveṣu mao maasaḥ vṛttayaḥ prāṇasya śrotra nimittāḥ viṣayāḥ vṛttayaḥ prasiddhāḥ kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ bṛ ityādyāḥ paripaṭhitāḥ gṛhyera śrotra irapekṣā bhaviṣyat viṣayā aparā atirekaḥ tarhi matam apratiṣiddham aumatam bhavati yāyāt yoga prasiddhāḥ maasaḥ vṛttayaḥ parigṛhyate bahu vṛtti mātreṇa prāṇasya draṣṭavyam upakaraṇa prāṇasya vṛtti mao yojayitavyam śreṣṭha aṇu adhikaraṇam ayam mukhyaḥ pratyetavyaḥ aṇu saukṣmya paricchedau paramāṇu tulya pañcabhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ sūkṣmaḥ utkrātau vibhu prāṇasya samāmāyate samaḥ samaḥ ebhiḥ tribhiḥ lokaiḥ samaḥ sarveṇa evamādiṣu pradeśeṣu ucyate ādhidaivikea samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpeṇa hairaṇyagarbheṇa etat vibhu āmāyate ādhyātmikea samaḥ prāṇasya paricchedaḥ pradarśyate tasmāt adoṣaḥ adhiṣṭhāam adhikaraṇam puaḥ prakṛtāḥ kim mahimā svasmai svasmai prabhavati āhosvit dhiṣṭhitāḥ prabhavati vicāryate prāptam tāvat yathāsvam mahimā pravarteraiti dhiṣṭhitāḥ prāṇāām pravṛttau abhyugamyamāāyām tāsām adhiṣṭhātrīṇām devatāām śārīrasya pralīyeta mahimā eṣām pravṛttiḥ prāpte idam ucyate tuśabdena pūrvapakṣaḥ vyāvartyate ādibhiḥ agi abhimāiībhiḥ devatābhiḥ adhiṣṭhitam karaṇa jātam kāryeṣu pravartate hetum vyācaṣṭhe āmaaāt agiḥ bhūtvā mukham prāviśat ityādi ageḥ ayam mukha praveśaḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ aṅgīkṛtya ucyate saṃbadham pratyākhyāya ageḥ mukhe kaścid saṃbadhaḥ vāyuḥ bhūtvā āsike prāviśat evamādi yojayitavyam brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ bhāti tapati evamādiā ādīām etam draḍhayati vai vācam prathamām atyavahat yadā mṛtyum atyamucyata evamādiā etam dyotayati adhidaivata vibhāge pratyāsattyā bhavati smṛtau adhyātmam prāhuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tattva darśiṇaḥ vaktavyam adhibhūtam vahis adhidaivatam ityādiā ādīām agi dhiṣṭhita prapañcam pradarśitam mahimā pravarteraiti ayuktam śaktāām śakaṭa ādīām aaḍuha adhiṣṭhitāām pravṛtti darśaāt upapattau āgamāt ādīām agi adhiṣṭhātām pravṛtti darśaāt upapattau āgamāt ādīām adhiṣṭhita devatāām adhiṣṭhātrīṇām śārīrasya parihriyate satīṣu prāṇāām adhiṣṭhātrīṣu devatāsu karaṇa saṃghāta śārīreṇa eṣām prāṇāām avagamyate śrutiḥ etat ākāśam auviṣaṇṇam cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ darśaāya yaḥ veda idam jighrāṇi gadhāya ghrāṇam evaṃjātīyakā śārīreṇa śrāvayati pratikaraṇam adhiṣṭhātrīṇām devatāām asmi ekaḥ ayam asmi bhoktā pratisaṃdhā avagamyate itya śārīrasya asmi puṇya pāpa upalepa duḥkha upabhoga pratilabdhum arhati śrutiḥ bhavati puṇyam amum gacchati ha vai apāpam gacchati śārīreṇa prāṇānām saṃbadhaḥ utkrāti auvṛtti darśaāt tam utkrāmatam utkrāmati prāṇam ūtkrāmatam aūtkrāmati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tasmāt satīṣu karaṇāām iyatrīṣu devatāsu śārīrasya apagacchati karaṇa pakṣasya pakṣasya idriyāṇi ayatra idriya adhikaraṇam mukhyaḥ ekaḥ ekādaśa aukrātāḥ idam saṃdihyate kim mukhyasya prāṇasya vṛtti bhedāḥ āhosvit tattva ātarāṇi kim tāvat prāptam mukhyasya vṛtti bhedāḥ kutas śrutiḥ mukhyam itarān tām khyāpayati hata rūpam asāma etasya rūpam abhavaḥ ekatva adhyavasāyaḥ itarathā ayāyyam prasajyeta ekatra mukhyasya lākṣaṇika āpadyeta tasmāt prāṇasya ādyāḥ vṛttayaḥ ādyāḥ ekādaśā prāpte brūmaḥ kutas kaḥ yam bhedaḥ prakṛtāḥ śreṣṭham varjayitvā avaśiṣṭāḥ ekādaśa idriyāṇi ucyate śrutau darśaāt etasmāt jāyate idriyāṇi evaṃjātīyakeṣu pradeśeṣu idriyāṇi maaḥ idriyāṇi darśaāt satyam etat smṛtau ekādaśa idriyāṇi śrotra saṃgṛhyate prāṇasya idriya śrutau smṛtau prasiddham bhedaḥ ayam tattva pakṣe tattva ekatve ekaḥ idriya vyapadeśam labhate labhate vipratiṣiddham tasmāt tattva atara bhūtāḥ mukhyāt kutas tattva atara bhūtāḥ śrūyate ha vācam ūcuḥ upakramya upasaṃhṛtya prakaraṇam ha imam āsayam prāṇam ūcuḥ asura vidhvaṃsiḥ mukhyasya prāṇasya upakramaṇāt vācam prāṇam evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ udāhartavyāḥ tasmāt tattva atara bhūtāḥ mukhyāt kutas tattva atara bhūtāḥ vailakṣaṇyam bhavati mukhyasya supteṣu ekaḥ jāgarti ekaḥ mṛtyuā āptaḥ āptāḥ utkrātibhyām idriyāṇām viṣaya āloca idriyāṇām prāṇasya evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyāt bhedaḥ idriyāṇām tasmāt eṣām tattva atara etasya rūpam abhavaḥ prāṇe idriyāṇi ayuktam paurvāparya ālocaāt vadiṣyāmi aham dadhre mṛtyuḥ śramaḥ bhūtvā upayeme tasmāt śrāmyati rūpeṇa mṛtyuā grasta ādīām abhidhāya imam madhyamaḥ prāṇam mṛtyunā abhibhūtam ayam vai śreṣṭha tām avadhārayati tasmāt parispada lābhasya āyatta ādīām matavyam tādātmyam idriyeṣu lākṣaṇika śrutiḥ etasya rūpam abhava tasmāt ākhyāyate viṣayasya idriyeṣu lākṣaṇikīm vṛttim prāṇāt ādīni idriyāṇi klṛptiḥ klṛpti adhikaraṇam sat prakriyāyām sṛṣṭim abhidhāya upadiśyate iyam aikṣata hatā aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi tāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām karavāṇi saṃśayaḥ kim kartṛkam idam āma vyākaraṇam āhosvit parameśvara kartṛkam prāptam tāvat kartṛkam idam āma vyākaraṇam kutas cāreṇa aham saṃkalayāi evaṃjātīyake prayoge cāra kartṛkam sat rājā kartṛkam sat āma vyākaraṇam devatāḥ ātmayā adhyāropayati vyākaravāṇi uttamapuruṣa prayogeṇa ḍittha ḍavittha āmasu ghaṭa śarāva rūpeṣu jīvasya vyākartṛ tasmāt kartṛkam idam āma vyākaraṇam prāpte abhidhatte klṛptiḥ tuśabde pakṣam vyāvartayati klṛptiḥ āma vyākriyā etat parameśvaram lakṣayati karaṇe yā iyam klṛptiḥ klṛptiḥ agiḥ ādityaḥ cadramāḥ vidyut kuśa kāśa palāśa paśu mṛga mauṣya pratyākṛti prativyakti aeka prakārā khalu parameśvarasya kṛtiḥ bhavitum arhati kutas iyam upakramya vyākaravāṇi uttamapuruṣa prayogeṇa brahmaṇaḥ vyākartṛ upadiśyate kṛrtṛka vyākaraṇasya adhyavasitam saṃbadhyate aupraviśyaḥ saṃbadhyate vyākaravāṇi vyākaravāṇi ayam viṣaye uttama aupacārikaḥ kalpyeta giri adī samudra aāvidheṣu aīśvarasya jīvasya
