avarohataḥ aevam avarohati yathāgatam aevam dhūma ākāśayoḥ avarohe saṃkīrtaāt yathāgatam pratīyate rātri asaṃkīrtaāt abhra upasaṃkhyāāt pratīyate yā śrutiḥ auśaya sadbhāva pratipāda āya udāhṛtā ye ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ khalu āuśayāt caraṇam cāritram ācāraḥ śīlam aarthātaram auśayaḥ bhukta phalāt karmaṇā utiriktam abhipretam śrutiḥ caraṇe vyapadiśati kārī cārī bhavati karmāṇi tāi sevitavyāi itarāṇi tāi tvayā upāsyāi tasmāt āuśaya eṣa ouśaya eṣā śrutiḥ kārṣṇājiiḥ ācāryaḥ mayate āarthakyam etat kasmāt puaścaraṇa śrautam śīlam vihāya lākṣaṇikaḥ auśayaḥ pratyāyyate śīlasya śrautasya pratiṣiddhasya sādhu asādhu rūpasya bhaviṣyati avaśyam śīlasya kiṃcid abhyupagatavyam ayathā āarthakyam śīlasya prasajyeta eṣa kutas jātam sat hīaḥ kaścid adhikṛtaḥ hīam vedāḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ tve ācārasya āarthakyam ādau jāte ārabhamāṇe ācāraḥ kaṃcid atiśayam ārapsyate kāri prasiddhiḥ tasmāt śīla upalakṣitam auśaya kāraṇam kārṣṇājieḥ matam saṃbhavati śīlāt padbhyām palāyitum pārayamāṇaḥ raṃhitum arhati ācāryaḥ pratyāyyete caraṇam aarthātaram aviśeṣeṇa mātre caratiḥ yaḥ lakṣaṇam puṇyam karoti tam laukikāḥ carati eṣa mahātmā viśeṣaḥ caraṇayoḥ tasmāt ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ praśasta karmāṇaḥ kapūya caraṇāḥ idita karmāṇaḥ aiṣṭa aiṣṭa kāri adhikaraṇam kāriṇaḥ dramasam gacchati ye kāriṇaḥ kim cadramasam gacchati uta gacchati cityate tāvat kāriṇaḥ cadramasam gacchati etat kasmāt cadra maṇḍalam aviśeṣeṇa kauṣītakiḥ samāmaati ye vai ke asmāt lokāt prayati cadramasam gacchati cadra prāptim avakalpate pañcamyām āhutau āhuti iyamāt tasmāt cadramasam āsīdeyuḥ yuktam cadra maṇḍale tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati cadramasam gacchati kasmāt bhogāya cadra ārohaṇam pratyavarohāya kaścid vṛkṣam ārohati puṣpa upādāāya pataāya bhogaḥ aiṣṭa cadramasi āsti tasmāt kāriṇaḥ cadramasam ārohati etare yama ālayam avagāhya puar imam lokam pratyavarohati evaṃbhūtau āroha avarohau bhavataḥ kutas darśaāt śrutiḥ prayatām aiṣṭa yama vaśya tām sāṃparāyaḥ pratibhāti bālam mūḍham ayam paras puas puarvaśam āpadyate me vaivasvatam saṃgamaam evaṃjātīyakam bahu yam prāpti bhavati smarati mauvyāsa prabhṛtayaḥ śiṣṭāḥ pure yama āyattam kapūya vipākam smarati āciketa upākhyā arakāḥ raurava pramukhāḥ paurāṇikaiḥ kutas cadram prāpuyuḥ abhiprāyaḥ viruddham idam yama āyattāḥ yātaāḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ ubhavati yāvatā teṣu raurava citragupta etya teṣu saptasu arakeṣu yamasya adhiṣṭhātṛ yama prayuktāḥ citragupta adhiṣṭhātāraḥ pañcāgi vettha asau saṃpūryate praśasya prativacaḥ avasare śrūyate etayoḥ pathoḥ bhūtaiḥ bhavati jāyasva mriyastva etat saṃpūryate etayoḥ pathoḥ etat kasmāt karmaṇī yāa pitṛyāṇayoḥ pathoḥ pratipade prakṛte ye ittham viduḥ pratipattavyaḥ yāaḥ pathāḥ prakīrtitaḥ iṣṭāpūrte dattam pratipattavyaḥ pitṛyāṇaḥ pathāḥ prakīrtitaḥ prakriyāyām etayoḥ pathoḥ etat bhavati ye pathi adhikṛtāḥ karmaṇā pitṛyāṇe eṣa kṣudrajatu usakṛt āvartī tṛtīyaḥ pathā bhavati tasmāt aiṣṭa kāribhiḥ cadramāḥ prāpyate etat cadra bimbam āruhya uvaruhya kṣudrajatu pratipatsyate āsti āroha āarthakyāt sarveṣu prayatsu cadra lokam prāpuvatsu asau lokaḥ prayadbhiḥ saṃpūryeta praśa viruddham prativacaam prasajyeta prativacaam dātavyam asau saṃpūryate avaroha asaṃpūraṇa upapattiḥ satyam avarohāt asaṃpūraṇam śrutiḥ asaṃpūraṇam etat asaṃpūraṇam etat lokaḥ saṃpūryate ārohāt saṃpūraṇam yuktam avarohasya kāriṣu aviśiṣṭa tve sthā okti āarthakya tuśabdaḥ śākhātarīya prabhavām aśeṣa gama āśaṅkām ucchiatti adhikṛta śākhātarīye vākye uvatiṣṭhate ye vai kecid adhikṛtāḥ asmāt lokāt prayati cat ramasam gacchati puaruktam lābha upapattaye cat ramasam gatum arhati pañcamyām āhutau āhuti iyamāt pratyucyate lābhāya iyamaḥ kutas prakāreṇa sthā jāyasva mriyasva etat pañcamyām āhutau vacasaḥ bhavati āhuti kīrtyate pañcamyām āhutau apām vacaḥ upadiśyate apañcamyām āhutau vacaḥ pratiṣidhyate vākyasya dvi yeṣām āroha avarohau saṃbhavataḥ pañcamyām āhutau dehaḥ udbhaviṣyati droṇa ādīām yoṣit viṣayā ekā āhutiḥ āsti dhṛṣṭadyuma ādīām yoṣit viṣaye dve āhutī staḥ bhavati ayatra bhaviṣyati balākā atareṇa sekam garbham dhatte rūḍhiḥ darśaāt caturvidhe grāme jarāyu ja aṇḍa ja sveda ja udbhid ja lakṣaṇe sveda ja udbhid jayoḥ atareṇa grāmya darśaāt āhuti ādaraḥ bhavati ayatra bhaviṣyati auteṣām khalu eṣām bhūtāām trīṇi bhavati āṇḍa jam jam udbhijjam atra trividhaḥ grāmaḥ śrūyate katham caturvidha grāmasya pratijñātam atra ucyate āṇḍa jam jam udbhijjam atra udbhijja sveda ja upasaṃgrahaḥ kṛtaḥ pratyetavyaḥ sveda ja udbhijjayoḥ bhūmi udaka udbheda prabhava tvasya tulya sthāvara udbhedāt vilakṣaṇaḥ jaṅgama udbhedaḥ ayatra sveda ja udbhijjayoḥ sābhāvya sābhāvya āpatti adhikaraṇam kāriṇaḥ dramasam āruhya tasmin yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā auśayā avarohati avaroha prakāraḥ parīkṣyate iyam avaroha śrutiḥ bhavati etam adhvāam puarivartate itam ākāśam ākāśāt vāyuḥ bhūtvā dhūmaḥ bhavati dhūmaḥ bhūtvā abhram bhavati abhram bhūtvā meghaḥ bhavati meghaḥ bhūtvā pravarṣati saṃśayaḥ kim svarūpam avarohataḥ pratipadyate kim sāmyam prāptam tāvat svarūpam pratipadyate kutas śrutiḥ bhavati itarathā lakṣaṇā lakṣaṇā viśaye śrutiḥ yāyyā lakṣaṇā bhūtvā dhūmaḥ bhavati akṣaraṇi āpattau avakalpate tasmāt pratipattiḥ prāpte brūmaḥ sāmyam pratipadyate cadra maṇḍale am mayam upabhoga ārabdham upabhoga kṣaye samam bhavati vāyoḥ vaśam eti dhūma ādibhiḥ saṃpṛcyate etat ucyate itam ākāśam ākāśāt evamādiā kutas etat etat mukhyaḥ vāyu avarohaḥ vibhu asaṃbaddha sādṛśya ayaḥ ghaṭate asaṃbhave āśrayaṇam yāyyam tulya atra upacaryate āticireṇa āticira adhikaraṇam akāśa vrīhi bhavati viśayaḥ kim dīrgham dīrgham kālam sādṛśyeṇa avasthāya sādṛśyam gacchati uta alpam alpam aiyamaḥ iyama kāriṇaḥ śāstrasya prāpte idam āticireṇa alpam alpam kālam bhāvena avasthāya varṣa dhārābhiḥ imām bhuvam āpatati kutas etat darśaāt vrīhi aataram viśiaṣṭi vai khalu takāraḥ ekaḥ chāt asyām prakriyāyām luptaḥ matavyaḥ duriṣprapatataram duriṣkramataram duḥkhataram asmāt vrīhi saraṇam bhavati atra duḥkham bhavati atra duḥkham pradarśaya pūrveṣu sukham duḥkha viśeṣaḥ ayam iṣprapataasya kāla alpatva aimittaḥ tasmin avadhau aiṣpatteḥ upabhoga tasmāt vrīhi tasmin avarohe tasmin avarohe paṭhyate vrīhi yavāḥ oṣadhi vaaspatayaḥ tila māṣāḥ jāyate saṃśayaḥ bhavati āhosvit kṣetrajña atara dhiṣṭhiteṣu sthāvara śarīreṣu saṃśleṣa gacchati kim tāvat prāptam bhavati kutas etat bhavati kutas etat bhavati kutas etat jaeḥ sthāvara bhāvasya smṛtyoḥ upabhoga sthāa paśu hiṃsā ādeḥ jātasya tasmāt mukhyam idam auśayiām vrīhi jama śva jama yoim sūkara yoim cāṇḍāla yoim mukhyam auśayiām śva jam duḥkha āvitam bhavati vrīhi jam prāpte brūmaḥ ayaiḥ jīvaiḥ adhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhi saṃsarga auśayiḥ pratipadyate bhavati saṃśleṣa vrīhi jāti sthāvaraiḥ saṃśleṣa kutas etat vyāpāram atareṇa kiṃcid vyāpāram parāmṛśati vrīhi jamaya tasmāā atra duḥkha auśayiām duḥkha abhipraiti parāmṛśati vyāpāram ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ kapūya caraṇāḥ vrīhi jamai vrīhi kaṇḍyamāeṣu pacyamāeṣu bhakṣyamāṇeṣu pravaseyuḥ yaḥ jīvaḥ abhimayate pravasati prasiddham saṃsarga auśayika āmaya dhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhi bhavati jaeḥ pratibrūyāt upabhoga sthāa sthāvara bhāvasya vayam upabhoga sthāa sthāvara bhāvasya avajāīmahe bhavatu ayeṣām sthāvara upagatāām etat upabhoga sthāam sthāvara upagatāām etat upabhoga sthāam sthāvara upabhuñjataḥ ācakṣmahe ce puar paśu hiṃsā ādhvarikam aiṣṭam avakalpate mukhyam vrīhi jama kalpaā aarthikā parihriyate adharma vijñāasya ayam dharmaḥ ayam adharmaḥ śāstram vijñāe kāraṇam idriya tayoḥ aiyata deśa kāla aimitta yasmin deśe kāle imitte yaḥ dharmaḥ uṣṭhīyate adharmaḥ bhavati śāstrāt ṛte adharma viṣayam kasyacid śāstrāt hiṃsā augraha ātmakaḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ dharmaḥ avadhāritaḥ katham aśuddhaḥ śakyate vaktum hiṃs śāstram viṣayām hiṃsām adharmaḥ avagamayati bāḍham utsargaḥ apavādaḥ yam agīṣomīyam paśum ālabheta utsarga apavādayoḥ vyavasthita viṣaya tasmāt viśuddham vaidikam śiṣṭaiḥ pratirūpam jāti sthāvara bhavitum arhati ucyate vaiśeṣikaḥ kaścid vrīhi saṃśleṣa upacaryate yogothaḥ itas vrīhi saṃśleṣa kāraṇam āmāyate yaḥ yaḥ yaḥ siñcati bhavati atra mukhyaḥ saṃbhavati cira jātaḥ prāpta yauvaḥ bhavati katham iva aupacaritam pratipadyate tāvat avaśyam abhyupagatavyaḥ vrīhi vrīhi sigbhāvasya ataram yoau retasi auśayiām auśaya upabhogāya jāyate śāstram ye ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ ityādi tasmāt avagamyate āvarohe brāhya avasare duḥkha āvitam bhavati tasmāt vrīhi saṃśleṣa auśayiām siddham śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ sadhye saṃdhyā adhikaraṇam saṃdhye saṃdhyam su apasthāam ācaṣṭe vede prayoga darśaāt saṃdhyam dvayoḥ sthāayoḥ prabodha saṃprasāda sthāayoḥ saṃdhau bhavati saṃdhyam tasmin saṃdhye tathya rūpā bhavitum arhati kutas pramāṇa bhūtā śrutiḥ sṛjate ityādi upasaṃhārāt avagamyate śākhiaḥ saṃdhye sthāe yaḥ eṣa supteṣu jāgarti kāmam kāmam puruṣaḥ kāmāḥ abhipreyate kāmyate ucyera śata āyuṣaḥ pautra vṛṇīṣva prakṛtya tvā bhājam karomi prakṛteṣu prayukta prājñam vākyaśeṣābhyām pratīmaḥ prājñasya idam prakaraṇam ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ityādi viṣayaḥ vākyaśeṣaḥ śukram amṛtam ucyate tasimat lokāḥ śritāḥ ātyeti kaḥ kartṛkā tathya rūpā samadhigatā jāgarita āśrayā svapā āśrayā bhavitum arhati śrutiḥ khalu āhuḥ jāgarita deśe eṣa suptaḥ svapa jāgaritayoḥ samāayāyatām śrāvayati tasmāt tathya rūpā saṃdhye prāpte pratyāha kārtsyeā abhivyakta tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati etat saṃdhye pāramārthikī saṃdhye kutas kārtsyeā abhivyakta paramārtha vastu dharmeṇa abhivyakta svapaḥ kim puaratra kārtsyam abhipretam deśa kā laimitta abādhaḥ paramārtha vastu viṣayāṇi abādhaḥ svape saṃbhāvyate tāvat svape ratha ādīām ucitaḥ deśaḥ saṃbhavati saṃvṛte deśe ratha vakāśam labhera etat dehāt svapam drakṣyati deśa ātarita dravya śrutiḥ dehāt svapam kulāyāt amṛtaḥ caritvā īyate mṛtaḥ kāmam bhedaḥ aiṣkrāte jatau sāmañjasyam aśuvīta ucyate suptasya jatoḥ kṣaṇa mātreṇa deśam paryetum viparyetum sāmarthyam saṃbhāvyate kvacid pratyāgama avarjitam svapam śrāvayati kuruṣu aham adya idrayā abhiplutaḥ svape pañcālāḥ abhigataḥ asmi pratibuddhaḥ dehāt apeyāt pañcāleṣu pratibudhyeta asau abhigataḥ kuruṣu pratibudhyate ayam tamaye pārśvasthāḥ śaya adeśe paśyati ayam deśātarāṇi svape paśyati tathābhūtāya iva bhavati paridhāvan paśyet vastu ākalayet śrutiḥ dehe svapam etat svapyayā carati upakramya sve parivartate upapatti kulāya śrutiḥ vyākhyātavyā iva kulāyāt amṛtaḥ caritvā yaḥ karoti iva śarīrāt bhavati bhedaḥ upi vipralambha abhyupagatavyaḥ kāla visaṃvādaḥ svape bhavati rajayām suptaḥ vāsaram bhārate varṣe svape kadācid bahū varṣa pūgāḥ ativāhayati svape buddhaye karmaṇe ucita vidyate karaṇa upasaṃhārāt ratha grahaṇāya ādīi kutas imeṣa mātreṇa sāmarthyam dārūṇi bādhyate ratha svapa dṛṣṭāḥ prabodhe svape sulabha bādhā bhavati ādya tayoḥ vyabhicāra darśaāt rathaḥ yam kadācid svape mauṣyaḥ mauṣyaḥ yam vṛkṣaḥ spaṣṭam ratha ādīām svape śrāvayati śāstram rathāḥ ratha yogāḥ bhavati ityādi tarhi kaścid svape ucyate svapaḥ bhavati bhaviṣyatoḥ sādhu asādhuoḥ śrūyate yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu striyam svapeṣu paśyati samṛddhim tathāpuruṣam kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa datam paśyati evamādibhiḥ svapaiḥ acirajīvi āvedyate śrāvayati svapa adhyāya svape dhayāi matra dravya aimittāḥ kecid svapāḥ bhavati bhavatu sūcakasya strī darśa ādeḥ bhavati vaitathyam bādhyamāa abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt svapasya vyākhyātavyam lāṅgalam imitta ucyate pratyakṣam lāṅgalam imitta suptaḥ ratha ādī sṛjate ucyate pratyakṣam suptaḥ ratha ādī sṛjati imitta duṣkṛtayoḥ vaktavyam jāgarite viṣaya idriya saṃyogāt vyatikarāt svayam tasmāt ratha vacaam śrutyā ratha sṛṣṭi vacaam bhaktyā vyākhyeyam vihatya svayam svea bhāsā svea prasvapiti eṣa supteṣu jāgarti auvādāt jīvaḥ ayam saṃkīrtyate śeṣeṇa śukram vyāvartya upadiśyate asi ityādi prakaraṇam virudhyate asmābhiḥ vyāpāraḥ pratiṣidhyate īśvara sarvāsu avasthāsu adhiṣṭhātṛ pāramārthikaḥ saṃdhyā āśrayaḥ sargaḥ sarga pratipādyate sargasya ātyatikam pratipāditam hita daaya atra samastasya prapañcasya ātmatva darśaāt prapañcaḥ vyavasthita rūpaḥ bhavati saṃdhyā āśrayaḥ prapañcaḥ bādhyate vaiśeṣikam idam saṃdhyasya uditam abhidhyāāt tāvat oṃśaḥ jīvaḥ ageḥ iva visphuliṅgaḥ agi visphuliṅgayoḥ daha aprakāśa aśaktī bhavataḥ īśvarayoḥ jñā aiśvarya śaktī jīvasya jñā aiśvarya vaśāt sāṃkalpikī svape ratha bhaviṣyati atra ucyate īśvarayoḥ aṃśa aṃśi pratyakṣam jīvasya īśvara viparīta kim puar jīvasya īśvara samāa āsti āsti vidyamāam avidyā vyavadhāāt puas sat parameśvaram abhidhyāyataḥ jatoḥ vidhūta dhvātasya timira tiraskṛtā iva dṛkśaktiḥ auṣadha vīryāt īśvara prasādāt saṃsiddhasya kasyacid āvirbhavati svabhāvataḥ kutas īśvarāt hetoḥ jīvasya badha mokṣau bhavataḥ īśvara aparijñāāt badhaḥ parijñāāt mokṣaḥ śrutiḥ jñātvā devam pāśa apahāiḥ kṣīṇaiḥ kleśaiḥ jama prahāṇiḥ abhidhyāāt dehabhede viśva aiśvaryam kevalaḥ āpta kāmaḥ evamādyā kasmāt puar jīvaḥ paramātma tiraskṛta jñā aiśvaryaḥ bhavati yuktam jñā aiśvaryayoḥ atiraskṛta visphuliṅgasya iva ucyate satyam etat jīvasya jñā aiśvarya tirobhāvaḥ idriya maaḥ viṣaya veda bhavati atra ageḥ daha aprakāśa saṃpaasya araṇi gatasya tirohite bhavataḥ bhasmacchaasya avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma upādhi aviveka bhrama kṛtaḥ jīvasya jñā aiśvarya tirobhāvaḥ jīvasya īśvarāt avayaḥ jīvaḥ īśvarāt tiraskṛta jñā aiśvarya kim jīvasya īśvarāt iyam aikṣata upakramya jīvasya satyam tattvam asi śvetaketo jīvāya upadiśati īśvara īśvarāt jīvaḥ tirohita jñā aiśvaryaḥ bhavati sāṃkalpikī jīvasya svape ratha ghaṭate yadi sāṃkalpikī svape ratha aiva aiṣṭam kaścid svapam paśyet kaścid aiṣṭam saṃkalpayate puaruktam jāgarita deśa śrutiḥ svapasya khyāpayati abhiprāyam svayaṃjyotiṣṭva śrutyā svape ratha abhāvasya darśita svapasya tulyaiḥ bhāsa abhiprāyam tasmāt upapaam svapasya adhikaraṇam svapa parīkṣitā suṣupta idāīm parīkṣyate etāḥ suṣupta viṣayāḥ śrutayaḥ bhavati kvacid śrūyate etat suptaḥ samastaḥ āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati āḍīḥ ukramya śrūyate tābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete āḍīḥ ukramya tāsu bhavati yadā suptaḥ svapam kaṃcaa paśyati asmi ekadhā bhavati yaḥ eṣa utar hṛdaye tasmin śete satā somya saṃpaaḥ bhavati svam itas bhavati bāhyam kiṃca veda ātaram saṃśayaḥ kim parasparaiḥ sthāam āhosvit paraspara ekam sthāam kim tāvat prāptam kutas kvacid paraspara vrīhi yava ādīām āḍī ādīām suṣuptau āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati purītati śete saptamībhiḥ nirdeśasya tulya saptamīirdeśaḥ satā somya bhavati eṣa saptamī arthasya vākyaśeṣaḥ āyataaiṣī jīvaḥ sat upasarpati prāṇam upaśrayate prakṛtasya upādāāt saptamī vākyaśeṣe saṃpadya viduḥ saṃpadyāmahe vijñā uparama lakṣaṇam suṣuptam viśiṣyate tasmāt vikalpea kadācid svāpāya upasarpati prāpte pratipādyate āḍīṣu ātmai prakṛtasya svapa darśaasya suṣuptam āḍīṣu samuccayea svāpāya upasarpati kutas sthāa śrūyate samuccaye saṃgṛhītam bhavati vikalpe eṣām pakṣe vrīhi yava vibhakti irdeśa mātreṇa āpatati ārtha samuccayayoḥ vibhakti irdeśa darśaāt prāsāde śete paryaṅke śete evamādiṣu āḍīṣu purītati brahmaṇi svapiti samuccayaḥ śrutiḥ tāsu bhavati yadā suptaḥ paśyati asmi ekadhā bhavati samuccayam prāṇasya suṣuptau śrāvayati upādāāt prāṇasya brahmatvam samadhigatam āugamāt atra iva āḍīḥ śrāvayati āsu āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati atara prasiddhasya brahmaṇā upratiṣedhāt āḍī dvāreṇa brahmaṇi avatiṣṭhate pratīyate āḍīṣu saptamī virudhyate āḍībhiḥ upasarpa sṛptaḥ āḍīṣu bhavati yaḥ gaṅgayā sāgaram gacchati gataḥ gaṅgāyām bhavati bhavati atra āḍī dvāra ātmakasya brahmaloka mārgasya āḍī āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati uktvā ataṃ kaḥ pāpmā spṛśati bruva āḍīḥ praśaṃsati pāpma sparśa hetum tejasā saṃpaaḥ bhavati tejasā āḍī gate pitta ākhye abhivyāpta karaṇaḥ bāhyā viṣayaḥ īkṣate athavā tejasā brahmaṇaḥ ayam irdeśaḥ śrutyatare brahmaṇi prayukta brahmaṇā bhavati āḍī dvāreṇa tam pāpmā spṛśati pāpma sparśa hetuḥ samadhigataḥ brahmaṇā samuccayaḥ samadhigataḥ bhavati purītataḥ prakriyāyām auguṇam sthāa jñāyate yaḥ eṣa utar hṛdaye tasmin śete hṛdaya sthāe prakṛte idam ucyate purītati śete purītat hṛdaya pariveṣṭaam ucyate hṛdaya śakyate purītati śete vaktum prākāra parikṣipte pure prākāre vartate ucyate hṛdaya ākāśasya brahmatvam samadhigatam dahara atra āḍī purītat samuccaya upitābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete upādāāt avagamyate sat prājñayoḥ prasiddham etāsu śrutiṣu trīṇi sthāāi saṃkīrtitāi āḍyaḥ purītat dvāra āḍyaḥ purītat brahmā ekam apāyi sthāam āḍyaḥ purītat jīvasya upādhi ādhāraḥ bhavati svatas jīvasya ādhāraḥ kaścid saṃbhavati vyatirekeṇa mahima pratiṣṭhita ādhāra suṣupte ādhāra ādheya abhiprāyeṇa ucyate katham tarhi tādātmya abhiprāyeṇa satā somya saṃpaaḥ bhavati svam itas bhavati abhilapyate rūpam suptaḥ bhavati kadācid jīvasya brahmaṇā āsti rūpasya apāyi svapa jāgaritayoḥ upādhi saṃparka vaśāt āpattim iva upaśamāt suṣupteḥ vivakṣyate svam itas bhavati supta avasthāyām kadācid satā ayuktam vijñā upaśama lakṣaṇam tāvat suṣuptam kvacid viśiṣyate saṃpaaḥ tāvat ekatvāt yuktam kam āḍīṣu purītati kiṃcid avijñāe kāraṇam śakyam vijñātum viṣaya ayat iva ayaḥ paśyet viṣayasya dūra kāraṇam avijñāe bāḍham yadi jīvaḥ svatas abhyupagamyeta viṣṇumitraḥ pravāsī gṛhāḥ jīvasya upādhi vyatirekeṇa paricchedaḥ vidyate upādhi gatam dūra kāraṇam yadi ucyeta upādheḥ upaśāta satī yuktam vayam tulya āḍi samuccayam pratipādayāmaḥ āḍyaḥ purītat etat vijñāa pratibaddham kiṃcid śrūyate phalavataḥ kasyacid aṅgam upadiśyate supti sthāam etat pratipādayāmaḥ jīvasya ātmatva avadhāraṇam tasmāt supti sthāam usmāt yasmāt kāraṇāt asmāt ātmaaḥ svāpa adhikāre śiṣyate kutas etat āgāt ityasya praśasya prativacaḥ avasare āgeḥ kṣudrā visphuliṅgāḥ vyuccarati asmāt ātmaaḥ āgamya viduḥ āgacchāmahe sthāeṣu pratibudhyate kadācid purītataḥ kadācid ātmaaḥ aśāsiṣyat tasmāt supti sthāam ausmṛti tasyāḥ puas sat pratibudhyamānaḥ kim yaḥ sat saṃpaaḥ pratibudhyate uta ayaḥ cityate prāptam tāvat aiyamaḥ kutas yadā jala rāśau kaścid jalabiduḥ prakṣipyate jala rāśiḥ bhavati puas uddharaṇe jalabiduḥ bhavati duḥsaṃpādam suptaḥ ekatvam saṃprasīdati puas utthātum arhati tasmāt īśvaraḥ ayaḥ jīvaḥ pratibudhyate prāpte idam jīvaḥ suptaḥ svāsthyam gataḥ puar uttiṣṭhati āyaḥ kasmāt ausmṛti vibhajya hetum darśayiṣyāmi tāvat utthātum arhati āyaḥ karmaṇaḥ aparedyus karmaṇaḥ aparedyus sāmikṛtasya karmaṇaḥ ayaḥ pravartitum utsahate atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt any pūrvedyus aparedyus karmaṇaḥ gamyate itas uttiṣṭhati kāraṇam aham adaḥ drākṣam au paścāt smaraṇam opapadyate ham asmi utthāam avagamyate puaḥ pratiyāyam pratiyoyā dravati etam lokam siṃhaḥ vṛkaḥ varāhaḥ kīṭaḥ pataṅgaḥ daṃśaḥ maśakaḥ bhavati bhavati evamādayaḥ śabdāḥ svāpa prabodha paṭhitā sāmañjasyam īyuḥ avagamyate ayathā syuḥ supta mātraḥ mucyate āpadyeta vada kim karmaṇā kṛtam yadi tāvat atare vyavaharamāṇaḥ jīvaḥ uttiṣṭhet tatratya vyavahāra lopa suptaḥ uttiṣṭhet kalpa āarthakyam yaḥ yasmi suptaḥ tasmi uttiṣṭhati suptaḥ uttiṣṭhati kaḥ uttiṣṭhet āpadyeta puas utthāam aupapaam īśvarasya utthāam pratyuktam aivṛtta avidya akṛta abhyāgama vipraṇāśau syātām tasmāt uttiṣṭhati āyaḥ puas jala rāśau jala bidurā uddhartum śakyate jīvaḥ otpatitum arhati parihriyate yuktam viveka jala bidoḥ auddharaṇam vidyate viveka kāraṇam avidyā vaiṣamyam durvivecayoḥ asmad jātīyaiḥ kṣīra udakayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ jīvaḥ vidyate yaḥ jalabiduḥ iva jalarāśeḥ vivicyeta sat upādhi saṃparkāt jīvaḥ upacaryate prapañcitam yāvat upādhi gatā tāvat vyavahāraḥ upādhi atara gatāyām jīvaḥ pratibudhyate yuktam ṛdha sampattiḥ mugdha adhikaraṇam yam mūrchitaḥ laukikāḥ kathayati kimavasthaḥ parīkṣāyām ucyate tisraḥ tāvat avasthāḥ sthasya jīvasya prasiddhāḥ jāgaritam svapaḥ suṣuptam caturthī śarīrāt apasṛptiḥ pañcamī kācid jīvasya śrutau smṛtau prasiddhā tasmāt catasṛṇām avasthāām ayatamā mūrchā prāpte brūmaḥ jāgarita avasthaḥ bhavitum arhati ayam idriyaiḥ viṣayāḥ īkṣate etat mugdhaḥ bhaviṣyati iṣukāraḥ viṣayāḥ īkṣate mugdhaḥ āyāḥ viṣayāḥ īkṣate iṣukāraḥ iṣum aham etāvatam kālam bhūvam mugdhaḥ labdha saṃjñaḥ tamasi aham etāvatam kālam prakṣiptaḥ bhūvam kiṃci mayā cetitam jāgrataḥ viṣaya viṣakta cetasaḥ dehaḥ vidhriyate mugdhasya dehaḥ dharaṇyām patati jāgarti svapā paśyati mṛtaḥ ūṣmaṇoḥ mugdhe jatau mṛtaḥ yam syāa mṛtaḥ saṃśayāḥ āsti hṛdaya deśam ālabhate iścaya usti āsti āsikā deśam yadi ūṣmaṇoḥ astitvam āvagacchati mṛtaḥ yam adhyavasāya dahaāya araṇyam ayati prāṇam ūṣmāṇam pratipadyate ayam mṛtaḥ adhyavasāya lābhāya bhiṣajyati diṣṭam gataḥ yamam gataḥ yama rāṣṭrāt pratyāgacchati tarhi suṣuptaḥ mugdhaḥ kadācid ciram occhvasiti vepathuḥ dehaḥ bhavati visphārite etre suṣuptaḥ tulya kālam puas puas ucchvasiti imīlite etre bhavataḥ dehaḥ vepate pāṇi peṣaṇa mātreṇa suṣuptam utthāpayati mugdham imitta bhedaḥ bhavati moha svāpayoḥ musala saṃpāta imitta amohasya aimitta svāpasya prasiddhiḥ mugdhaḥ suptaḥ ardha mugdha avagacchāmaḥ katham puar ardha mugdha śakyate vaktum yāvatā suptam tāvat śrutyā satā somya saṃpaaḥ bhavati atra steoḥ teo bhavati ai tam setum ahar rātre tarataḥ jarā mṛtyuḥ śokaḥ sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ityādi jīve duṣkṛtayoḥ bhavati sukhi pratyayaḥ duḥkhi pratyayaḥ suṣupte vidyate mugdhe tau pratyayau vidyete tasmāt upādhi upaśamāt kṛtsa bhavitum arhati ārdha atra ucyate brūmaḥ brūmaḥ ṛdha jīvasya brahmaṇā bhavati kim tarhi suṣupta pakṣasya bhavati mugdha brūmaḥ darśite mohasya vaiṣamye dvāram etat maraṇasya yadā avaśeṣam bhavati maase pratyāgacchataḥ yadā bhavati ūṣmāṇau apagacchataḥ tasmāt ardha saṃpattim icchati pañcamī kācid prasiddhā eṣa kādācitkīyam prasiddhā prasiddhā eṣā āyurvedayoḥ ardha saṃpatti pañcamī gaṇyate aavadyam adhikaraṇam brahmaṇā jīvaḥ upādhi upaśamāt idāīm svarūpam satī liṅgāḥ śrutayaḥ viṣayāḥ karmā kāmaḥ gadhaḥ rasaḥ evamādyāḥ liṅgāḥ asthūlam aṇu hrasvam adīrgham evamādyāḥ iḥ liṅgāḥ kim āsu śrutiṣu pratipattavyam uttāyatara yadā ayatara uta irviśeṣam mīmāṃsyate augrahāt prāpte brūmaḥ tāvat svatas brahmaṇaḥ ekam vastu svatas upetam viparītam avadhārayitum śakyam tarhi upādhi upādhi ayādṛśasya svabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati svacchaḥ sphaṭikaḥ alaktaka upādhi asvacchaḥ bhavati bhrama asvaccha abhi iva īśasya avidyā pratyupasthāpita samasta rahitam pratipattavyam viparītam pratipāda apareṣu vākyeṣu aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam evamādiṣu apāsta samasta upadiśyate cea svatas vai kasmāt pratividyam brahmaṇaḥ ākārāḥ upadiśyate catuṣpād ṣoḍaśa kalam vāmaī lakṣaṇam trailokya vaiśvāara uditam evaṃjātīyakāḥ tasmāt brahmaṇā abhyupagatavyam obhaya brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati ayam upādhi ākāra bhedasya ayathā śāstram prasajyeta brūmaḥ kasmāt atadvacaāt upādhi bhedam abhedam brahmaṇaḥ śrāvayati śāstram yaḥ ayam asyām pṛthivyām umṛta puruṣaḥ yaḥ ayam adhyātmam umṛta puruṣaḥ yam yaḥ yam ityādi bhiākāra brahmaṇaḥ śāstrīyaḥ śakyate vaktum bhedasya upāsa abhede tātparyāt bhoktā bhogyam preritāram matvā sarvam proktam trividham me samastasya bhogya iyatṛ lakṣaṇasya prapañcasya svabhāva tām katham ākāravat upadeśiīṣu ākāra upadeśiīṣu viṣayāsu śrutiṣu satīṣu ākāram avadhāryate uttaram paṭhati arūpavat ākāra rahitam avadhārayitavyam kasmāt pradhā sthūlam aṇu hrasvam adīrgham aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ atarā divyaḥ amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ ajaḥ etat aaparam aataram abāhyam ayam evamādīi vākyāi atara pradhāāi etat pratiṣṭhāpitam atra tasmāt evaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu yathāśrutam irā ākāram avadhārayitavyam itarāṇi ākāravat viṣayāṇi tāi teṣu virodhe yathāśrutam āśrayitavyam virodhe bhavati eṣa viigamaāyām hetuḥ ubhayīṣu śrutiṣu satīṣu ākāram avadhāryate puar viparītam kā tarhi ākāravat viṣayāṇām śrutīām gatiḥ prakāśavat sauraḥ ādramasaḥ vyāpya avatiṣṭhamānaḥ teṣu ṛju vakra iva pratipadyate brahmā ākāra tām iva pratipadyate ālambaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ākāra upāsa virudhyate vaiyarthyam ākāravat viṣayāṇām vākyāām bhaviṣyati veda vākyāām kasyacid kasyacid aarthavat yuktam pratipattum pramāṇa purastāt pratijñātam opādhi brahmaṇoḥ ti virudhyate brūmaḥ upādhi nimittasya vastu aupapatteḥ upādhīnām avidyā pratyupasthāpita satyām aisargikyām avidyāyām veda vyavahāra avatāraḥ avocāma ta śrutiḥ caitaya atara rahitam kṛtsaḥ rasa ghaaḥ kṛtsaḥ aghaaḥ etat bhavati āsye otar caitayādayat rūpam caitayam irataram svarūpam saidhavaghaasya lavaṇa rasaḥ irataraḥ bhavati rasātaram atho śrutiḥ ādeśaḥ eti eti ayat viditāt viditāt adhiyataḥ iva ārtate prāpya maasā evamādyā bādhvaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca śrūyate ha uvāca adhīhi bho tūṣṇīm babhūva tam ha dvitīye vacaḥ uvāca brūmaḥ khalu smṛtiṣu jñeyam pravakṣyāmi jñātvā amṛtam sattā ucyate evamādyāsu viśva dharaḥ ārāyaṇaḥ āradam uvāca eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yamām paśyasi ārada guṇaiḥ yuktam mām jñātum arhasi ayam maasa atītaḥ upadeśyaḥ upādhi nimittām apāramārthikīm viśeṣavat tām abhipretya jala upādīyate śāstreṣu ayam vivasvā apaḥ kriyate rūpaḥ devaḥ kṣetreṣu ajaḥ yam ekaḥ bhūtātmā bhūte bhūte vyavasthitaḥ ekadhā bahudhā jala cadravat evamādiṣu atra pratyavasthīyate jala tulya sūrya mūrtebhyaḥ viprakṛṣṭa deśam mūrtam jalam gṛhyate yuktaḥ sūrya pratibimba udayaḥ mūrtaḥ asmāt bhūtāḥ viprakṛṣṭa deśāḥ upādhayaḥ āaya tasmāt ayuktaḥ yam dṛṣṭātaḥ atra pratividhīyate bhāktva matarbhāvāt yuktaḥ ayam dṛṣṭātaḥ aṃśa dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ kvacid kaṃcid vivakṣitam aṃśam muktvā sārūpyam keacid darśayitum śakyate sārūpye darśa āt śrutiḥ brahmaṇaḥ upādhiṣu atarau praveśam puras cakre dvipadaḥ puras cakre catuṣpadaḥ puras pakṣī bhūtvā puras āviśat tasmāt yuktam etat tasmāt viparīta siddham atra kecid dve adhikaraṇe kalpayati prathamam tāvat kim pratyastamita aśeṣa prapañcam ākāram uta prapañcavat ākāra upetam dvitīyam pratyastamita prapañca tve kim sat lakṣaṇam uta bodha lakṣaṇam uta lakṣaṇam atra vayam vadāmaḥ āarthakyam adhikaraṇa atara ārambhasya yadi tāvat brahmaṇaḥ irā kartavyam ayam prayāsaḥ irā kṛtam uttaram adhikaraṇam prakāśavat etat vyartham bhavet bhavat sat lakṣaṇam bodha lakṣaṇam śakyam baktum ityādi katham jīvasya ātmatveā upadiśyeta bodha lakṣaṇam sat lakṣaṇam śakyam vaktum upalabdhavyaḥ ityādi katham irasta sattākaḥ bodhaḥ abhyupagamyeta āpi lakṣaṇam śakyam vaktum abhyupagama virodha sattā vyāvṛttyā bodhe bodha vyāvṛttayā sattayā upetam adhikaraṇa pratiṣiddham prapañca prasajyeta adoṣaḥ svabhāva aupapatteḥ sattā eṣa bodhaḥ bodhaḥ sattā paraspara vyāvṛttiḥ yadi ucyeta kim sat lakṣaṇam uta bodha lakṣaṇam uta lakṣaṇam ayam sūtrāṇi viṣayāsu śrutiṣu ākāre brahmaṇi parigṛhīte avaśyam vaktavyā itarāsām śrutīām gatiḥ sūtrāṇi arthavattarāṇi āhuḥ śrutayaḥ śrutayaḥ aākāra pratipatti lakṣyate katham ye paravidyā adhikāre kecid prapañcāḥ ucyate yuktāḥ harayaḥ śatā daśa ayam vai vai daśa sahasrāṇi evamādayaḥ bhavatu pravilaya etat aaparam aataram abāhyam upasaṃhārāt ye ucyate maomayaḥ śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ evamādayaḥ pravilaya kratum kurvīta evaṃjātīyake prakṛtea śrutyā evaṃjātīyakāām guṇāām lakṣaṇayā pravilaya avakalpate sādhāraṇe pravilaya tve pradhā eṣām yathopadeśam kvacid durita kṣayaḥ kvacid aiśvairya kvacid krama muktiḥ avagamyate pārthagarthyam vākyāām yāyyam ekavākyatvam katham eṣām ekavākyatā utprekṣyate vaktavyam eyoga prayāja darśa pūrṇamāsa vākyeṣu iyoga vastu paryavasāyi etat vistareṇa pratiṣṭhāpitam atra kiṃviṣayaḥ atra vaktavyam puruṣaḥ vyāpāre dvaita prapañca pravilayaḥ bhaviṣyati apravilāpite dvaita prapañce tattva ābodhaḥ bhavati tattva avabodha pratyaīka bhūtaḥ dvaita prapañcaḥ pravilāpyaḥ svarga kāmasya upadiśyate apavarga kāmasya prapañca pravilayaḥ tamasi vyavasthitam ghaṭa tattvam avabubhutsamāea pratyaīka tamaḥ pravilāpyate tattvam avabubhutsamāea pratyaīka bhūtaḥ prapañcaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ svabhāvaḥ prapañcaḥ prapañca svabhāvam tea tattva avabodhaḥ bhavati atra vayam pṛcchāmaḥ kaḥ yam prapañca pravilayaḥ kimagi pratāpa saṃparkāt ghṛta kāṭhiya pravilayaḥ iva prapañca pravilayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvit cadre avidyā kṛtaḥ brahmaṇi āma prapañcaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ yadi tāvat vidyamānaḥ ayam prapañcaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ ādhyātmikaḥ bāhyaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ ucyeta mātreṇa aśakyaḥ pravilāpayitum pravilaya uśakya viṣayaḥ pravilayaḥ kṛtaḥ idāīm abhaviṣyat avidyā adhyastaḥ brahmaṇi ayam prapañcaḥ pravilāpyate brūyāt āvedayitavyam ekam advitīyam satyam asi tasmin āvedite svayam utpadyate avidyā bādhyate avidyā adhyastaḥ sakalaḥ yam āma prapañcaḥ svapa prapañca pravilīyate āvedite kuru prapañca pravilayam prapañca pravilayaḥ jāyeta brahmaṇi prapañca pravilayaḥ jāyeta brahmaṇi avidyā adhyasta sarpa prapañca pravilayaḥ bhavati kṛtam kriyate prapañca avasthāyām prapañca pakṣasya pakṣasya vikalpe jīvasya pravilāpita kasya prapañca vilaye iyogaḥ ucyeta kasya iyoga eṣṭha mokṣaḥ uvāptavyaḥ ucyeta dvitīye aiyojya svabhāvam jīvasya svarūpam avidyā kṛtam pratipādite brahmaṇi iyojya iyoga draṣṭavya śabdāḥ paravidyā paṭhitāḥ tattva abhimukhīkaraṇa pradhāāḥ tattva avabodha pradhāāḥ bhavati idam paśya idam ākarṇaya evaṃjātīyakeṣu praṇidhā kuru ucyate jñāam kuru abhimukhasya jñāam kadācid jāyate jāyate tasmāt tam jñā viṣayaḥ darśayitavyaḥ jñāpayitu kāmaḥ tasmin darśite svayam yathāviṣayam yathāpramāṇam jñāam utpadyate pramāṇa atareṇa ayathā ṛthe ayathājñāam iyuktasya yadi ayathā jñāam kuryāt ayathā jñāam kim tarhi māasī svayam ayathā utpadyeta bhrātiḥ pramāṇa jayam viṣayam kārayitum śakyate vārayitum śakyate tatram vastu tatram iyoga kiṃca ayat iyoga eṣṭha paryavasyati māye abhyupagatam aiyojya ātmatvam jīvasya apramāṇakam śāstram aiyojya ātmatvam ācakṣīta avabodhe iyuñjīta śāstrasya dvi viruddha prasajyeyātām iyoga tāyām hāiḥ kalpaā evamādayaḥ doṣāḥ keacid parihartum śakyāḥ tasmāt vākyāi eyoga ekavākya ayuktam vākyeṣu iyoga sadbhāve ekatvam prapañca upadeśeṣu asiddham ekaḥ iyogaḥ śakyam āśrayitum prayāja darśa pūrṇamāsa vākyeṣu aṃśe yuktam ekatvam kaścid ekatva kara oṃśo bhā guṇāḥ prapañca pravilaya upakāriṇaḥ prapañca vilayaḥ bhā upakārī paraspara virodhi prapañca deśa apekṣaṇam dharmiṇi yuktam samāveśayitum tasmāt asmad uktaḥ ākāravat ākāra upadeśāām yuktataraḥ adhikaraṇam dve vāva brahmaṇaḥ rūpe mūrtam amūrtam upakramya mahābhūtāi pravibhajya amūrta rasasya uditasya rūpāṇi darśayitvā puas paṭhyate ādeśaḥ eti eti etasmāt eti ayat kaḥ pratiṣedhasya viṣayaḥ jijñāsāmahe atra idam viśeṣitam kiṃcid pratiṣedhyam atra pratiṣedhyam kim samarpyate eti paratvāt añ prayogasya ayam saṃihita ālambaḥ evaṃśabda sama ha sma upādhyāyaḥ kathayati evamādiṣu saṃihitam atra dvayam prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ yasya dve rūpe saṃśayaḥ upajāyate kim ayam pratiṣedhaḥ rūpe ubhayam āhosvit ekataram yadā ekataram kim rūpe pariśiaṣṭi āhosvit rūpe pariśiaṣṭi ubhayam āśaṅkāmahe dvau etau pratiṣedhau dvis eti prayogāt tayoḥ prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam pratiṣidhyate apareṇa bhavati matiḥ athavā pratiṣidhyate arham prapañcaḥ gocara arhaḥ abhyāsaḥ prāpte brūmaḥ tāvat pratiṣedhaḥ śūya vāda kaṃcid paramārtham ālambya aparamārthaḥ pratiṣidhyate rajju sarpa pariśiṣyamāṇe kasmiṃścid avakalpate koyaḥ pariśiṣyeta pariśiṣyamāṇe yaḥ pratiṣeddhum ārabhyate pratiṣeddhum aśakya paramārtha aupapattiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ bravāṇi ityādi upakrama asaḥ bhavati veda ityādi idā upalabdhavyaḥ ityādi avadhāraṇa veda atavya ākopa brahmaṇaḥ abhiprāyeṇa abhidhīyate mahatā satyam evamādiāḥ pratipādya paṅkasya dūrāt asparśaam varam pratipāda prakriyā eṣā ṛtate prāpya etat bhavati aśuddha buddha svabhāvam tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ prapañcam avagatavyam etat ucyate etāvattvam prakṛtam mūrta amūrta lakṣaṇam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam eṣa prakṛtam prapañcitam pūrvasmin rathe adhidaivatam adhyātmam jaitam aparam rūpam amūrta rasa uditam vyapāśrayam māhāraja upamābhiḥ darśitam amūrta rasasya puruṣasya grāhya yogi aupapatteḥ etat prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam pratiṣedhakam upaīyate gamyate tvea ṣaṣṭhyā prapañcite tadīye dvaye rūpavataḥ jijñāsāyām idam upakrātam ādeśaḥ eti eti brahmaṇaḥ āspadam idam samastam eti eti pratiṣiddham yuktam kāryasya brahmaṇaḥ kalpa atra iyam āśaṅkā kartavyā katham śāstram svayam brahmaṇaḥ dvayam darśayitvā svayam puas paṅkasya dūrāt asparśaam varam brahmaṇaḥ dvayam irdiśati prasiddham idam dvayam brahmaṇi kalpitam parāmṛśati pratiṣedhya tvāya śuddhabrahma pratipādaāya dvau etau pratiṣedhau dve mūrta amūrte pratiṣedhataḥ pūrvaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ rāśim uttaraḥ asaā rāśim athavā eti eti vīpsā iyam yāvat kiṃcid utprekṣyate sarvam bhavati parigaṇita pratiṣedhe kriyamāṇe yadi kim ayat bhavet vīpsāyām satyām samastasya viṣaya jātasya aviṣayaḥ pratyagātmā iva ārtate tasmāt prapañcam brahmaṇi kalpitam pariśiaṣṭi itas eṣaḥ prapañca ayat pratiṣedhe kriyamāṇe kim ayat brūyāt eṣā eti eti ādiśya tam ādeśam puariḥ vakti eti eti kaḥ ṛthaḥ etasmāt brahmaṇaḥ vyatiriktam eti eti ucyate svayam āsti ayatparam apratiṣiddham yadā puar akṣarāṇi yojyate etasmāt aiti prapañca rūpāt ādeśaāt brahmaṇaḥ etat āmadheya viṣayam yojayitavyam āmadheya satyasya satyam vai satyam eṣa satyam brahmāvasāe pratiṣedhe bhavati abhāvāvasāe pratiṣedhe kim satyasya satyam ucyeta tasmāt brahmāvasāaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ ābhāvāvasāaḥ adhyavasyāmaḥ pratiṣiddhāt prapañca jātāt ayat kasmai gṛhyate ucyate avyakta maidriya grāhyam dṛśya sākṣi śrutiḥ cakṣuṣā gṛhyate vācā āyaiḥ devaiḥ tapasā karmaṇā vāsaḥ eṣaḥ eti eti gṛhyaḥ gṛhyate dreśyam grāhyam yadā eṣa ityādyā smṛtiḥ avyaktaḥ yam acityaḥ yam avikāryaḥ yam ucyate ityādyā saṃrādhae saṃrādha kāle paśyati saṃrādha am katham katham katham katham saṃrādha kāle paśyati vyatṛṇat svayaṃbhūḥ tasmāt parāṅ paśyati kaścid dhīraḥ aikṣat āvṛtta icche viśuddha sattvaḥ tam paśyate evamādyā smṛtiḥ ye viidrāḥ jita śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ saṃyata idriyāḥ paśyati yoga ātmae amaḥ yogiaḥ tam prapaśyati bhagavatam evamādyāḥ saṃrādhya saṃrādhaka apara ātmaoḥ aya ucyate savitṛ prabhṛtayaḥ aṅguli karaka udaka prabhṛtiṣu karmasu upādhi viśeṣāḥ iva avabhāsate svābhāvikīm ātmatām jahati upādhi imittaḥ ayam bhedaḥ svatas aikātmyam prājñayoḥ abhedaḥ pratipādyate svābhāvika abhedasya avidyā bhedasya avidyām vidhūya jīvaḥ prājñea ekatām gacchati yaḥ ha vai paramam veda bhavati brahmā apyeti ityādi tasmin saṃrādhya saṃrādhaka matātaram upayasyati mata viśuddhaye kvacid prājñayoḥ bhedaḥ tam paśyate dhyātṛ dhyātavya tvea draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya tvea parātparam upaiti divyam bhūtāyataraḥ yamayati kvacid tayoḥ abhedaḥ asi aham asmi eṣa ataraḥ eṣa ataryāmī amṛtaḥ vyapadeśe yadi abhedaḥ ātataḥ gṛhyate darśaāt atra tattvam bhavitum arhati ahiḥ abhedaḥ bhedaḥ athavā etat pratipattavyam sāvitraḥ āśrayaḥ savitā bhājau bhavataḥ upayastam etat bhavitum arhati avidyā badhasya mokṣaḥ yadi puas paramārthataḥ baddhaḥ kaścid deśa bhūtaḥ abhyupagamyeta pāramārthikasya badhasya tiraskartum aśakya vaiyarthyam prasajyeta atra ubhau abhedau śrutiḥ tulya vyapadiśati abhedam bhedam prasiddham āvadati atara vivakṣayā tasmāt eṣaḥ siddhātaḥ itas eṣaḥ siddhātaḥ yatkāraṇam parasmāt ātmaoyam śāstram draṣṭā evamādi ādeśaḥ eti eti etat aaparam aataram abāhyam vyatirikta prapañcaiḥ ākaraṇāt eṣaḥ gamyate etat asmāt ayat tattvam āsti vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kāicid vākyāi brahmaṇaḥ ayat tattvam pratipādayati iva parihāram abhidhātum ayam upakramaḥ kriyate umāa sambadha brahmaṇaḥ ayat tattvam bhavitum arhati kutas umāa saṃbadha tāvat yaḥ setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ abhihitasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃkīrtayati jala saṃtā viccheda kare mṛd dāru pracaye prasiddhaḥ prayuktaḥ laukika setoḥ iva setoḥ rayasya vastu ostitvam gamayati tarati prayogāt laukikam setum tītrvā jāṅgalam asetum setum tītrvā setum gamyate umā bhavati etat catuṣpād aṣṭāśapham ṣoḍaśa kalam idam paricchiam kārṣāpaṇa vastu prasiddham brahmaṇā upi umāāt vastuā bhavitavyam gamyate bhavati satā somya saṃpaaḥ bhavati arāṇām agareṇa jīvāām brahmaṇā vyapadiśati suṣuptau gamyate eam gamayati yaḥ eṣa utarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ ādhāram īśvaram vyapadiśya akṣi ādhāram īśvaram vyapadiśati yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ atideśam karoti etasya rūpam amuṣya rūpam yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau avadhikam īśvara vyapadiśati ye amuṣmāt parāñcaḥ lokāḥ iṣṭe kāmāām ye etasmāt arvāñcaḥ lokāḥ iṣṭe idam māgadhasya rājyam idam vaidehasya etebhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ prāpte pratipādyate tuśabde pradarśitām prāptim pradarśitām prāptim brahmaṇaḥ kiṃcid bhavitum arhati pramāṇa kiṃcid pramāṇam upalabhāmahe sarvasya jaimataḥ vastu jātasya brahmaṇaḥ bhavati kāraṇāt kāryasya vyatiriktam kiṃcid ajam saṃbhavati sat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam sarvavijñāa pratijñāāt vyatirikta vastu astitvam avakalpate vyapadeśāḥ vyatiriktam tattvam sūcayati ucyate tāvat brahmaṇaḥ bāhyasya sadbhāvam pratipādayitum kṣamate setuḥ kim kalpyeta etat yāyyam haṭhaḥ aprasiddha kalpaā bāhya vastu tām prasañjayatā mṛd dāru maya prāsaṅkṣyata aja setusāmāyāt prayuktaḥ śliṣyate vidhāraka setusāmāyam ātman setuḥ iva setuḥ prakṛtaḥ stūyate setum tītrvā taratiḥ atikrama vartate vyākaraṇam tīrṇaḥ prāptaḥ ucyate atikrātaḥ umā abhidhīyate umā vyatirikta vastu astitva pratipatti kimarthaḥ tarhi upāsa yāvat catuṣpād aṣṭāśapham ṣoḍaśakalam evaṃrūpā buddhiḥ katham brahmaṇi sthirā dvāreṇa brahmaṇaḥ kriyate brahmaṇi sarvaiḥ puṃbhiḥ śakyā buddhiḥ sthāpayitum mada madhyama uttama puṃsām maa ākāśayoḥ adhyātmam adhidaivatam pratīkayoḥ āmātayoḥ catvāraḥ pādāḥ kalpyate catvāraḥ agi saṃbadhiḥ athavā kārṣāpaṇe vyavahāra prācuryāya kalpyate sarvadā vyavahartum īśate kraya vikraye sthā sūtre dvayoḥ parihāraḥ abhidhīyate saṃbadha sthā etau vyapadeśau upapadyete saṃbadha vyapadeśe tāvat ayam upādhi sthā udbhūtasya vijñāasya upādhi upaśame yaḥ upaśamaḥ paramātmā upādhi upacaryate parimita brahmaṇaḥ upādhi upacaryate prakāśasya sauryasya ādramasasya upādhi upajāta viśeṣasya upādhi upaśamāt bhavati upādhi sūcī pāśa upādhi etau saṃbadha vyapadeśau bhavataḥ atra īdṛśaḥ saṃbadhaḥ svam itas bhavati saṃbadha apāyi ghaṭate upādhi tirobhāvāt svam itas bhavati bhedaḥ saṃbhavati bahutara īśvara śrutiḥ ākāśasya vyapadeśam upapādayati yaḥ yam bahirdhā puruṣāt yaḥ yam puruṣaḥ yaḥ yam hṛdaye tathāya vyapadeśā saṃprati pakṣam atareṇa upasaṃharati tathāya pratiṣedhā brahmaṇaḥ vastu ataram gamyate adhastāt aham adhastāt adhastāt sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ aḥ sarvam veda idam sarvam idam sarvam eha kiṃca yasmāt aparam kiṃcid etat aaparam aataram abāhyam evamādīi vākyāi sthāi pariṇetum aśakyāi vyatiriktam vastu ataram vārayati sarvātara atarātmā avagamyate siddham bhavati ayathā sidhyet vyapadeśeṣu mukhyeṣu aṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu paricchedaḥ ātmaaḥ prasajyeta ādīām vastu vastu atarāt vyāvartate paricchedaḥ ātmaaḥ prasajyeta avagamyate vacaḥ ayam tāvai eṣa utar hṛdaye gataḥ ityaḥ jyāyāt ivaḥ jyāyā ākāśāt ityaḥ gataḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ yam evamādayaḥ yāyāḥ uvabodhayati adhikaraṇam brahmaṇaḥ vyāvahārikyām īśitṛ īśitavya vibhāga avasthāyām ayam ayaḥ svabhāvaḥ varṇyate etat vyāmiśra lakṣaṇam gocaram trividham prasiddham jatūām kim etat karmaṇaḥ bhavati āhosvit īśvarāt bhavati vicāraṇā tāvat pratipādyate īśvarāt bhavitum arhati kutas adhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhārāḥ vidadhat deśa kāla abhijña karmiṇām aurūpam saṃpādayati karmaṇaḥ kāla atara bhavati aupapaam autpatteḥ etat viaśyat kālam svāurūpam viaśyati kāla ātaritam kartrā bhokṣyate pariśudhyati saṃbadhāt aupapatteḥ yatkālam sukham duḥkham ātmaā bhujyate prasiddham asaṃbaddhasya sukhasya duḥkhasya laukikāḥ ucyeta mā utpādaḥ kāryāt apūrvāt utpatsyate opapadyate apūrvasya acetaasya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samasya cetaeā pravartitasya pravṛtti aupapatteḥ astitve pramāṇa arthāpattiḥ pramāṇam īśvara arthāpatti kṣayāt kevalam īśvaram hetum kalpayāmaḥ kim tarhi īśvaram hetum śrutiḥ bhavati vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ vasudāaḥ evaṃjātīyakāḥ jaimiiḥ jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ phalasya dātāram hetoḥ śrūyate tāvat ayam svarga kāmaḥ yajeta evamādiṣu vākyeṣu viṣaya upagamāt yāgaḥ svargasya utpādakaḥ gamyate ayathā aauṣṭhātṛkaḥ yāgaḥ āpadyeta vaiyarthyam karmaṇaḥ opapadyate parityaktaḥ iyam pakṣaḥ eṣa prāmāṇyāt śrutiḥ pramāṇam ayam śrutaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ autpādya kim karmaṇaḥ sūkṣmā kācid phalasya tarkyate ayam prakāreṇa īśvaraḥ dadāti aupapam avicitrasya kāraṇasya vicitra aupapatteḥ airghṛṇya auṣṭhā avaiyarthya tasmāt dharmāt ācāryaḥ īśvaram hetum kevalāt karmaṇaḥ apūrvāt kevalāt ayam pakṣaḥ tuśabdena vyāvartyate apekṣāt apekṣāt īśvarāt siddhātaḥ kutas adharmayoḥ kārayitṛ tve īśvaraḥ hetuḥ phalasya dātṛ tve eṣa sādhu kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ uiīṣate eṣaḥ asādhu kārayati tam yam adhas ayam bhagavadgītāsu yaḥ yaḥ yām yām taum bhaktaḥ śraddhayā arcitum icchati acalām śraddhām tām vidadhāmi aham śraddhayā yuktaḥ ārādhaam īhate labhate kāmāḥ mayā ahitāḥ īśvara hetukāḥ sṛṣṭayaḥ īśvarasya aurūpāḥ prajāḥ sṛjati doṣāḥ prayata īśvarasya prasajyate śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ vedāta coda vedāta adhikaraṇam tasmin tasmin bhavitum arhati kutas coda abheda hetavaḥ ākṛṣyate saṃyoga coda ākhyā prayataḥ tādṛśaḥ codyate juhuyāt yaḥ ha vai jyeṣṭham śreṣṭham veda vājasaeyiām chadogāām tādṛśī jyeṣṭhaḥ bhavati rūpam ubhayatra uta jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha āvitam tattvam dravya devate yāgasya rūpam vijñeyam rūpam vijñāasya rūpyate samākhyā tasmāt vedāta vijñāāām pañcāgi vaiśvāara śāṇḍilya evamādiṣu yojayitavyam ye āma hetvābhāsāḥ ārabhya parihṛtāḥ kaṃcid āśaṅkya pariharati etat vijñāāām vājasaeyiḥ pañcāgi vidyām prastutya ṣaṣṭham aparam agim āmaati āgiḥ āgiḥ bhavati ādiā chadogāḥ tam saṃkhyayā upasaṃharati ha yaḥ etā pañcāgī vedaḥ yeṣām guṇaḥ usti yeṣām katham ubhayeṣām ekā upapadyeta atra śakyate pratyetum saṃvāde caturaḥ śrotra maāṃsi chadogāḥ āmaati vājasaeyiḥ pañcamam āmaati vai prajāpatiḥ prajāyate ha prajayā paśubhiḥ yaḥ veda āvāpa udvāpa vedya bhedaḥ bhavati vedya bhedaḥ dravya iva yāgasya eṣa evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhedaḥ yadi ṣaṣṭhasya āgeḥ saṃbhavati ubhayatra bhedaḥ bhavitum arhati ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ atirātraḥ bhidyate paṭhyate chadogaiḥ tam pretam diṣṭam itas gayaḥ harati vājasaeyiḥ sāṃpādikeṣu pañcasu agiṣu auvṛttāyāḥ samidh dhūma kalpaāyāḥ samidh samidh ityādi samāmaati upāsa eṣa guṇaḥ śakyate chadogaiḥ upasaṃhartum chadogaiḥ upasaṃhartum atra āśaṅkyaḥ sāṃpādikā āgi abhiprāyā eṣā āuvāda bhūtā samavāyiī adoṣaḥ saṃvāda adhikasya guṇasya virudhyate āvāpa udvāpa vedya bhedaḥ bhedaḥ āśaṅkyaḥ kasyacid vedya aṃśasya āvāpa udvāpayoḥ bhūyasaḥ vedya rāśeḥ abheda avagamāt tasmāt aikavidyam samācāra taiyamaḥ ātharvaṇikāām vidyām vrata apekṣaṇāt apekṣaṇāt bhedaḥ pratyucyate eṣa dharmaḥ vidyāyāḥ katham idam avagamyate veda vrata ātharvaṇikāḥ idam adhikṛta viṣayāt etad adhyaya upaiṣadadhyayaa dharmaḥ eṣaḥ auteṣām etām vidyām vadeta śirovratam vidhivat yaiḥ cīrṇam saṃyoga ekā saṃkīryeta eṣa dharmaḥ etām pratyavamarśāt vidyāyāḥ gratha gratha saṃyogī eṣa dharmaḥ taiyamaḥ savāḥ saurya śata oda paryatāḥ ātharvaṇa udita ekāgī abhisaṃbadhāt iyamyate ayam dharmaḥ svādhyāya saṃbadhāt tasmāt aavadyam ekatvam vedaḥ upi ekatvam vedya ekatva vedāḥ padam āmaati etam bahvṛcāḥ mahati ukthe mīmāṃsate etam agau adhvaryavaḥ etam mahāvrate chadogāḥ bhayam vajram udyatam kāṭhake uktasya īśvara guṇasya bhaya tvasya taittirīyake yadā eṣa kurute bhayam bhavati bhayam vājasaeyake prādeśa saṃpāditasya vaiśvāarasya chādogye siddha upādāam yaḥ etam prādeśa abhivimāam ātmāam vaiśvāaram upāste ayatra upāsaa vidhāāt upādāt adhikaraṇam idam vedāta tve vijñāāām ayatra uditāām vijñāa guṇāām ayatra samāe vijñāe bhavati yaḥ guṇāām ekatra vijñā upakāraḥ ayatra ubhayatra ekam vijñāam tasmāt śeṣāṇām agihotra dharmāṇām ekam agihotra upasaṃharaṇam yadi vijñā abhedaḥ bhavet prakṛti vikṛti vijñā aikatve aivam prapañcaḥ ārabhya bhaviṣyati ayathātvam iā ayathātva adhikaraṇam vājasaeyake ha devāḥ ūcuḥ hata asura yajñe udgīthe atyayāma ha vācam ūcuḥ udgāye prakramya parigrahaḥ paṭhyate ha imam āsayam prāṇam ūcuḥ udgāya tebhyaḥ eṣa udagāyat chādogye pitat ha devāḥ udgītham ājahruḥ abhibhaviṣyāmaḥ prakramya parigrahaḥ paṭhyate ha yaḥ ayam mukhyaḥ tam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire ubhayatra praśaṃsayā adhyavasīyate saṃśayaḥ kim atra bhedaḥ āhosvit ekatvam kim tāvat prāptam pūrveṇa ekatvam au yuktam ekatvam prakrama ayathā prakramate vājasaeyiḥ ayathā chadogāḥ udgāya vājasaeyia udgīthasya chadogāḥ udgītha tveatam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire katham ekatvam eṣa etāvatā viśeṣeṇa apagacchati aviśeṣasya bahutarasya asura saṃgrāma upakrama asura atyaya abhiprāyaḥ udgītha upayāsaḥ saṃkīrtaam vīryāt asura vidhvaṃsaam bahavaḥ ṛthāḥ ubhayatra aviśiṣṭāḥ pratīyate vājasaeyake udgītha sāma ādhikaraṇyam prāṇasya eṣaḥ vai udgīthaḥ tasmāt chādogye lakṣayitavyam tasmāt atra yāyyam bhedaḥ atra yāyyaḥ kasmāt prakrama prakrama bhedaḥ chādogye tāvat om etat udgītham upāsīta udgītha avayavasya oṃkārasya upāsya prastutya rasatama upavyākhyāam kṛtvā khalu etasya akṣarasya upavyākhyāam bhavati tam udgītha avayavam oṃkāram asura ākhyāyikā dvāreṇa tamprāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire yadi udgītha śabdena anuprāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire yadi udgītha śabdena anuprāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire yad sakalā bhaktiḥ abhipreyeta tasyāḥ udgātā ṛtvij upakramaḥ uparudhyeta lakṣaṇā prasajyeta upakrama tatreṇa vākye upasaṃhāreṇa bhavitavyam tasmāt atra tāvat udgītha avayave oṃkāre upadiśyate vājasaeyake avayava grahaṇe sakalā bhaktiḥ āvedyate udgāye tasyāḥ udgātā ṛtvij prasthāātaram udgītha sāmāādhikaraṇyam prāṇasya udgātṛ tve didarśayiṣitasya prāṇasya pratipāda ekatvam āvahati sakala bhakti viṣaye udgītha vaiṣamyam prāṇasya udgātṛ parityajyate udgītha udgātṛ bhāvasya upāsa tvea upadiśyamāa vīryeṇa udgātā audgātram karoti śrāvitam vācā prāṇe udagāyat chāyā okāra mātreṇa yuktam abhyudaya vākye paśu vākye tredhā dātre puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam kuryāt ityādi irdeśa sāmye upakrama abhyudaya vākye paśu vākye yāga upakrama bhedaḥ paramātma adhyāsa sāmye ebhyaḥ jyāyāḥ parāyaṇam eṣa paras varīyāḥ udgīthaḥ eṣaḥ viśiṣṭam udgītha upāsaam akṣi gata hiraṇya śmaśru udgītha upāsaāt śākhāyām śākhātara stheṣu evaṃjātīyakeṣu upāsaeṣu any ucyeta atra yāyyam ekā opapadyate etat varīyaḥ atra yāyyataram augatam bāhyam udgītha laukikaiḥ vyavahartṛbhiḥ upacaryate etat bhedeṣu udgītha bhedāām agihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīām kāṭhaka gratha paripaṭhitāām kāṭhaka bhaviṣyati āsti kaścid evaṃjātīyakaḥ hetuḥ bhavatu saṃvarga vyāptyā adhikaraṇam om etat udgītham upāsīta atra udgītha śabdayoḥ sāmāādhikaraṇye śrūyamāṇe adhyāsa apavāda ekatva pakṣāṇām pratibhāsaāt katamaḥ utra pakṣaḥ yāyyaḥ vicāraḥ dvayoḥ vastuoḥ dvayoḥ vastuoḥ evartitāyām ayatara buddhau buddhiḥ adhyasyate tasmi buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhiḥ adhyasta buddhau adhyasta buddhau buddhau adhyasyamāāyām āma buddhiḥ buddhyā iva ṛtate pratimā viṣṇu adhyāsaḥ akṣare udgītha buddhiḥ adhyasyeta udgīthe buddhiḥ kasmiṃścid vastui mithyā buddhau paścāt upajāyamāā yathārthā buddhiḥ bhavati idriya saṃghāte buddhiḥ ātmayā iva buddhyā diś bhrāti buddhiḥ diś yāthātmya buddhyā buddhyā udgītha buddhiḥ iva ṛtyeta udgītha buddhyā buddhiḥ ekatvam udgītha śabdayoḥ aatirikta vṛtti dvijottamaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhūmidevaḥ viśeṣaṇam om etasya akṣarasya grahaṇa prasaṅge audgātra viśeṣasya samarpaṇam īlam utpalam āaya udgīthaḥ yaḥ oṃkāraḥ tam upāsīta etasmin sāmāādhikaraṇya vākye pakṣāḥ pratibhāti āyatamaiḥ aiḥ prāptau idam ucyate caśabdaḥ ūyam tuśabda sthā aiveśī trayaḥ pakṣāḥ sāvadyāḥ paryudasyate pakṣaḥ ekaḥ iḥ avadyaḥ upādīyate adhyāse tāvat yā buddhiḥ adhyasyate āvṛtti prasajyeta kalpyeta śrūyate āpayitā ha vai bhavati ityādi aya āpti odgītha adhyāsa apavāde mithyājñā ai upayoga avagamāt kadācid oṃkārāt okāra buddhiḥ iva rteta udgīthāt udgītha buddhiḥ idam vākyam vastu tattva pratipāda aparam ekatva pakṣaḥ saṃgacchate dvaya uccāraṇam samarpaṇāt hautra viṣaye ādhvaryava viṣaye akṣare oṃkāra vācye udgītha prasiddhiḥ sakalāyām sāmaḥ dvitīyāyām bhaktau udgītha vācyāyām oṃkāra prasiddhiḥ pakṣaḥ parigṛhyate veda sādhāraṇyāt vyāpi mā udgītha viśeṣyate katham udgītha avayava bhūtaḥ oṃkāraḥ gṛhyeta pakṣe lakṣaṇā udgītha avayava satyam etat lakṣaṇāyām saṃikarṣa viprakarṣau bhavataḥ adhyāsa pakṣe arthātara buddhiḥ arthātare viprakṛṣṭā lakṣaṇā pakṣe avayavaḥ samarpyate saṃikṛṣṭā samudāyeṣu pravṛttāḥ śabdāḥ avayaveṣu dṛṣṭāḥ hetoḥ om etat etasya audgītham etat viśeṣaṇam etat ayatra abheda adhikaraṇam saṃvāde śraiṣṭhya āvitasya prāṇasya upāsya vasiṣṭha āvitāḥ uktāḥ guṇāḥ prāṇe puas pratyarpitāḥ vai aham vasiṣṭha asmi vasiṣṭhaḥ usi ityādiā ayeṣām saṃvādeṣu ha vai devatāḥ ahaṃśreyase evaṃjātīyakeṣu prāṇasya śraiṣṭhyam vasiṣṭha guṇāḥ uktāḥ saṃśayaḥ kim vasiṣṭha guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ uta āsyera eti prāptam tāvat āsyera eti kutas evaṃśabda saṃyogāt yaḥ vidvā prāṇe iḥśreyasam viditvā vedyam vastu iva idyate evaṃśabdaḥ saṃihita avalambaḥ śākhātara paripaṭhitam evaṃjātīyakam jātam śakoti ivedayitum tasmāt sthaiḥ guṇaiḥ iḥ ākāṅkṣa prāpte pratyāha ire guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ vasiṣṭha ayatra kutas ekam vijñāam abhiam pratyabhijñāyate saṃvāda sārūpyāt abhede vijñāasya katham guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ evaṃśabdaḥ evaṃjātīyakam jātam vedya tvāya samarpayati atra ucyate yadi vājasaeyi brāhmaṇa gatam jātam saṃśabditam saṃihita tasmin vijñāe vājasaeyi brāhmaṇa gatam evaṃśabditam saṃśabditam śākhā gatam jātam śākhā gatāt viśiṣyate bhavati kecid śrūyate teṣu saṃśayaḥ kimāat dharmāḥ yāvataḥ śrūyate tāvataḥ pratipattavyāḥ kim yathāśruti vibhāgam prāptāyām idam ucyate brahmaṇaḥ dharmāḥ pratipattavyāḥ kasmāt ekam viśeṣyam bhidyate tasmāt sārvatrika dharmāṇām priyaśiraḥ dharmāḥ saṃkīryera taittirīyake āada mayam aam prakramya āmāyate priyam modaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ pramodaḥ uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ āadaḥ puccham pratiṣṭhā uttaram paṭhati ādīām dharmāṇām taittirīyake yatkāraṇam priyam modaḥ pramodaḥ paraspara bhoktratara upacita apacita rūpā saṃbhavataḥ ekam advitīyam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ priyaśiraḥ dharmāḥ kośa dharmāḥ upadiṣṭam asmābhiḥ atra parasmi brahmaṇi parikalpyate draṣṭavya tve sutarām ayatra dharmān dharmān ācāryeṇa pradarśitam priyaśiraḥ dharmeṣu etavyaḥ saṃyat vāma satyakāma teṣu upāsyasya brahmaṇaḥ ekatve prakrama abhede ayoya dharmāṇām dve āryau ekam ṛpatim upāsāte chatreṇa ayā cāmareṇa ayā upāsya tve upāsa abhedaḥ vyavasthā bhavati upacita apacita vyavahāre saguṇe brahmaṇi parasmin brahmaṇi ādīām dharmāṇām kvacid śrutāām sāmāyāt dharmāḥ pratipāda ucyamāāḥ sāmāyāt pratipādyasya brahmaṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ ekatvāt pratīyera eti vaiṣamyam pratipatti prayojaāḥ ādhyāāya prayojaā ādhyāādhikaraṇam kāṭhake paṭhyate idriyebhyaḥ parāḥ bahuṣu artheṣu bhedaḥ bahutva bahūyā iva prabhavati bahūarthā paratva pratipādayitum tasmāt eṣām paratva pratipādaam prāpte brūmaḥ puruṣaḥ ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pratipādyate yuktam eṣām kasmāt prayojaa itareṣu kiṃcid prayojaam śrūyate puruṣe idriya śrutiḥ icāyya mukhāt pramucyate kāṣṭhā viṣayam ādaram darśaya pratipatti apara pravāha uktiḥ ādhyāāya samyak darśaāya samyak darśa ādhyāam upadiśyate ādhyāam pradhāam itas pratipatti iyam idriya pravāha uktiḥ yatkāraṇam eṣa sarveṣu gūḍha utmā prakāśate agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ prakṛtam vivakṣitam gamyate durvijñāa tām saṃskṛta mati gamya tām vijñāāya yacchet maasī vidadhāti āumāikam atra prakāraḥ āśaya atiśayaḥ puruṣe lakṣyate etareṣu viṣṇoḥ paramam padam ukte kim adhvaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam asyām ākāṅkṣāyām parama pada pratipatti ayam āmāyaḥ avasīyate gṛhīti adhikaraṇam aitareyake śrūyate idam ekaḥ agre āsīt kiṃca miṣat īkṣata lokāḥ sṛjai imān lokāḥ asṛjata ambhaḥ marīcīḥ maramā apaḥ ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim śabdena abhilapyate uta ayaḥ kaścid kim tāvat prāptam paramātmā abhilapyaḥ bhavitum arhati kasmāt vākyāvaya darśaāt vākyāvayaḥ sutarām paramātma viṣayaḥ utpatteḥ ekatva īkṣaṇa sraṣṭṛ vacaāt ucyate sṛṣṭi vacaāt sraṣṭari parigṛhyamāṇe mahābhūta ādau vaktavyā ādau ucyate lokāḥ mahābhūta saṃiveśa viśeṣāḥ ambhaḥ prabhṛtī tve apareṇa keacid īśvareṇa kriyata smṛtyoḥ śrutiḥ bhavati idam agre āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ ityādyā smṛtiḥ vai śarīrī prathamaḥ vai puruṣaḥ ucyate ādikartā bhūtāām agre samavartata aitareyiṇaḥ retasaḥ prajāpateḥ devāḥ atra pūrvasmi prakaraṇe prajāpati kartṛkām vicitrām sṛṣṭim āmaati idam agre āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ atra ekatva avadhāraṇam utpatteḥ īkṣaṇam ceta gām āayat śvam āayat āayat abruve evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyāḥ viśeṣaḥ laukikeṣu viśeṣavatsu ātmasu prasiddhaḥ tasmāt viśeṣavān kaścid prāpte brūmaḥ gṛhyate itareṣu sṛṣṭi śravaṇeṣu tasmāt vai etasmāt saṃbhūtaḥ evamādiṣu grahaṇam itarasmin laukika prayoge pratyagātmā mukhyaḥ gṛhyate bhavitum arhati idam agre āsīt evamādau puruṣavidhaḥ evamādi ātaram śrūyate bhavet viśeṣavataḥ grahaṇam atra puaḥ viśeṣaṇam uttaram īkṣata lokāḥ sṛjā imān llokāḥ asṛjata evamādi tasmāt grahaṇam yāyyam avayāt avaya darśaāt paramātma grahaṇam parihartavyam atra ucyate bhavet upapaam paramātmanaḥ grahaṇam kasmāt paramātma grahaṇe utpatteḥ ekatva avadhāraṇam āñjasam avakalpate ayathā aāñjasam parikalpyeta sṛṣṭi vacaam atara mahābhūta sṛṣṭi aataram yojayiṣyāmi sṛjataḥ etat atara vāyu sṛṣṭi aataram ayūyujam atara prasiddhaḥ viśeṣaḥ atareṣu upasaṃhartavyaḥ bhavati yaḥ ayam evamādiḥ avadhāraṇa āuguṇyeā grahītavyaḥ ayam sakalaḥ kathā prabadhaḥ vivakṣitaḥ śakyate vaktum vivakṣitam ambhaḥ prabhṛtīām lokāām lokapālāām sṛṣṭim śiṣṭvā upadiśya sraṣṭā katham vidam mat ṛte vīkṣya idam praviveśa etam sīmāam vidārya etayā dvārā prāpadyata vācā abhivyāhṛtam yadi prāṇe abhiprāṇitam evamādiā karaṇa vivecaa pūrvakam kaḥ ham vīkṣyase etam tatamam apaśyat ātmatva darśaam avadhārayati upariṣṭāt eṣa eṣaḥ idraḥ ityādiā samastam jātam mahābhūtaiḥ aukramya sarvam prajñāetram prajñāe pratiṣṭhitam prajñāetraḥ lokaḥ pratiṣṭhā prajñāam ātmatva darśaam avadhārayati tasmāt aapavādam aparā vājasaeyaka ikatamaḥ vijñā prāṇeṣu puruṣaḥ śabdena upakramya ātmatām avadhārayati upasaṃharati vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ajaroma romṛta ubhayaḥ chādogye tusat somya idam agre āsīt ekam advitīyam atareṇa upakramya asi tādātmyam upadiśati saṃśayaḥ tulya ārthatvam atulya ārthatvam atulya ārthatvam tāvat prāptam atulya āmāayoḥ sāmyam yuktam pratipattum vājasaeyake tattva gamyate chādogye upakrama chadogāām udarke tādātmya satyam upakrama upasaṃhārasya tādātmya prāpte abhidhīyate sat somya idam agre āsīt atra chadogāām bhavitum arhati katamaḥ atra vājasaeyiām kasmāt upakrama āvayāt upakrame kaḥ parihāraḥ abhidhīyate bhavet ye āśrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam sarvavijñāam avadhārya saṃpipādayiṣayā asadevaḥ gṛhītau satyām ayathā yaḥ yam mukhyaḥ vijñātaḥ sarvavijñāam saṃpadyeta utpatteḥ ekatva ādhāraṇam jīvasya svāpa avasthāyām paricoda pūrvakam puas puas tattvam asi avadhāraṇam sarvam etat tādātmya pratipāda āyām avakalpate tādātmya saṃpāda āyām atra upakrama tatratva upayāsaḥ yāyyaḥ upakrame sāmāya upakramaḥ gate viśeṣeṇa
