pratipādya abheda siddham ākhyā ākhyā adhikaraṇam chadogāḥ vājasaeyiaḥ saṃvāde śva maryādam prāṇasya vāsaḥ āmaati chadogāḥ tasmāt vai etat śiṣyataḥ purastāt upariṣṭāt adbhiḥ paridadhati vidvāṃsaḥ śrotriyāḥ śiṣyataḥ ācāmati aśitvā ācāmati etam aamaagam tasmāt evaṃvid śiṣya ācāmet aśitvā ācāmet etam aamaagam kurute prāṇasya pratīyate kim ubhayam vidhīyate uta vicāryate kim tāvat prāptam ubhayam vidhīyate kutas ubhayasya ubhayam etat arham athavā ācamaam vidhīyate vispaṣṭā tasmāt evaṃvid śiṣya ācāmet aśitvā ācāmet prāpte brūmaḥ vidheya ākhyāāt prāptam idam prāyatyā prasiddham avākhyāyate iyam śrutiḥ tasyāḥ mūlam ucyate viṣaya āātvāt sāmāya viṣayā smṛtiḥ saṃbaddham prāyatyā ācamaam prāpayati śrutiḥ paṭhitā viṣayam ācamaam vidadhatī vidadhyāt smṛtyoḥ iyam śrutiḥ saṃyogi ācamaam vidhāsyati śakyam āśrayitum pūrvasya pratyabhijñāyamāa vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt prāptam ubhayatas prāṇasya aa gata saṃkalpaḥ vākyea ācamaīyāsu apsu upadiśyate ayam aagata ācamaa yāyyam ācamaasya avidheya svayam aagata asaṃkalpasya vidheya ācamaasya arthatā abhyupagatā bhavati prāyatya arthatā paridhā arthatā kriyātara kriyātaram prāyatyā puruṣasya abhyupagamyate tadīyāsu apsu kriyātaram paridhā prāṇasya abhyupagamyate aavadyam idam kiṃca kṛmibhyaḥ kīṭa pataṃgebhyaḥ atra tāvat abhyavahāraḥ codyate śakyam vaktum aśabda aśakya sarvam iyam codyate sāhacaryāt apaḥ vāsaḥ atra codyate prasiddhāsu ācamaīyāsu apsu paridhā adṛṣṭiḥ codyate yuktam ardhavaiśasam saṃbhavati ācāmati kṣamaḥ mayataḥ satyam vidheye apām vidhīyate upapāditam vispaṣṭā ācamae vibhaktiḥ pratyuktam ācamaasya vidhitsita etam atra kāṇvāḥ paryavasyati ityādi tasmāt pāṭhe evaṃvid vāsaḥ vidhīyate pratipattavyam yaḥ upi ayam abhyupagamaḥ kvacid vidhīyatām kvacid vāsas vijñāam sādhuḥ apaḥ vāsaḥ ādikāyāḥ aikarūpyāt tasmāt vāsaḥ vijñāam vidhīyate ācamaam yāyyam vājasaeyi śākhāyām agi rahasye vijñātā guṇāḥ śrūyate aam upāsīta maaḥ mayam bhā rūpam evamādayaḥ tasyām śākhāyām bṛhadāraṇyake puas paṭhyate maaḥ yam puruṣaḥ bhās satyaḥ tasmin hṛdaye vrīhiḥ yavaḥ eṣa sarvasya īśāḥ sarvasya sarvam idam praśāsti idam kiṃca saṃśayaḥ kim iyam ekā agi rahasya bṛhat āraṇyakayoḥ uta dve vidye kim tāvat prāptam bhedaḥ vyavasthā kutas pauaruktya bhiāsu adhyetṛ veditṛ pauaruktya parihāram ālocya ekatvam adhyavasāya ekatra atiriktāḥ guṇāḥ upasaṃhriyate saṃvāda puas śākhāyām adhyetṛ veditṛ aśakya parihāre pauaruktye viprakraṣṭa deśa sthā ekā bhavitum arhati atra aparam vidhā saṃbhavati atiriktāḥ guṇāḥ samāḥ ubhayatra āmāyate maomaya tasmāt āyoya prāpte brūmahe bhavati śākhāyām bhavitum arhati upāsya maomayatva guṇakam ubhayatra upāsyam upāsyam rūpam vidyāyāḥ abhede bhedam adhyavasātum śakumaḥ pauaruktya udhyavasitaḥ eti ucyate vibhāga ekam vidhā aparam vidhā kiṃcid apaṭhitam agi rahasye bṛhadāraṇyake paṭhitavyam eṣa sarvasya īśaḥ ityādi paṭhitam aomayaḥ ityādi paṭhitavyam eṣa viprakṛṣṭa deśām śāṇḍilya vidyām pratyabhijñāpya tasyām īśa upadiśyate ayathā katham tasyām ayam abhidhīyate arthavati vākye saṃjāte prāpta aṃśa parāmarśasya upapadyamāa pratyabhijñā upekṣitum śakyate tasmāt atra ekatvam upapaam bṛhadāraṇyake satyam upakramya satyam asau ādityaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ yaḥ ayam dakṣiṇa ikṣa puruṣaḥ satyasya brahmaṇaḥ adhidaivatam adhyātmam āyata aviśeṣam upadiśya vyāhṛti saṃpādya dve upaiṣadau ādiśyete upaiṣadahaḥ adhidaivatam upaiṣadaham adhyātmam saṃśayaḥ kim avibhāge ubhe upaiṣadau ubhayatra ausaṃdhātavye uta vibhāge ekā adhidaivatam ekā adhyātmam sūtreṇa upakramate śāṇḍilya uktaḥ ayatra evaṃjātīyake viṣaye bhavitum arhati abhisaṃbadhāt ekā iyam adhidaivatam adhyātmam adhītā upakrama vyatiṣakta pāṭhāt katham tasyām uditaḥ dharmaḥ tasyām yaḥ ācārye kaścid augama ācāraḥ coditaḥ gata iraṇya gate tulya bhavati tasmāt upaiṣadoḥ ubhayatra prāpte pratividhatte ubhayatra kasmāt katham sthā upaibadhaḥ ucyate yaḥ eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ ādhidaivikam prakṛtyā upaiṣat ahar śrāvayati yaḥ yam dakṣiṇa īkṣa puruṣaḥ ādhyātmikam prakṛtyā upaiṣat aham etat saṃihita avalambaam tasmāt āyata vyapāśrayeṇa upaiṣadau upadiśyete kutas ubhayatra ekaḥ ayam adhidaivatam adhyātmam puruṣaḥ satyasya brahmaṇaḥ satyam etat upaiṣad avasthasya bhavitum arhati ayam dṛṣṭātaḥ ācārya apāye ācāryasya tiṣṭhataḥ bhavati tiṣṭhataḥ araṇyayoḥ ācārya apāyāt dharmasya araṇya ubhayatra tulyavat adṛṣṭātaḥ tasmāt vyavasthā evaṃjātīyakāām dharmāṇām vyavasthā darśaam bhavati etasya rūpam amuṣya rūpam yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau katham ucyate dharmāḥ akṣi puruṣe upasaṃharati etasya rūpam ityādi tasmāt vyavatiṣṭhete upaiṣadau adhikaraṇam jyeṣṭhāḥ saṃbhṛtāi agre jyeṣṭham divam ātatai rāṇāyaīyāām khileṣu vīrya dyuiveśa prabhṛtayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ vibhūtayaḥ paṭhyate upaiṣadi śāṇḍilya prabhṛtayaḥ vidyāḥ paṭhyate tāsu vidyāsu vibhūtayaḥ upasaṃhriyera vicāraṇāyām paṭhati prabhṛtayaḥ vibhūtayaḥ śāṇḍilya prabhṛtiṣu opasaṃhartavyāḥ āyata śāṇḍilya hṛdaya āyata atvam brahmaṇaḥ eṣa me hṛdaye dahara daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma upakosala akṣi āyata atvam yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ etāsu vidyāsu pratīyate ādhidaivikyaḥ etāḥ vibhūtayaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ tāsām kutas etāsu avetāsu ādhidaivikyaḥ vibhūtayaḥ śrūyate jyāyāḥ divaḥ jyāyāḥ ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ eṣaḥ bhāmaīḥ eṣa sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti yau ava ayam tāvā eṣa utar hṛdaye ubhe yāvāpṛthivī samāhite evamādyāḥ ayā vidyāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalā ādyāḥ satyam etat atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ pratyupasthāpitāsu viprakṛṣṭa deśāsu vidyāsu viprakṛṣṭa deśa guṇāḥ upasaṃhriyera eti yuktam śāṇḍilya gocarāḥ guṇāḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta saṃbadha mātreṇa ucyate ekam upāsyate sthitiḥ varīyaḥ darśaāt tasmāt śāṇḍilya aupasaṃhāraḥ iva adhikaraṇam tāṇḍiām paiṅgiām rahasyabrāhmaṇe puruṣaḥ yajñaḥ kalpitaḥ tadīyam āyuḥ tredhā vibhajya dīkṣā bhāvea dīkṣā bhāvea dharmāḥ samadhigatāḥ āśīḥ matra prayoga taittirīyakāḥ kaṃcid yajñam kalpayati evaṃviduṣaḥ yajñasya yajamāaḥ śraddhā patī saṃśayaḥ kim uktāḥ yajñasya dharmāḥ taittirīyakeṣu upasaṃhartavyāḥ kim opasaṃhartavyāḥ prāptau ācakṣmahe opasaṃhartavyāḥ kasmāt pratyabhijñā ābhāvāt ācāryaḥ iva tāṇḍiām paiṅgiām taittirīyāṇām vilakṣaṇam saṃpādaam vilakṣaṇam prātar madhyaṃdina sāyam kiṃcid maraṇa avabhṛtha sāmāyam alpīyaḥ bhūyasā taittirīyake puruṣasya śrūyate viduṣaḥ yajñasya sama adhikaraṇe ṣaṣṭhyau vidvā yaḥ yajñaḥ puruṣasya mukhyam vyadhikaraṇe ṣaṣṭhyau viduṣaḥ yaḥ yajñaḥ bhavati puruṣasya mukhyaḥ satyām gatau mukhyaḥ āśrayitavyaḥ puruṣasya vaiyadhikaraṇyeā evaṃviduṣaḥ siddhavat auvāda śrutau satyām puruṣasya bhedaḥ saṃyāsām vidyām purastāt upadiśya paśyataḥ śeṣaḥ eṣa āmāyaḥ svatatra pratīmaḥ ekam auvākayoḥ upalabhāmahe brahmaṇaḥ mahimā māyaḥ āyuḥ abhivṛddhi phalaḥ ṣoḍaśam varṣa śatam jīvati yaḥ veda samabhivyāhārāt tasmāt śākhātara adhītāām dharmāṇām āśīḥ matra ādīām taittirīyake adhikaraṇam sarvam pravidhya hṛdayam pravidhya dhamaīḥ pravṛjya śirobhiḥ pravṛjya tridhā vipṛktaḥ ityādiḥ tāṇḍiām savitar prasuva yajñam ityādiḥ śāṭyāyaiām śvetāśvaḥ ityādiḥ kaṭhāām taittirīyāṇām śam o mitraḥ śam ityādiḥ vājasaeyiām upaiṣad ārambhe pravargya brāhmaṇam paṭhyate devāḥ ha vai satram ityādi kauṣītakiām agiṣṭoma brāhmaṇam vai agiṣṭomaḥ ahar brahmaṇā upayati imṛta āpuvati yaḥ etat ahar upayati kim pravidhi matrāḥ karmāṇi vidyāsu upasaṃhriyera kim upasaṃhriyera mīmāṃsāmahe kim tāvat pratibhāti eṣām vidyāsu kutas samīpe pāṭhāt eṣām opalabhāmahe bāḍham saṃidhi saṃidheḥ tve saṃbhavati akasmāt asau āśrayitum yuktaḥ eṣām matrāṇām viṣayam kiṃcid sāmarthyam paśyāmaḥ katham pravargya ādīni karmāṇi tve pratipadyemahi eṣa sāmarthyam tāvat matrāṇām viṣayam kiṃcid śakyam kalpayitum hṛdaya saṃkīrtaāt prāyeṇa upāsaeṣu dvāreṇa hṛdayam pravidhya evaṃjātīyakāām matrāṇām upāsaeṣu matra viiyogaḥ bhūḥ evamādiḥ pravargya ādīām karmaṇām viiyuktāām satām aviruddhaḥ vidyāsu viiyogaḥ vājapeyaḥ iva bṛhaspatisavasya prāpte brūmaḥ eṣām vidyāsu kasmāt hṛdayam pravidhya evaṃjātīyakāām matrāṇām hṛdaya bhiāḥ abhisaṃbaddhāḥ upaiṣat uditābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ tābhiḥ saṃgatum sāmarthyam hṛdayasya hṛdayasya upāsa eṣu upayogāt dvārakaḥ upayastaḥ eti ucyate hṛdaya saṃkīrtaasya upayogaḥ kathaṃcid utprekṣyeta hṛdaya atra matra hṛdayam pravidhya dhamaīḥ pravṛjya evaṃjātīyakaḥ sakalaḥ matra vidyābhiḥ abhisaṃbadhyate abhicāra viṣayaḥ eṣaḥ ṛthaḥ tasmāt ābhicārikeṇa karmaṇā sarvam pravidhya etasya matrasya abhisaṃbadhaḥ savitar prasuva yajñam prasava karmaṇā saṃbadhaḥ pramāṇa atara ādau sartavyaḥ matrāṇām keṣāṃcid keṣāṃcid keṣāṃcid pramāṇa atareṇa atareṣu rahasya paṭhitāām satām saṃidhi mātreṇa upapattiḥ durbalaḥ saṃidhiḥ tatre samavāye pāra daurbalyam viprakarṣāt atra karmaṇām upapattiḥ eṣām vidyābhiḥ aikārthyam kiṃcid vājapeye bṛhaspatisavasya spaṣṭam viiyogātaram vājapeye iṣṭvā bṛhaspatisave yajeta pravargyaḥ balīyasā viiyuktaḥ durbale viiyogam arhati agṛhyamāṇa tve pramāṇayoḥ balavat abalavatoḥ pramāṇayoḥ agṛhyamāṇa saṃbhavati balavat abalavat tasmāt evaṃjātīyakāām matrāṇām karmaṇām saṃidhi pāṭha mātreṇa āśaṅkitavyam saṃidhi pāṭhaḥ saṃtoṣṭavyam upāya tāṇḍiām śrutiḥ aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam cadra adhikaraṇam śrutiḥ aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam cadra adhikaraṇam iva rāhoḥ mukhāt pramucya dhūtvā akṛtam kṛtātmā lokam abhisaṃbhavāmi ātharvaṇikāām vidvāḥ āma rūpāt vimuktaḥ upaiti divyam śāṭyāyaiaḥ paṭhati putrāḥ dāyam upayati suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣataḥ pāpa kṛtyām kauṣītakiaḥ vidhūute priyā jñātayaḥ sukṛtam upayati apriyāḥ duṣkṛtam kvacid duṣkṛtayoḥ śrūyate kvacid tayoḥ vibhāge priyaiḥ apriyaiḥ kvacid ubhayam ubhayam śrūyate tāvat kiṃcid vaktavyam śrūyate arthāt hāam saṃipatati ātmīyayoḥ duṣkṛtayoḥ āvaśyaka hāasya hāam śrūyate upāyaam saṃipatet vicikitsāyām aśravaṇāt asaṃipātaḥ tara gocara śākhātarīyasya śravaṇasya kartṛkam duṣkṛtayoḥ kartṛkam tayoḥ āvaśyaka katham ākṣipyeta tasmāt saṃipātaḥ hāau upāyaasya asyām prāptau paṭhati hāau hāau etasyām kevalāyām śrūyamāṇāyām upāyaam saṃipatitum arhati hā śeṣaḥ upāya samadhigataḥ kauṣītakirahasye tasmāt upāya āu aśravaṇāt tara gocara āvaśyaka saṃipātaḥ ucyate bhavet eṣā vyavasthā uktiḥ yadi auṣṭheyam kiṃcid ayatra ayatra saṃkīrtyate ittham mahābhāgā yad viduṣaḥ bhūte vidhūyete suhṛd durhṛtsu arthe asmi kvacid ayatra hāa śrutau prakarṣa lābhāya prasiddhā arthavāda atara arthavāda atara pravṛttiḥ ekaviṃśaḥ vai itas asau ādityaḥ evamādiṣu katham ekaviṃśatā ādityasya abhidhīyeta apekṣyamāṇe rthavāda ātare māsāḥ ṛtavaḥ trayaḥ lokāḥ asau ādityaḥ ekaviṃśaḥ asmi triṣṭubhau bhavataḥ idriya tvāya evamādi vādeṣu idriyam vai triṣṭubh evamādi arthavāda atara upāyaa vādasya katham ayadīye upeyete upāya samuccāraya arthām hāāu sūcayati vivakṣāyām upāya arthasya hāāu brūyāt tasmāt vicāra prasaṅgea pradarśa idam sūtram upādāam kuśāḥ vāaspatyāḥ sthata mā pāta etasmin game kuśāām aviśeṣeṇa audumbaryaḥ kuśāḥ āśrīyate kvacid asuracchada sāma viśeṣeṇa paurvāparya prasaṅge chadāṃsi pūrvāṇi ṣoḍaśi stotre keṣāṃcid kāla prāptau samaya adhyuṣite sūrye ārca kāla pratipattiḥ aviśeṣeṇa upagāaṃ kecid samāmaati viśeṣeṇa bhāllaviḥ eteṣu kuśa hāau upāya āvayaḥ śrutyatara kṛtam śrutyatare abhyupagacchataḥ ayāyyaḥ satyām gatau dvādaśalakṣaṇyām paryudāsaḥ pratiṣedhe athavā etāsu sūtreṇa etat citayitavyam duṣkṛtayoḥ hāam abhidhīyate kim arthātaram prāpayitavyam smaraṇāt dodhūyate dhvaja agrāṇi cālyamāeṣu dhvaja agreṣu prayoga darśaāt tasmāt cālaam vidhūaam abhidhīyate cālaam duṣkṛtayoḥ kaṃcid kālam pratibadhaāt prāpayya prativaktavyam hāāveva eṣa vidhūaa vartitum arhati upāyaa parigraha bhūtayoḥ duṣkṛtayoḥ aprahīṇayoḥ paraiḥ upāyam saṃbhavati yadi idam parakīyayoḥ duṣkṛtayoḥ āñjasam saṃbhāvyate āuguṇyena śakyate kvacid idam śrūyamāṇam kuśācchada upagāa vidhūa śrutyā apekṣyamāṇam sārvatrikam irṇaya kāraṇam dhvaja agra duṣkṛtayoḥ mukhyam saṃbhavati adravya aśvaḥ romāṇi tyaja rajaḥ romāṇi śātayati aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam brāhmaṇam dhātūām smaraṇa sāmparāye sāṃparāya adhikaraṇam pathā paryaṅka stham abhiprasthitasya duṣkṛtayoḥ viyogam kauṣītakiaḥ paryaṅka āmaati etam yāam pathāam āsādya āgi lokam āgacchati āgacchati virajām tām maasā atyeti vidhūute kim yathāśrutam pratipattavyam āhosvit ādau dehāt apasarpaṇe vicāraṇāyām prāmāṇyāt yathāśruti pratipatti prasaktau paṭhati dehāt apasarpaṇe idam duṣkṛta hāam bhavati hetum ācaṣṭe viduṣaḥ saṃparetasya saṃprepsataḥ atarāle duṣkṛtābhyām kiṃcid prāptavyam yad katicid kṣaṇāḥ akṣīṇe kalpeyātām viruddha tayoḥ kṣayaḥ yadā abhimukhī bhavitum arhati tasmāt ayam duṣkṛta kṣayaḥ paścāt paṭhyate śākhiaḥ tāṇḍiaḥ śāṭyāyaiaḥ prāc avasthāyām aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam putrāḥ dāyam upayati suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣataḥ pāpa kṛtyām chadataḥ yadi dehāt apasṛptasya pathā prasthitasya ardha pathe duṣkṛta kṣayaḥ abhyupagamyeta patite dehe yama eyama abhyāsa ātmakasya duṣkṛta kṣaya hetoḥ yatasya aupapattiḥ hetukasya duṣkṛta kṣayasya tasmāt sādhaka avasthāyām pūrvakam draṣṭavyam imitta aimittikayoḥ upapattiḥ tāṇḍi śāṭyāya eśrutyoḥ saṃgatiḥ adhikaraṇam kvacid śrūyate saṃśayaḥ kim pathāḥ śrūyate hāāva viśeṣeṇa yāaḥ pathāḥ saṃipatet uta kvacid saṃipatet kvacid tāvat hāāva viśeṣeṇa upāya āu uktā bhavitum arhati asyām prāptau ācakṣmahe yāasya pathaḥ vibhāge bhavitum arhati kvacid arthavatī gatiḥ kvacid aviśeṣeṇa ayathā aviśeṣeṇa etasyām gatau aṅgīkriyamāṇāyām puṇya pāpe vidhūya irañjaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti asyām śrutau deśa atara prāpaṇī gatiḥ virudhyeta katham irañjaogatā deśa ataram gacchet gatavyam paramam sāmyam deśa atara prāpti āyattam āarthakyam atra mayāmahe kvacid arthavatī gatiḥ ūrthaḥ paryaṅka saguṇeṣu upāsaeṣu paryaṅka ārohaṇam brahmaṇā gadha evamādi bahu deśa atara prāpti āyattam śrūyate arthavatī gatiḥ samyak darśae upalabdhiḥ ekatva darśi āpta kāmāām dagdha aśeṣa kleśa bījāām ārabdha āśaya kṣapaṇa vyatirekeṇa apekṣitavyam kiṃcid aarthikā gatiḥ eṣa draṣṭavyaḥ prāptau deśa atara prāpaṇaḥ pathā apekṣyate ārogya prāptau vibhāgam caturtha adhyāye ipuṇataram upapādayiṣyāmaḥ aiyamaḥ sarvāsām auma ābhyām aiyama adhikaraṇam saguṇāsu vidyāsu gatiḥ arthavatī paramātma saguṇāsu vidyāsu kāsucid gatiḥ śrūyate paryaṅka upakosala pañcāgi dahara adhikaraṇam śāṇḍilya ṣoḍaśakala vaiśvāara saṃśayaḥ kim yāsu eṣā gatiḥ śrūyate tāsu iyamyeta uta aiyamea sarvābhiḥ evaṃjātīyakābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ abhisaṃbadhyeta kim tāvat prāptam iyamaḥ śrūyate bhavitum arhati prakaraṇasya iyāmaka yadi śrūyamāṇā gatiḥ vidyātaram gacchet ādīām prāmāṇyam hīyeta sarvasya ādikā ekā gatiḥ upakosala pañcāgi tulya paṭhyate tasmāt aiyamaḥ prāpte paṭhati aiyamaḥ sarvāsām abhyudaya prāpti phalāām guṇāām vidyāām aviśeṣeṇa eṣā devayā ākhyā gatiḥ bhavitum arhati aiyama uktaḥ śrutiḥ ye ittham viduḥ pañcāgi vidyāvatām devayāam avatārayati iye ceme iraṇye śraddhā tapaḥ upāsate vidyātara śīliām pañcāgi vidbhiḥ samāa mārga tām gamayati katham vidyātara śīliām iyam gatiḥ śraddhā tapaḥ parāyaṇāām ta eṣa kevalābhyām śraddhā tapobhyām atareṇa balam eṣā gatiḥ labhyate ārohati kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ dakṣiṇāḥ yati āvidvāṃsaḥ tapasviḥ śrutyatarāt tasmāt śraddhā tapobhyām vidyātara upalakṣaṇam vājasaeyiḥ pañcāgi adhikāre dhīyate yaḥ etat viduḥ ye amī araṇye śraddhām satyam upāsate śraddhālavaḥ ye satyam upāsate vyākhyeyam brahmaṇi prayukta pañcāgi vidām itthaṃvittayā upātta tara parāyaṇāām etat upādāam yāyyam ye etau pathau viduḥ kīṭāḥ pataṅgāḥ idam dadaśūkam mārga dvaya bhraṣṭāām kaṣṭām adhogatim gamayatī śrutiḥ yāa pitṛyāṇayoḥ bhāvayati eṣām smṛtiḥ śukla kṛṣṇe gatī jagataḥ śāśvate mate ekayā puas puas devayāasya pathaḥ upakosala pañcāgi ubhayatra aucita ārtham tasmāt aiyamaḥ yāvat adhikaraṇam viduṣaḥ ataram utpadyate cityate vidyāyāḥ saṃpattau kaivalyaiḥ citā odaaḥ bhavet citā saṃbhavati tṛpyet cityate upapaā iyam citā vidām keṣāṃcid itihāsa purāṇayoḥ atara darśaāt veda ācāryaḥ purāṇa ṛṣiḥ kali dvāparayoḥ saṃdhau kṛṣṇadvaipāyaaḥ saṃbabhūva smarati vasiṣṭhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ imi śāpāt apagata dehaḥ puar brahmā ādeśāḥ mitrāvaruṇābhyām saṃbabhūva bhṛgu ādīām brahmaṇaḥ māasa putrāṇām vāruṇe yajñe utpattiḥ saatkumāraḥ brahmaṇaḥ māasaḥ putraḥ svayam rudrāya vara pradāāt prādurbabhūva dakṣa ārada prabhṛtīām bhūyasī atara utpattiḥ kathyate smṛtau śrutau matra arthavādayoḥ prāyeṇa upalakṣyate kecid patite dehe dehātaram ādadate kecid yoga aiśvarya vaśāt samadhigata sakala veda eteṣām atara darśaāt prāptam vidyāyāḥ pākṣikam ahetu uttaram ucyate veda pravarta hetuṣu adhikāreṣu sthiteḥ asau bhagavā savitā sahasra yuga paryatam jagataḥ dhikāram caritvā avasāe udaya astamaya varjitam ūrdhvaḥ udetya udetā āstametā ekalaḥ madhye sthātā vartamāā ārabdha kṣaye tāvat ciram vimokṣye saṃpatsye īśvarāḥ parameśvareṇa teṣu teṣu adhikāreṣu samyagdarśae kaivalya hetau akṣīṇa karmāṇaḥ yāvat adhikāram avatiṣṭhate aviruddham sakṛt pravṛttam phalāt āāya āśayam ativāhayataḥ svātatryeṇa gṛhāt iva gṛhātaram ayam ayam deham saṃcarataḥ parimuṣita smṛtaye idriya prakṛti vaśi yugapad adhitiṣṭhati jātismarāḥ ucyate vyudasya svam deham jāakam deham āviśya vyudya paścāt svam deham āviveśa yadi upayukte sakṛt pravṛtte ātaram atara ārambha kāraṇam āvirbhavet ayat adagdha bījam ataram prasajyeta brahmavidyāyāḥ pākṣikam ahetu śaṅkyeta iyam āśaṅkā yuktā jñāāt bīja dāhasya śrutiḥ bhidyate hṛdayagrathiḥ chidyate saṃśayāḥ kṣīyate karmāṇi dṛṣṭe parāvare lambhe vipramokṣaḥ evamādyā smṛtiḥ edhāṃsi samiddhaḥ giḥ bhasmasāt kurute karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute rohati puas jñā dagdhaiḥ kleśaiḥ evamādyāḥ avidyā kleśa dāhe kleśa bījasya āśayasya deśa dāhaḥ deśa prarohaḥ agi dagdhasya śāli bījasya deśa prarohaḥ pravṛtta phalasya āśayasya iṣoḥ iva vega kṣayāt tāvat ciram śarīrapātau adhikṣepa karaṇāt tasmāt jñā phalasya aaikātika śrutiḥ aviśeṣeṇa jñāā mokṣam yaḥ yaḥ devāām abudhyata abhavat ṛṣīṇām mauṣyāṇām jñāātareṣu aiśvarya phaleṣu āsaktāḥ syuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ paścāt aiśvarya kṣaya darśae irviṇṇāḥ paramātma jñāe pariiṣṭhāya prāpuḥ brahmaṇā saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare kṛtātmā aḥ praviśati padam smaraṇāt jñāasya viraha āśaṅkā upapattiḥ phale svarga ādau aubhava ārūḍhe āśaṅkā bhavet aubhava ārūḍham jñā sāṃkṣāt aparokṣāt asi siddha asi vākyasya mṛtaḥ bhaviṣyasi pariṇetum śakyaḥ ha etat paśya ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham mauḥ abhavam sūryaḥ samyak darśa kālam tasmāt aikātikī viduṣaḥ kaivalya sāma āya adhikaraṇam vājasaeyake śrūyate etat vai gārgi brāhmaṇāḥ abhivadati sthūlam aṇu hrasvam dīrgham lohitam seham ityādi ātharvaṇe śrūyate parā yayā adhigamyate dreśyam grāhyam gotram varṇam ityādi ayatra viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa dvāreṇa śrāvyate kvacid kecid atiriktāḥ viśeṣāḥ pratiṣidhyate tāsām buddhīām kim sarvāsām uta vyavasthā saṃśaye vibhāgāt vyavasthā prāptau ucyate viṣayāḥ buddhayaḥ sarvāḥ avaroddhavyāḥ sāmāya viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa rūpaḥ pratipāda prakāraḥ pratipādyam pratyabhijñāyate kim ayatra kṛtāḥ buddhayaḥ ayatra syuḥ āad atra rūpāṇi rūpāṇi viśeṣaḥ prapañca ayam citā bhedaḥ coditāsu puroḍāśa pradā amatrāṇām ageḥ veḥ hotram veḥ adhvaram evamādīām udgātṛ veda utpāām adhvaryubhiḥ bhavati adhvaryu kartṛka puroḍāśa pradā viśeṣaṇāām kvacid akṣareṇa abhisaṃbadhaḥ kāṇḍe vyatikrame veda saṃyogaḥ atra adhikaraṇam dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā vṛkṣam pariṣasvajāte tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam abhicākaśīti adhikāre matram ātharvaṇikāḥ śvetāśvatarāḥ paṭhati kaṭhāḥ ṛtam pibatau sukṛtasya parame parārdhye chāyā ātapau āgayaḥ ye triṇāciketāḥ kim atra uta vidyāāātvam saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam vidyāāātvam kutas darśaāt dvā suparṇāḥ atra abhoktṛ ṛtam pibatau atra vedya rūpam vidyām bhidyāt prāpte ekatvam kutas aayoḥ matrayoḥ dvi upetam vedyam rūpam darśitaḥ bhedaḥ darśitaḥ bhedaḥ e ti ucyate ubhau etau matrau dvitīyam īśvaram pratipādayataḥ dvā suparṇāḥ atra tāvat ubhicākaśīti aśaāya atītaḥ paramātmā pratipādyate vākyaśeṣe juṣṭam yadā paśyati ayam īśam mahimā ṛtam pibatau atra jīve pibati pibati upacaryate paramātma prakaraṇam etat ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt viṣayaḥ atra vākyaśeṣaḥ bhavati yaḥ setuḥ īja au atra etat prapañcitam vedya bhedaḥ tasmāt triṣu eteṣu paurvāparya ālocae paramātma avagamyate tādātmya vivakṣayā paramātma abheda vicāra avatāraḥ tasmāt prapañca eṣa prayogaḥ tasmāt atarā atara adhikaraṇam aparokṣāt yaḥ ataraḥ dvis uṣastaka hola praśayoḥ airataryeṇa vājasaeyiḥ saṃśayaḥ āā āā tāvat prāptam abhyāsa ayathā aarthakam tasmāt bhedaḥ bhedaḥ prāpte pratyāha sarvātaraḥ ubhayatra aviśiṣṭaḥ pṛcchayate pratyucyate dvau ātmau dehe sarvātarau saṃbhavataḥ āñjasam sarvātaratvam avakalpeta pañcabhūta samūhe dehe pṛthivyāḥ utarāḥ adbhyaḥ utaram āpekṣika itaratve mukhyam sarvātaratvam bhavati athavā śrutyataram ekaḥ devāḥ gūḍhaḥ vyāpī atarātmā atre samasteṣu grāmeṣu ekaḥ sarvātaraḥ āmāyate aayoḥ brāhmaṇayoḥ tasmāt vedya aikyāt ayathā aupapattiḥ ayathā aupapattiḥ parihartavyam atra ucyate atara ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake asi śvetaketo avakṛtvā upi upadeśe bhedaḥ bhavati bhaviṣyati katham avakṛtvā upi upadeśe bhedaḥ bhavati upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām avagamāt mā bhagavān āvijñāpayatu arthasya puas puas upakṣepāt parisamāpti upakrama upasaṃhārau tāvat viṣayau dṛśyeta aparokṣāt dvitīye praśe evakāram prayuñjāaḥ praśa gatam ākṛṣyamāṇam pūrvasmin brāhmaṇe karaṇa vyatiriktasya ātmaaḥ sadbhāvaḥ kathyate uttarasmin aśaāya atīta viśeṣaḥ kathyate upapattiḥ tasmāt ekā viśiṃṣati vyatihāra adhikaraṇam sau yaḥ sau ham prakṛti aitareyiṇaḥ jābālāḥ vai aham asmi bhagavaḥ iham vai asi saṃśayaḥ kim vyatihāreṇa rūpā matiḥ kartavyā uta rūpā rūpā tāvat atra īśvareṇa ekatvam muktvā kiṃcid citayitavyam yadi citayitavya viśeṣaḥ parikalpyeta saṃsāriṇaḥ īśvara ātmatvam īśvarasya saṃsāri ātmatvam saṃsāriṇaḥ tāvat īśvara ātmatve utkarṣaḥ bhavet īśvarasya saṃsāri tve ikarṣaḥ kṛtaḥ tasmāt aikarūpyam mateḥ vyatihāra āmāyaḥ ekatva dṛḍhīkāra prāpte pratyāha yam ādhyāāya āmāyate guṇāḥ prabhṛtayaḥ ādhyāāya āmāyate viśiṃṣati samā mātāraḥ uccāraṇe aham asmi aham asi rūpāyām matau kartavyāyām bhavati ayathā idam aarthakam au viśeṣe devatāyāḥ saṃsāri ikarṣaḥ prasajyeta aikātmyasya ekatva dṛḍhīkāraḥ āpadyeta vayam ekatva dṛḍhīkāram vārayāmaḥ kim tarhi vyatihāreṇa dvirūpā matiḥ kartavyā aikarūpā upapādayāmaḥ phalatas ekatvam dṛḍhībhavati upadeśe guṇaḥ īśvaraḥ prasidhyati tasmāt ayam ādhyātavyaḥ viṣaye upasaṃhartavyaḥ bhavati adhikaraṇam yaḥ ha etam yakṣam prathama jam veda satyam ityādiā vājasaeyake vidyām saāma upāsaām vidhāya satyam asau ādityaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ yaḥ ayam dakṣiṇa īkṣa puruṣaḥ ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim dve vidye kim vai ekā dve tāvat prāptam saṃyogaḥ bhavati jayati imān lokān pāpmāam jahāti upariṣṭāt ākarṣaṇam upāsya ekatvāt prāpte brūmaḥ ekā iyam kutas satyam ākarṣaṇāt ākarṣaṇam upāsya ekatvāt aitadevam vispaṣṭāt kāraṇātarāt bhedaḥ pratīyate etat atra saṃbhaveta satyam ākarṣaṇāt pūrvavidyā saṃbaddham satyam ākṛṣyate ekavidyā aiścayaḥ puaruktam atara vidyātaram atra ucyate aham atara upadeśasya stāvakam idam atara śravaṇam adoṣaḥ arthavādāt phale kalpayitavye tve avayaveṣu śrūyamāṇāi phalāi avayaviyām upasaṃhartavyāi bhavati tasmāt iyam ekā guṇāḥ prayoge upasaṃhartavyāḥ kecid puarasmin sūtre idam vājasaeyakam akṣi viṣayam vākyam chādogye yaḥ eṣa utarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ udāhṛtya iyam akṣi viṣayā ubhayatra ekā kṛtvā guṇāḥ vājasaeyibhyaḥ chadogāām upasaṃhāryāḥ sādhu lakṣyate chādogye udgītha vyapāśrayā vijñāyate madhya avasāeṣu bhavati iyam ṛgagiḥ sāma upakrametasya ṛc sāma geṣṇau tasmāt udgīthaḥ madhyeye gāyati upasaṃhāre aivam vājasaeyake kiṃcid prakrama vyavasthā yuktā āyata adhikaraṇam idam asmi pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma smi prastutya chadogāḥ eṣaḥ apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ vijighatsaḥ pipāsaḥ kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ ityādi vājasaeyiḥ vai eṣa mahāḥ ajaḥ yaḥ yam prāṇeṣu yaḥ eṣa tar hṛdaye tasmin śete sarvasya vaśī ityādi paraspara kim saṃśaye idam ucyate devadattaḥ dattaḥ satyabhāmā bhāmā mahābhāṣya etat chādogye hṛdaya ākāśasya jātam vājasaeyake vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ atra saṃbadhyeta vājasaeyake vaśi chādogye eṣaḥ apahata pāpmā atra saṃbadhyeta kutas āyataādi sāmāyāt ubhayatra hṛdayam vedyaḥ īśvaraḥ evamādi bahu sāmāyam viśeṣaḥ chādogye hṛdaya ākāśasya vājasaeyake āśrayasya brahmaṇe dahara atra chādogye pratiṣṭhāpita ayam atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ guṇā chādogye upadiśyate yaḥ amaḥ vidya vrajati etān akāmāḥ kāmāām vedya vājasaeyake upadiśyamāam urdhvam vimokṣāya brūhi saṅgaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ vaśi jātam vājasaeyake saṃkīrtyate upariṣṭāt eṣaḥ eti eti ityādi irguṇam upasaṃharati guṇavataḥ brahmaṇaḥ ekatvāt vibhūti pradarśaāya ayam sūtritaḥ draṣṭavyam ādarāt alopaḥ adhikaraṇam chādogye vaiśvāara vidyām prakṛtya śrūyate bhaktam prathamam āgacchet homīyam yām prathamām āhutim juhuyāt tām juhuyāt prāṇāya svāhā ityādi āhutayaḥ vihitāḥ tāsu parastāt agihotra prayuktaḥ yaḥ etat vidvāḥ agihotram juhoti kṣudhitā bālāḥ mātaram paryupāsate bhūtāyagihotram upāsate idam vicāryate kim bhoja lope prāṇāgihotrasya uta bhaktam bhakta āgama asaṃyoga bhakta āgama bhoja bhoja lope prāṇāgihotrasya prāpte lupyeta tāvat kasmāt ādarāt vaiśvāara jābālāām śrutiḥ ha vai juhuyāt atithi bhojaasya prāthamyam svāmi bhojaam prathamam prāpayatī ādaram karoti yā prāthamya lopam sahate prāthamyavataḥ gihotrasya lopam saheta bhoja bhakta āgama asaṃyogāt bhoja lope prāpitaḥ dravya vidhā prākṛte gihotre prabhṛtīām dravyāṇām iyata gihotra prāptau satyām bhakta dravya vidhā idam vākyam bhaktam lope mukhyasya prāptam adbhiḥ dravyeṇa viruddhea uttaram paṭhati upasthita itas vacaāt bhojae tasmāt bhoja dravyāt prathama upaipatitāt kasmāt vacaāt bhaktam prathamam āgacchet homīyam siddha bhakta upaipāta parāmarśe parārtha dravya sādhya tām vidadhāti satyaḥ katham bhoja lope dravya ātaram pratidhāpayeyuḥ atra prākṛta āgihotra juhoti uddeśa gataḥ gihotra vidhāpayet yuktā arthavāda gataḥ gihotra vidhāpayitum arhati prāptau abhyupagamyamāāyām agi uddharaṇa prāpyera saṃbhavaḥ agi uddharaṇam tāvat homa adhikaraṇa bhāvāya ayam agau homaḥ bhoja ārtha vyāghāta bhoja ārtha upaīta dravya saṃbadhāt āsyaḥ eṣa homaḥ jābāla śrutiḥ pūrvaḥ utithibhyaḥ uśīyāt āsya ādhārām imām homaiḥ vṛttim uraḥ vediḥ lomāi barhiḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ āsyam āhavaīyaḥ vedi śrutiḥ atra sthaṇḍila draṣṭavyā āgihotre vedi aṅgāām saṃpipādayiṣita saṃyogāt upasthā dharmāḥ kecid kathaṃcid virudhyate tasmāt bhoja pakṣe matra dravya saṃyogāt homāḥ darśa avacaam bhoja pakṣe prāthamya vidhā vacaasya atibhāraḥ ityatā śakyate darśayitum tasmāt bhoja lope gihotrasya pratibadhaḥ taiḥ adhikaraṇam vyapāśrayāṇi om etat udgītham upāsīta evamādīi kim syuḥ karmasu parṇa mayī uta godoha vicārayāmaḥ kim tāvat prāptam ityāi kutas prayoga vaca parigrahāt udgītha dvāreṇa kratu atara saṃspṛśyate eṣām vākyeṣu śravaṇam āpayitā ha vai bhavati ityādi vartamāna apadeśa rūpatvāt arthavāda apāpa śloka tasmāt paṭhitāām juhū dvāreṇa kratu praveśāt paṭhita ityatā udgītha upāsāām prāpte brūmaḥ taiḥ dhāraṇāiyamaḥ udgītha yāthātmyaiḥ dhāraṇāi rasatamaḥ āptiḥ samṛddhiḥ ādityaḥ evamādi ityavat karmasu iyamyera kutas aityatvam evaṃjātīyakāām śrutiḥ kurutaḥ yaḥ etat veda yaḥ veda viduṣaḥ abhyaujñāāt prastāva vijñā vihīāām prastotṛ ādīām yāja ādhyavasā adarśaāt prastotar yāḥ prastāvam avāyattā tām avidvā prastoṣyasi tām avidvā udgāsyasi tām avidvā pratihariṣyasi evaṃjātīyakasya vyapāśrayasya vijñāasya karmaṇaḥ siddhi pratibadhaḥ samṛddhiḥ atiśaya viśeṣaḥ kaścid ubhau kurutaḥ yaḥ etat veda yaḥ veda avidyā karoti śraddhayā upaiṣadā vīryavattaram bhavati vidvat avidvat prayogayoḥ tarap prayogāt tarap prayogāt vīryavat gamyate aityatve vidyāyāḥ ityatve katham vihīam upasaṃhāre vīryavat sthitiḥ sāma śiṣyate kalpate ha asmai lokāḥ ūrdhvāḥ āvṛttāḥ evamādi idam śravaṇam arthavāda yuktam pratipattum āpadyeta upadeśe vāda upapattiḥ prayāja itikartavya ākāṅkṣasya kratoḥ tādarthye yuktam arthavāda ārabhya adhīteṣu parṇa mayī godoha ādīām akriyā ātmakāām āśrayam atareṇa godoha ādīām appraṇaya lābhāt bailva ādīām yūpa lābhāt upapaaḥ parṇa mayī evaṃvidhaḥ kaścid āśrayaḥ prakṛtaḥ juhū āśrayatām vivakṣitvā phale vidhim vivakṣataḥ bhedaḥ upāsaāām vidhā udgītha āśrayāṇām phale virudhyate tasmāt kratu āśrayāṇi saṃyogāt aityāi udgītha upāsaāi draṣṭavyam kalpasūtra kārāḥ adhidaivatam vāyuḥ saṃvargaḥ atra adhidaivatam vāva saṃvargaḥ atra adhyātmam ādīām saṃśayaḥ kim imau vāyu prāṇau upagatavyau syātām uta apṛthak apṛthak tāvat prāptam tattva tattve yāyyam śrutiḥ kasmāt ayam vibhāga asatya ādhyā apṛthaktve aarthakaḥ tattva tattva abhede aucita abheda śloka upayāsasya tattva abheda abhiprāyeṇa upapadyamānasya udita dhyeya bhedaiḥ ākaraṇa sāmarthya eṣām prāṇāām deveṣu prāṇeṣu vyapadiśati vai pañcāye pañcāye daśa kṛtam upasaṃharati tasmāt idrāya rājñe puroḍāśam ekādaśa kapālam idrāya adhirājāya idrāya rājñe asyām ityatas idrā pradā āśaṅkāyām rāja yathāyāsam pṛthaktvāt pradā pṛthaktvam bhavati tattva abhede ādhyeya aṃśa pṛthaktvāt ādhyā apṛthaktvam saṃkarṣe dravya yāga bhedaḥ vidyate aivam bhedaḥ usti upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām upadeśeṣu ekavidyā vidhā apratīteḥ aikye pravṛtti bhedaḥ bhavati gihotre iva sāyam prātar kāla abhipretya pradāa tāt adhikaraṇam vājasaeyi ogi rahasye vai idam agre sadā āsīt etasmin brāhmaṇe ṣaṭtriṃśatam sahasrāṇi apaśyat ogī arka ama oma yāma aścitaḥ ityādi citaḥ citaḥ citaḥ śrotra citaḥ citaḥ ogi citaḥ agī sāṃpādikā teṣu saṃśayaḥ kim bhūtāḥ uta svatatrāḥ kevala ātmakāḥ upraveśe prāpte svātatryam tāvat pratijāīte bhūyāṃsi liṅgāi brāhmaṇe kevalavidyā eṣām upodbalayati kiṃca imāi bhūtāi saṃkalpayati kṛtiḥ aha etāḥ evaṃvide sarvadā svapate evaṃjātīyakāi pūrvasmin kāṇḍe samavāye pāra daurbalyam viprakarṣāt svatatrāḥ etegayaḥ pūrvasya mayasya ageḥ viṣayaḥ ayam svatatraḥ satyam etat evaṃjātīyakam bhavati etat sāṃpādika āgi praśaṃsā asatyām ayasyām prāptau prakaraṇam bādhitum utsahate tasmāt sāṃpādikāḥ etegayaḥ syuḥ māasa daśarātrasya avivākye pṛthivyā pātreṇa samudrasya somasya prajāpataye devatāyai gṛhyamāṇasya māasāya iva graha kalpaḥ śeṣaḥ bhavati ayam agi kalpaḥ atideśaḥ eṣām agīām upraveśam upodbalayati ṣaṭtriṃśat sahasrāṇi agayoḥ ṛkāḥ ekaikaḥ sāmāye atideśaḥ pravartate pūrveṇa eṣām dyotayati tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati ātmakāḥ svatatrāḥ maaścit yogayaḥ syuḥ bhūtāḥ ha citaḥ ha evaṃvidaḥ citā bhavati darśaāt eteṣām svātatrye purastāt darśitam atra asatyām ayasyām prāptau asādhakam kasyacid arthasya apāsya adhyavasitam uttaram paṭhati sāmarthya atikraya aśeṣa adhyavasāya svātatrya pakṣaḥ bādhitavyaḥ ādeḥ balīyāṃsi vākyāi sthitam sūtre svātatrya pakṣam sādhayati katham śrutiḥ tāvat ha citaḥ sarvadā bhūtāi svapate vākyam ha evaṃvidaḥ citāḥ bhavati itividyā citaḥ avadhāraṇām iyam śrutiḥ pīḍitā iyatā aarthakam avadhāraṇam bhavet rūpam eṣām abāhya sādhaatvam abāhya sādhaatve māasagraha avadhāraṇam bhaviṣyati svapate jāgrate evaṃvide sarvadā sātatya darśam eṣām svātatrī kalpate sāṃpādike maye gihotre prāṇam juhoti vācam prāṇe juhoti uktvā ucyate aate amṛte āhutī svapan satatam juhoti prayogasya kāla eṣām prayogaḥ kalpeta idam arthavāda yāyyam vispaṣṭaḥ vidhāyakaḥ liṅ yuktam saṃkīrtaa mātrasya arthavāda eṣām saṃkīrtaam kalpayitum śakyate sātatya darśaāt tathābhūtam kalpyate eṣām svātatrya saṃkalpayati kṛtiḥ ityādi vākyam evaṃvide saṃbadham eṣām ācakṣāṇam kratu saṃbadham mṛṣyate tasmāt svātatrya pakṣaḥ jyāyāḥ aubadha prajñātara itas prakaraṇam upamṛdya svātatryam pratipattavyam avayavāḥ maasā adhīyata maasā acīyata maasā grahāḥ agṛhyata saṃpad phalaḥ ayam aubadhaḥ pratyakṣāḥ avayavāḥ saṃpadā lipsitavyāḥ atra udgītha upāsa avat aupraveśi āśaṅkitavyam vairūpyāt atra aṅgam kiṃcid ādāya ṣaṭtriṃśat sahasrāṇi graha ādīn kalpayati iyam āyuṣasya ahar su dṛṣṭā satī āropyate draṣṭavyam aubadhāt svātatryam atideśa yathāsaṃbhavam yojayitavyam ekaikaḥ mayasya āgeḥ māhātmyam atidiśa ādaram pūrveṇa uttareṣām śakyam vaktum vyāpāreṇa pūrvaḥ upakaroti uttare upakartum śakuvati pūrvapakṣe atideśaḥ upodbalakaḥ sāmāyā itideśaḥ pravartate asmad pakṣe agitva sāmāyeātideśa pratyuktam aubadha kāraṇebhyaḥ svātatryam prajñātara prajñātarāṇi śāṇḍilya prabhṛtīi karmabhyaḥ prajñātarebhyaḥ svatatrāṇi bhavati rājasūya paṭhitāyāḥ utkarṣaḥ rājayajña rājasūyasya kāṇḍe kratu arthāyām varṇa traya saṃyogāt māasa pratyucyate kalpyam uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ kevala kiṃcid kasyacid adhikaraṇam avabaddhāḥ avabaddha adhikaraṇam samāptā prāsaṅgikī kathā saṃprati prakṛtām āvartāmahe om etat udgītham upāsīta lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta auktham uktham vai prajāḥ idam uktham iyam upayāsaḥ kim tāvat prāptam śākhā gateṣu udgītha vidhīyera eti kutas udgītham upasīte sāmāya vihitāām ākāṅkṣāyām saṃikṛṣṭe viśeṣeṇa ākāṅkṣā vṛtteḥ atilaṅghaea śākhātara upādāe kāraṇam tasmāt pratiśākham vyavasthā prāpte tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati vyavatiṣṭhera auvartera kutas udgītha śākhā vyavasthāyām udgītham upāsīta sāmāya śrutiḥ pravṛttā satī viśeṣe pīḍitā etayāyyam śrutiḥ balīyasī sāmāya āśrayaḥ tasmāt svara udgītha śākhā gateṣu udgītha evaṃjātīyakāḥ pratyayāḥ syuḥ matra athavā atra śaṅkitavyaḥ katham aya śākhā gateṣu udgītha aya śākhā vihitāḥ pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ matra avirodha matrāṇām karmaṇām guṇāām śākhātara utpāām śākhātare upasaṃgrahaḥ yeṣām asau viiyogaḥ kukkuṭaḥ asi aśmā ādatte kuṭaruḥ asi yeṣām samidh prayājāḥ āmātāḥ teṣu āmāyate ṛtavaḥ vai prayājāḥ samāḥ atra hotavyāḥ yeṣām jāti viṣayaḥ matra varṇaḥ chāgasya vapāyāḥ medasaḥ ubrūhi evamādi matrāṇām vedātare parigrahaḥ bahvṛca paṭhitasya sūktasya yaḥ jātaḥ prathamaḥ adhvaryave sajaīyam śasyam atra parigrahaḥ tasmāt āśrayāṇām aṅgāām auvṛttiḥ āśritāām pratyayāām bhūmaḥ kratu bhūma adhikaraṇam prācīaśālaḥ aupamayavaḥ asyām ākhyāyikāyām vyastasya samastasya vaiśvāarasya upāsaam śrūyate vyasta upāsaam tāvat aupamayava kam ātmāam upāsse divam bhagavaḥ rājā eti ha uvāca eṣa vai su tejāḥ vaiśvāaraḥ yam ātmāam upāsse ityādi samasta upāsaam ha vai etasya ātmaaḥ vaiśvāarasya mūrdhā su tejāḥ viśva rūpaḥ vartmā saṃdehaḥ bahulaḥ vastiḥ rayiḥ pādau ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim vyastasya samastasya uta samastasya kim tāvat prāptam pratyavayavam su prabhṛtiṣu upāsse pada tasmāt tava sutam prasutam āsutam kule ityādi syuḥ prāptam abhidhīyate bhūmaḥ padārtha ātmakasya samastasya vaiśvāara upāsaasya jyāyastvam asmi vākye vivakṣitam bhavitum arhati avayava upāsaāām kratu kratuṣu darśa pūrṇamāsa prabhṛtiṣu sāmastye pradhā prayogaḥ ekaḥ vivakṣyate vyastāām prayogaḥ prayāja ādīām kutas etat jyāyāḥ śrutiḥ bhūmaḥ vākyatā avagamāt ekam idam vākyam vaiśvāara viṣayam paurvāparya ālocaāt pratīyate prācīaśāla prabhṛtayaḥ uddālaka avasāāḥ ṣaṭ ṛṣayaḥ vaiśvāara pariiṣṭhām pratipadyamāāḥ aśvapatim kaikeyam rājāam abhyājagmuḥ upakramya ekaikasya ṛṣeḥ upāsyam prabhṛtīām ekaikam śrāvayitvā mūrdhā eṣaḥ ha uvāca ityādiā mūrdha vidadhāti mūrdhā vyapatiṣyat yamām āgamiṣyaḥ ityādiā vyasta upāsaam puas vyasta upāsaam vyāvartya samasta upāsaam sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu sarveṣu ātmasu amatti bhūma āśrayam su prabhṛtiṣu śravaṇam draṣṭavyam upāsse pratyavayavam ākhyāta śravaṇam abhiprāya āuvāda vyasta upāsa vidhā tasmāt samasta upāsa pakṣaḥ śreyāḥ kecid atra samasta upāsa pakṣam jyāyāṃsam pratiṣṭhāpya jyāyas vacaāt kila vyasta upāsa pakṣam kalpayati ayuktam ekavākyatā avagatau satyām kalpa āyāyya mūrdhā vyapatiṣyat evamādi idam spaṣṭe sthe samasta upāsa avagame abhāvasya pūrvapakṣe vaktum aśakya sautrasya pramāṇavat abhiprāyeṇa adhikaraṇam pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe satyām sutejaḥ prabhṛtīām śrutau samastasya upāsaam prāptā buddhiḥ samasyaḥ upāsiṣyate vedya abhede bhedaḥ vijñātum śakyate vedyam rūpam vidyāyāḥ dravya daivatam iva yāgasya vedyaḥ īśvaraḥ āātve avagamyate kham kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ evamādiṣu ekaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ ha pitā mātā evamādiṣu vedya ekatvāt ekatvam āātvam pakṣe atara paratvāt arthakam tasmāt śākhā vihitam vedya vyapāśrayam jātam upasaṃhartavyam kārtsyāya prāpte pratipādyate vedya abhede evaṃjātīyakā bhiā bhavitum arhati kutas bhavati bhedaḥ kratum kurvīta evamādiḥ bhedaḥ hetuḥ samadhigataḥ purastāt atare bhedaḥ yathāsaṃbhavam hetavaḥ yojayitavyāḥ auvedaḥ ityādiṣu bhedaḥ avagamyate ayajati ityādi bhedaḥ eṣām atara katham bhedaḥ eṣa aubadha vedya īśvarasya upāsyasya prakaraṇam vyāvṛttāḥ guṇāḥ śiṣyate prāṇasya upāsyasya abhede ayādṛś guṇaḥ upāsitavyaḥ ayādṛś guṇaḥ ayatra aubadha bhedaḥ vijñāyate atra ekaḥ vidhayaḥ śakyam vaktum viigamaāyām pratiprakaraṇam guṇāḥ śrāvayitavyāḥ pratiprakaraṇam idam airākāṅkṣya avagamāt aikavākya atra vaiśvāara iva aparā bhūtvā ekavākyatām iyuḥ vedya aimitte tve bhūtvā tām iyuḥ vedya aimitte tve iraṅkuśe pratijñāyamāe samasta śakyaḥ pratijñāyeta tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate etasmin adhikaraṇe draṣṭavyam adhikaraṇam vicāryate kim āsām icchayā samuccayaḥ athavā sthita tāvat bhedasya samuccaya aiyame kiṃcid kāraṇam samuccaya aiyamaḥ ityatā śrutiḥ kāraṇam kāraṇam aiyamaḥ vidyātara adhikṛtasya vidyātara pāriśeṣyāt yāthākāmyam āpadyate au āsām yāyyaḥ kham kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ evamādyāḥ tulya īśvara prāpti phalā lakṣyate eṣa samā phaleṣu svarga sādhaeṣu karmasu yāthākāmya darśaāt tasmāt yāthākāmya prāptau ucyate āsām bhavitum arhati samuccayaḥ kasmāt aviśiṣṭa aviśiṣṭam āsām upāsya viṣaya sākṣātkaraṇam sākṣātkṛte upāsye viṣaye īśvara ādau dvitīyam aarthakam sākṣātkaraṇasya samuccaya pakṣe citta vikṣepa sākṣātkaraṇa sādhyam śrutayaḥ yasya syādaddhā vicikitsā itidevaḥ bhūtvā devāḥ apyeti evamādyāḥ smṛtayaḥ sadā bhāvitaḥ evamādyāḥ tasmāt phalāām vidyāām ayatamām ādāya tatparaḥ yāvat upāsya viṣaya sākṣātkaraṇe prāptam samuccīyeraa kāmya adhikaraṇam pratyudāharaṇam yāsu kāmyāsu vidyāsu saṃ yaḥ etam diśām vatsam veda rodam roditi yaḥ āma upāste yāva āmaḥ gatam yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati evamādyāsu ātmīyam sādhayatīṣu sākṣātkaraṇa samuccīyera samuccīyera pūrvasya ityasya hetoḥ adhikaraṇam udgītha ye āśritāḥ pratyayāḥ veda traya vihitāḥ kim samuccīyera kim syuḥ saṃśaye eṣām āśrayāḥ stotra saṃbhūya bhavati pratyayāḥ āśrayāḥ stotra triṣu vedeṣu śiṣyate āśritāḥ pratyayāḥ opadeśa kṛtaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ aṅgāām āśrayāṇām pratyayāām praṇava udgītha ekatva vijñā māhātmyāt udgātā utpaam kṣatam hautrāt karmaṇaḥ pratisamādadhāti bruva vedātara uditasya pratyayasya veda udita upasaṃhāram sūcayati guṇam āśrayam satam oṃkāram veda traya sādhāraṇam śrāvayati iyam trayī vartate om āśrāvayati om śaṃsati om udgāyati sādhāraṇyāt sādhāraṇyam darśam athavā yadi guṇāḥ udgītha prayoga sādhāraṇāḥ syuḥ āśrayāṇām pratyayāām sahabhāvaḥ udgītha grāhiṇā prayoga sādhāraṇāḥ śrāvyate sahabhāvāt sahabhāvaḥ āśritāām upāsaāām bhavitum arhati kutas veda vihitāām aṅgāām stotra ādīām sahabhāvaḥ śrūyate graham gṛhītvā camasam ūīya stotram upākaroti stutam auśaṃsati prastotar sāma gāya hotar etat yaja ityādiā aivam upāsaāām śrutiḥ eṣām sahabhāvam prāpayet brūmaḥ upāsaāām prayoga vacaḥ kratu arthāām udgītha ādīām sahabhāvam prāpayet udgītha upāsaāi kratu āśrayāṇi godoha avocām apṛthak pratibadhaḥ atra ayam āśrayaḥ viśeṣaḥ aṅgāām upāsaāām kratu dvayam akāraṇam upāsa asahabhāvasya pratiprayogam kārtsya upasaṃhārāt āśritāām vijñātum śakyam prayukta upāsaāām tatrāṇi kāmam mā aiyamam arhati tasmāt darśaāt śrutiḥ asahabhāvam pratyayāām evaṃvid ha vai brahmā yajñam ṛtvijaḥ bhiḥ akṣati upasaṃhāre vijñāavatā brahmaṇā paripālya saṃkīrtyeta tasmāt upāsaāām samuccayaḥ śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ adhikaraṇam asmāt svatatrāt sidhyati ācāryaḥ kutas etat avagamyate tarati śokam yaḥ ha vai paramam veda brahmā bhavati veda tāvat ciram vimokṣye saṃpatsye yaḥ apahata pāpmā upakramya lokān kāmān yaḥ tam ātmāam auvidya vai are draṣṭavyaḥ upakramya are khalu evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ kevalāyāḥ vidyāyāḥ śrāvayati atra pratyavatiṣṭhate yeṣu jaimiiḥ vrīhi prokṣaṇa viṣaya dvāreṇa saṃbadhi tasmi avagata prayojae jñāe yā śrutiḥ jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ ayeṣu dravya karmasu yasya parṇa mayī juhūḥ bhavati pāpam ślokam śrṛṇoti āṅkte bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte prayāja aūyājāḥ ijyate varma vai etat yajñasya kriyate varma yajamāāya bhrātṛvya abhibhūtyai evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ arthavādaḥ katham ārabhya adhītasya jñāasya kratu praveśaḥ āśaṅkyate dvāreṇa vākyāt avyabhicāriṇā kaścit dvāreṇa nimittaḥ vyabhicāri dvāram laukika vaidika sādhāraṇyāt tasmāt dvāreṇa jñāasya kratu saṃbadha vijñāasya vaidikebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ aupayogāt vyatirikta jñāam laukikeṣu karmasu upayujyate dṛṣṭārtha pravṛtti vaidikeṣu dehapāta kāla phaleṣu pravṛttiḥ opapadyate upayujyate vijñāam apahata pāpma asaṃsārya viṣayam aupaiṣadam pravṛtti aṅgam saṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ draṣṭavya apahata pāpma viśeṣaṇam bhaviṣyati prasādhitam etat asaṃsāri kāraṇam saṃsāriṇaḥ pāramārthikam svarūpam upaiṣatsu upadiśyate satyam prasādhitam dvāreṇa ākṣepa samādhāe kriyete dārḍhyāya darśaāt bhavati uddālaka ādīām vagamyate kevalāt jñāāt kimartham karmāṇi kuryuḥ videta kimartham parvatam vrajet yāyāt karoti śraddhayā upaiṣadā vīryavattaram bhavati vidyāyāḥ kevalāyāḥ samavārambhaṇāt tam karmaṇī samavārabhete ārambhe sāhitya darśaāt svātatryam vidyāyāḥ vidhāāt ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya yathāvidhāam guroḥ atiśeṣeṇa abhisamāvṛtya kuṭumbe śucau deśe svādhyāyam adhīyāaḥ evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ samasta veda vijñāavataḥ adhikāram tasmāt vijñāasya svātatryeṇa atra adhītya adhyaya vedasya śrūyate eṣa dṛṣṭārtha veda adhyayam avabodha paryatam sthitam iyamāt karmāṇi jijīviṣet śatam samāḥ tvayi lipyate are etat vai jarā maryam satram agihotram jarayā asmām ucyate mṛtyuḥ evaṃjātīyakāt iyamāt vidyāyāḥ prāpte pratividhatte tuśabdāt pakṣaḥ viparivartate opapadyate kasmāt yadi saṃsārī bhoktā vyatirekeṇa upadiṣṭaḥ prakāreṇa arthavāda adhikaḥ tāvat asaṃsārī īśvaraḥ saṃsāri rahita upahata pāpma viśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā karmaṇām pravartakam bhavati pratyuta karmāṇi ucchiatti vakṣyati atra tasmāt ūtaḥ ya matam bhagavataḥ tiṣṭhati prabhṛtibhiḥ hetvābhāsaiḥ cālayitum śakyate tam īśvaram śrutayaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhayam vajram udyatam etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya sṛjate evamādyāḥ saṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ vedya aukarṣaṇam kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ prāṇea prāṇiti sarvātaraḥ yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ upakramya etam uvyākhyāsyāmi evamādi mahataḥ iḥśvasitam etat ṛgvedaḥ śokam moham jarām mṛtyum atyeti upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ evamādibhiḥ śeṣaiḥ satyām upadidikṣāyām atyata abheda abhiprāyam pārameśvaram śārīrasya pāramārthikam svarūpam upādhi kṛtam śārīra tattvam asi draṣṭṛ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ sarvam etat vistareṇa asmābhiḥ purastāt varṇitam darśaam darśaāt śeṣaḥ atra brūmaḥ darśaam tve vidyāyāḥ śrutiḥ bhavati etat ha sma vai vidvāṃsaḥ āhuḥ ṛṣayaḥ kāvaṣeyāḥ kimarthāḥ vayam adhyeṣyāmahe kimarthāḥ vayam yakṣyāmahe etat ha sma vai juhavāṃcakrire etam vai tam am viditvā brāhmaṇāḥ eṣaṇāyāḥ vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ eṣaṇāyāḥ vyutthāya bhikṣā caryam carati evaṃjātīyakāḥ yājñavalkya ādīām vidām akarma eṣṭha are khalu ha uktvā yājñavalkyaḥ pravavrāje ityādi śrutibhyaḥ yakṣyamāṇaḥ vai bhagavataḥ ham asmi etat darśaam vaiśvāara viṣayam saṃbhavati upādhikāyām sāhitya darśaam atra puaruktam atra brūmaḥ asārvatrikī karoti eṣā śrutiḥ viṣayā abhisaṃbadhāt udgītha om etat udgītham upāsīta atra śata tam karmaṇī samavārabhete etat samavārambha vacam asvātatrye vidyāyāḥ pratyucyate utra draṣṭavyaḥ ayam avārabhate ayam śatam ābhyām dīyatām ukte vibhajya dīyate pañcāśat ekasmai pañcāśat aparasmai idam mumukṣu viṣayam kāmayamāaḥ saṃsāri viṣaya upasaṃhārāt kāmayamāaḥ mumukṣoḥ saṃsāri viṣaye vihitā pratiṣiddhā parigṛhyate vihitam pratiṣiddham prāpta āuvādi idam etat uttaram paṭhati adhyaya ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya atra adhyaya mātrasya adhyavasyāmaḥ avidyā adhikāraḥ karmasu prasajyeta eṣa prasañjyeta vayam adhyaya prabhavam avabodhaam kāraṇam vārayāmaḥ kim tarhi svātatryeṇa kāraṇatām pratipadyate etat pratipādayāmaḥ kratvatara jñāam kratvatara adhikāreṇa apekṣyate etat draṣṭavyam iyamāt atra abhidhīyate kurva karmāṇi jijīviṣet evamādiṣu iyama śravaṇeṣu viduṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ usti aviśeṣeṇa stuta yeumatiḥ kurve karmāṇi atra aparaḥ viśeṣaḥ ākhyāyate yadi atra vidvā kurve saṃbadhyeta etat draṣṭavyam lipyate are vakṣyati etat bhavati yāvajjīvam kurvati tvayi viduṣi puruṣe lepāya bhavati stūyate vidvāṃsaḥ pratyakṣīkṛta phalāḥ avaṣṭambhāt atara sādhaeṣu prajā prayojaā parāmṛśati śrutiḥ bhavati vājasaeyiām etat ha sma vai vidvān hetoḥ kāraka lakṣaṇasya samastasya prapañcasya avidyā kṛtasya āmaati sarvam abhūt ke kam paśyet ke kam jighret ityādiā siddhim ucchittiḥ prasajyeta tasmāt svātatryam vidyāyāḥ āśrameṣu śrūyate vidyāyāḥ vaidikāi karmāṇi etat ūrdhvaretasaḥ āśramāḥ śrūyate vedaḥ vaidikeṣu śabdeṣu avagamyate trayaḥ dharmaskadhāḥ ye imā iraṇye śraddhā tapaḥ upāsate tapaḥ śraddhe ye upavasati araṇye etam pravrājiḥ lokam icchataḥ pravrajati brahmacaryāt pravrajet evamādiṣu ūrdhvaretaḥ prasiddham tasmāt svātatryam vidyāyāḥ parāmarśa adhikaraṇam trayaḥ skadhāḥ ityādayaḥ ye śabdāḥ ūrdhvaretasām āśramāṇām sadbhāvāya udāhṛtāḥ pratipāda āya prabhavati eṣu śabdeṣu āśramātarāṇām jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ vidhim kutas atra atara eṣu trayaḥ skadhāḥ atra tāvat prathamaḥ tapaḥ dvitīyaḥ brahmacārī ācārya kula vāsī puṇya lokāḥ bhavati parāmarśa pūrvakam āśramāṇām aātyatika saṃkīrtya ātyatika saṃstha stūyate saṃsthaḥ umṛta eti parāmarśe āśramāḥ gamyate satyam gamyate ācārābhyām prasiddhiḥ virodhe ādaraṇīyāḥ bhaviṣyati adhikṛta viṣayāḥ gārhasthyam ūrdhvaretobhiḥ parāmṛṣṭam prathamaḥ satyam gṛhastham karmaṇām prasiddham astitvam tasmāt ayam pratyakṣā śrutiḥ āśramātaram vīra hā eṣa devāām yogim udvāsayate ācāryāya priyam dhaam āhṛtya mā vyavacchetsīḥ putrasya lokaḥ paśavaḥ viduḥ evamādyā ye imā iraṇye śraddhā tapa upāsate tapaḥ śraddhe ye upavasati araṇye āśramātara saṃdigdham tapaḥ dvitīyaḥ evamādiṣu etam lokam icchataḥ pravrajati saṃstavaḥ yam brahmacaryāt pravrajet vispaṣṭam idam pratyakṣam jābālāām satyam etat etām śrutim ayam vicāra draṣṭavyam auṣṭheyam auṣṭheyam āśramātaram ācāryaḥ āuṣṭheya dhikṛta āuṣṭheyam āśramātaram imām matim irākaroti gārhasthya āśramātaram aicchatā pratipattavyam kutas samā parāmarśa śrutiḥ trayaḥ skadhāḥ ityādyā atara vihitam gārhasthyam parāmṛṣṭam āśramātaram pratipattavyam atara prāptayoḥ ivīta prācīāvītayoḥ upavīta vākye tasmāt auṣṭheya etam lokam icchataḥ pravrajati samabhivyāhāraḥ ye cema iraṇye śraddhā tapaḥ upāsate pañcāgi tapaḥ dvitīyaḥ ityādiṣu āśrama ātarābhidhāam saṃdigdham eṣa iścaya sadbhāvāt trayaḥ skadhāḥ skadha pratijñātam bhūyāṃsaḥ dharmāḥ śakyate liṅgaḥ gṛha āśramaḥ ekaḥ brahmacārī āśramaiḥ deśaḥ tapaḥ ye imā iraṇye araṇya śraddhā tapobhyām āśrama tasmāt ayam āśramātarasya parāmarśa ekavākyatā pratītiḥ uparudhyeta pratīyate caṃ atra ekavākyatā puṇya phalāḥ trayaḥ skadhāḥ saṃsthatā phalā satyam etat satīm ekavākyatā pratītim parityajya abhyupagatavyaḥ atarasya ādarśaāt vispaṣṭāt āśrama ātara pratyayāt guṇavāda kalpaayā ekavākyatva yoja adhastāt samidham ekavākya pratītau vidhīyate dhāraṇam lakṣaṇe dhāraṇe āśrama parāmarśa śrutiḥ kalpyate yadā ayam āśramātarāṇām saṃstha tāvat saṃstava avaśyam vidheyā abhyupagatavyā kim caturṣu āśrameṣu yasya kasya cit āhosvit parivrājakasya vivektavyam yadi brahmacaryāteṣu āśrameṣu parāmṛśyamāeṣu parivrājakaḥ parāmṛṣṭaḥ caturṇām āśramāṇām parāmṛṣṭa āśrami aupapatteḥ yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati ath parāmṛṣṭaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāj saṃsthaḥ setsyati tapaḥ vaikhāasa grāhiṇā parāmṛṣṭaḥ parivrāj kecid ayuktam satyām gatau parivrājakaḥ grahaṇam arhati atra brahmacāri gṛhamedhiau asādhāraṇea svea svea viśeṣaṇea viśeṣitau bhikṣu vaikhāasau yuktam tapaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ kāya kleśa pradhā tapaḥ rūḍheḥ bhikṣoḥ dharmaḥ idriya saṃyama lakṣaṇayā catuṣṭve prasiddhāḥ āśramāḥ tritve parāmṛśyate ayāyyam utra bhavati trayaḥ puṇya bhājaḥ ekaḥ umṛta pṛthaktve uvakalpate bhavati devadatta yajñadattau mada prajñau ayataraḥ ayoḥ mahā prajñaḥ bhavati devadatta yajñadattau mada prajñau viṣṇumitraḥ mahā prajñaḥ tasmāt trayaḥ āśramiṇaḥ puṇya bhājaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāj katham saṃstha pravartamāaḥ saṃbhava parivrājakaḥ avatiṣṭheta rūḍhi āśrama mātrāt prāpteḥ jñā āarthakya atra ucyate saṃsthaḥ brahmaṇi parisamāptiḥ taiṣṭha abhidhīyate āśramāṇām saṃbhavati āśrama pratyavāya parivrājakasya saṃyāsāt pratyavāyaḥ saṃbhavati tadīyaḥ dharmaḥ saṃsthāyāḥ upodbalakaḥ virodhī brahmaiṣṭha upabṛṃhitam āśrama vihitam vyatikrame pratyavāyaḥ yāsaḥ brahmā brahmā brahmā vai tapāṃsi yāsaḥ atyarecayat saṃyāsa yoga atayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ smṛtayaḥ ityādyāḥ saṃsthasya tasmāt parivrājakasya āśrama mātrāt prāpteḥ jñā āāarthakya eṣaḥ āvatarati parāmarśe āśramāṇām pārivrājyam tāvat saṃstha lakṣaṇam labhyeta jābāla śrutim āśramātara vidhāyiīm ayam ācāryeṇa vicāraḥ pravartitaḥ vidyate āśramātara śrutiḥ pratyakṣā brahmacaryam samāpya gṛhī bhavet gṛhī bhūtvā vaī bhavet vaī bhūtvā pravrajet yadi itarathā brahmacaryāt pravrajet gṛhāt iyam śrutiḥ aadhikṛta viṣayā śakyā vaktum vratī avratī sātakaḥ sātakaḥ ityādiā jñā paripāka pārivrājyasya parivrāj vivarṇa vāsāḥ muṇḍa uparigrahaḥ śuciḥ adrohī bhaikṣāṇaḥ bhūyāya bhavati tasmāt siddhāḥ ūrdhvaretasām āśramāḥ siddham vidhāāt vidyāyāḥ svātatryam upādāāt iāpūrva adhikaraṇam eṣa rasāām rasatamaḥ paramaḥ parārdhyaḥ aṣṭamaḥ udgīthaḥ iyam ṛgagiḥ sāma ayam vāva lokaḥ idam uktham iyam evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ kim udgītha ādeḥ āhosvit upāsa āvidhi saṃśaye yuktam udgītha aṅgāi upādāya iyam juhūḥ ādityaḥ kūrmaḥ svargaḥ lokaḥ āhavaīyaḥ ityādyāḥ juhū etya āsām śrutīām yuktam tāyām apūrvaḥ ṛthaḥ vihitaḥ bhavati tāyām āarthakyam vidhāyakasya stutiḥ upayujyate ekavākya arthe vidhīām syuḥ atra atara vihitāām udgītha ādīām iyam atara paṭhitā stutiḥ apratipadyamāā aarthikā iyam juhūḥ ityādi saṃidhau amātam vaiṣamyam tasmāt evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ udgītham upāsīta sāma upāsīta aham uktham asmi vidyāt ityādayaḥ vispaṣṭāḥ śabdāḥ śrūyate prayojaa tāyām vyāhayera smaraṇam kuryāt kriyeta kartavyam bhavet pañcamam etat vedeṣu iyatam lakṣaṇam liṅ smarati prakaraṇam śrāvyate āpayitā ha vai kāmāām bhavati eṣa kalpate ha asmai lokāḥ ūrdhvāḥ āvṛttāḥ tasmāt udgītha śrutayaḥ adhikaraṇam ha yājñavalkyasya dve bhārye babhūvatuḥ maitreyī kātyāyaī pratardaaḥ ha vai daivodāsiḥ idrasya priyam dhāma upajagāma jāaśrutiḥ ha pautrāyaṇaḥ śraddhā deyaḥ bahu dāyī bahu pākyaḥ āsa evamādiṣu saṃśayaḥ kim imāi prayoga arthāi āhosvit saṃihita pratipatti imāḥ ākhyā aśrutayaḥ ākhyā sāmāyāt ākhyā prayogasya pāriplave codita pradhā matra prayoga kasmāt pāriplavam ācakṣīta prakṛtya mauḥ vaivasvataḥ rājā evamādi kāicid viśeṣyate ākhyā sāmāyāt aarthakam idam viśeṣaṇam bhavet tasmāt etāḥ ākhyā aśrutayaḥ ekavākyatā upabadhāt tve ākhyāāām saṃihita pratipāda upayogi yāyyā ekavākyatā upabadhāt saṃihitābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ ekavākyatā praroca upayogāt pratipatti saukarya upayogāt maitreyībrāhmaṇe tāvat vai are draṣṭavyaḥ ityādyayā ekavākyatā asmi ityādyayā atra vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ ityādyayā ātman o vapām udakhidat evamādīām gatāām ākhyāām saṃihita tasmāa āgīdha etat viśiṣya abhidhīyate yaḥ divā praiti raśmī ūrdhvam ākramate yaḥ rātrau vidvā rātri prāyaṇa aparādha mātreṇa ūrdhvam ākrameta pākṣika phalā apravṛttiḥ tasyām rātrau uparataḥ hara āgamam udīkṣeta yogiḥ ayam ahar kāla viiyogaḥ āvṛttaye yoga sāṃkhye śraute viṣaya pramāṇa smārtasya kāla viiyogasya śrauteṣu vijñāeṣu avatāraḥ agiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam dhūmaḥ rātriḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ vai puruṣaḥ asmāt lokāt praiti āgacchati vijihīte ratha cakrasya kham ūrdhvam ākramate ādityam āgacchati etasmāt ādityāt vāyoḥ darśaāt abda ādityayoḥ atarāle vāyuḥ iva īśayitavyaḥ kasmāt puarageḥ paratva darśaāt arciṣoataram vāyuḥ iva īśyate eṣa viśeṣaḥ vadāmaḥ śrutiḥ etam yāam āsādya āgi lokam āgacchati vāyu lokam varuṇa lokam ucyate kevalaḥ tra pāṭhaḥ paurvāparyeṇa avasthitaḥ krama vacaḥ kaścid padārtha upadarśa amātram atra kriyate etam etam āgacchati ratha cakra mātreṇa chidreṇa ūrdhvam ākramya ādityam āgacchati avagamyate kramaḥ tasmāt sūktam vājasaeyiḥ māsebhyaḥ lokam lokāt ādityam lokāt abhisaṃbhaveyuḥ chadoga chādogya vājasaeyakayoḥ ekatra lokaḥ vidyate paratra saṃvatsaraḥ dvaya pratyayāt ubhau ubhayatra grathayitavyau māsa saṃbadhāt saṃvatsaraḥ pūrvaḥ paścimaḥ lokaḥ vivektavyam taḍitaḥ sambadhāt taḍit adhikaraṇam ādityāt cadramasam cadramasaḥ vidyutam asyāḥ vidyutaḥ upariṣṭāt varuṇa lokam ayam saṃbadhyeta vidyut varuṇayoḥ yadā viśālāḥ vidyutaḥ jīmūta udareṣu praṛtyati prapatati vidyotate staayati varṣiṣyati brāhmaṇam apām varuṇa prasiddhiḥ varuṇāt adhi sthāātara pāṭha varuṇa ādīām iva īśaḥ vaiśeṣika sthāā vidyut atyā ādau ātivāhika adhikaraṇam teṣu saṃśayaḥ kim uta bhogabhūmayaḥ athavā mārga bhūtāḥ tāvat prāptam upadeśasya kaścid grāmam agaram gaccha itas amum girim yagrodham adīm grāmam agaram prāpsyasi arciṣaḥ har ahar āpūryamāṇapakṣam ityādi bhogabhūmayaḥ prāptam agi lokam āgacchati ityādi prāṇiām bhāṣyate mauṣya lokaḥ pitṛ lokaḥ lokaḥ brāhmaṇam ahar rātreṣu lokeṣu sajjate ityādi aceta eṣām ātivāhika aupapattiḥ cetaāḥ puruṣāḥ durgeṣu mārgeṣu ativāhyāḥ ativāhayati prāpte brūmaḥ bhavitum arhati kutas vidyutam puruṣaḥ māavaḥ etā gamayati siddha gamayitṛ viṣayam upakṣīṇam viśeṣaṇasya yadi puruṣāḥ gamayitāraḥ prāptāḥ māavāḥ yuktam viśeṣaṇam amāavaḥ agamakam vyāmohāt ye tāvat mārga gāḥ saṃpiṇḍita karaṇa grāmāḥ asvatatrāḥ ādīām acetaa asvātatryam abhimāiaḥ cetaā viśeṣāḥ atiyātrāyām gamyate matta mūrchita saṃpiṇḍita karaṇāḥ bhavati avasthita ādīnām mārga upapattiḥ rātrau pretasya ahar abhisaṃbhavaḥ purastāt dhruva bhavati eṣām arciṣaḥ haḥ ityādi nirdeśaḥ ātivāhika tve virudhyate arciṣā hetuā ahar abhisaṃbhavati ahar hetuā āpūryamāṇapakṣam prasiddheṣu ātivāhikeṣu evaṃjātīyakaḥ gaccha itas balavarmāṇam jayasiṃham kṛṣṇaguptam upakrame rciḥ abhisaṃbhavati saṃbadha saṃbadha viśeṣaḥ kaścid upasaṃhāre etāḥ gamayati upakrame saṃpiṇḍita karaṇa saṃbhavaḥ aupabhuñjāeṣu gatṛṣu gamayitum śakyate bhogabhūmi agi svāmikam lokam prāptaḥ ativāhyate vāyu svāmikam prāptaḥ yojayitavyam katham ātivāhika pakṣe varuṇa saṃbhavaḥ vidyutaḥ adhi varuṇa upakṣiptāḥ vidyutaḥ prāpteḥ amāavasya puruṣasya gamayitṛ uttaram paṭhati vidyut abhisaṃbhavaāt ūrdhvam puruṣeṇa lokam gacchati avagatavyam etya lokam gamayati gamayitṛ varuṇa śakyate varṇayitum dvitīya viṣaya bodha ātmaā abhiiṣpadyate ācāryaḥ upayāsāt pāramārthika caitaya vyavahāra pūrvasya upayāsa vagatasya brāhmasya aiaiśvarya rūpasya pratyākhyāāt ācāryaḥ saṃkalpa adhikaraṇam hārdavidyāyām śrūyate yadi pitṛ kāmaḥ bhavati pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ityādi saṃśayaḥ kim saṃkalpaḥ kevalaḥ pitṛ samutthāe hetuḥ uta imitta atara sahitaḥ śravaṇe imitta atara yuktā gama hetubhyaḥ pitṛ bhavati muktasya viparītam kalpitam bhaviṣyati rājñaḥ iva saṃkalpita siddhi karīm sādhaātara sāmagrīm sulabhām yokṣyate saṃkalpa samutthāāḥ pitṛ maoratha vijṛmbhita cañcala puṣkalam bhogam samarpayitum paryāptāḥ syuḥ prāpte brūmaḥ kevalāt kutas pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ityādikā śrutiḥ imittātara apekṣāyām pīḍyeta imittātaram yadi bhavatu prayata atara saṃpādyam imittātaram iṣyate vadhya saṃkalpa avagamye rthe sāmāyataḥ kramate saṃkalpa balāt eṣām yāvat sthairya upapattiḥ prākṛta saṃkalpa tvā saṃkalpasya āaya avadhya saṃkalpa vidvāḥ bhavati āsya ayaḥ dhipatiḥ bhavati saṃkalpaya satyām gatau saṃkalpayati śrutiḥ etat yaḥ am vrajati etān satyā kāmān sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati adhikaraṇam pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati tāvat saṃkalpa sādhaam siddham idriyāṇi prāpta aiśvaryasya viduṣaḥ samīkṣyate tāvat ācāryaḥ śarīrasya idriyāṇām viduṣaḥ kasmāt kāmā paśya ramate yaḥ yadi maasā idriyaiḥ vihareta tasmāt idriyāṇām mokṣe jaimiiḥ jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ śarīrasya idriyasya muktam ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādiā ekadhābhāva vikalpam ekavidha śarīrabhede āñjasī yadi bhūmavidyāyām ayam ekadhābhāva paṭhyate idam saguṇa avasthāyām aiśvaryam bhūmavidyā saṃkīrtyate upatiṣṭhate ucyate aha ācāryaḥ darśaāt ubhayavidha sādhu yadā tām saṃkalpayati śarīraḥ bhavati yadā aśarīra tām aśarīraḥ saṃkalpa saṃkalpa vaicitryāt aha ahaḥ satram bhavati darśaāt idam tavabhāve sadhya yadā taoḥ idriyasya śarīrasya saṃdhye idriya viṣayeṣu vidyamāeṣu mātrāḥ pitṛ kāmāḥ bhavati mokṣe syuḥ etat puaḥ jāgarite pitṛ kāmā bhavati muktasya adhikaraṇam atra muktasya tridhā kim śarīrāṇi dāruyatra sṛjyate kim asmat bhavati vīkṣā maasoḥ aupapatteḥ śarīreṇa itarāṇi śarīrāṇi prāpte pratipadyate pradīpaḥ ekaḥ āpadyate ekaḥ vidvāḥ aiśvarya āpadya śarīrāṇi āviśati kutas śāstram ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati pañcadhā saptadhā avadhā ityādi jīvātara āveśe śarīrāṇām pravṛttiḥ saṃbhavati maasoḥ aupapatteḥ yoga eṣa aparāṇi śarīrāṇi saṃkalpa srakṣyati sṛṣṭeṣu teṣu upādhi adhiṣṭhātṛ yokṣyate eṣā yoga śāstreṣu yoga prakriyā katham muktasya āveśa lakṣaṇam aiśvaryam abhyupagamyate yāvatā dvitīyam vibhaktam salilaḥ ekaḥ draṣṭā advaitaḥ bhavati evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ vijñāam vārayati uttaram paṭhati sampattyoḥ ayatara apyayaḥ suṣuptam svam apītaḥ bhavati tasmāt eam svapiti apyeti tayoḥ ayatarām avasthām etat kvacid suṣupta avasthām ucyate kvacid kaivalya avasthām katham avagamyate etat vaśāt etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya pretya sarvam bhūt suptaḥ kaṃcaa kāmam kāmayate kaṃcaa svapam paśyati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ etat svarga avasthātaram etat aiśvaryam upavarṇyate tasmāt adoṣaḥ asaṃihita adhikaraṇam ye saguṇa upāsa īśvara sāyujyam vrajati kim iravagraham aiśvaryam bhavati āhosvit sāvagraham saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam iraṅkuśam eṣām aiśvaryam bhavitum arhati svārājyam smai devāḥ balim āvahati sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ prāpte paṭhati vyāpāram varjayitvā ayat aṇima ātmakam aiśvaryam muktāām bhavitum arhati vyāpāraḥ asiddhasya īśvarasya kutas asaṃihita īśvaraḥ vyapāra idhi kṛtaḥ tam prakṛtya tam prakṛtya aveṣaṇa vijijñāsaa pūrvakam aṇima aiśvaryam śrūyate samaaska eteṣām aaikamatye kasyacid abhiprāyaḥ kasyacid saṃhāra abhiprāyaḥ kadācid kasyacid saṃkalpa mau ayasya saṃkalpaḥ samarthyeta parameśvara ākūta tatratvam vyavatiṣṭhate svārājyam ityādi irava graham aiśvaryam viduṣām yāyyam parihartavyam atra ucyate ādhikārikaḥ yaḥ savitṛ īśvaraḥ āyattā iyam svārājya ucyate yatkāraṇam maasaspatim yaḥ maasām patiḥ siddhaḥ īśvaraḥ tam prāpa etat bhavati ausāreṇa vākpatiḥ cakṣuṣpatiḥ śrotra patiḥ vijñāa patiḥ bhavati ayatra yathāsaṃbhavam asiddha īśvara āyattam aiśvaryam yojayitavyam amuktam pārameśvaram rūpam kevalam gocaram savitṛ adhiṣṭhāam dvi rūpām mahimā jyāyāḥ puruṣaḥ pādaḥ pādasya amṛtam divi iḥ rūpam prāpuvati śakyam vaktum kratu dvirūpe parameśvare iḥ guṇam rūpam avāpya guṇaḥ avatiṣṭhate guṇe iḥ avagraham aiśvaryam avāpya avagrahaḥ avatiṣṭhate draṣṭavyam jyotiṣaḥ smṛtī sūryaḥ bhāti cadra tārakam imāḥ vidyutaḥ bhāti kutas yam agiḥ bhāsayate sūryaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ pāvakaḥ jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham abhiprāyaḥ itas aiśvaryam yasmāt eṣām śrūyate tam apaḥ vai khalu mīyate etām devatām bhūtāy avati ha evaṃvidam bhūtāy avati etasyai devatāyai sāyujyam salokatām jayati ityādi liṅgebhyaḥ sātiśaya tavat aiśvaryasya eṣām prasajyeta uttaram bhagavā ācāryaḥ paṭhati parvaṇā pathā ye lokam ukta viśeṣaṇam gacchati ha vai madīyam saraḥ yasmi aśvatthaḥ somasavaḥ yasmi aparājitā pūḥ brahmaṇaḥ yasmin prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam veśma yaḥ ekadhā matra arthavāda pradeśeṣu prapañcyate tam prāpya cadra lokāt iva bhukta bhogāḥ āvartate kutas eti puar etea pratipadyamāā imam māavam āvartam āvartate lokam abhisaṃpadyate abhisaṃpadyate āvartate aiśvaryasya varṇitam atra samyak darśa avidhvasta tamasām asiddha irvāṇa parāyaṇāām siddhā saguṇa śaraṇāām āvṛtti sūtra abhyāsaḥ parisamāptim dyotayati śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācārya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ śrīmat śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣyam saṃpūrṇam murat
